17O||1||1||Nish haink eh gy-kione ayns lhing Ahasuerus (shoh yn Ahasuerus shen ren reill  voish India eer gys Ethiopia, harrish shey-feed as shiaght rheamyn)    
17O||1||2||Ayns ny laghyn shen, tra va ree Ahasuerus ny hoie er stoyl-reeoil e reeriaght,  va ayns Shushan yn phlaase reeoil,    
17O||1||3||Ayns y trass vlein jeh e reill, ren eh cuirraghyn da ooilley e phrinceyn, as  e harvaantyn; pooaraghyn Phersia as Media, ard gheiney as princeyn ny rheamyn ec  y traa cheddin kionfenish.    
17O||1||4||Tra hoilshee eh magh berchys e reeriaght ghloyroil, as onnor e ard-ooashley  reeoil, ymmodee laghyn, eer nuy-feed laa.    
17O||1||5||As lurg da ny laghyn shoh ve harrish, ren y ree cuirraghyn da ooilley yn pobble  va ry-gheddyn ayns Shushan y phlaase, chammah da ard as injil son shiaght laa, ayns  cooyrtyn garey plaase y ree,    
17O||1||6||Raad va curtanyn baney, geayney, as gorrym, sheeynt er coyrdyn dy heeidey purple,  lesh loopyn argid, as pillaryn marble: as nyn ynnydyn-soie dy airh, as argid, er  laare dy phurple, as gorrym, as bane, as doo,    
17O||1||7||As hirveish ad jough orroo ayns siyn airhey (va ny siyn jeh dagh sorch) as palchey  dy feeyn reeoil, cooie rish stayd y ree.    
17O||1||8||As va'n giu cordail rish y leigh, cha row fer erbee eginit: son shoh myr doardee  yn ree da ooilley fir-oik e hie, dy row dy chooilley ghooinney dy ghoaill myr baillish.     
17O||1||9||Ren Vashti yn ven-rein myrgeddin cuirraghyn son ny mraane, ayns thie reeoil  Ahasuerus.    
17O||1||10||Er y chiaghtoo laa, tra va cree yn ree gennal lesh feeyn, doardee eh Mehuman,  Biztha, Harboua, Bigtha, as Abagtha, Zethar, as Carcas, ny shiaght ard fir-oik, va  shirveish fenish Ahasuerus yn ree,    
17O||1||11||Dy chur lhieu Vashti yn ven-rein kiongoyrt rish y ree, ceau yn attey reeoil  dy yeeaghyn da'n pobble as ny princeyn yn aalid eck, son v'ee feer aalin dy yeeaghyn  urree.    
17O||1||12||Agh dob Vashti yn ven-rein dy heet er sarey yn ree liorish ny fir-oik: va'n  ree, er-y-fa shen, feer jymmoosagh, as ren e chorree lostey cheu-sthie jeh.    
17O||1||13||Eisht dooyrt y ree rish ny deiney creeney, va toiggal cooishyn (son shoh va  cliaghtey yn ree dy ghoaill y choyrle ocsyn va tushtagh ayns leigh as briwnys: 
17O||1||14||As ny ard-gheiney jeu shoh va Carshena, Shethar, Admatha, Tarshish, Meres,  Marsena, as Memucan, shiaght princeyn Phersia as Media, as fir-choyrlee kinjagh y  ree, as ayns ard phooar ayns y reeriaght).   
17O||1||15||Cre nee mayd rish Vashti yn ven-rein cordail rish y leigh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel  ee er choyrt biallys da sarey yn ree Ahasuerus, liorish e hirveishee?   
17O||1||16||As dreggyr Memucan ayns fenish y ree as ny princeyn, Cha nee da'n ree ny-lomarcan  ta'n ven-rein er n'yannoo aggair, agh myrgeddin da ooilley ny princeyn, as da ooilley  yn pobble t'ayns slane reeriaght ree Ahasuerus.   
17O||1||17||Son shoh ta'n ven-rein er n'yannoo ayns clashtyn ooilley ny mraane, myr shen  dy jean ad beg y hoiaghey jeh ny deiney oc, tra hed y skeeal magh, Doardee ree Ahasuerus  Vashti yn ven-rein dy heet stiagh kiongoyrt rish, agh cha daink ee.   
17O||1||18||Yn ansoor cheddin ver ooilley mraane seyr Phersia as Media nish, da ooilley  princeyn y ree, ta er chlashtyn jeh ymmyrkey yn ven-rein. As bee shoh oyr lane mee  viallys as anvea.   
17O||1||19||My s'gooidsave lesh y ree, lhig da jannoo sarey reeoil, as lhig da ve scruit  mastey leighyn ny Persianee, as ny Medeyn, nagh bee er ny chaghlaa, nagh jig Vashti  arragh ayns fenish ree Ahasuerus, as lhig da'n ree stowal y stayd reeoil eck er unnane  elley ta ny share na ish.   
17O||1||20||As tra vees sarey yn ree er ny ockley magh trooid e slane reeriaght (son s'mooar  te) ver ooilley ny mraane onnor da ny deiney oc, chammah ard as injil.   
17O||1||21||As va'n choyrle mie ayns shilley yn ree, as ny princeyn, as ren y ree cordail  rish goan Vemucan:   
17O||1||22||Son hug eh screeunyn trooid ooilley rheamyn y ree gys dy chooilley ard cordail  rish nyn aght screeuee, as gys dy chooilley phobble lurg nyn ghlare hene, dy row  dy chooilley ghooinney dy ymmyrkey reill ayns e hie hene, as dy beagh shoh er ny  ockley magh ayns glare dy chooilley phobble. 
17O||2||1||Lurg ny reddyn shoh, tra va farg ree Ahasuerus er ny veeinaghey dy chooinee  eh er Vashti, as ny v'ee er n'yannoo, as y decree hie magh noi eck.   
17O||2||2||Eisht dooyrt fir-oik y ree va shirveish er, Lhig da moidynyn aegey as aalin  v'er ny gheddyn da'n ree:   
17O||2||3||As lhig da'n ree pointeil fir-oik ayns ooilley rheamyn e reeriaght, dy haglym  cooidjagh ooilley ny moidynyn aegey as aalin gys Shushan y phlaase, gys thie ny mraane,  fo kiarail Hege shamyrlin y ree, oaseir ny mraane, as lhig da spiceyn-oonlee cour  glenney v'er ny choyrt daue:   
17O||2||4||As lhig da'n voidyn share by-haittin lesh y ree, ve yn ven-rein ayns ynnyd Vashti.  As va'n raa cordail rish aigney yn ree, as shen myr ren eh.   
17O||2||5||Nish ayns Shushan y phlaase, va Hew dy row, enmyssit Mordecai, mac Jair, mac  Shimei, mac Kish, ny Venjamite:   
17O||2||6||Va goit ersooyl veih Jerusalem, ayns y chappeeys marish Jeconiah ree Yudah,  ren Nebuchadnezzar ree Vabylon y chur lesh ersooyl.   
17O||2||7||As va Hadassah (ta shen Esther) inneen e naim troggit liorish, son cha row ayr  ny moir eck, as va'n ven aeg aalin as stoamey, ee ghow Mordecai (lurg baase yn ayr  as y voir eck) son e lhiannoo hene.   
17O||2||8||Myr shen haink eh gykione, tra va sarey as oardagh y ree er ny chlashtyn, as  tra va ymmodee moidynyn er nyn jaglym cooidjagh gys Shushan y phlaase fo currym Hegai,  dy row Esther myrgeddin er ny choyrt lh'ee gys thie yn ree, fo kiarail Hegai, 
17O||2||9||As by-laik lesh y ven aeg, as yeeagh eh foayr jee, as hug eh jee chelleeragh  spiceyn oonlee ry-hoi glenney, marish lheid ny reddyn as va cooie er e son, as shiaght  mraane aegey va dy hirveish urree, ass thie yn ree, as phoint eh jeeish as da ny  mraane eck, yn reih ynnyd va ayns thie ny mraane.    
17O||2||10||Cha row Esther foast er n'insh quoi va'n sleih-mooinjerey, ny'n kynney eck:  son va Mordecai er choyrt currym gyere urree, nagh n'inshagh ee eh.    
17O||2||11||As huill Mordecai dy chooilley laa roish cooyrt thie ny mraane dy vriaght kys  va Esther, as cre'n erree harragh urree.    
17O||2||12||Nish tra haink shayll dagh moidyn mygeayrt, dy gholl stiagh gys ree Ahasuerus,  erreish j'ee v'er ve daa vee jeig, cordail rish cliaghtey mraane, (son shoh myr va  nyn laghyn glennee cooilleenit, ta shen dy ghra shey meeaghyn lesh myrrh, as shey  meeagh yn lesh spiceyn millish, as lesh reddyn elley cooie son mraane y ghlenney.)    
17O||2||13||Eisht er yn aght shoh haink dagh ben aeg gys y ree, va, cre-erbee hirragh ee  coyrt jee, dy gholl maree ass thie ny mraane, gys plaase y ree.    
17O||2||14||Ayns yn astyr hie ee stiagh, as er laa-ny-vairagh haink ee magh, gys yn nah  hie va cour ny mraane fo currym Shaashgaz shamyrder y ree, va currym ny co-lhiabbee  er: cha daink ee arragh stiagh gys y ree, mannagh ghow yn ree taitnys aynjee, as  fegooish yn ennym ec ve eit. 
17O||2||15||Nish tra va coorse Esther, inneen Abihail, naim Mordecai (va er ghoaill ee  son e lhiannoo hene) er jeet mygeayrt dy gholl stiagh gys y ree, cha hir ee veg,  agh ny ren Hegai shamyrder y ree, va currym ny mraane er phointeil: as va Esther  dy mooar soit j'ee son e aalid, 'sy chilley ocsyn ooilley honnick ee.   
17O||2||16||Myr shoh va Esther goit stiagh liorish ree Ahasuerus, gys e phlaase reeoil,  ayns y jeihoo vee (ta shen yn vee Tebeth) 'sy chiaghtoo vlein jeh e reill.   
17O||2||17||As bynney lesh y ree Esther, erskyn ooilley ny mraane, as hooar ee foayr as  aigney mie ayns e hilley, erskyn ooilley ny moidynyn; myr shen dy hoie eh yn crown  reeoil er y chione eck, as ren eh ee yn ven-rein, ayns ynnyd Vashti:   
17O||2||18||Eisht ren y ree cuirraghyn mooar da ooilley e phrinceyn, as e ir-oik, eer cuirraghyn  Esther, as ren eh mial keeshyn ny rheamyn, as hug eh giootyn, cordail rish stayd  y ree.   
17O||2||19||As tra va ny moidynyn er nyn jaglym cooidjagh yn nah cheayrt, eisht hoie Mordecai  ayns giat y ree.   
17O||2||20||Cha hoilshee Esther foast yn sleih mooinjerey, ny yn kynney eck; myr va Mordecai  er harey ee: son ren Esther er  raa 
17O||2||21||Ayns ny laghyn shen (choud as va Mordecai ny hoie ayns giat y ree) va jees  jeh shamyrderyn y ree, Bigthan as Teresh jeusyn va freayll yn dorrys, lhieent lesh  farg, as fieau er caa dy stroie ree Ahasuerus:   
17O||2||22||As hooar Mordecai fys er shoh, as dinsh eshyn eh da Esther yn ven-rein, as  ren Esther y chooish y hoilshaghey da'n ree, ayns ennym Vordecai.   
17O||2||23||As tra va briaght jeant 'sy chooish, ve er ny gheddyn magh; v'ad ny-neesht,  er-y-fa shen, croghit er billey: as ve scruit ayns lioar ny recortyssyn fenish y  ree. 
17O||3||1||Lurg ny reddyn shoh, ren ree Ahasuerus soiaghey seose Haman mac Hammedatha yn  Agagite, as hrog eh gys ard-olk eh, as hoie eh eh erskyn ooilley ny princeyn va marish.    
17O||3||2||As ren ooilley sharvaantyn y ree, va ayns giat y ree, croymmey as ooashley choyrt  da Haman, son shen myr doardee yn ree mychione echey: agh cha chroym Mordecai, chamoo  hug eh ooashley da.   
17O||3||3||Eisht dooyrt sharvaantyn y ree, va ayns giat y ree, rish Mordecai, Cre'n-fa  t'ou brishey sarey yn ree?   
17O||3||4||Nish haink eh gy-kione, tra loayr ad rish gagh-laa, as nagh dug eh geill daue,  dy dinsh ad da Haman, dy yeeaghyn cre'n erree harragh er Mordecai, as e chooish,  son v'eh er n'insh daue, dy row eh ny Hew.   
17O||3||5||As tra honnick Haman, nagh chroym Mordecai huggey, as nagh dug eh ooashley da,  eisht va Haman lane dy sproght.    
17O||3||6||As cha beeagh lesh e laueyn y choyrt er Mordecai ny-lomarcan, son v'ad er n'insh  da mychione pobble Vordecai: hir Haman er-y-fa shen, caa dy stroie ooilley ny Hewnyn  va trooid magh slane reeriaght Ahasuerus, eer pobble Vordecai.    
17O||3||7||Ayns y chied vee (ta shen yn vee Nisan) ayns y nah vlein yeig jeh reill Ahasuerus,  hilg ad Pur, ta shen, yn lot, fenish Haman, laa lurg laa, as veih mee dy mee, gys  y nah vee yeig, ta shen, yn vee Adar.    
17O||3||8||As dooyrt Haman rish ree Ahasuerus, Ta ashoon dy leih t'er skeayley dy lhean  mastey dty phobble, ayns dy chooilley ard jeh dty reeriaght, as ta leighyn oc er-lheh  noi leighyn dy chooilley phobble, chamoo t'ad freayll leighyn y ree, er-y-fa shen  cha vel eh son vondeish y ree dy chur raad daue.    
17O||3||9||My s'gooidsave lesh y ree, lhig da oardagh ve jeant, dy bee ad er nyn stroie:  as eeck-yms jeih thousane talent dy argid gys tashtaghyn y ree, liorish ny laueyn  ocsyn vees currym yn obbyr shoh orroo.    
17O||3||10||As ghow yn ree fainey jeh e laue, as hug eh eh da Haman mac Hammedatha yn Agagite,  noid ny Hewnyn.    
17O||3||11||As dooyrt y ree rish Haman, Lhiat hene yn argid, as y sleih myrgeddin, dy yannoo  roo lurg dty aigney hene.    
17O||3||12||Eisht va scrudeyryn y ree er ny eam yn trass laa yeig jeh yn chied vee, as  ve scruit cordail rish ooilley ny doardee Haman dauesyn v'ayns pooar fo yn ree, gys  ny kiannoortyn va harrish dy chooilley heer, as fir reill dagh pobble, cordail rish  yn aght screeuee oc hene, as gys dy chooilley ashoon lurg nyn ghlare; ayns ennym ree Ahasuerus  hie eh er scrieu, as ve sealit lesh fainey 
17O||3||13||As hie ny screeunyn lesh postyn gys ooilley cheeraghyn y ree, dy choyrt mow,  dy varroo, as dy stroie ooilley ny Hewnyn, chammah aeg as shenn, cloan aegey as mraane  'syn un laa, eer y trass laa yeig jeh'n nah vee yeig (ta shen yn vee Adar) as dy  ghoaill y chooid oc son spooilley.    
17O||3||14||Va copy yn order son dagh cheer, er ny ockley magh da dy chooilley phobble,  ad dy ve aarloo er y laa shen.    
17O||3||15||Hie ny postyn magh ayns fiyr, liorish sarey yn ree, as va'n oardagh jeant ayns  Shushan y phlaase: as hoie yn ree as Haman sheese dy iu, agh va (ny Hewnyn ayns)  ard-valley Shushan dy mooar seaghnit.
17O||4||1||Tra cheayll Mordecai kys myr ve kiarit, raip Mordecai e choamrey as hug eh er  aanrit-sack lesh leoie, as hie eh magh gys mean yn ard-valley, as cheayn eh lesh  coraa ard as sharroo.    
17O||4||2||As haink eh roish giat y ree: son cha row unnane erbee dy gholl stiagh er giat  y ree ayns aanrit-sack.   
17O||4||3||As ayns dy chooilley heer, raad erbee dy daink oardagh y ree, va dobberan trome  mastey ny Hewnyn, as trostey, as keayney, as yllaghey, as lhie ymmodee ayns aanrit  sack as leoie.   
17O||4||4||Er shoh haink sharvaantyn Esther, as ny shamyrderyn eck, as dinsh ad shoh jee:  eisht va'n ven-rein erskyn towse seaghnit, as hug ee coamrey dy chur er Mordecai,  as dy ghoaill jeh yn aanrit-sack: agh cha ghow eh eh.   
17O||4||5||Eisht deie Esther son Hatach fer jeh shamyrderyn y ree, va pointit dy hirveish  urree, as hug ee lesh chaghteraght gys Mordecai, dy gheddyn fys kys va shoh, as cre'n-fa  ve.   
17O||4||6||Er shoh hie Hatach magh gys Mordecai, ayns straid yn ard-valley, va roish giat  y ree.
17O||4||7||As dinsh Mordecai dasyn ooilley ny v'er daghyrt da, as mychione yn sym dy argid  yiall Haman dy eeck stiagh gys tashtaghyn y ree, son kied dy stroie ny Hewnyn.    
17O||4||8||Hug eh da myrgeddin copy jeh'n oardagh v'er ny choyrt ec Shushan dy stroie ad  dy yeeaghyn eh da Esther, as dy choyrt jee toiggal jeh, as dy churmal ee dy gholl  stiagh gys y ree, dy yannoo aghin huggey, as dy ghuee son foayr ayns lieh yn pobble  eck.   
17O||4||9||As haink Hatach, as dinsh eh da Esther goan Vordecai.   
17O||4||10||Reesht loayr Esther rish Hatach, as hug ee eh er chaghteraght gys Mordecai;    
17O||4||11||Ta fys ec ooilley sharvaantyn y ree, as pobble cheeraghyn y ree, quoi-erbee,  lhig da ve dooinney ny ben, hig fenish y ree gys y chooyrt sodjey-stiagh, gyn ad  veeit, ta un leigh ayn dy chur ad gy-baase, er-lhimmey jeusyn huc nee yn ree sheeyney  magh yn lorg airh reeoil, dy choyrt e vioys da: agh cha vel mish er ve eit dy heet fenish  y ree rish jeih laghyn as feed.
17O||4||12||As dinsh ad da Mordecai goan Esther.
17O||4||13||Eisht doardee Mordecai dy ansoor Esther, Ny smooinee rhyt hene, dy jean uss  scapail ayns thie yn ree veg share na ooilley ny Hewnyn.   
17O||4||14||Son my vees oo ooilley cooidjagh dty host ec y traa shoh, eisht nee feaysley  as livrey-ys da ny Hewnyn troggal veih boayl elley, agh bee uss as thie dty ayrey  er nyn stroie: as quoi ec ta fys, nagh vel oo er jeet gys y reeriaght, cour lheid  y traa shoh?   
17O||4||15||Eisht doardee Esther daue dy chur yn ansoor shoh da Mordecai.   
17O||4||16||Immee as chaggil cooidjagh ooilley ny Hewnyn t'ayns Shushan, as trosht-jee  er my hon's, as ny jean-jee gee ny giu son three laa, oie ny laa: neem's as my vraane  aegey myr geddyn trostey, as eisht hem stiagh gys y ree, red nagh vel cordail rish  y leigh: as my ta mee kiarit son cherraghtyn, lhig dou cherraghtyn.
17O||4||17||Er shoh hie Mordecai roish, as ren eh cordail rish ooilley ny va Esther er  harey eh.
17O||5||1||Nish haink eh gy-kione er y trass laa, dy dug Esther urree e coamrey reeoil,  as hass ee ayns y chooyrt sodjey stiagh jeh thie yn ree, jeeragh er thie yn ree:  as va'n ree ny hoie er e stoyl-reeoil ayns thie yn ree, jeeragh er giat y thie.    
17O||5||2||As ve myr shen, tra honnick y ree Esther yn ven-rein shassoo ayns y chooyrt,  dy dooar ee foayr ayns e hilley: as heeyn y ree magh da Esther yn lorg airh reeoil  v'ayns e laue: myr shen hayrn Esther er gerrey, as venn ee rish kione y lorg-reeoil.    
17O||5||3||Eisht dooyrt y ree, Cre ta dty yeearree, ven-rein Esther? as cre ta dty aghin?  bee eh eer er ny choyrt dhyt, gys derrey lieh yn reeriaght.   
17O||5||4||As dreggyr Esther, My s'gooidsave lesh y ree, lhig da'n ree as Haman cheet yn  laa jiu gys ny cuirraghyn ta mec er chiarail er e hon.   
17O||5||5||Eisht dooyrt y ree, ny lhig da Haman lhiggey shaghey dy yannoo myr ta Esther  er ghra: myr shen haink y ree as Haman gys ny cuirraghyn, va Esther er n'aarlaghey.    
17O||5||6||As dooyrt y ree rish Esther, ec y yien feeyney, Cre ta dty accan? as bee eh  giallit dhyt: as cre ta dty yeearree? gys eer y derrey lieh jeh'n reeriaght, vees  eh cooilleenit. 
17O||5||7||Eisht dreggyr Esther, as dooyrt ee, My accan, as my yeearree te;     
17O||5||8||My ta mee er gheddyn foayr ayns shilley yn ree, as my s'gooidsave lesh y ree  dy yialdyn dou my accan, as dy chooilleeney my yeearree, lhig da'n ree as Haman cheet  gys y yien ta mee kiarail er nyn son, as neem's mairagh myr ta'n ree er ghra.     
17O||5||9||Eisht hie Haman magh yn laa shen ayns ard-voggey, as gennallys e chree: agh  tra honnick Haman Mordecai ayns giat y ree, nagh hass eh seose, as nagh chroym eh  huggey, v'eh ayns farg dewil noi Mordecai.    
17O||5||10||Ny-yeih, chum Haman er hene, as tra haink eh thie, hug eh fys er e chaarjyn,  as Zeresh e ven.    
17O||5||11||As dinsh Haman daue mychione gloyr e verchys, as earroo mooar e chloan, as  ooilley yn ooashley va'n ree stowal er, as kys v'eh er hoiaghey seose eh erskyn ny  princeyn, as ard-gheiney yn ree.    
17O||5||12||Dooyrt Haman ny sodjey, Cha ren Esther y ven-rein cuirrey dooinney erbee marish  y ree gys y yien v'ee er n'aarlaghey agh mee hene, as mairagh myrgeddin t'ee er m'y   chuirrey dy ve marish y ree.    
17O||5||13||Ny-yeih cha vel ooilley shoh jannoo ven y vie dou, choud as ta mee fakin Mordecai  yn Ew ny hoie ec giat y ree.    
17O||5||14||Eisht dooyrt Zeresh e ven, as ooilley e chaarjyn rish, Lhig da criy ve troggit  jeih cubityn as da-eed er yrjid, as mairagh  loayr uss rish y ree, son Mordecai dy  ve croghit er: eisht immee uss dy gennal marish y ree gys y yien. As by-laik lesh  Haman y choyrle shoh, as doardee eh criy dy ve jeant.         
17O||6||1||Er yn oie shen cha daink cadley er y ree, as doardee eh lioar recortyssyn y  reeriaght dy ve er ny choyrt, lesh huggey, as v'ad lhaiht ayns clashtyn y ree.    
17O||6||2||As ve er ny gheddyn scruit, dy row Mordecai er hoilshaghey mychione Bigthana  as Teresh, jees jeh shamyrderyn y ree, va currym y dorrys orroo, hug nyn goyrle dy  cheilley dy chur ree Ahasuerus gy-baase.   
17O||6||3||As dooyrt y ree, Lesh cre'n ooashley as onnor ta Mordecai er ny ve cooilleenit  son shoh? Eisht dooyrt fir-oik y ree va mygeayrt-y-mysh, Cha vel veg jeant er e hon.
17O||6||4||As dooyrt y ree, Quoi t'ayns y chooyrt? (nish va Haman er jeet gys y chooyrt  mooie jeh thie yn ree, dy loayrt rish y ree, son Mordecai dy ve croghit er y chriy  v'eh er chiarail ny chour.   
17O||6||5||As dooyrt fir-oik y ree rish, Cur-my-ner ta Haman ny hassoo 'sy chooyrt. As  dooyrt y ree, Lhig da cheet stiagh.   
17O||6||6||Er shoh haink Haman stiagh: as dooyrt y ree rish, Cre vees jeant rish y dooinney,  s'gooidsave lesh y ree dy hroggal gys y stayd smoo dy ard-ooashley? (nish smooinee  Haman ayns e chree, Quoi ayns smoo ghoghe y ree taitnys dy hroggal gys ard-ooashley  syrjey na mee hene?)   
17O||6||7||As dreggyr Haman y ree, Da'n dooinney ta'n ree aggindagh dy hoilshaghey yn onnor  shoh,   
17O||6||8||Lhig da'n coamrey reeoil, lheid as ta'n ree cliaghtey ceau, ve er ny choyrt  lesh, as cabbyl-markiagh y ree, as y crown reeoil t'er e chione:   
17O||6||9||As lhig da'n coamrey shoh, as y cabbyl ve livreit da fer jeh princeyn s'ooasle  y ree, dy choamrey yn dooinney lesh, ayn ta'n ree er ghoaill taitnys dy hroggal gys  yn ard-ooashley shoh, as cur-jee lhieu eh markiagh trooid straidyn yn ard-valley,  as fockley magh roishyn, Shoh myr vees jeant son y dooinney s'gooidsave lesh y ree dy choamrey  lesh ooashley.   
17O||6||10||Eisht dooyrt y ree rish Haman, Jean siyr, as gow yn coamrey, as y cabbyl, myr  t'ou hene er ghra, as jean eer myr shoh rish Mordecai yn Ew, ta ny hoie ec giat y  ree: ny lhig da veg ve faagit gyn jannoo jeh ny t'ou er ghra.   
17O||6||11||Eisht ghow Haman yn coamrey as y cabbyl, as choamree eh Mordecai, as hug eh  lesh eh er mooin chabbyl trooid straidyn yn ard-valley, as ren eh fockley magh roish,  Myr shoh vees eh jeant rish y dooinney, ayn ta'n ree goaill taitnys dy hroggal yn  ard-ooashley shoh.
17O||6||12||As haink Mordecai reesht gys giat y ree: agh ren Haman siyr gys e hie, dobberan,  as lesh e chione coodit.   
17O||6||13||As dinsh Haman da Zeresh e ven, as da ooilley e chaarjyn, dy chooilley nhee  v'er daghyrt da. Eisht dooyrt e gheiney creeney, as Zeresh e ven, rish, My ta Mordecai  jeh sluight ny Hewnyn, roishyn t'ou er n'yannoo toshiaght dy huittym, cha vod oo  cosney er, agh tuittee oo son shickyrys fosyn.   
17O||6||14||As choud as v'ad foast loayrt rish, haink shamyrderyn y ree, as ayns siyr dy  chur lhieu Haman gys ny cuirraghyn va Esther er gheddyn aarloo. 
17O||7||1||Myr shen haink y ree as Haman gys ny cuirraghyn, marish Esther yn ven-rein.    
17O||7||2||As dooyrt y ree reesht rish Esther er y nah laa, ec y yien-feeyney, Cre ta dty  yeearree, ven-rein Esther? as bee eh ayd: as cre ta dty aghin? as bee eh cooilleenit  gys eer yn derrey lieh jeh'n reeriaght.   
17O||7||3||Eisht dreggyr Esther yn ven-rein, as dooyrt ee, My ta mee er gheddyn foayr ayns  dty hilley's, O ree, as my s'gooidsave lesh y ree, lhig da my vioys 've aym er my  accan, as my phobble er my aghin.   
17O||7||4||Son ta shin creckit, mish as my phobble, dy ve stroit, dy ve coyrt gy-baase,  as dy herraghtyn: agh dy beagh shin creckit son deiney bondiaght, as mraane bondiaght,  cha beign er vosley my veeal, ga nagh voddagh y noid lhiasaghey 'yannoo da'n ree  son y coayll.   
17O||7||5||Eisht dreggyr ree Ahasuerus, as dooyrt eh rish Esther yn ven-rein, Quoi eh-hene?  as c'raad t'eh sloys da ayns e chree dy yannoo shoh?
17O||7||6||As dooyrt Esther, Yn noid, as y tranlaasagh, yn Haman custey shoh: eisht huitt  aggle er Haman fenish y ree as y ven-rein.   
17O||7||7||As dirree yn ree veih'n yien-feeyney ayns e eulys, as hie eh gys garey yn phlaase;  as hass Haman seose dy yannoo aghin son e vioys gys Esther yn ven-rein: son honnick  eh dy row olk kiarit n'oi liorish y ree.   
17O||7||8||Eisht haink y ree ass garey yn phlaase gys room y yien-feeyney, as va Haman  er duittym er y chouch er va Esther ny soie. Eisht dooyrt y ree, Vel eh son goaill  er-egin yn ven-rein myrgeddin roish my hooillyn ayns my hie hene? Cha row yn fockle  ny sleaie ass beeal y ree nagh choodee ad eddin Haman.
17O||7||9||As dooyrt Harbonah, fer jeh shamyrderyn y ree, kiongoyrt rish y ree, Cur-my  ner ta'n chriy jeh jeih cubityn as da-eed er yrjid, va Haman er hroggal son Mordecai  v'er hoilshaghey yn olk va kiarit noi yn ree, ny hassoo roish thie Haman. Eisht dooyrt  y ree, Crogh-jee eh-hene er.   
17O||7||10||Myr shen hrogh ad Haman er y chriy v'eh er chiarail son Mordecai. Eisht va  jymmoose y ree er ny veeinaghey. 
17O||8||1||Er y laa shen livrey ree Ahasuerus thie Haman noid ny Hewnyn, gys Esther yn  ven-rein: as haink Mordecai kionfenish y ree; son va Esther er hoilshaghey cre v'eh  jeeish.   
17O||8||2||As ghow yn ree yn fainey v'eh er ghoaill voish Haman, as hug eh eh da Mordecai.  As hoie Esther Mordecai harrish thie Haman.   
17O||8||3||As loayr Esther reesht fenish y ree, as huitt ee sheese ec e chassyn, as ghuee  ee lesh jeir, dy lhiettal olkys Haman yn Agagite, as e ghrogh choyrle va ayns e chree  noi 
17O||8||4||As heeyn y ree magh yn lorg airh reeoil gys Esther. Er shoh dirree Esther, as  hass e kiongoyrt rish y ree:   
17O||8||5||As dooyrt ee, My s'gooidsave lesh y ree, as my ta mee er gheddyn foayr ayns  e hilley, as my chooish cairagh kiongoyrt rish y ree, as mee hene pleasal ayns e  hooillyn, lhig da order 've jeant dy yannoo dyn bree ny screeunyn currit magh liorish  Haman mac Hammedatha yn Agagite, dy stroie ny Hewnyn t'ayns ooilley rheamyn y ree: 
17O||8||6||Son kys oddym's surranse dy akin lheid y chragh dy heet er my phobble? ny kys  oddym's gymmyrkey toyrt-mow my chynney. 
17O||8||7||Eisht dooyrt ree Ahasuerus rish Esther yn ven-rein, as rish Mordecai yn Ew,  Cur-my-ner, ta mee er livrey gys Esther thie Haman, as eh-hene t'ad er chroghey er  y chriy, son dy hrog eh e laue noi ny Hewnyn. 
17O||8||8||Scrieu-jee myrgeddin ayns lieh ny Hewnyn, myr sailliu, ayns ennym y ree, as  seal-jee eh lesh fainey yn ree: son yn order ta scruit ayns ennym y ree, as sealit  lesh fainey yn ree, cha jig lesh dooinney er bee goll n'oi.   
17O||8||9||Eisht va scrudeyryn y ree er nyn eam ec y traa cheddin 'sy trass vee (ta shen  yn vee Sivan) er y trass laa as feed jeh'n vee cheddin, as ve scruit (cordail rish  ooilley ny va Mordecai er harey) gys ny Hewnyn, as gys ny kiannoortyn, as ny briwnyn,  as fir reill ny cheeraghtyn, voish India gys Ethiopia, shey-feed as shiaght rheamyn,  gys dagh rheam cordail rish y scrieu oc hene, as gys dy chooilley phobble lurg nyn  ghlare, as gys ny Hewnyn cordail rish y scrieu, as y ghlare oc hene.   
17O||8||10||As scrieu eh ayns ennym ree Ahasuerus, as seal eh eh lesh fainey yn ree, as  hug eh screeunyn lesh postyn er cabbil, as markee er muleyn, camelyn, as dromedareeyn  aegey:
17O||8||11||Lioroo va'n ree er lowal da ny Hewnyn, va ayns dy chooilley ard-valley, dy  haglym ad-hene cooidjagh, as dy hassoo son nyn mioys, dy stroie, dy varroo, as dy  choyrt mow slane pooar y pobble, as y rheam yinnagh soiagh orroo, chammah cloan veggey  as mraane, as dy ghoaill yn chooid oc son spooilley: 
17O||8||12||Er un laa, ayns ooilley rheamyn ree Ahasuerus, ta shen dy ghra, er yn trass  laa yeig jeh'n nah vee yeig ta shen, yn vee Adar.   
17O||8||13||Va copy jeh'n order son sarey dy ve er ny choyrt ayns dy chooilley rheam, focklit  magh gys dy chooilley phobble: as dy beagh ny Hewnyn aarloo ry-hoi yn laa shen, dy  ghoaill cooilleen er nyn noidyn:   
17O||8||14||Myr shen hie ny postyn va markiagh er muleyn, as camelyn magh, ayns dy chooilley  hiyr, myr v'ad eginit liorish sarey yn ree; as va'n decree focklit magh ec Shushan  y phlaase.   
17O||8||15||As hie Mordecai magh veih fenish y ree, ayns coamrey reeoil dy ghorrym as bane,  as lesh crown mooar dy airh, as lesh garmad sheeidey purple: as va ard-voggey as  gennallys trooid ooilley ard-valley Shushan:   
17O||8||16||Va ec ny Hewnyn, soilshey, as gennallys, as boggey, as ooashley.   
17O||8||17||As ayns dy chooilley rheam, as ayns dy chooilley ard-valley, raad erbee dy  daink sarey as decree yn ree, va boggey as gennallys, cuirraghyn as laa dy yien mie:  as haink ymmodee jeh pobble y cheer harrish gys credjue ny Hewnyn: as v'ad ayns aggle  roish ny Hewnyn.
17O||9||1||Nish ayns y nah vee yeig (ta shen yn vee Adar) er y trass laa yeig jeh'n vee  cheddin, myr va'n traa tayrn er-gerrey, dy row sarey as decree yn ree dy ve cooilleenit,  er y laa va noidyn ny Hewnyn treishteil dy gheddyn barriaght harrystoo, (ga dy row  eh kiarit er aght elley, dy row ec ny Hewnyn laue yn eaghtyr harrish nyn noidyn.)    
17O||9||2||Haggil ny Hewnyn ad-hene cooidjagh ayns nyn ard-valjyn, trooid magh ooilley  rheamyn ree Ahasuerus, dy gholl laue roosyn va son cur mow ad; as cha dod dooinney  erbee shassoo roue: son huitt yn aggle oc er dy chooilley phobble.   
17O||9||3||As ren ooilley fir-reill ny rheamyn, as ny kiannoortyn, as ny briwnyn, as offishearyn  y ree, cooney lesh ny Hewnyn: er-yn-oyr dy row aggle Vordecai er duittym orroo.    
17O||9||4||Son va Mordecai pooaral ayns thie yn ree, as hie goo jeh magh trooid ooilley  ny cheeraghyn: son daase y chooilley shoh Mordecai ny smoo as ny smoo.   
17O||9||5||Myr shoh woaill ny Hewnyn ooilley nyn noidyn lesh foyr y chliwe, as lesh cragh,  as toyrt-mow, as ren ad cre bailloo rish nyn noidyn.   
17O||9||6||As ayns Shushan y phlaase, varr as stroie ny Hewnyn queig cheead dooinney.    
17O||9||7||As Parshandatha, as Dalphon, as Aspatha,   
17O||9||8||As Poratha, as Adalia, as Aridatha,    
17O||9||9||As Parmashta as Arisai as Aridai, as Vejezatha,    
17O||9||10||Jeih mec Haman mac Hanmedatha, noid ny Hewnyn, ren ad y varroo; agh er y spooilley  cha dug ad nyn laue.
17O||9||11||Er y laa shen, va'n earroo ocsyn va stroit ayns Shushan y phlaase, er ny choyrt  stiagh gys v ree.   
17O||9||12||As dooyrt y ree rish Esther yn ven-rein, Ta ny Hewnyn er varroo as er stroie  queig cheead dooinney ayns Shushan y phlaase, as jeih mec Haman; cre t'ad er n'yannoo  ayns rheamyn elley yn ree? nish cre ta dty accan? as bee eh ayd: as cre sodjey t'ou  dy yeearree? as bee eh cooilleenit.   
17O||9||13||Eisht dooyrt Esther, My s'gooidsave lesh y ree, lhig da ve lowit da ny Hewnyn  t'ayns Shushan dy yannoo mairagh, cordail rish decree yn laa shoh, as lhig da jeih  mec Haman ve croghit er y chriy.   
17O||9||14||As doardee yn ree shen dy ve jeant: as haink y decree magh ayns Shushan, as  hrogh ad jeih mec Haman.   
17O||9||15||As haggil ny Hewnyn v'ayns Shushan ad-hene cooidjagh, er y chiarroo laa yeig  myrgeddin jeh'n vee Adar, as varr ad three cheead dooinney ayns Shushan: agh er y  spooilley cha dug ad laue. 
17O||9||16||Agh ny Hewnyn elley v'ayns rheamyn y ree, haggil ad ad-hene cooidjagh, as hass  ad seose son nyn mioys, as va fea oc veih nyn noidyn, as varr ad jeh nyn noidyn three-feed  as queig thousaneyn jeig; agh cha dug ad laue er y spooilley.   
17O||9||17||Er y trass laa yeig jeh'n vee Adar, as er y chiarroo laa yeig jeh'n vee cheddin,  ghow ad fea, as ren ad eh laa son cuirraghyn as gien mie.   
17O||9||18||Agh haggil ny Hewnyn va ec Shushan cooidjagh er y trass laa yeig as er y chiarroo  laa yeig jeh'n vee cheddin, as er y wheiggoo laa yeig ghow ad fea, as ren ad eh laa  son cuirraghyn as gennallys.   
17O||9||19||Er shoh ren Hewnyn ny baljyn-cheerey, as cummaltee ny baljyn-foshlit, yn chiarroo  laa yeig jeh'n vee Adar, laa son gennallys, as cuirraghyn, as ard feailley, as dy  stowal giootyn er y cheilley.   
17O||9||20||As scrieu Mordecai ny reddyn shoh,as hug eh screeunyn gys ooilley ny Hewnyn  v'ayns ooilley rheamyn ree Ahasuerus, chammah foddey as gerrit,   
17O||9||21||Shoh dy gholl myr leigh ny mast' oc, ad dy reayll yn chiarroo laa yeig jeh'n  vee Adar, as y wheiggoo laa yeig jeh'n vee cheddin dy chooilley vlein;   
17O||9||22||Son dy dooar ny Hewnyn er ny laghyn shen fea veih nyn noidyn, as dy row yn  vee shen er ny hyndaa veih trimshey gys gennallys, as veih dobberan, gys laa bannee:  dy yannoo laghyn dy chuirraghyn as gien mie, as dy choyrt giootyn yn derrey yeh gys  y jeh elley, as cooney gys ny boghtyn.   
17O||9||23||As chiare ny Hewnyn dy yannoo myr v'ad er n'ghoaill toshiaght, as myr va Mordecai  er scrieu huc.   
17O||9||24||Er-yn-oyr dy row Haman, mac Hammedatha yn Agagite, ard noid ooilley ny Hewnyn,  er chiarail olk noi ny Hewnyn dy stroie ad, as dy row eh er cheau Pur (ta shen yn  lot) dy chur mow as dy yiarey ad jeh.
17O||9||25||Agh tra haink Esther fenish y ree, doardee eh liorish screeunyn, dy beagh yn  olk v'eh er chiarail noi ny Hewnyn chyndait er e chione hene, as dy beagh eh-hene  as e vec croghit er y chriy.
17O||9||26||Er-y-fa shen, denmys ad ny laghyn shen Purim, lurg ennym Pur, er coontey ooilley  focklyn y screeuyn shoh, as shen ny v'ad er n'akin mychione y chooish shoh, as ny  va er jeet orroo,
17O||9||27||Doardee ny Hewnyn, as ghow ad orroo hene, as er nyn sluight, as er ooilley  ny ren lhiantyn huc; nagh lhiggagh ad sheese yn daa laa shoh, dy reayll ad feailley  cordail rish yn order, as cordail rish yn traa pointit dy chooilley vlein;
17O||9||28||As dy beagh ny laghyn shoh er nyn vreayll ayns imraa as cooinaghtyn, trooid  dy chooilley heeloghe, ayns dy chooilley lught-thie, as dy chooilley rheam, as dy  chooilley ard-valley: as nagh row ny laghyn shoh jeh Purim dy ve lhiggit sheese mastey  ny Hewnyn, ny yn chooinaghtyn jeu dy herraghtyn veih nyn sluight.
17O||9||29||Eisht scrieu Esther yn ven-rein, inneen Abihail, as Mordecai yn Ew, lesh slane  pooar, dy choyrt ayns bree yn screeuyn elley shoh son Purim.    
17O||9||30||As hug eh ny screeunyn magh gys ooilley ny Hewnyn v'ayns ny shey-feed as shiaght  rheamyn jeh reeriaght Ahasuerus, lesh goan dy hee as dy hickyrys;    
17O||9||31||Dy reayll ny laghyn shoh jeh Purim, ayns nyn imbagh cooie, myr va Mordecai  yn Ew, as Esther yn ven-rein er choyrt currym orroo, as myr v'ad er n'oardaghey er  nyn son hene, as son nyn sluight er coontey yn trostey as y dobberan oc.    
17O||9||32||As va ny cooishyn shoh mychione Purim jeant mie liorish decree Esther: as ve  currit er recort.  
17O||10||1||As hug ree Ahasuerus y cheer, as ellanyn ny marrey fo keesh.
17O||10||2||As ooilley obbraghyn e phooar, as e niart, as y stayd ooasle, huggey va'n ree  er hroggal Mordecai, nagh vel ad scruit ayns lioar recortyssyn reeaghyn Vedia as  Phersia?    
17O||10||3||Son va Mordecai yn Ew yn fer by-niessey da ree Ahasuerus, as ard mastey ny  Hewnyn as soit jeh liorish earroo e chaarjyn, imneagh son maynrys e phobble, as cur  er y hoshiaght shee ooilley e chynney. 
32O||1||1||Nish haink goo yn Chiarn gys Jonah mac Amittai gra,
32O||1||2||Trog ort, immee gys Nineveh yn ard valley mooar shen, as trog seose dty choraa  noi eck, son ta'n mee chraueeaght oc er jeet seose kiongoyrt rhym.
32O||1||3||Agh dirree Jonah seose dy roie er-chea gys Tarshish veih fenish y Chiarn, as  hie eh sheese gys Joppa; as hooar eh lhong goll gys Tarshish: myr shen deeck eh yn  leagh-shiaullee, as hie eh er boayrd, dy gholl maroo gys Tarshish, veih fenish y  Chiarn. 
32O||1||4||Agh hug y Chiarn magh geay vooar er yn aarkey, as va sterrym dorrinagh ayns  y cheayn, myr shen dy row yn lhong ayns gaue brishey.
32O||1||5||Eisht va aggle er ny marrinee, as deie ad dagh dooinney gys e yee, as hilg ad  magh yn chooid v'er boayrd 'sy cheayn, dy eddrymaghey yn lhong: agh va Jonah ersooyl  sheese 'sy chabbane, as lhie eh, as v'eh trome ny chadley.
32O||1||6||Myr shen haink mainshtyr y lhong huggey, as dooyrt eh rish, Kys t'ou cadley  myr shoh, y chadlag? irree, eie er dty Yee, my she shen dy jean Jee smooinaghtyn  orrin, nagh bee mayd caillit.
32O||1||7||As dooyrt ad, dagh fer rish e heshey, Tar-jee, as lhig dooin lottyn y hayrn,  dy vod fys y ve ain, quoi by-chyndagh ta'n olk shoh er jeet orrin. Myr shen hilg  ad lottyn, as huitt y  lot er Jonah.
32O||1||8||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Insh dooin, ta shin guee ort, quoi by-chyndagh ta'n olk  shoh er jeet orrin: cre ta dty aght beaghee? as cre voish t'ou? cre'n cheer t'ou  jeh? as cre'n sleih t'ou jeh?
32O||1||9||As dooyrt eh roo, She Hebrew mee, as ta mee goaill aggle roish y Chiarn, Jee  ny flaunys, t'er chroo yn aarkey as y thalloo chirrym.
32O||1||10||Eisht va ny deiney erskyn-towse agglagh, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou uss  er n'yannoo shoh? (son va fys ec ny deiney dy row eh er-chea veih fenish y Chiarn,  son v'eh er n'insh daue).
32O||1||11||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre nee mayd rhyt, dy vod y keayn ve kiune dooin? (son  va'n keayn freaney, as erskyn-towse stermagh).
32O||1||12||As dooyrt eh roo, Trog-jee mee seose, as tilg-jee mee magh 'sy cheayn; myr  shen vees y keayn kiune diuish: son ta fys aym dy nee by-chyndagh rhym's ta'n sterrym  mooar shoh er jeet erriu.
32O||1||13||. Ny-yeih, ren ny deiney gymmyrt dy doccaragh, dy chosney yn thalloo, agh cha  voddagh ad roshtyn, son va'n keayn freaney, as dowil-dorrinagh noi oc.
32O||1||14||Shen-y-fa, deie ad gys y Chiarn, as dooyrt ad, Ta shin guee ort, O Hiarn, ta  shin guee ort, ny lhig dooin cherraghtyn son bioys yn dooinney shoh, as ny cur gys  nyn lieh yn uill gyn-loght; son t'ou uss, O Hiarn, er n'yannoo myr s'gooidsave lhiat.
32O||1||15||Myr shen hrog ad seose Jonah, as hilg ad eh magh 'sy cheayn, as ghow yn aarkey  kiunid veih freaney.
32O||1||16||Eisht ghow ny deiney aggle roish y Chiarn erskyn-towse, as ren ad breearrey  dy hebbal oural da'n Chiarn.
32O||1||17||Nish va'n Chiarn er chiarail eeast mooar dy lhuggey seose Jonah, as va Jonah  ayns bolg yn eeast, three laa as three oieghyn. 
32O||2||1||Eisht ghow Jonah padjer gys y Chiarn e Yee veih bolg yn eeast,
32O||2||2||As dooyrt eh, Deie mee kyndagh rish my heaghyn gys y Chiarn, as ren eh my chlashtyn;  veih diunid yn oaie deie mee, as cheayll oo my choraa   
32O||2||3||Son t'ou er my hilgey ayns y diunid, ayns mean ny marrey, as haink ny thooillaghyn  mygeayrt-y-moom, ta ooilley ny ushtaghyn as ny tonnyn ayd's er n'gholl harrym.
32O||2||4||Eisht dooyrt mee Ta mee ceaut magh ass dty hilley; agh ny yeih nee'm jeeaghyn  reesht lesh dty hiamble casherick.
32O||2||5||Haink ny ushtaghyn mygeayrt-y-moom, eer gys my annym: ren y diunid m'y chruinnaghey  mygeayrt, va'n amlagh cast mysh my chione.
32O||2||6||Hie mee sheese choud's undin ny sleityn; bee yn thalloo as ny barryn eck my-geayrt-y-moom  dy bragh, mannagh jean oo my vioys y livrey veih toyrt-mow, O Hiarn my Yee.
32O||2||7||Tra ren my annym gannooinaghey cheu sthie jee'm, chooinee mee er y Chiarn, as  haink my phadjer stiagh hood, gys dty hiamble casherick.
32O||2||8||T'adsyn, ta cur geill da fardalyssyn breagagh, treigeil nyn myghin hene.
32O||2||9||Agh chebb-yms oural dhyt lesh y choraa dy hoyrt-booise, eeck-ym shen ny ta mee  er vreearrey: ta saualtys veih'n Chiarn.
32O||2||10||As hug y Chiarn currym er yn eeast, as hilg eh magh Jonah er y thalloo chirrym.
32O||3||1||As haink goo yn Chiarn gys Jonah yn nah cheayrt, gra,
32O||3||2||Trog ort, immee gys Nineveh yn ard valley mooar shen, as jean preacheil ayn  ny goan ver-ym royd.
32O||3||3||Myr shen dirree Jonah, as hie eh gys Nineveh cordail rish goo yn Chiarn: (nish  va Nineveh ard-valley feer vooar jeh jurnah three laa.)
32O||3||4||As ghow Jonah toshiaght dy gholl stiagh 'syn ard-valley lesh jurnah laa, as  dockle eh magh e choraa, as dooyrt eh, Foast ec kione da-eed laa, as bee Nineveh  er ny stroie.
32O||3||5||Myr shen ren sleih Nineveh credjal ayns Jee, as doardee ad laa troshtee, as  hug ad orroo aanrit-sack veih'n vooinjer b'yrjey jeu, dy jarroo gys yn vooinjer b'inshley  jeu.
32O||3||6||Son haink y goo gys ree Nineveh, as dirree eh veih e stoyl-reeoil, as hug eh  jeh e choamrey-reeoil, as choodee eh eh-hene lesh aanrit-sack as lhie eh 'sy leoie.
32O||3||7||As doardee eh eam dy v'er ny ockley-magh, as er ny hoilshaghey trooid Nineveh  (liorish sarey yn ree as e gheiney ooasle) gra, Ny lhig da dooinney ny baagh, shelloo  ny shioltane blaystyn nhee erbee; ny lhig daue goaill beaghey, ny giu ushtey.
32O||3||8||Agh lhig da dooinney as baagh ve er ny choodaghey lesh aanrit-sack, as geamagh  dy jeean gys Jee: dy jarroo lhig daue chyndaa dy chooilley unnane veih e ghrogh-raad,  as veih'n tranlaase t'ayns nyn laueyn.
32O||3||9||Quoi ec ta fys my nee Jee chyndaa as meiyghey, as e ymmoose hrome y lhiettal,  nagh jean mayd cherraghtyn?
32O||3||10||As honnick Jee nyn obbraghyn, dy hyndaa ad veih nyn ghrogh-raad, as ren Jee  meiyghey mychione yn olk, v'eh er chiarail dy choyrt orroo, as cha dug eh orroo eh.
32O||4||1||Agh va Jonah erskyn-towse jymmoosagh, as v'eh feer chorree.
32O||4||2||As ghow eh padjer gys y Chiarn, as dooyrt eh, Guee-ym ort, O Hiarn, nagh nee  shoh va my raa, choud as va mee foast ayns my heer hene? shen-y-fa chossyn mee roym  (dy gholl) gys Tarshish: son va fys aym dy vel oo Jee graysoil as myghinagh, moal  gys corree, as jeh kenjallys vooar, as meiygh chreeagh ayns kerraghey.
32O||4||3||Shen-y-fa nish, O Hiarn, gow, ta mee guee ort, my vioys voym; son te ny share  dooys dy gheddyn baase, na dy ve bio.
32O||4||4||Eisht dooyrt y Chiarn, Vel uss jannoo dy mie, ayns dy vel oo corree?
32O||4||5||Er shoh hie Jonah magh ass yn ard valley as hoie eh er cheu-har jeh'n ard valley,  as hrog eh bwaag da hene ayns shen, as hoie eh fo yn scadoo echey, dy chur-my-ner  cre'n erree harragh er yn ard-valley.
32O||4||6||As chiare yn Chiarn Jee gourd, as hug eh er gaase seose harrish Jonah, son scadoo  harrish e chione, dy gherjaghey eh ayns e hrimshey. My shen ghow Jonah boggey erskyn-towse  jeh'n ghourd.
32O||4||7||Agh chiare Jee beishteig, moghrey yn laa er-giyn, as woaill eh yn gourd, dy  ren eh fioghey.
32O||4||8||As haink eh gy-kione, tra dirree yn ghrian, dy doardee Jee geay-niar fowanagh;  as cha lajer shen va chiass ny greiney er kione Yonah, dy huitt eh my-neealloo, as  yeearree eh ayns e chree, dy gheddyn baase, as dooyrt eh, Te ny share dooys dy ve  marroo na dy ve bio.
32O||4||9||As dooyrt Jee rish Jonah, Vel uss jannoo dy mie, dy vel dty chorree er ny vrasnaghey  son y ghourd? As dooyrt eh, Ta mee jannoo dy mie dy ve corree, eer gys sproght baaish.
32O||4||10||Eisht dooyrt y Chiarn, Ta chymmey er ve ayd's jeh'n ghourd, er y hon cha vel  oo er laboragh, chamoo she uss hug er gaase, son daase eh ayns oie, as hie eh naardey  ayns oie.
32O||4||11||As nagh lhisin's sparail Nineveh yn ard-valley mooar shen, ayn ta ny smoo na  shey feed thousane persoon, nagh vel fys oc er nyn laue yesh shaghey nyn laue chiare,  as myrgeddin ymmodee maase?  
40N||1||1||Lioar sheeloghe Yeesey Creest, mac Ghavid, mac Abraham 
40N||1||2||Hooar Abraham Isaac, as hooar Isaac Jacob, as hooar Jacob Judas as e vraaraghyn.   
40N||1||3||As hooar Judas Phares as Zarah rish Thamar, as hooar Phales Esrom, as hooar Esrom  Aram. 
40N||1||4||As hooar Aram Aminadab, as hooar Aminadab Naason, as hooar Naason Salmon 
40N||1||5||As hooar Salmon Booz rish Rachab, as hooar Booz Obed rish Ruth, as hooar Obed  Jesse. 
40N||1||6||As hooar Jesse David yn ree, as hooar David yn ree Solomon reeish v'er ny ve ben  Urias. 
40N||1||7||As hooar Solomon Roboam, as hooar Roboam Abia, as hooar Abia Asa: 
40N||1||8||As hooar Asa Josaphat, as hooar Josaphat Joram, as hooar Joram Ozias. 
40N||1||9||As hooar Ozias Joatham, as hooar Joatham Achaz, as hooar Achaz Ezekias. 
40N||1||10||As hooar Ezekias Manasses, as hooar Manasses Amon, as hooar Amon Josias. 
40N||1||11||As hooar Josias Jechonias as e vraaraghyn, mysh traa yn chappeeys Babylonagh.   
40N||1||12||As rish earish yn chappeeys Babylon agh hooar Jechonias Salathiel, as hooar Salathiel  Zorobabel. 
40N||1||13||As hooar Zorobabel Abiud, as hooar Abiud Eliakim, as hooar Eliakim Azor. 
40N||1||14||As hooar Azor Sadoc, as hooar Sadoc Achim, as hooar Achim Eliud. 
40N||1||15||As hooar Eliud Eliazar, as hooar Eliazar Matthan, as hooar Matthan Jacob. 
40N||1||16||As hooar Jacob Joseph sheshey Voirrey, j'eeish ruggyr Yeesey, ta enmyssit Creest.   
40N||1||17||Myr shen ta ooilley ny sheelogheyn veih Abraham gys David, kiare sheelogheyn  jeig: as veih David derrey'n chappeeys ayns Babylon, kiare sheelogheyn jeig: as veih'n  chappeeys ayns Babylon derrey Creest kiare sheelogheyn jeig. 
40N||1||18||Nish shoh myr haink (Yeesey) Creest er y theihll: Erreish da e voir Moirrey  ve nasht rish Joseph, roish my daink ad dy vaghey cooidjagh, v'ee ry-akin dy ve corrym  liorish yn Spyrryd Noo. 
40N||1||19||As myr va Joseph e sheshey ny ghooinney cairal, as neu-wooiagh dy choyrt ee gys  nearey foshlit, v'eh smooinaghtyn dy scarrey 
40N||1||20||Agh choud as va ny reddyn shoh er e aigney, cur-my-ner haink ainle y Chiarn huggey  ayns ashlish, gra, Yoseph, vac Ghavid, ny bee aggle ort dy ghoaill hood Moirrey dty  ven: son shen t'er ny ghientyn aynjee, te jeh'n Spyrryd Noo. 
40N||1||21||As ver ee mac son y theihll, as nee oo genmys eh Yeesey, son sauee eh e phobble  veih nyn beccaghyn. 
40N||1||22||(Shoh myr va er ny chooilleeney ooilley ny loayr y Chiarn liorish y phadeyr,  gra 
40N||1||23||Cur-my-ner nee moidyn gientyn, as ver ee mac son y theihll, as nee ad genmys  eh Emmanuel, ta shen dy ghra, Jee marin.) 
40N||1||24||Tra va Joseph eisht er n'irree veih cadley, ren eh myr va ainle y Chiarn er chur  roish, as ghow eh thie e ven: 
40N||1||25||As cha row veg echey dy yannoo r'ee, derrey hug ee e ynrycan mac son y theihll,  as denmys eh yn ennym echey Yeesey. 
40N||2||1||Nish tra rug Yeesey ayns Bethlehem dy Yudea, rish lhing ree Herod, cur-my-ner haink  deiney-creeney veih'n shiar gys Jerusalem,
40N||2||2||Gra, Cre vel ree ny Hewnyn t'er jeet er y theihll? son honnick shin y rollage  echey ayns y shiar, as ta shin er jeet dy chur ooashley da. 
40N||2||3||Tra cheayll ree Herod shoh, v'eh dy mooar seaghnit, as ooilley Jerusalem marish.   
40N||2||4||As tra v'eh er symney cooidjagh ooilley ny ard-saggyrtyn, as scrudeyryn y phobble,  denee eh jeu cre'n raad va Creest dy heet er y theihll. 
40N||2||5||As dooyrt adsyn rish, Ayns Bethlehem dy Yudea: son shoh myr te scruit liorish  y phadeyr: 
40N||2||6||As uss Vethlehem ayns cheer Yudea, cha nee oo sloo ta mastey princeyn Yuda: son  assyd's hig Kiannoort nee reill my phobble Israel. 
40N||2||7||Eisht hug Herod fys follit er ny deiney creeney, as deysht eh ad dy imneagh mychione  y traa haink yn rollage rish. 
40N||2||8||As hug eh ad gys Bethlehem, gra, Immee-jee, as shir-jee magh dy jeidjagh son y  lhiannoo, as tra vees shiu er gheddyn magh eh, tar-jee lesh fys hym's, dy voddym's  neesht cheet as ooashley 'choyrt da. 
40N||2||9||Erreish daue v'er chlashtyn y ree, jimmee ad rhymboo, as cur-my-ner hie yn rollage  honnick ad ayns y shiar er e toshiaght roue, derrey haink ee, as hass ee erskyn yn  ynnyd raad va'n lhiannoo. 
40N||2||10||Tra honnick ad y rollage, va boggey erskyn-towse orroo. 
40N||2||11||As goll stiagh 'sy thie, hooar ad y lhiannoo marish Moirrey e voir, as gliooney  sheese, hug ad ooashley da as fosley ny tashtaghyn oc, heb ad giootyn da; airh, as  frankincense, as myrrh. 
40N||2||12||As myr va Jee er chur raaue daue ayns ashlish, gyn ad dy hyndaa gys Herod, ghow  ad raad elley gys nyn jeer hene.
40N||2||13||As tra v'ad er n'immeeaght, cur-my-ner haink ainle y Chiarn gys Joseph ayns ashlish,  gra, Trog ort, gow yn lhiannoo as e voir, cosne royd gys Egypt, as fuirree ayns shen  derrey ver-yms fys hood: son shirree Herod y lhiannoo dy stroie eh. 
40N||2||14||Eisht dirree eh, as ghow eh yn lhiannoo, as e voir ayns yn oie, as hie eh roish  er-chea gys Egypt: 
40N||2||15||As shen-y raad v'eh derrey baase Herod: as shoh myr va cooilleenit shen loayr  y Chiarn liorish y phadeyr, gra, Magh ass Egypt deie mee er my vac. 
40N||2||16||Eisht Herod toiggal dy row eh mollit liorish ny deiney-creeney, v'eh erskyn-towse  eulyssagh, as hug eh magh sarey, as varr eh ooilley ny lhiennoo-mec v'ayns Bethlehem,  as ayns ooilley ny ardjyn shen, veih daa vlein dy eash as fo, corrym rish y traa  v'eh dy imneagh er vriaght jeh ny deiney creeney. 
40N||2||17||Shen y traa va cooilleenit ny va loayrit liorish Jeremy yn phadeyr, gra, 
40N||2||18||Ayns Rama va eam treih er ny chlashtyn, yllaghey as keayney, as dobberan hrimshagh,  Rachel keayney son e cloan, as gobbal dy ve er ny gherjaghey, er-yn-oyr nagh row  ad er-mayrn. 
40N||2||19||Agh lurg baase Herod, cur-my-ner haink ainle y Chiarn ayns ashlish gys Joseph  ayns Egypt, 
40N||2||20||Gra, Irree, as gow yn lhiannoo as e voir, as immee gys cheer Israel: son t'adsyn  marroo va shleeuit er bioys y lhiannoo. 
40N||2||21||As dirree eh, as ghow eh yn lhiannoo as e voir, as haink eh gys cheer Israel.   
40N||2||22||Agh clashtyn dy row Archelaus reill ayns Judea, ayns ynnyd e ayr Herod, va aggle  er dy gholl gys shen: agh myr va Jee er chur roish ayns ashlish, hyndaa eh gys ardjyn  Ghalilee. 
40N||2||23||As jimmee eh dy chummal ayns ard-valley enmyssit Nazareth: as shoh myr va cooilleenit  shen loayr ny phadeyryn, Bee eh enmyssit ny Nazarene. 
40N||3||1||Ayns ny laghyn shen haink Ean Bashtey, preacheil ayns faasagh Yudea, 
40N||3||2||As gra, Gow-jee arrys: son ta reeriaght Yee er gerrey. 
40N||3||3||Son shoh eshyn va loayrit jeh liorish y phadeyr Esaias, gra, Coraa fer geamagh  ayns yn aasagh, Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, jean-jee ny cassanyn echey jeeragh. 
40N||3||4||As v'ec Ean cheddin coamrey dy fynney chamel, as cryss liare mysh e veeghyn; as  va e veaghey locustyn as mill feie. 
40N||3||5||Eisht hie magh huggey Jerusalem as ooilley Judea, as Ooilley yn cheer mygeayrt  Jordan. 
40N||3||6||As goaill-rish nyn beccaghyn v'ad er nyn mashtey liorish ayns Jordan. 
40N||3||7||Agh tra honnick eh ymmodee jeh ny Phariseeyn as ny Sadduceeyn cheet gys e vashtey,  dooyrt eh roo, O shiuish heeloghe dy ard-nieughyn, quoi t'er chur raaue diu dy hea  veih yn jymmoose ta ry-heet? 
40N||3||8||Cur-jee magh nish er-y-fa shen messyn cooie dy arrys. 
40N||3||9||As ny smooinee-jee dy ghra, riu hene, Ta Abraham ain son nyn ayr: son ta mee gra  riu, dy vel Jee pooaral eer jeh ny claghyn shoh dy hroggal seose cloan da Abraham   
40N||3||10||As nish hene ta'n teigh er ny choyrt gys fraue ny biljyn: shen-y-fa ta dy chooilley  villey nagh vel gymmyrkey magh mess mie, dy ve giarit sheese as tilgit ayns yn aile.   
40N||3||11||Ta mish dy jarroo bashtey shiu lesh ushtey gys arrys: agh t'eshyn ta cheet my  yei ny s'pooaral ny mish, ny braagyn echey cha vel mee feeu dy ymmyrkey: bashtee  eshyn shiu lesh y Spyrryd Noo as lesh aile. 
40N||3||12||Ta'n cleayst echey ayns e laue, as nee eh dy bollagh e laare-vooie y ghlenney,  as gowee eh e churnaght stiagh ayns e hie-tashtee: agh loshtee eh yn choau lesh aile  nagh bee er ny vooghey. 
40N||3||13||Eisht haink Yeesey veih Galilee gys Jordan, dy ve bashtit liorish Ean. 
40N||3||14||Agh va Ean noi shen, gra, Ta feme aym's dy ve er my vashtey liort's, as vel uss  cheet hym's? 
40N||3||15||Dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Cur raad dou nish: son shoh myr te cooie dooin  dy chooilley chairys y chooilleeney. Eisht lhig eh da. 
40N||3||16||As lurg da Yeesey ve bashtit, hie eh seose jeeragh ass yn ushtey: as cur-my-ner  va ny niaughyn er nyn vosley er-e-skyn, as honnick eh Spyrryd Yee cheet neose myr  calmane, as soie er. 
40N||3||17||As cur-my-ner, coraa veih niau, gra, Shoh my vac ennoil, jeh ta mee dy mooar  soiaghey.   
40N||4||1||Eisht va Yeesey er ny leeideil liorish Spyrryd Yee gys yn aasagh, dy v'er ny violaghey  liorish y drogh-spyrryd. 
40N||4||2||As tra v'eh er drostey da-eed laa as da-eed oie v'eh ny lurg shen accryssagh.   
40N||4||3||As haink y mioleyder huggey, gra, My she mac Yee oo, cur sarey da ny claghyn shoh  dy ve jeant nyn arran. 
40N||4||4||Agh dreggyr eshyn, gra, Te, scruit, Cha nee liorish arran ny lomarcan nee dooinney  beaghey, agh liorish dy chooilley ockle ta cheet magh ass beeal Yee. 
40N||4||5||Eisht ghow y drogh-spyrryd lesh seose eh gys yn ard-valley casherick, as hoie  eh eh er beinn toor syrjey yn chiamble, 
40N||4||6||As dooyrt eh rish, My she Mac Yee oo tilg oo hene sheese: son te scruit, Ver eh  currym da e ainleyn my-dty-chione, as ayns nyn laueyn nee ad oo y ymmyrkey, nagh  bwoaill oo ec traa erbee dty chass noi chlagh. 
40N||4||7||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Te scruit myrgeddin, Cha jean oo yn Chiarn dty Yee y violaghey.   
40N||4||8||Reesht hug y drogh-spyrryd lesh eh seose er slieau feer ard, as yeeagh eh da ooilley  reeriaghtyn y theihll as y ghloyr oc: 
40N||4||9||As dooyrt eh rish, Ooilley shoh ver-ym's dhyt's, my huittys oo sheese, as ooashley  chur dou. 
40N||4||10||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish, Ass my enish oo, Noid-ny-hanmey: son te scruit, Ver  oo ooashley da'n Chiarn dty Yee, as eshyn ynrycan nee oo shirveish. 
40N||4||11||Eisht daag y drogh-spyrryd eh, as cur-my-ner haink ainleyn as ren ad shirveish  er. 
40N||4||12||Nish tra cheayll Yeesey dy row Ean ny phryssoonagh, jimmee eh dy lhiattee gys  Galilee.
40N||4||13||As faagail Nazareth, haink eh dy chummal ayns Capernaum, ta rish oirr ny marrey,  rish ardjyn Zabulon as Nephthalim: 
40N||4||14||As shoh myr va cooilleenit shen ny loayr Esaias yn phadeyr, gra 
40N||4||15||Thalloo Zabulon, as thalloo Nephthalim, er slyst ny marrey, cheu elley dy Yordan,  Galilee ny Ashoonee: 
40N||4||16||Ta'n pobble va nyn soie ayns dorraghys, er vakin soilshey mooar: as orroosyn  va nyn soie ayns cheer as scadoo'n vaaish, ta soilshey er n'irree seose. 
40N||4||17||Veih yn traa shen ren Yeesey toshiaght dy phreacheil, as dy ghra, Gow-jee arrys,  son ta reeriaght niau er-gerrey. 
40N||4||18||As myr va Yeesey shooyl liorish keayn Ghalilee, honnick eh daa vraar, Simon  va enmyssit Peddyr, as Andreays e vraar, cur magh lieen 'sy cheayn: (son v'ad nyn  eeasteyryn) 
40N||4||19||As dooyrt eh roo, Eiyr-jee orrym's, as neem's shiu nyn eeasteyryn dy gheiney.   
40N||4||20||As chelleeragh daag ad nyn lieenteenyn, as deiyr ad er. 
40N||4||21||As goll er e hoshiaght veih shen, honnick eh daa vraar elley, Jamys mac Zebedee  as Ean e vraar, ayns lhong marish Zebedee nyn ayr, karraghey nyn lieen: as deie eh  orroo. 
40N||4||22||As chelleeragh daag ad y lhong as nyn ayr, as deiyr ad er. 
40N||4||23||As hie Yeesey mygeayrt ooilley Galilee, gynsaghey ayns nyn gialteenyn, as preacheil  sushtal y reeriaght, as lheihys dy chooilley hingys, as dy chooilley ghoghan mastey'n  pobble. 
40N||4||24||As hie goo jeh magh trooid ooilley Syria: as hug ad lhieu huggey ooilley ny aslayntee,  fo doghanyn as pianyn, adsyn va seaghnit lesh drogh-spyrrydyn, sleih ass nyn geeayl,  as an-lheiltee, as ren eh ad y lheihys. 
40N||4||25||As deiyr er chaglym mooar dy leih veih Galilee, as Decapolis, as Jerusalem, as  Judea, as veih cheu elley dy Yordan. 
40N||5||1||As fakin lheid ny earrooyn dy leih, hie eh seose er slieau: as tra v'eh er hoie sheese,  haink e ynseydee huggey 
40N||5||2||As hrog eh seose e choraa, as dynsee eh ad, gra, 
40N||5||3||Bannit t'adsyn ta imlee ayns spyrryd: son lhieusyn reeriaght niau. 
40N||5||4||Bannit t'adsyn ta dobberan: son bee ad er nyn gherjaghey. 
40N||5||5||Bannit t'adsyn ta meen surransagh: son bee yn thalloo oc ayns eiraght.  
40N||5||6||Bannit t'adsyn ta accryssagh as paagh lurg yn ynrickys: son bee ad er nyn yannoo  magh. 
40N||5||7||Bannit ta'n vooinjer vyghinagh: son bee myghin er ny hoilshaghey daue. 
40N||5||8||Bannit t'adsyn ta glen ayns cree: son ver ad Jee my-ner. 
40N||5||9||Bannit t'adsyn ta tayrn sleih gys shee: son bee ad enmyssit nyn gloan dy Yee.   
40N||5||10||Bannit t'adsyn ta surranse tranlaase er graih cairys: son lhieusyn reeriaght  niau. 
40N||5||11||Bannit ta shiuish tra vees shiu oltooanit, as tranlaasit, as dy chooilley ghrogh-ghoo  currit ass nyn lieh dy aggairagh er y choontey aym's. 
40N||5||12||Gow-jee boggey, as bee-jee erskyn towse gennal: son s'mooar ta nyn leagh ayns  niau: son shoh myr ren ad tranlaase er ny phadeyryn va rhymbiu. 
40N||5||13||Shiuish sollan y thallooin: agh my ta'n sollan er choayl e vlass, kys hig e  vree ayn reesht? cha vel ymmyd erbee sodjey ny chour, agh dy ve tilgit magh, as stampit  fo cassyn deiney. 
40N||5||14||Shiuish soilshey yn theihll Cha vod ard-valley ta soit er cronk ve follit. 
40N||5||15||Chamoo ta sleih foaddey cainle, as dy choyrt ee fo saagh; agh ayns cainleyr,  as t'ee cur soilshey da'n slane lught-thie. 
40N||5||16||Lhig da'n soilshey euish myr shen soilshean fenish deiney, dy vod ad fakin ny  obbraghyn mie eu, as gloyr y choyrt da nyn ayr t'ayns niau. 
40N||5||17||Ny smooinee-jee dy daink mish dy chur naardey yn leigh as ny phadeyryn: cha  nee dy chur naardey haink mee, agh dy chooilleeney. 
40N||5||18||Son dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Derrey nee yn aer as yn ooir lheie ersooyl,  cha bee un ockle, ny'n floag sloo er ny ghoaill veih'n leigh, derrey vees ooilley  jeant mie. 
40N||5||19||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen vrishys unnane jeh ny annaghyn sloo shoh, as ynsys myr  shen, bee eh enmyssit yn fer sloo ayns reeriaght niau: agh quoi erbee nee nyn yannoo  as nyn ynsaghey, bee eh enmyssit mooar ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||5||20||Son ta mee gra riu, Mannagh bee yn ynrickys euish erskyn ynrickys ny Scrudeyryn  as ny Phariseeyn, cha vod shiu er aght erbee goll stiagh ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||5||21||Ta shiu er chlashtyn dy row eh er ny ghra rish nyn shenn-ayryn, Cha jean oc dunverys:  as quoi-erbee nee dunverys, hig eh fo kerraghey yn vriwnys. 
40N||5||22||Agh ta mish gra riuish, Quoi-erbee ta fargagh rish e vraar gyn oyr, dy jig eshyn  neesht fo kerraghey yn vriwnys: as quoi erbee jir rish e vraar, Raca: dy jig eh fo  briwnys yn ard-whuaiyl: agh quoi-erbee jir, Uss ommydan, dy bee eh ayns gaue aile  niurin, 
40N||5||23||Shen-y-fa tra hebbys oo dty oural ec yn altar, my chooinys oo ayns shen dy vel  nhee erbee ec dty vraar dt'oi 
40N||5||24||Faag ayns shen dty oural roish yn altar, as immee royd, jean coardail rish dty  vraar hoshiaght, as eisht tar, as cheb dty oural. 
40N||5||25||Coard dy tappee rishyn ta streeu rhyt, choud as vees shiu goll cooidjagh er y  raad, er-aggle dy der eshyn oo fo laue yn vriw, as dy der yn briw oo fo currym y  tidoor, as dy bee oo tilgit ayns pryssoon. 
40N||5||26||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Nagh jig oo magh ass shen, derrey t'ou er n'eeck  yn farling s'jerree. 
40N||5||27||Ta shiu er chlashtyn dy row eh er ny ghra rish nyn shenn-ayryn, Cha brish oo  poosey. 
40N||5||28||Agh ta mish gra riu, Quoi-erbee ta jeeaghyn er ben, dy chur saynt j'ee, dy vel  eh er vrishey poosey r'ee hannah ayns e chree. 
40N||5||29||As my ta dty hooill yesh dy dty hayrn gys peccah, pluck assyd ee, as tilg void  ee: son te ny share dhyt unnane jeh dty hooillyn y choayl, na dty slane corp dy ve  tilgit ayns niurin. 
40N||5||30||As my ta dty laue yesh dy dty hayrn gys peccah, giare jeed, as tilg void ee:  son te ny share dhyt unnane jeh dty oltyn y choayl, na dty slane corp dy ve tilgit  ayns niurin. 
40N||5||31||Ve er ny ghra, Quoi-erbee ver e ven voish, lhig da screeuyn-scarree y chur jee.   
40N||5||32||Agh ta mish gra riu, Quoi-erbee scarrys rish e ven, agh son oyr maarderys, dy  vel eh cur urree poosey y vrishey: as quoi-erbee phoosys ish ta scart, t'eh ny vaarderagh.   
40N||5||33||Myrgeddin ta shiu er chlashtyn dy row eh er ny ghra rish nyn shenn-ayryn, Cha  jean oo loo-oaiagh y ghoaill, agh cooilleenee oo gys y Chiarn dty vreearaghyn. 
40N||5||34||Agh ta mish gra riu, Ny loo-jee er aght erbee; edyr liorish niau, son she stoyl-reeoil  Yee eh: 
40N||5||35||Ny liorish y thalloo, son shen stoyl e choshey: ny liorish Jerusalem, son shen  ard-valley yn Ard-ree. 
40N||5||36||Chamoo looys oo liorish dty chione, er-yn-oyr nagh vod oo un renaig y yannoo  bane ny doo. 
40N||5||37||Agh lhig da'n ghlare eu ve, She, she, Cha nee, cha nee: son cre-erbee ta harrish  shoh, te cheet veih yn olk. 
40N||5||38||Ta shiu er chlashtyn dy row eh er ny ghra, Sooill son sooill, as feeackyl son  feeackyl. 
40N||5||39||Agh ta mish gra riu, Ny shir-jee aggair y chooilleeney: agh quoi-erbee woaillys  oo er y lieckan yesh, chyndaa huggey yn lieckan elley. 
40N||5||40||As my ta fer erbee dy dty eignagh ec y leigh, as goaill ersooyl dty chooat, lhig  dty chloagey lesh myrgeddin. 
40N||5||41||As quoi-erbee chionnys ort dy gholl un veeley marish, gow marish jees. 
40N||5||42||Cur dasyn ta jannoo aghin hood, as veihsyn ta shirrey geeasaght void, ny chyndaa  ersooyl. 
40N||5||43||Ta shiu er chlashtyn dy row eh er ny ghra, Ver oo graih da dty naboo, as feoh  da dty noid. 
40N||5||44||Agh ta mish gra riu, Bee-jee dooie da nyn noidyn, bannee-jee adsyn ta gwee mollaght  diu, jean-jee mie dauesyn ta cur dwoaie diu, as gow-jee padjer er nyn son ocsyn ta  dy goanlyssagh jannoo tranlaase erriu: 
40N||5||45||Dy vod shiu ve cloan nyn Ayr t'ayns niau, son t'eshyn cur er e ghrian girree  er mie as sie, as cur fliaghey neose er y vooinjer chairagh as neu-chairagh. 
40N||5||46||Son my ta shiu graihagh orroosyn ta graihagh erriuish, cre'n leagh ta nyn gour?  nagh vel eer ny publicanee jannoo yn lheid cheddin? 
40N||5||47||My she da nyn mraaraghyn ny lomarcan ta shiu coyrt oltaghey-bea, cre smoo ta  shiu dy yannoo na feallagh elley? nagh vel ny eer publicanee jannoo myr shen? 
40N||5||48||Bee-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen slane-ynrick, eer myr ta nyn Ayr t'ayns niau slane-ynrick.
40N||6||1||Gow-jee tastey, nagh jean shiu nyn  ghiastyllys fenish deiney, dy ve er ny akin lioroo:  er-nonney cha vow shiu leagh veih'n Ayr eu t'ayns niau. 
40N||6||2||Shen-y-fa tra t'ou jannoo dty ghiastyllys, ny jean cayrn y heidey royd, myr ny  crauee oalsey ayns ny margaghyn, as ayns ny straidyn, er-chee cosney moylley'n theay.  Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Shen nyn leagh. 
40N||6||3||Agh tra t'ou uss jannoo dty ghiastyllys, ny lhig da fys y ve ec dty laue-chiare  cre ta dty laue yesh dy yannoo: 
40N||6||4||Dy vod dty yeirk ve follit: as nee dty Ayr ta fakin ny ta jeant dy follit, dty  leagh y chur dhyt dy foshlit. 
40N||6||5||As tra vees oo goaill padjer, cha jean oo myr ny crauee-oalsey: son shynney  lhieu syn shassoo seose ayns ny margaghyn, as ayns king ny straidyn dy ghoaill padjer,  er-chee dy v'er ny akin liorish deiney. Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy vel ad er  gheddyn nyn leagh. 
40N||6||6||Agh uss, tra t'ou goaill padjer, immee stiagh ayns dty hiamyr; as dooney dty ghorrys,  guee gys dty Ayr dy follit, as nee dty Ayr ta fakin ny ta jeant dy follit, leagh  y chur dhyt dy foshlit. 
40N||6||7||As ayns nyn badjeryn, ny gow-jee lhieu harrish as harrish myr ny Ashoonee: son  er-lhieu dy vow ad clashtyn liorish nyn ymmodee goan fardalagh. 
40N||6||8||Ny bee-jee shiuish er-y fa shen goll roosyn: son ta fys ec nyn Ayr cre ta nyn  ymmyrch, roish my jean shiu aghin huggey 
40N||6||9||Shen y fa er yn aght shoh gow-jee padjer: Ayr ain t'ayns niau, Casherick dy row  dty ennym. 
40N||6||10||Dy jig dty reeriaght. Dty aigney dy row jeant er y thalloo, myr te ayns niau.   
40N||6||11||Cur dooin nyn arran jiu as gagh laa. 
40N||6||12||As leih dooin nyn loghtyn, myr ta shin leih dauesyn ta jannoo loghtyn nyn 'oi.   
40N||6||13||As ny leeid shin ayns miolagh, agh livrey shin veih olk: Son lhiat's y reeriaght,  as y phooar, as y ghloyr, son dy bragh, Amen. 
40N||6||14||Son my leihys shiuish da deiney nyn loghtyn, leihee nyn Ayr flaunyssagh myrgeddin  diuish. 
40N||6||15||Agh mannagh leihee shiuish da deiney nyn loghtyn, cha jean yn Ayr eu nyn loghtyn  y leih diuish. 
40N||6||16||As tra vees shiu trostey, ny bee-jee groymagh myr ny crauee-oalsey, son t'adsyn  caghlaa cummey nyn eddin, er-chee deiney dy chur tastey da'n trostey oc. Ta mee shickyrys  diu, dy nee shoh (ooilley) nyn leagh. 
40N||6||17||Agh uss, tra t'ou trostey, jean dty chione y ooillaghey, as dty eddin y oonlaghey:   
40N||6||18||Nagh bee oo ry-akin liorish deiney dy hrostey, agh liorish dty Ayr t'ayns folliaght:  as nee dty Ayr ta fakin ayns folliaght, uss y chooilleeney dy foshlit. 
40N||6||19||Ny stoyr-jee seose berchys diu hene er y thalloo, raad ta'n lhemeen as y mergey  cur-mow, as raad ta maarlee brishey stiagh as geid: 
40N||6||20||Agh stoyr-jee seose berchys diu hene ayns niau, raad nagh vel y lhemeen ny'n  mergey cur mow, as raad nagh vel maarlee brishey stiagh as geid. 
40N||6||21||Son raad ta nyn stoyr, shen-y-raad vees y cree eu myrgeddin. 
40N||6||22||Ta yn tooill soilshey yn chorp: shen-y-fa my ta'n tooill gyn foill, bee soilshey  ec ooilley dty chorp. 
40N||6||23||Agh my ta assee er dty hooill, bee dty slane corp ayns dorraghys. My ta'n soilshey  ta aynyd's er-y-fa shen ny ghorraghys, nagh mooar yn dorraghys eh! 
40N||6||24||Cha vod dooinney erbee daa vainshter y hirveish: son edyr ver eh dwoaie da'n  derrey yeh, as graih da'n jeh elley; ny bee eh jeidjagh da'n derrey yeh,ny soiaghey  beg jeh'n jeh elley. Cha vod shiu Jee as Mammon y hirveish. 
40N||6||25||Er-yn-oyr shoh ta mee gra riu, Ny bee Jee ro-imneagh son nyn mea, cre ee-ys,  ny cre iu-ys shiu: ny foast son nyn girp cre ver shiu miu: Nagh vel y vea ny smoo  dy ve soit jeh na'n beaghey, as y corp na'n coamrey? 
40N||6||26||Cur-jee my-ner eeanlee yn aer: son cha vel ad cuirr ny buinn, ny chymsaghey stiagh  ayns soaltyn; foast ta nyn Ayr flaunyssagh dyn meaghey ad. Nagh vel shiuish foddey  share na adsyn? 
40N||6||27||Quoi jiuish liorish imnea erbee oddys un chubit y chur gys e yrjid hene? 
40N||6||28||As cre'n-fa ta shiu imneagh son coamraghyn? Gow-jee tastey jeh lilleeyn ny magheragh  kys t'ad gaase; cha vel ad tooilleil, chamoo t'ad sneeu. 
40N||6||29||As foast ta mee gra riu, nagh row Solomon hene ayns ooilley e ghloyr er ny choamrey  myr unnane jeu shoh. 
40N||6||30||My ta Jee er-y-fa shen myr shoh coamrey blaa ny magheragh, ta jiu ayn, as mairagh  ceaut ayns yn oghe, nagh jean eh foddey smoo shiuish y choamrey, O gheiney faase  chredjuagh? 
40N||6||31||Ny bee-jee er-y-fa shen imneagh, gra, Cre nee mayd gee? ny cre nee mayd giu?  ny kys yiow mayd coamrey? 
40N||6||32||(Son lurg ooilley ny reddyn shoh ta ny Ashoonee imneagh) agh ec yn Ayr flaunyssagh  euish ta fys, dy vel shiu feme dy chooilley nhee jeu shoh. 
40N||6||33||Agh shir-jee hoshiaght reeriaght Yee as e chairys, as bee shiu jeant magh lesh  ooilley ny reddyn shoh. 
40N||6||34||Ny bee-jee er-y-fa shen ayns imnea erbee son y laa mairagh, son tra hig y laa  mairagh, hig e chiarail marish s'lioar da'n laa t'ayn e heaghyn hene. 
40N||7||1||Ny jean-jee briwnys, as cha bee shiu er nyn mriwnys. 
40N||7||2||Son lesh y vriwnys cheddin ta shiuish briwnys, bee shiu hene er nyn mriwnys: as  lesh y towse ta shiuish towse, bee eh er ny howse diu reesht. 
40N||7||3||As cre'n-fa t'ou cronnaghey yn brinneen t'ayns sooill dty vraarey, agh cha vel  geill ayd da'n darrag t'ayns dty hooill hene? 
40N||7||4||Ny kys jir oo rish dty vraar, Lhig dou yn brinneen y ghoaill ass dty hooill, as  cur-my-ner ta darrag ayns dty hooill hene? 
40N||7||5||Er-crauee-oalsey, tilg hoshiaght yn darrag ass dty hooill hene; as eisht nee oo  dy baghtal fakin dy ghoaill yn brinneen ass sooill dty vraarey. 
40N||7||6||Ny cur-jee shen ny ta casherick da ny moddee, chamoo hilgys shiu ny pearlyn  eu roish muckyn, er-aggle dy stamp ad orroo fo chosh, as dy jyndaa ad reesht, as  shiu y lhottey. 
40N||7||7||Yeearree-jee, as yiow shiu: shir-jee, as nee shiu feddyn: cronk-jee, as yiow  shiu fosley. 
40N||7||8||Son ta dy chooilley unnane ta geearree, geddyn: as y fer ta shirrey feddyn: as  dasyn ta cronkal, bee'n dorrys er ny osley. 
40N||7||9||Ny quoi yn dooinney ny mast' euish, ver clagh da e vac, my hirrys eh arran? 
40N||7||10||Ny my hirrys eh eeast, der eh ard-nieu da? 
40N||7||11||Shen-y-fa my ta fys euish ta nyn beccee, kys dy choyrt giootyn mie da nyn gloan,  cre woad smoo nee'n Ayr eu t'ayns niau nheeghyn mie y choyrt dauesyn ta jannoo aghin  huggey.
40N||7||12||Shen-y-fa dy chooilley nhee cre erbee bailliuish deiney dy yannoo riuish, jean-jee  shiuish y lheid cheddin roosyn: son shoh yn leigh as ny phadeyryn 
40N||7||13||Immee-jee stiagh er y ghiat coon; son lhean ta'n giat, as feayn ta'n raad ta  leeideil gys toyrt-mow, as shimmey ta goll er: 
40N||7||14||Er-yn-oyr dy nee chion ta'n giat, as coon ta'n raad ta leeideil gys bea, as s'tiark  ad ta dy haaghey eh. 
40N||7||15||Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie jeh phadeyryn foalsey, ta cheet hiu ayns coamrey keyrragh,  agh cheu-sthie t'ad nyn moddee-oaldey jollyssagh. 
40N||7||16||Ver shiu enney orroo liorish nyn messyn. Vel mess y villey-feeyney er ny heiy  jeh drineyn, ny mess y villey-figgagh jeh onnaneyn? 
40N||7||17||Myr shen ta dagh billey mie tilgey mess mie: agh ta drogh-villey tilgey drogh  vess. 
40N||7||18||Cha vod billey mie drogh-vess y chur magh: ny drogh-villey mess mie. 
40N||7||19||Bee dy chooilley villey nagh vel gymmyrkey magh mess mie, giarit sheese, as ceaut  ayns yn aile. 
40N||7||20||Shen-y-fa liorish nyn messyn ver shiu enney orroo.
40N||7||21||Cha nee dy chooilley unnane jir rhym's, Hiarn, Hiarn, hed stiagh er reeriaght  niau: agh eshyn ta jannoo aigney my Ayrey t'ayns niau. 
40N||7||22||Jir ymmodee rhym's 'sy laa shen, Hiarn, Hiarn, nagh vel shin er n'yannoo phadeyrys  ayns dt'ennym's? as ayns dt'ennym er chastey drogh-spyrrydyn? as ayns dt'ennym er  n'yannoo ymmodee obbraghyn yindyssagh? 
40N||7||23||As eisht neem's fockley-magh orroo, Cha row aym rieau ainjys erbee erriu: reue-jee  voym, O shiuish ghrogh-yantee. 
40N||7||24||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen ta clashtyn ad shoh my ghoan's, as jannoo ymmyd mie  jeu soylee-ym eh gys dooinney creeney hrog e hie er creg: 
40N||7||25||As haink y fliaghey neose, as dhatt ny thooillaghyn, as heid ny geayghyn, as  cheau ad er y thie shen: as cha huitt eh, son dy row yn undin echey er creg. 
40N||7||26||As dy chooilley unnane ta clashtyn ad shoh my ghoan's, as nagh vel jannoo ymmyd  mie jeu, bee eh er ny hoylaghey gys dooinney ommijagh, hrog e hie er y gheinnagh:
40N||7||27||As huitt y fliaghey, as dhatt ny thooillaghyn, as heid ny geayghyn, as cheau  ad er y thie shen: as huitt eh, as s'mooar va e lhieggey! 
40N||7||28||As haink eh gy-kione, erreish da Yeesey v'er loayrt ny goan shoh, dy row yn pobble  ayns ard-yindys jeh'n ynsaghey echey. 
40N||7||29||Son dynsee eh ad myr fer ayns slane pooar, as cha nee myr ny Scrudeyryn.
40N||8||1||Tra v'eh er jeet neose jeh'n clieau, deiyr earrooyn mooarey dy leih er.
40N||8||2||As cur-my-ner haink lourane, as hug eh ooashley da, gra, Hiarn, my she dt'aigney  eh, foddee oo mish y yannoo glen.
40N||8||3||As heeyn Yeesey magh e laue, as venn eh rish, gra, My aigney's eh, bee er dty  ghlenney. As chelleeragh va'n louraanys echey er ny ghlenney. 
40N||8||4||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Jeeagh nagh n'insh oo shoh da dooinney erbee, agh immee  royd, as jeeagh oo hene da'n taggyrt, as cheb yn oural doardee Moses son feanish  daue. 
40N||8||5||As tra va Yeesey er n'gholl stiagh ayns Capernaum, haink centurion huggey, guee  er,
40N||8||6||As gra, Hiarn, ta my er-mooinjerey ny lhie ching ec y thie jeh'n chingys-craaee,  ayns stayd feer treih. 
40N||8||7||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Hig-yms, as nee'm eh y lheihys. 
40N||8||8||As dreggyr yn centurion, gra, Hiarn, cha vel mee feeu oo dy heet stiagh fo my  chlea: agh ynrycan loayr y fockle, as bee my harvaant er ny lheihys. 
40N||8||9||Son ta mish mee hene my ghooinney ayns pooar, as sidooryn aym foym: as ta mee  gra rish y dooinney shoh, Immee, as t'eh goll: as rish fer elley, Tar, as t'eh cheet:  as rish my harvaant, Jean shoh, as t'eh dy yannoo eh. 
40N||8||10||Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, ghow eh yindys, as dooyrt eh roosyn va geiyrt er, Dy  firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Lheid y credjue lajer shoh, cha vel mee er gheddyn ayns  Israel hene. 
40N||8||11||As ta mee gra riu, dy jig ymmodee veih yn niar as veih yn neear, as dy soie ad  sheese marish Abraham, as Isaac, as Jacob, ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||8||12||Agh bee cloan y reeriaght er nyn yiooldey magh gys y dorraghys sodjey-mooie:  ayns shen vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn. 
40N||8||13||As dooyrt Yeesey rish y centurion, Immee royd, as 'naght myr t'ou er chredjal,  myr shen dy jig oo jeh. As va e er-mooinjerey er ny lheihys ayns yn oor cheddin.   
40N||8||14||As tra va Yeesey er jeet stiagh ayns thie Pheddyr, honnick eh moir e ven ny  lhie, as ching ayns y chiassaghey. 
40N||8||15||As venn eh rish y laue eck, as daag yn chiassaghey ee: as ren ee girree, as shirveish  orroo. 
40N||8||16||Tra va'n fastyr er jeet, hug ad lhien huggey ymmodee va drogh-spyrrydyn ayndoo:  as deiyr eh magh ny spyrrydyn lesh fockle, as laanee eh ooilley ny va ching. 
40N||8||17||Myr shoh va cooilleenit shen ny loayr Esaias y phadeyr, gra, Ghow eh-hene er  ny aslayntyn ainyn, as dymmyrk eh nyn ghoghanyn. 
40N||8||18||Nish tra honnick Yeesey earrooyn mooarey dy leih mygeayrt y mysh, hug eh sarey  dy gholl gys y cheu elley. 
40N||8||19||As haink scrudeyr dy row huggey, as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, eiyr-yms ort raad  erbee dy jed oo. 
40N||8||20||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Ta tuill ec ny shynnee, as idd ec eeanlee yn aer, agh  cha vel ec mac y dooinney wheesh boayl aaght son e chione. 
40N||8||21||As dooyrt fer elley jeh e ynseydee rish, Hiarn, lhig dou hoshiaght goll thie  dy oanluckey my ayr. 
40N||8||22||Agh dooyrt Yeesey rish, Eiyr orrym's, as lhig da ny merriu nyn merriu y oanluckey.   
40N||8||23||As tra v'eh er ghoaill lhuingys, hie e ynseydee marish. 
40N||8||24||As cur-my-ner hrog sterrym mooar ayns yn aarkey, myr shen dy row ny tonnyn brishey  harrish y lhong: agh v'eshyn ny chadley. 
40N||8||25||As haink e ynseydee huggey, as ghooisht ad eh, gra, Hiarn, saue shin: bee mayd  caillit. 
40N||8||26||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu agglagh, shiuish dy chredjue moal? Eisht dirree  eh, as hug eh yn gheay, as yn aarkey fo-harey as va kiuney vooar ayn. 
40N||8||27||Agh ghow ny deiney yindys, gra, Cre'n dooinney eh shoh, dy vel ny eer geayghyn  as y faarkey ayns biallys da! 
40N||8||28||As tra v'eh er jeet gys y cheu elley, gys cheer ny Gergesenee haink daa ghooinney  va drogh-spyrrydyn ayndoo magh ny whail, veih mastey ny hoiaghyn, as cha keoi shen  v'ad, nagh by-lhoys da dooinney erbee goaill yn raad shen. 
40N||8||29||As cur-my-ner deie ad, gra, Cre'n eie t'ayd orrin, Yeesey Vac Yee? vel oo er  jeet dy nyn dorchaghey roish y traa? 
40N||8||30||As tammylt voue va beiyhaghey griagh mooar dy vuckyn. 
40N||8||31||As ghuee ny drogh-spyrrydyn er, gra, My eiyrys oo magh shin, lhig dooin goll  stiagh ayns ny muckyn. 
40N||8||32||As dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee reue. As tra v'ad er jeet ass ny deiney, hie ad stiagh  ayns y ghriagh dy vuckyn: as cur-my-ner roie yn slane griagh gour nyn mullee lesh  yn eaynee gys y cheayn, as v'ad baiht ayns ny ushtaghyn.
40N||8||33||As roie ny bochillyn roue, as haink ad gys yn ard-valley, as dinsh ad dy chooilley  nhee: as mychione ny deiney va seaghnit lesh ny drogh-spyrrydyn. 
40N||8||34||As cur-my-ner, haink y slane ard-valley magh quail Yeesey, as tra honnick ad  eh, ghuee ad er, eh dy gholl roish ass ny ardjyn oc. 
40N||9||1||As ghow eh lhuingys, as hioill eh harrish, as haink eh gys e ard-valley hene. 
40N||9||2||As cur-my-ner, hug ad lhieu huggey dooinney doghanit lesh y chingys craaee, ny  lhie er lhiabbee: as Yeesey goaill tastey jeh'n chredjue oc, dooyrt eh rish y varter,  Vac, bee dy yien mie, ta dty pheccaghyn er ny leih dhyt. 
40N||9||3||Er shoh, dooyrt shiartanse jeh ny scrudeyryn roo hene, T'eh shoh loayrt goan mollaghtagh.   
40N||9||4||As Yeesey toiggal ny smooinaghtyn oc, dooyrt, Cre'n-fa ta drogh smooinaghtyn troggal  ayns ny creeaghyn eu? 
40N||9||5||Son cre sassey dy ghra, Ta dty pheccaghyn er ny leih dhyt? ny dy ghra, Irree seose  as shooill? 
40N||9||6||Agh dy vod fys y ve eu, dy vel pooar ec Mac y dooinney er y thalloo dy leih peccaghyn:  (eisht dooyrt eh rish y varter) Irree, trog lhiat dty lhiabbee, as immee royd gys  dty hie. 
40N||9||7||As dirree eh seose as jimmee eh gys e hie. 
40N||9||8||Agh tra honnick y pobble shoh, ghow ad yindys, as hug ad moylley da Jee, v'er  choyrt lheid y phooar da deiney. 
40N||9||9||As tra yn Yeesey er n'gholl veih shen, honnick eh dooinney va enmyssit Mian, ny  hoie ec boayrd y cheesh: as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym's. As dirree eh seose, as  deiyr eh er. 
40N||9||10||As haink eh gy-kione, myr va Yeesey ny hoie ec bee ayns y thie, cur-my-ner  haink ymmodee publicanee as peccee, as hoie ad sheese marishyn as marish e ynseydee.   
40N||9||11||Tra honnick ny Phariseeyn shoh, dooyrt ad rish e ynseydee, Cre'n-fa ta'n mainshter  eu gee marish publicanee as peccee? 
40N||9||12||Agh cheayll Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel feme ocsyn ta slane er yn er-lhee,  agh ec sleih chingey. 
40N||9||13||Agh immee-jee shiuish, as ynsee-jee cre ta dy ve toiggit liorish y raa shoh,  S'bare lhiam myghin na oural: son cha daink mish dy eamagh er y vooinjer chairagh,  agh er peccee gys arrys. 
40N||9||14||Eisht haink huggey ynseydee Ean, as dooyrt ad, Cre'n-fa ta shinyn as ny Phariseeyn  trostey dy mennick, agh cha vel y vooinjer ayd's trostey? 
40N||9||15||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Vod caarjyn y dooinney-poosee dobberan, choud as ta dooinney  yn phoosee maroo? agh hig ny laghyn, tra vees dooinney yn phoosee er ny ghoaill ersooyl  voue, as shen y traa nee ad trostey. 
40N||9||16||Cha vel dooinney erbee cur peesh dy eaddagh noa er shenn gharmad: son ta'n pheesh  goaill e laane ass y gharmad, as ta'n assee wheesh shen smessey, 
40N||9||17||Chamoo ta sleih coyrt feeyn noa ayns shenn voteilyn: er-nonney ta ny boteilyn  scoltey, as ta'n feeyn er ny gheayrtey, as ta ny boteilyn dy choayl orroo; agh t'ad  cur feeyn noa ayns boteilyn noa, as t'ad ny neesht sauchey. 
40N||9||18||Choud as v'eh loayrt ny goan shoh roo, cur-my-ner haink fer-reill, as hug eh  ooashley da, gra, Ta m'inneen eer nish paartail: agh tar, as cur dty laue urree,  as bee ee bio. 
40N||9||19||As hrog Yeesey, as deiyr eh er, as myr shen ren e ynseydee. 
40N||9||20||(As cur-my-ner haink ben cheu-e-chooylloo, va doghanit lesh roie-folley rish  daa vlein jeig, as venn ee rish oirr e gharmad. 
40N||9||21||Son dooyrt ee r'ee hene, My oddym agh bentyn rish e gharmad bee-ym er my lheihys.   
40N||9||22||Agh hyndaa Yeesey mygeayrt, as tra honnick eh ee, dooyrt eh, Inneen bee dy yien  mie; ta dty chredjue er dty laanaghey. As va'n ven er ny lheihys veih yn oor shen  magh.) 
40N||9||23||As tra va Yeesey er jeet stiagh ayns thie yn er-reill, as tra honnick eh ny bardoonee,  as y cheshaght ooilley 'syn un chiaull.
40N||9||24||Dooyrt eh roo, Scugh-jee, son cha vel y ven-aeg marroo, agh ny cadley. As hie  ad son craidey mysh. 
40N||9||25||As tra va'n sleih er skeayley, hie eh stiagh, as ghow eh ee er laue, as dirree  yn ven-aeg. 
40N||9||26||As hie goo magh jeh shoh trooid ooilley yn cheer. 
40N||9||27||As tra va Yeesey er n'immeeaght veih shen, deiyr daa ghooinney doal er gyllagh  as gra, Jean myghin orrin, Vac 
40N||9||28||As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh ayns y thie, haink ny deiney doal huggey: as dooyrt  Yeesey roo, Vel shiu credjal dy voddym shoh y yannoo? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Ta Hiarn.
40N||9||29||Eisht venn eh rish ny sooillyn oc, gra Cordail rish nyn gredjue dy row nyn aghin  eu. 
40N||9||30||As va ny sooillyn oc er nyn vosley, as hug Yeesey currym gyere orroo, gra, Jeeagh  Jee nagh vow dooinney erbee fys er. 
40N||9||31||Agh tra v'adsyn er n'gholl roue, hug ad goo jeh magh trooid ooilley yn cheer  shen. 
40N||9||32||Erreish daue shoh v'er n'gholl ersooyl, cur-my-ner, hug ad lhieu huggey dooinney  balloo va drogh-spyrryd ayn. 
40N||9||33||As tra va'n drogh-spyrryd er ny chastey, ren y balloo loayrt: as ghow yn pobble  yindys, gra, Cha row rieau lheid shoh er ny akin ayns Israel. 
40N||9||34||Agh dooyrt ny Phariseeyn, Liorish yn ard ghrogh-spyrryd t'eshyn castey drogh-spyrrydyn.   
40N||9||35||As hie Yeesey mygeayrt ooilley ny ard-valjyn as ny baljyn-cheerey oc, gynsaghey  ayns ny kialteenyn oc, as preacheil sushtal yn reeriaght, as lheihys dy chooilley  hingys, as dy chooilley ghoghan mastey'n pobble. 
40N||9||36||Agh tra honnick eh yn chaglym mooar dy leih, v'eh er ny veiyghey lesh chymmey  orroo, er-yn-oyr dy row ad tooillit, as er nyn skeayley noon as noal, myr kirree  fegooish bochilley. 
40N||9||37||Eisht dooyrt eh rish e ynseydee, Ta'n fouyr dy jarroo palchey, agh s'coan ta  ny beayneeyn. 
40N||9||38||Guee-jee shiuish, er-y-fa shen, er Chiarn y fouyr, eh dy chur magh labreeyn gys  y fouyr echey.
40N||10||1||As tra v'eh er n-eamagh er e ghaa ostyl jeig huggey, hug eh daue pooar harrish spyrrydyn  neu-ghlen dy chastey ad, as dy lheihys dy chooilley vonney dy hingys, as dy chooilley  ghoghan. 
40N||10||2||As shoh va enmyn yn daa ostyl yeig; Yn chied-er, Simon, ta enmyssit Peddyr, as  Andreays e vraar, Jamys mac Zebedee, as Ean y braar echeysyn 
40N||10||3||Philip as Parlane, Thomase, as Mian yn publican, Jamys mac Alpheus, as Lebbeus  va slennooit Thaddeus. 
40N||10||4||Simon yn Canaanite, as Yuaase Iscariot, ren myrgeddin eh y vrah. 
40N||10||5||Yn ghaa-yeig shoh hug Yeesey magh, as doardee eh daue, gra, Ny immee-jee raad  ny Hashoonee, ny gys ard-valjyn ny Samaritanee. 
40N||10||6||Agh immee-jee hoshiaght gys kirree cailjey thie Israel. 
40N||10||7||As myr vees shiu goll, jean-jee preacheil, gra, Ta reeriaght niau er-gerrey. 
40N||10||8||Slaanee-jee sleih chingey, glen-jee ny louranee, jean-jee ny merriu y aa-vioghey,  as drogh-spyrrydyn y chastey: nastee ta shiu er gheddyn, as dy nastee cur-jee veue.   
40N||10||9||Ny kiare-jee son airh, ny argid, ny prash y ve eu ayns nyn sporranyn: 
40N||10||10||Ny spagey son y raad, ny daa chooat, ny braagyn, ny lorg: (son ta'n obbree toilliu  e veaghey). 
40N||10||11||As ard-valley ny balley erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, Jean-jee briaght quoi ayn  ta feeu, as marishyn gow-jee aaght derrey hed shiu reue. 
40N||10||12||As tra hed shiu stiagh ayns thie, bannee-jee daue. 
40N||10||13||As my vees y thie feeu, lhig da'n shee eu cheet er: agh mannagh bee eh feeu,  lhig da'n shee eu chyndaa hiu hene reesht. 
40N||10||14||As quoi-erbee nagh der oltaghey bea diu, as nash der geill da ny goan eu: tra  aagys shiu yn thie ny'n ard-valley shen, crie-jee veue joan nyn goshey. 
40N||10||15||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy bee eh ny sassey da cheer Sodom as Gomorrah,  ec laa ny briwnys, na da'n ard-valley shen. 
40N||10||16||Cur-my-ner ta mish dy choyrt shiu magh myr kirree mastey moddee oaldey: Bee-jee  er-y-fa shen tastagh myr ard-nieughyn, as oney myr calmaneyn. 
40N||10||17||Agh bee-jee er nyn dwoaie roish deiney, son livrey-ee ad shiu seose gys ny coonceilyn,  as scuitchee ad shiu ayns nyn quaiylyn oc.
