40N||10||18||As bee shiu er nyn goyrt fenish kiannoortyn as reeaghyn er y choontey aym's,  myr shoh gymmyrkey feanish dauesyn, as da ny Ashoonee. 
40N||10||19||Agh tra ver ad stiagh shiu, ny bee-jee imneagh cre'n aght, ny cre nee shiu gra,  son bee eh er ny choyrt diu ayns yn oor cheddin cre nee shiu y ghra. 
40N||10||20||Son cha nee shiuish ta loayrt, agh spyrryd yn Ayr eu ta loayrt ayndiu. 
40N||10||21||As livreyee braar seose e vraar gys baase, as yn ayr e lhiannoo: as nee cloan  girree magh noi nyn ayr as nyn moir, as bee ad feanishyn baaish orroo. 
40N||10||22||As ver yn ymmodee feoh diu er coontey yn ennym aym's: agh eshyn nee shassoo magh  gys y jerrey, bee eh er ny hauail. 
40N||10||23||Agh tra nee ad tranlaase erriu ayns un ard-valley, cosne-jee reue gys ard-valley  elley: son ta mee shickyrys diu, nagh bee shiu er n'gholl harrish ard-valjyn Israel  derrey vees Mac y dooinney er jeet. 
40N||10||24||Cha vel y scoillar erskyn e vainshter ny'n charvaant erskyn e hiarn. 
40N||10||25||S'lioar da'n scoillar dy ve myr e vainshter, as y charvaant myr e hiarn: my t'ad  er cheau Beelzebub er mainshter y thie, cre woad smoo nee ad e vooinjer y oltooaney.   
40N||10||26||Ny gow-jee er-y-fa shen aggle roue: son cha vel nhee erbee follit nagh jir gys  soilshey: ny nhee erbee keillit, nagh jig er-ash. 
40N||10||27||Shen ta mish dy insh diu ayns folliaght fockle-jee shiuish magh eh dy foshlit:  as shen ta shiu er chlashtyn myr hannish voym's, jean-jee y phreacheil er mullagh  ny dhieyn. 
40N||10||28||As ny bee aggle erriu rouesyn varrys y corp, agh nagh jarg er yn annym y varroo:  agh bee-jee ayns aggle smoo roishyn oddys annym as callin neesht y stroie ayns niurin.   
40N||10||29||Nagh vel daa sparroo er nyn greck son farling? as cha duitt unnane oc marroo  er y thalloo fegooish oardagh yn Ayr eu. 
40N||10||30||Agh ta eer renaigyn nyn ghing ooilley er nyn earroo. 
40N||10||31||Ny bee-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen ayns aggle, ta ny smoo dy ve soit jiuish na jeh  ymmodee sperriu. 
40N||10||32||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen ghoys rhym's kiongoyrt rish deiney, goym's rishyn myrgeddin  kiongoyrt rish my Ayr t'ayns niau. 
40N||10||33||Agh quoie-erbee obbys mish kiongoyrt rish deiney, eshyn neem's myrgeddin y obbal  kiongoyrt rish my Ayr t'ayns niau. 
40N||10||34||Ny smooinee-jee dy daink mish dy chur lhiam shee er y thalloo: cha daink mee  dy chur lhiam shee, agh cliwe. 
40N||10||35||Son ta mish er jeet dy scarrey dooinney veih e ayr, as yn inneen veih e moir,  as y ven-chleuin veih e moir-'sy-leigh 
40N||10||36||As noidyn dooinney vees adsyn jeh'n lught-thie echey hene. 
40N||10||37||Eshyn ta ny s'graihee er ayr ny moir na orrym's, cha vel eh feeu jee'm: as eshyn  ta ny s'graihee er mac ny inneen na orrym's cha vel eh feeu jee'm. 
40N||10||38||As eshyn nagh jean e chrosh y ymmyrkey, as geiyrt orrym's, cha vel eh feeu jee'm.
40N||10||39||Eshyn ta aggindagh e vioys y hauail, caillee eh eh: agh eshyn chaillys e vioys  er my ghraih's, nee eh eh y hauail. 
40N||10||40||Eshyn ta soiaghey jiuish, t'eh soiaghey jeem's: as eshyn ta soiaghey jeem's,  t'eh soiaghey jehsyn t'er my choyrt. 
40N||10||41||Eshyn ta cur oltaghey-bea da phadeyr ayns ennym phadeyr, yiow eh leah phadeyr  as eshyn ta cur oltaghey-bea da dooinney cairagh ayns ennym dooinney cairagh, yiow  eh leagh dooinney cairagh. 
40N||10||42||As quoi-erbee ver agh cappan dy ushtey feayr da unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey  shoh dy iu, son dy vel eh credjal aynym's, dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, nagh jean  eh er aght erbee e leagh y choayl.
40N||11||1||As haink eh gy-kione, erreish da Yeesey v'er choyrt ny curmyn shoh da e ghaa ostyl  jeig dy jagh eh veih shen dy ynsaghey, as dy phreacheil ayns ny ard-valjyn mygeayrt.   
40N||11||2||Nish tra va Ean er chlashtyn ayns y phryssoon jeh obbraghyn Chreest, hug eh jees  jeh e ynseydee hene er chaghteraght huggey, 
40N||11||3||Dy ghra rish, Nee uss eh va dy heet ny vel shin dy yeeaghyn son fer elley? 
40N||11||4||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee, as soilshee-jee da Ean ny reddyn ta  shiu dy chlashtyn as dy akin: 
40N||11||5||Ta ny doail geddyn nyn soilshey, as ny croobee shooyll, ny louraanee er nyn ghlenney,  ny beuyr clashtyn, ny merriu er nyn mioghey, as yn sushtal er ny phreacheil da ny  boghtyn. 
40N||11||6||As bannit ta eshyn nagh jean beg y hoiaghey jeem's. 
40N||11||7||As myr v'ad goll roue, ren Yeesey toshiaght dy ghra rish y pobble mychione Ean,  Cre hie shiu magh gys yn aasagh dy akin? Nee cuirtlagh criht lesh y gheay?
40N||11||8||Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Dooinney coamrit ayns garmad moyrnagh? Cur-my-ner,  t'adsyn ta ceau coamrey moyrnagh ayns cooyrtyn reeoil. 
40N||11||9||Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Nee phadeyr? dy jarroo ta mee gra riu, as fer syrjey  na phadeyr. 
40N||11||10||Son shoh eh, my-e-chione te scruit, Cur-my-ner ta mee cur my haghter magh royd,  dy chiartaghey'n raad kiongoyrt rhyt. 
40N||11||11||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, ny mast' ocsyn t'er ve ruggit jeh mraane, cha vel  fer syrjey na Ean Bashtey er droggal: ny-yeih ta'n fer sloo t'ayns reeriaght niau  ny syrjey na eshyn.
40N||11||12||As er-dy laghyn Ean Bashtey derrey nish, ta sleih chionney stiagh gys reeriaght  niau, as t'adsyn ta cheet lesh jeeanid cosney stiagh ayn. 
40N||11||13||Son ren ooilley ny phadeyryn as y leigh phadeyrys derrey Ean. 
40N||11||14||As my ta shiu booiagh goaill-rish, shoh Elias va ry-hoi cheet. 
40N||11||15||Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn lhig da clashtyn. 
40N||11||16||Agh cre gys nee'm yn cheeloghe shoh y hoylaghey? T'ad goll-rish cloan ta nyn  soie ayns ny margaghyn, as geamagh da ny sheshaghyn oc. 
40N||11||17||As gra, Ta shin er n'yannoo bingys diu, as cha vel shiu er ghaunsin: ta shin  er hroggal bardoon diu, as cha vel shiu er ghobberan. 
40N||11||18||Son cha daink Ean gee ny giu, as t'ad gra, Ta drogh-spyrryd ayn. 
40N||11||19||Haink Mac yn dooinney gee as giu, as t'ad gra, Cur-my-ner dooinney jollyssagh,  as iuder feeyney, carrey dy publicanee as dy pheccee: agh ta creenaght er ny heyrey  liorish e cloan hene. 
40N||11||20||Eisht ren eh toshiaght dy phlaiynt er ny ard-valjyn, ayndoo va'n chooid smoo  jeh e obbraghyn yindyssagh er nyn yannoo, er-yn-oyr nagh ghow ad arrys. 
40N||11||21||Smerg dhyt's Chorazin, smerg dhyt's Vethsaida: son dy beagh ny obbraghyn yindyssagh  er ny ve jeant ayns Tyre as Sidon t'er ny ve jeant ayndiuish, veagh ad er ghoaill  arrys foddey er-dy-henney ayns aanrit-sack as leoie 
40N||11||22||Agh ta mee gra riu, Dy bee kerraghey s'eddrym er ny choyrt er Tyre as Sidon ec  laa ny briwnys, na vees er ny choyrt erriuish. 
40N||11||23||As uss, Chapernaum, ta dty ooashley roshtyn gys niau, bee oo er dty hilgey sheese  gys niurin: son dy beagh ny obbraghyn yindyssagh er ve jeant ayns Sodom, t'er ve  jeant aynyd's, veagh eh er ve er-mayrn gys y laa t'ayn jiu. 
40N||11||24||Agh ta mee gra riu, dy bee kerraghey sassey er ny choyrt er thalloo Sodom ec  laa ny briwnys, na vees ort's. 
40N||11||25||Ec y traa shen dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh, Ta mee cur booise dhyt, O Ayr,  Hiarn niau as thalloo, er-yn-oyr dy vel oo er cheiltyn ny reddyn shoh vouesyn ta  creeney as tushtagh, as dy vel oo er hoilshaghey ad da oikanyn. 
40N||11||26||Shen dy jarroo myr te, Ayr, son shen myr ve mie ayns dty hilley's. 
40N||11||27||Ta dy chooilley nhee er ny livrey dooys liorish my Ayr: as cha nhione da dooinney  erbee yn Mac, agh yn Ayr: chamoo shione da dooinney erbee yn Ayr, agh y Mac, as eshyn  da s'gooidsave lesh yn Mac eh y hoilshaghey. 
40N||11||28||Tar-jee hym's ooilley shiuish ta deinagh as trome laadit, as neem's shiu y  ooraghey. 
40N||11||29||Gow-jee my whing erriu, as ynsee-jee voym's, son ta mee meen as imlee ayns cree:  as yiow shiu fea da nyn amneenyn. 
40N||11||30||Son ta my whing aashagh, as my errey eddrym. 
40N||12||1||Ec y traa shen hie Yeesey trooid magher arroo-er y doonaght, as va e ostyllyn accryssagh,  as ghow ad toshiaght dy phluckey ny jeeassyn arroo, as dy ee. 
40N||12||2||Agh tra honnick ny Phariseeyn ad, dooyrt ad rish, Cur-my-ner ta dty vooinjer's  jannoo shen nagh vel lowal dy ve jeant er y doonaght. 
40N||12||3||Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Nagh vel shiuish er lhaih cre ren David, tra v'eh hene as  e heshaght accryssagh. 
40N||12||4||Kys hie eh stiagh ayns thie Yee, as d'ee eh yn arran casherick, nagh row lowit  dasyn dy ee, agh da ny saggyrtyn ny-lomarcan? 
40N||12||5||Er-nonney, nagh vel shiu er lhaih ayns y leigh, kys er laghyn y doonaght ta ny  saggyrtyn ayns y chiamble brishey yn doonaght, as foast cha vel peccah er ny choyrt  ass nyn lieh? 
40N||12||6||Agh ta mish gra riuish, dy vel ayns shoh fer syrjey na'n chiamble. 
40N||12||7||Agh dy beagh fys er ve euish, cre ta er ny hoiggal liorish y raa shoh, Share lhiam  myghin na oural, cha beagh shiu er gheyrey yn vooinjer neu-chyndagh. 
40N||12||8||Son ta Mac y dooinney ny Hiarn er y doonaght hene. 
40N||12||9||As tra v'eh er n'gholl veih shen, hie eh stiagh ayns nyn synagogue. 
40N||12||10||As cur-my-ner, va dooinney ayns shen va'n laue echey er shyrgaghey: as, dy vod  dagh oyr plaiynt y ve oc noi Yeesey, denee ad jeh, gra, Vel eh lowal dy lheihys er  laghyn y doonaght? 
40N||12||11||As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi yn dooinney ny mast' eu, vees un cheyrrey echey, as my  huittys ee ayns jeeg er y doonaght, nagh daare eh greme urree, as nagh drog eh ass  ee? 
40N||12||12||Nagh vel dooinney eisht foddey share na keyrrey? Shen-y-fa te lowal dy yannoo  mie er y doonaght. 
40N||12||13||Eisht dooyrt eh rish y dooinney, Sheeyn magh dty laue: as heeyn eh magh ee; as  va'n laue echey er ny lheihys myr y laue elley. 
40N||12||14||Eisht hie ny Phariseeyn magh, as hug ad nyn goyrle dy-cheilley n'oi, kys oddagh  ad eh y stroie. 
40N||12||15||Agh tra va fys ec Yeesey er, jimmee eh veih shen: as deiyr earrooyn mooarey dy  leih er, as ren eh ad ooilley y lheihys. 
40N||12||16||As hug eh currym daue, gyn ad dy vrah eh: 
40N||12||17||As shoh myr va cooilleenit shen ny loayr Esaias y phadeyr, gra, 
40N||12||18||Cur-my-ner, my hirveishagh hene ta mee er reih, my er-graihagh hene, eer taitnys  my anmey: ver-yms yn spyrryd aym's ersyn, as soilshee eh briwnys da ny Ashoonee.   
40N||12||19||Cha bee eh streeuagh ny anveaagh, chamoo chluinnys fer erbee e choraa ayns ny  straidyn. 
40N||12||20||Cuirtlagh vroojit cha jean eh y vrishey, as y bite giare-cheaut cha der eh ass,  derrey ver eh magh briwnys ayns barriaght.
40N||12||21||As ayns yn ennym echeysyn nee ny Ashoonee treishteil. 
40N||12||22||Eisht hug ad lhieu huggey dooinney seaghoit lesh drogh-spyrryd, doal as balloo:  as ren eh eh y lheihys, myr shen dy ren eshyn va doal as balloo chammah loayrt as  fakin. 
40N||12||23||As ghow ooilley yn pobble yindys, as dooyrt ad, Nagh nee shoh mac Ghavid? 
40N||12||24||Agh tra cheayll ny Phariseeyn shoh, dooyrt ad, Cha vel eh shoh castey drogh spyrrydyn,  agh liorish Beelzebub prince ny drogh-spyrrydyn. 
40N||12||25||As Yeesey toiggal ny smooinaghtyn oc, dooyrt roo, Ta dy chooilley reeriaght ta  girree magh n'oi hene goll naardey: as ard-valley ny thie erbee ta girree-magh fo-my-cheilley,  cha vod ad shassoo. 
40N||12||26||As my ta Satan castey Satan, t'eh girree-magh n'oi hene: kys eisht oddys y reeriaght  echey shassoo? 
40N||12||27||As my ta mish liorish Beelzebub castey drogh-spyrrydyn, quoi liorish ta nyn mooinjer  hene dy chastey ad? adsyn er-y-fa shen vees ny briwnyn eu. 
40N||12||28||Agh my ta mish liorish spyrryd Yee castey drogh-spyrrydyn, eisht ta reeriaght  Yee er jeet hiuish. 
40N||12||29||Er-nonney, kys oddys fer goll stiagh ayns thie yn treanagh, as e chooid y ghoaill  er-niart, mannagh geulee eh hoshiaght yn treanagh, as eisht nee eh e hie y roostey?   
40N||12||30||Eshyn nagh vel lhiam, t'eh m'oi: as eshyn nagh vel chymsaghey marym, t'eh skeayley.   
40N||12||31||Shen-y-fa ta mee gra riu, Bee dy chooilley pheccah as raa mollaghtagh er ny  leih da deiney: agh goan mollaghtagh noi yn Spyrryd Noo cha bee er nyn leih da deiney.   
40N||12||32||As quoi-erbee loayrys fockle noi Mac y dooinney, bee eh er ny leih da: agh quoi  erbee loayrys noi yn Spyrryd Noo, cha bee eh er ny leih da, edyr 'sy theihll shoh,  ny 'sy theihll ta ry-heet. 
40N||12||33||Edyr jean-jee yn billey mie, as e vess mie; er-nonney jean-jee yn billey olk,  as e vess olk: son liorish e vess, ta enney er ny choyrt er y villey. 
40N||12||34||O shiuish heeloghe dy ard-nieughyn, kys oddys shiuish ta olk shiu hene, reddyn  mie y loayrt? son ass laanid y chree ta'n beeal loayrt. 
40N||12||35||Ta dooinney mie ass stoyr mie yn chree echey, cur magh reddyn mie: as drogh ghooinney  ass y drogh-stoyr cur magh drogh reddyn. 
40N||12||36||Agh ta mee gra riu, Dy chooilley ghrogh-ockle nee deiney y loayrt, dy der ad  coontey er y hon ec laa ny briwnys. 
40N||12||37||Son liorish dty ghoan bee oo er dty heyrey, as liorish dty ghoan bee oo er dty  gheyrey. 
40N||12||38||Eisht dreggyr shiartanse jeh ny scrudeyryn as jeh ny Phariseeyn, gra, Vainshter,  baillhien cowrey y akin void. 
40N||12||39||Agh dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Ta drogh-heeloghe as neu-ghooghyssagh shirrey  cowrey, agh cha bee cowrey erbee er ny chur daue, agh cowrey yn adeyr Jonas. 
40N||12||40||Son myr va Jonas three laghyn as three oieghyn ayns bolg y whale: myr shen bee  Mac y dooinney three laghyn as three oieghyn ayns cree yn thallooin. 
40N||12||41||Nee deiney Nineveh girree seose ayns briwnys, as y cheeloghe shoh y gheyrey,  er-yn-oyr dy ghow ad arrys ec preacheil Yonas, as cur-my-ner, ta fer syrjey na Jonas  ayns shoh. 
40N||12||42||Nee ben-rein y jiass girree seose ayns briwnys noi yn cheeloghe shoh, as ad y  gheyrey: son haink ish veih ardjyn sodjey magh y thallooin, dy chlashtyn creenaght  Solomon, as cur-my-ner ta fer s'ooasle na Solomon ayns shoh. 
40N||12||43||Tra ta'n spyrryd neu-ghlen er n'gholl ass dooinney, t'eh shooyll trooid faasaghyn  fadane, chee aash, agh ayns fardail. 
40N||12||44||Eisht t'eh gra, Chyndaa-ym gys my hie, ass haink mee; as tra t'eh cheet, t'eh  dy gheddyn eh follym, sceabit, as soit magh dy stooamey. 
40N||12||45||Eisht t'eh goll, as cur lesh marish shiaght spyrrydyn elley ta ny smessey na  eh hene, as t'ad goll shagh as cummal ayns shen: as ta stayd yerrinagh yn dooinney  shen ny s'doogh na'n toshiaght. Eer myr shoh hig eh dy ve er y cheeloghe vee chrauee  shoh. 
40N||12||46||Choud as v'eh foast loayrt rish y pobble, cur-my-ner va e voir as e vraaraghyn  nyn shassoo mooie, shirrey loayrt rish. 
40N||12||47||Eisht dooyrt fer rish, Cur-my-ner, ta dty voir as dty vraaraghyn nyn shassoo  mooie, shirrey loayrt rhyt. 
40N||12||48||Agh dreggyr eshyn yn fer dinsh shoh da, gra, Quoi my voir? as quoi my vraaraghyn?   
40N||12||49||As heeyn eh magh e laue lhieusyn va sheer geiyrt er, as dooyrt eh, Cur-my-ner  my voir, as my vraaraghyn. 
40N||12||50||Son quoi-erbee nee aigney my Ayrey t'ayns niau, eh shen my vraar, as my huyr  as my voir.
40N||13||1||Yn laa cheddin hie Yeesey magh ass y thie, as hoie eh sheese rish oirr ny  marrey.   
40N||13||2||As va earrooyn mooarey dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh huggey, myr shen dy jagh  eh er board lhong, as hoie eh sheese, as va ooilley yn pobble nyn shassoo er y traie.   
40N||13||3||As loayr eh mooarane reddyn roo ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey, gra, Cur-jee my-ner,  hie correyder magh dy chuirr. 
40N||13||4||As myr v'eh cuirr, huitt paart jeh'n rass rish oirr y raad, as haink ny eeanlee,  as d'ee ad seose eh. 
40N||13||5||Huitt paart er thalloo cloaie, raad nagh row mooarane ooir as daase eh er-y-chooyl,  er-yn-oyr nagh row diunid hallooin echey: 
40N||13||6||As tra ghow yn ghrian niart, ve fiojit; as er-yn-oyr nagh row eh er n'ghoaill  fraue, ren eh shymley ersooyl. 
40N||13||7||As huitt paart mastey drineyn: as daase ny drineyn seose as phloogh ad eh. 
40N||13||8||Agh huitt cooid elley jeh ayns thalloo mie, as dymmyrk eh mess, paart keead-filley  paart three-feed-filley, as paart jeih fillaghyn as feed. 
40N||13||9||Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn. 
40N||13||10||As haink e ostyllyn huggey, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou loayrt roo ayns  coraaghyn-dorraghey? 
40N||13||11||Dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Er-yn-oyr dy vel eh er ny choyrt diuish folliaghtyn  reeriaght niau y hoiggal, agh dauesyn cha vel eh er ny choyrt. 
40N||13||12||Son quoi-erbee ta echey, dasyn vees er ny choyrt, as bee towse s'feoiltey er  ny choyrt da: agh quoi-erbee nagh vel echey, veihsyn vees shen ny ta echey, er ny  ghoaill ersooyl. 
40N||13||13||Shen-y-fa ta mee loayrt roo ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: er-yn-oyr, ga dy vel ad  fakin, cha vel ad cur-my-ner: as clashtyn cha vel ad cur geill, chamoo t'ad toiggal.   
40N||13||14||As ayndoosyn ta cooilleenit phadeyrys Esaias, ta gra, Ayns clashtyn, cluinnee  shiu, agh cha jean shiu toiggal: as ayns fakin, hee shiu, agh cha der shiu my-ner   
40N||13||15||Son ta cree yn phobble shoh er n'aase roauyr, as ta ny cleayshyn oc moal dy chlashtyn,  as ny sooillyn oc t'ad er n'yeigh; er-aggle dy vaikagh ad lesh nyn sooillyn, as dy  gluinnagh ad lesh nyn gleayshyn, as dy doiggagh ad lesh nyn gree, as dy beagh ad  er nyn jyndaa, as dy jinnin ad y lheihys 
40N||13||16||Agh bannit ta ny sooillyn euish, son t'ad fakin, as ny cleayshyn eu, son t'ad  clashtyn. 
40N||13||17||Son dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy vel ymmodee phadeyryn as deiney cairagh er  ve aignagh dy akin ny reddyn ta shiuish dy akin, agh cha vel ad er vakin ad: as dy  chlashtyn ny reddyn ta shiuish dy chlashtyn, agh cha vel ad er chlashtyn ad. 
40N||13||18||Clasht-jee er-y-fa shen coraa-dorraghey yn chorreyder. 
40N||13||19||Quoi-erbee ta clashtyn goo yn reeriaght, as nagh vel dy hoiggal eh, ta'n drogh  er cheet, as tayrtyn lesh shen ny va cuirt ayns e chree: shoh eh ghow yn rass rish  oirr y raad. 
40N||13||20||Agh eshyn ghow yn rass ayns ynnydyn claghagh, shen eh ta clashtyn y goo, as jeeragh  lesh boggey dy ghoaill eh: 
40N||13||21||Foast cha vel fraue echey ayn hene agh t'eh cummal rish son tammylt: agh tra  ta seaghyn as tranlaase cheet er, er coontey yn ghoo chelleeragh ta e chredjue failleil.   
40N||13||22||Eshyn myrgeddin ghow yn rass mastey ny drineyn, yn fer ta clashtyn y goo: as  ta kiarail y theihll shoh, as molteyrys berchys plooghey yn goo, as te cheet dy ve  ne vessoil. 
40N||13||23||Agh eshyn ghow yn rass ayns thalloo mie, shen eh ta clashtyn y goo as dy hoigg  eh, as t'eh tilgey mess, as gymmyrkey, paart keead-filley, paart three feed, as paart  jeih fillaghyn as feed. 
40N||13||24||Coraa-dorraghey elley loayr eh roo gra, Ta reeriaght niau er ny hoylaghey gys  dooinney chuirr rass mie ayns e vagher: 
40N||13||25||Agh choud as va sleih nyn gadley haink e noid, as chuirr eh coggyl mastey y churnaght,  as jimmee eh roish. 
40N||13||26||Agh tra va'n chass er n'aase, as e n'gholl my-yeish, eisht haink y coggyl rish  myrgeddin. 
40N||13||27||Er shen haink fir-vooinjerey yn er-thie, as dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter, nagh chuirr  uss rass mie ayns dty vagher? cre voish eisht ta'n coggyl t'ayn? 
40N||13||28||Dooyrt eshyn roo, Noid t'er n'yannoo shoh. Dooyrt ny fir-vooinjerey rish, Nailt  eisht shin dy gholl as dy ghaartlian ass eh? 
40N||13||29||As dooyrt eshyn, Cha naill-ym; er aggle ayns gaartlian yn coggyl, dy n'astyrt  shiu yn churnaght myrgeddin ass ny fraueyn marish. 
40N||13||30||Lhig-jee daue ny-neesht gaase cooidjagh derrey'n fouyr: as ayns earish yn ouyr  jir-yms rish ny beayneeyn, Chymsee-jee cooidjagh hoshiaght yn coggyl ayns bunneeyn  ry-hoi lostey; agh tayrn-jee yn churnaght stiagh ayns my hoalt. 
40N||13||31||Coraa-dorraghey elley loayr eh roo, gra, Ta reeriaght niau goll-rish grine  dy rass mustard ghow dooinney, as chuirr eh ayns e vagher eh.
40N||13||32||As ga dy nee eh sloo jeh dy chooilley rass: foast tra te er n'aase, eh smoo ta  mastey lossreeyn, as te cheet dy ve ny villey: myr shen dy vel eeanlee yn aer cheet  as goaill fastee ayns ny banglaneyn echey. 
40N||13||33||Coraa-dorraghey elley loayr eh roo, Ta reeriaght niau goll-rish soorid ren  ben y ghoaill as coodaghey seose ayns three towseyn dy veinn, derrey va'n clane soorit.
40N||13||34||Ooilley ny goan shoh loayr Yeesey rish y pobble ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey, as  fegooish coraa-dorraghey, cha loayr eh roo: 
40N||13||35||As shoh myr va cooilleenit shen loayr y phadeyr, gra, Foshlym my veeal dy loayrt  coraaghyn-dorraghey, soilshee-ym magh reddyn t'er ve follit er-dy hoshiaght y theihll.   
40N||13||36||Eisht hug Yeesey yn cheshaght ersooyl, as hie eh stiagh ayns y thie: as haink  huggey adsyn va sheer marish, gra, Soilshee dooin coraa dorraghey coggyl yn vagheragh.   
40N||13||37||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo Eshyn chuirr yn rass mie, Mac yn dooinney:
40N||13||38||Yn magher yn seihll: yn rass mie cloan y reeriaght: agh y coggyl cloan y drogh-er:   
40N||13||39||Yn noid chuirr ad yn Jouyl: yn fouyr jerrey yn theihll: as ny beayneeyn ny ainleyn.
40N||13||40||Myr, er-y-fa shen, ta'n coggyl er ny haglym, as er ny lostey ayns yn aile; shen  myr vees eh ec jerrey'n theihll. 
40N||13||41||Ver yn Mac dooinney magh e ainleyn, as teiyee ad ass e reeriaght dy chooilley  nhee ta tayrn sleih gys peccah, as adsyn ta cur rish yn olk; 
40N||13||42||As tilgee ad ad ayns coirrey aileagh: ayns shen vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn.   
40N||13||43||Eisht nee yn chloan chairagh soilshean magh myr y ghrian, ayns reeriaght nyn  Ayrey. Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn. 
40N||13||44||Reesht ta reeriaght niau goll-rish berchys follit ayns magher: yn verchys cheddin  tra ta dooinney dy gheddyn magh t'eh dy choodaghey eh, as ayns boggey jeh t'eh goll  as creck ooilley ny t'echey, as kionnaghey yn magher cheddin. 
40N||13||45||Reesht ta reeriaght niau dy ve soylit rish marchan va shirrey pearlyn costal:   
40N||13||46||As tra v'eh er gheddyn un phearl dy phrice vooar, hie eh, as chreck eh ooilley  ny v'echey, as chionnee eh eh. 
40N||13||47||Reesht ta reeriaght niau goll-rish lieen va cuirt 'sy cheayn as haare jeh dy  chooilley horch dy eeast. 
40N||13||48||As tra ve lane, hayrn ad eh gys thalloo, as hoie ad sheese, as haggil ad yn eeast  mie ayns siyn, agh cheau ad yn drogh eeast ersooyl. 
40N||13||49||Shen myr vees eh ec jerrey yn theihll: hig ny ainleyn magh, as scarree ad yn  vee chrauee veih mastey yn chloan chairal; 
40N||13||50||As tilgee ad ad ayns coirrey dy aile: ayns shen vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn.   
40N||13||51||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Vel shiu er hoiggal ooilley ny reddyn shoh? Dooyrt adsyn rish,  Ta shin, Hiarn. 
40N||13||52||Eisht dooyrt eh roo, Shen-y-fa ta dy chooilley scrudeyr, ta ynsit gys reeriaght  niau, goll-rish dooinney ta ny er-thie (mie) ta cur magh ass e hashtaghyn reddyn  noa as shenn. 
40N||13||53||As haink eh gy-kione, tra va Yeesey erreish ny coraaghyn-dorraghey shoh y loayrt,  dy jimmee eh veih shen. 
40N||13||54||As tra v'eh er jeet gys e heer hene, dynsee eh ad ayns ny synagogueyn oc, ayns  wheesh as dy row ad atchimagh, as dy dooyrt ad, Cre voish ta creenaght as mirrillyn  y dooinney shoh? 
40N||13||55||Nagh nee shoh mac y teyr? Nagh vel e voir enmyssit Moirrey, as e vraaraghyn Jamys  as Joses, as Simon, as Judas? 
40N||13||56||As nagh vel ny shayraghyn echey ooilley marin? cre voish eisht ta ooilley ny  reddyn t'ec y dooinney shoh? 
40N||13||57||As v'ad jymmoosagh rish. Agh dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cha vel phadeyr gyn ooashley,  agh ayns e heer hene, as ayns e hie hene. 
40N||13||58||As cha nhimmey mirril dobbree eh ayns shen, kyndagh rish y vee-chredjue oc. 
40N||14||1||Ec y traa shen cheayll Herod yn Tetrarch jeh goo Yeesey, 
40N||14||2||As dooyrt eh rish e ir-oik, Shoh Ean Bashtey, t'eh er n'irree veih ny merriu,  as er-yn-oyr shen ta mirrillyn er nyn obbraghey 
40N||14||3||Son va Herod er ghoaill Ean, as er choyrt eh ayns geulaghyn 'sy phryssoon, er  coontey Herodias ben e vraar Philip.  
40N||14||4||Son va Ean er ghra rish, Te noi yn leigh, ee dy ve ayd son ben.  
40N||14||5||As tra baillish v'er choyrt eh gy-baase v'eh ayns aggle roish y pobble, er-yn-oyr  dy row ad dy ghoaill eh son phadeyr.  
40N||14||6||Agh er y laa v'er ny reayll corrym rish y laa ruggyr Herod, ghaunse inneen Herodias  ayns yn enish oc, as ghow Herod lane boggey j'ee.  
40N||14||7||Er shen ghiall eh lesh breearrey, dy choyrt-jee cre erbee hirragh ee.  
40N||14||8||As dooyrt ish, myr va e moir er chur roee, Cur dou ayns shoh kione Ean Bashtey  er claare.  
40N||14||9||As by-hrimshey lesh y ree: ny-yeih e coontey yn vreearrey, as y vooinjer v'ec  gien marish, doardee eh (yn kione) dy v'er ny livrey huic.  
40N||14||10||As hug eh fys yn kione dy ve giarit jeh Ean ayns y phryssoon.  
40N||14||11||As va'n kione er ny choyrt er claare as livreit gys y ven-aeg, as hug ish lh'ee  eh gys e moir.  
40N||14||12||As haink e ynseydee, as hrog ad y corp, as doanluck ad eh, as hie ad, as dinsh  ad da Yeesey.  
40N||14||13||Tra cheayll Yeesey jeh, ghow eh lhuingys, as jimmee eh veih shen gys ynnyd  faasagh er-lheh: as tra cheayll y pobble jeh, deiyr ad er ry nyn gosh ass ny ard-valjyn.   
40N||14||14||As hie Yeesey magh, as honnick eh chaglym mooar dy leih, as v'eh er ny veiyghey  lesh chymmey orroo, as laanee eh adsyn va ching.  
40N||14||15||As tra va'n fastyr er, haink e ostyllyn huggey, gra, She boayl faasagh shoh,  as te nish lesh yn anmys; lhig y raad da'n cheshaght, dy vod ad goll roue gys ny  baljyn cheerey, as beaghey y chionnaghey daue hene.
40N||14||16||Agh dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cha lhiass daue goll roue cur-jee shiuish beaghey daue   
40N||14||17||As dooyrt ad rish, Cha vel ain ayns shoh agh queig bwilleenyn, as daa eeast.   
40N||14||18||Dooyrt eshyn, Cur-jee lhieu ad ayns shoh hym's.  
40N||14||19||As doardee eh yn pobble dy hoie sheese er y faiyr, as ghow eh ny queig bwilleenyn  as y daa eeast, as yeeagh eh seose gys niau, as vannee eh, as vrish eh, as hug eh  ny bwilleenyn da ny ostyllyn, as hirveish adsyn ad er y pobble.  
40N||14||20||As ren ad ooilley gee, as v'ad jeant magh: as hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh daag ad,  lane daa vaskad jeig. 
40N||14||21||As adsyn v'er n'ee v'ad queig thousane dooinney, cheu-mooie jeh mraane as cloan.   
40N||14||22||As chelleeragh hug Yeesey er e ostyllyn goaill lhuingys, as goll harrish gys  y cheu elley roish, choud as v'eshyn lhiggey yn raad da'n pobble. 
40N||14||23||As tra v'eh er chur y pobble ersooyl, hie eh-hene er-lheh seose er slieau, dy  ghoaill padjer: as tra va'n fastyr er jeet, v'eh ayns shen ny-lomarcan. 
40N||14||24||Agh va'n lhong nish ayns mean ny marrey, eiyrit noon as noal lesh ny tonnyn:  son va'n gheay nyn 'oi. 
40N||14||25||As ayns y chiarroo arrey jeh'n oie, haink Yeesey huc, shooyll er y cheayn. 
40N||14||26||As tra honnick ny ostyllyn eh shooyll er y cheayn, v'ad atchimagh, gra, She scaan  t'ayn; as deie ad magh ayns aggle. 
40N||14||27||Agh chelleeragh loayr Yeesey roo, gra, Bee-jee dy yien mie, she mish t'ayn, ny  gow-jee aggle. 
40N||14||28||As dreggyr Peddyr eh, gra, Hiarn, my she oo t'ayn, abbyr rhym cheet hood er yn  ushtey. 
40N||14||29||As dooyrt eh, Tar royd. As tra va Peddyr er jeet neose ass y lhong, huill eh  er yn ushtey, dy gholl gys Yeesey. 
40N||14||30||Agh gennaghtyn yn gheay rastagh, v'eh agglit: as aarloo dy gholl fo, dyllee eh,  gra, Hiarn, saue mee. 
40N||14||31||As ayns y tullogh, heeyn Yeesey magh e laue, as haare eh eh, as dooyrt eh rish,  O ghooinney faase-chredjuagh, cre'n-fa v'ou mee-ouryssagh? 
40N||14||32||As tra v'ad er n'gholl er-board y lhong, huitt yn gheay. 
40N||14||33||Eisht haink yn cheshaght-lhuingey, as hug ad ooashley da, gra, Ayns firrinys  oo Mac Yee. 
40N||14||34||As tra v'ad er jeet harrish, haink ad gys cheer Ghennesaret. 
40N||14||35||As tra hoig cummaltee yn voayl shen quoi v'eh, hug ad fys magh gys ooilley yn  cheer mygeayrt, as hug ad lhieu huggey ooilley adsyn va doghanit. 
40N||14||36||As ghuee ad er, ynrycan dy ventyn rish oirr e gharmad: as whilleen as venn rish,  v'ad er nyn lheihys. 
40N||15||1||Eisht haink gys Yeesey scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn veih Jerusalem, gra, 
40N||15||2||Cre'n-fa ta dty ostyllyn brishey oardaghyn y chanstyr? son cha vel ad niee nyn  laueyn ec goaill beaghey. 
40N||15||3||Agh dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-oyr ta shiuish brishey sarey Yee liorish  nyn oardaghyn? 
40N||15||4||Son hug Jee sarey, gra, Cur arrym da dty ayr as da dty voir: as, Eshyn ta gwee  mollaght er ayr ny moir, lhig da ve currit dy baase. 
40N||15||5||Agh ta shiuish gra, Quoi-erbee jir rish ayr ny moir, Yn chooid-choonee shen oddagh  uss jerkal rish voym's, te gioot er ny chasherickey gys Jee. 
40N||15||6||As nagh lhiass da cooney sodjey 'choyrt da e ayr ny e voir. Ta shiu myr shoh jannoo  sarey Yee gyn vree liorish ny oardaghyn eu. 
40N||15||7||Chrauee-oalsey, s'mie ren Esaias phadeyrys jiuish, gra, 
40N||15||8||Ta'n pobble shoh tayrn er-gerrey dou lesh nyn meeal, as cur ooashley dou lesh  nyn meillyn, agh ta'n cree oc foddey voym. 
40N||15||9||Agh ayns fardail t'ad cur ooashley dou, gynsaghey son y goo aym's oardaghyn deiney.   
40N||15||10||As deie eh er y pobble, as dooyrt eh roo, Eaisht-jee as toig-jee. 
40N||15||11||Cha nee shen ta goll stiagh ayns veeal ta jannoo dooinney neu-ghlen: agh ny ta  cheet magh ass y veeal, shen ta jannoo neu-ghlen jeh. 
40N||15||12||Eisht haink e ostyllyn huggey, as dooyrt ad rish, Vel fys ayd dy rowl ny Phariseeyn  jymmoosagh, tra cheayll ad raa shoh?
40N||15||13||Agh dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh, Bee dy chooilley villey, nagh vel my Ayr flaunyssagh  er hoiaghey, er ny astyrt ass ny fraueyn. 
40N||15||14||Lhig-jee daue: she leeideilee doal ad ta kione y vooinjer ghoal. As my ta'n doal  shooyll kione y doal, tuittee ad ny-neesht ayns y jeeg. 
40N||15||15||Eisht dreggyr Peddyr, as dooyrt eh rish, Soilshee dooinyn yn coraa-dorraghey  shoh. 
40N||15||16||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Vel shiuish neesht foast fegooish tushtey? 
40N||15||17||Nagh vel shiu foast toiggal, cre-erbee ta goit stiagh ayns y veeal, dy vel eh  goll sheese ayns y volg, as goll magh trooid y chorp? 
40N||15||18||Agh ta ny reddyn ta cheet magh ass y veeal, cheet veih'n chree, as t'ad shen  jannoo dooinney neu-ghlen. 
40N||15||19||Son magh veih'n chree ta cheet drogh smooinaghtyn, dunverys, brishey-poosey,  maarderys, maarlys, feanish foalsey, goan mollaghtagh. 
40N||15||20||Ad shoh ny reddyn ta jannoo dooinney neu-ghlen: agh dy ee lesh laueyn nagh ve  nieet, cha vel shen jannoo dooinney neu-ghlen. 
40N||15||21||Eisht hie Yeesey veih shen, as jimmee eh gys ardjyn Tyre as Sidon. 
40N||15||22||As cur-my-ner va ben va ny Canaanite, haink magh ass ny ardjyn shen, geamagh  as gra, Jean myghin orrym, O Hiarn, vac Ghavid; s'mooar ta my inneen er ny torchaghey  lesh drogh-spyrryd. 
40N||15||23||Agh cha dug eh fockle dy ansoor jee. As haink e ostyllyn, as ghuee ad er, gra,  Lhig y raad j'ee, son t'ee gyllagh nyn yei. 
40N||15||24||Agh dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh, Cha vel mish er my choyrt, agh gys kirree-cailjey  thie Israel. 
40N||15||25||Eisht haink ee, as hug, ee ooashley da, gra, Hiarn, cooin lhiam. 
40N||15||26||Agh dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh, Cha vel eh cooie arran ny clienney y ghoaill, as  y hilgey eh gys ny moddee. 
40N||15||27||S'feer shen, Hiarn, dooyrt ish: foast ta ny moddee gee jeh'n vrooillagh ta tuittym  jeh boayrd nyn mainshter. 
40N||15||28||Er shen dansoor Yeesey, as dooyrt eh r'ee, O ven, s'mooar ta dty chredjue: yn  aghin t'ou dy yeearree dy row ayd. As va'n inneen eck er ny lheihys veih'n oor cheddin.   
40N||15||29||As jimmee Yeesey veih shen, as haink eh er-gerrey da faarkey Ghalilee, as hie  eh seose er slieau, as hoie eh ayns shen. 
40N||15||30||As haink earrooyn mooarey dy leih huggey, as nyn mast' oc va croobee, doail,  balloo, baccee, as ymmodee elley, as hug ad ad nyn lhie ec cassyn Yeesey, as ren  eh ad y lheihys. 
40N||15||31||Ayns wheesh as dy ghow ooilley'n pobble yindys, tra honnick ad ny balloo loayrt,  ny baccee slane, ny croobee shooyll as ny doail fakin, as ren ad Jee Israel y ghloyraghey.   
40N||15||32||Eisht deie Yeesey er e ostyllyn, as dooyrt eh, Ta chymmey aym er y pobble,  er-yn-oyr dy vel ad er ve marym nish three laa, as cha vel monney beaghey oc dy ghoaill:  as cha der-ym ad ersooyl nyn drostey, er aggle dy gannooinee ad er y raad. 
40N||15||33||Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Cre raad yiow mayd wheesh shen dy arran 'syn aasagh,  as  magh lheid yn earroo mooar dy leih?
40N||15||34||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cre-woad bwilleen t'eu? Dooyrt adsyn, Shiaght, as kuse fardalagh  dy eeastyn beggey. 
40N||15||35||As doardee eh da'n pobble dy hoie er y thalloo. 
40N||15||36||As ghow eh ny shiaght bwilleenyn, as ny eeastyn, as hug e booise, as vrish eh,  as hug eh ad da e ostyllyn, as hirveish adsyn er y pobble ad. 
40N||15||37||As ren ad ooilley gee, as v'ad er nyn yannoo magh: as hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh  va er-mayrn lane shiaght baskadyn. 
40N||15||38||As v'adsyn ren gee, kiare thousane dooinney, marish mraane as cloan. 
40N||15||39||As hug eh ersooyl yn pobble, as ghow eh lhuingys, as haink eh gys ardjyn Vagdala.     
40N||16||1||As haink ny Phariseeyn as ny Sadduceeyn dy phrowal eh, as hir ad er, eh dy yeeaghyn  cowrey ennagh daue veih niau. 
40N||16||2||Dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Tra ta'n fastyr er, jir shiuish, Bee emshyr aalin  ayn: son dy vel jirgid 'syn aer. 
40N||16||3||As ayns y voghrey, Bee emshyr vroghe ayn jiu; son ta'n aer jiarg as dullyr. O  shiuish chrauee-oalsey, ta toiggal eu kys dy ghoaill baght jeh neeal yn aer, as nagh  vod shiu baght y ghoaill jeh cowraghyn ny hearishyn? 
40N||16||4||She drogh-heeloghe as neu-ghooghyssagh ta shirrey cowrey, as cha bee cowrey er  ny chur daue, agh cowrey yn adeyr Jonas. As daag eh ad, as jimmee eh roish. 
40N||16||5||Nish tra va e ostyllyn er n'aagail y cheu elley, v'ad er yarrood arran y chur 
40N||16||6||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Gow-jee twoaie, as bee-jee er nyn arrey noi soorid  ny Phariseeyn as ny Sadduceeyn. 
40N||16||7||As loayr ad re-cheilley, gra, Ta shoh er yn oyr nagh dug shin lhien arran. 
40N||16||8||Tra hoig Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh roo, Gheiney faase-chredjuagh, cre'n-fa ta shiu  resooney riu hene son nagh dug shiu lhieu arran? 
40N||16||9||Nagh vel shiu foast toiggal, as nagh vel cooinaghtyn eu er ny queig bwilleenyn  ren magh ny queig thousaneyn, as cre whilleen baskad d'ooilliagh v'eu? 
40N||16||10||Ny er ny shiaght bwilleenyn ren magh ny kiare thousaneyn, as cre-woad baskad hrog  shiu? 
40N||16||11||Kys te nagh vel shiu goaill eu hene nagh nee er arran va mee cheet, agh shiu  dy ghoaill twoaie jeh soorid ny Phariseeyn as ny Sadduceeyn? 
40N||16||12||Eisht hoig ad nagh dug eh raaue daue noi soorid arran, agh noi ynsagh ny Phariseeyn  as ny Sadduceeyn. 
40N||16||13||Tra va Yeesey er jeet gys ardjyn Cesarea Philippi, denee eh jeh e ostyllyn,  gra, Cre ta deiney dy ghra my-mychione's, Mac y dooinney, quoi mee hene? 
40N||16||14||Dooyrt adsyn, Ta paart gra dy nee Ean Bashtey oo, as paart Elias, as ta feallagh  elley gra dy nee Jeremias oo, ny fer jeh ny phadeyryn. 
40N||16||15||Dooyrt eshyn roo, Agh quoi ta shiuish gra, dy vel mee? 
40N||16||16||Dreggyr Simon Peddyr, as dooyrt eh, Uss yn Creest, Mac y Jee bio. 
40N||16||17||Dansoor Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Bannit t'ou uss Simon mac Jona: son cha nee  feill as fuill t'er hoilshaghey shoh dhyt's agh my Ayr t'ayns niau. 
40N||16||18||As ta mee myrgeddin gra rhyt, Dy nee uss Peddyr, as dy nee er y chreg shoh trog-ym's  my agglish: as cha vow giattyn niurin yn varriaght urree. 
40N||16||19||As ver-yms dhyt's ogheryn reeriaght niau: as cre-erbee chianglys oo er y thalloo,  bee eh kianlt ayns niau: as cre-erbee eayslys oo er y thalloo, bee eh er ny eaysley  ayns niau. 
40N||16||20||Eisht hug eh currym er e ostyllyn gyn ad dy insh da dooinney erbee, dy nee eshyn  va Yeesey yn Creest. 
40N||16||21||Veih yn traa shen magh ren Yeesey toshiaght dy hoilshaghey da e ostyllyn, kys  dy beign da goll seose gys Jerusalem, as goll fo mooarane surranse veih'n chanstyr,  as ny ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn, as dy beagh eh er ny choyrt gy baase, agh  dy n'irragh eh reesht er y trass laa. 
40N||16||22||Eisht ghow Peddyr eh er-lheh, as ghow eh toshiaght dy choyrlaghey eh, gra, Foddey  dy row eh void, Hiarn, lheid shoh dy haghyrt dhyt. 
40N||16||23||Agh hyndaa eshyn, as dooyrt eh rish Peddyr, Ass my enish, y violeyder, t'ou cur  ribbey ayns my raad: son cha vel ennaghtyn ayd jeh ny reddyn ta bentyn rish Jee,  agh jeh ny reddyn ta bentyn rish deiney. 
40N||16||24||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish e ostyllyn My ta dooinney erbee aggindagh geiyrt orrym's,  lhig da eh-hene y obbal, as e chrosh y hroggal, as geiyrt orrym. 
40N||16||25||Son quoi-erbee baillish e vioys y hauail, caillee eh eh: as quoi-erbee chaillys  e vioys er my ghraih's, sauee eh eh. 
40N||16||26||Son cre'n vondeish t'ec dooinney, my chosnys eh yn seihll ooilley, as e annym  hene y choayl? ny cre nee dooinney y choyrt ayns coonrey son e annym? 
40N||16||27||Son hig Mac y dooinney ayns gloyr e Ayrey, as e ainleyn casherick marish: as  ec y traa shen cooilleenee eh da dy chooilley ghooinney cordail rish e obbraghyn.   
40N||16||28||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy vel paart nyn shassoo ayns shoh, nagh jean blashtyn  er y baase, derrey hee ad Mac y dooinney cheet ayns e reeriaght. 
40N||17||1||As ec kione shey laa, ghow Yeesey Peddyr, as Jamys, as Ean e vraar, as hug eh lesh  ad er-lheh seose er slieau ard, 
40N||17||2||As va'n cummey echey er ny chaghlaa kiongoyrt roo, as ren yn eddin echey soilshean  myr y ghrian, as va'n coamrey echey gial myr y soilshey. 
40N||17||3||As cur-my-ner, honnick ad Moses as Elias taggloo rish. 
40N||17||4||Eisht dreggyr Peddyr as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Hiarn, s'maynrey dooin dy hannaghtyn  ayns shoh: my she dty aigney's eh, lhig dooin ayns shoh troggal three cabbaneyn:  cabbane er dty hon's, as cabbane son Moses, as cabbane son Elias. 
40N||17||5||Choud as v'eh foast loayrt, ren bodjal sollys skeayley harrystoo: as cur-my-ner  haink coraa ass y vodjal, gra, Shoh my vac ennoil, ayn ta mee goaill slane taitnys,  eaisht-jee rishyn. 
40N||17||6||As tra cheayll ny ostyllyn eh, huitt ad sheese er nyn eddin gys y thalloo, son  s'mooar yn aggle v'orroo. 
40N||17||7||As haink Yeesey as venn eh roo, as dooyrt eh, Trog-jee erriu, as ny gow-jee aggle.   
40N||17||8||As tra hrog ad seose nyn sooillyn, cha vaik ad fer erbee, agh Yeesey ny-lomarcan.   
40N||17||9||As myr v'ad cheet neose jeh'n clieau hug Yeesey currym orroo, gra, Ny insh-jee  yn ashlish da unnane erbee, derrey vees Mac yn dooinney er n'irree veih ny merriu.   
40N||17||10||As denee e ostyllyn jeh, gra, Cre'n-oyr jir ny scrudeyryn dy vel Elias dy heet  hoshiaght? 
40N||17||11||Dansoor Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Hig Elias dy jarroo hoshiaght, as lhiassee eh  dy chooilley nhee: 
40N||17||12||Agh ta mish gra riu, dy vel Elias er jeet hannah, as cha dug ad geill da, agh  t'ad er ghellal rish lurg nyn aigney hene as er yn aght cheddin nee Mac y dooinney  neesht surranse lioroo. 
40N||17||13||Eisht hoig e Ostyllyn dy nee er Ean Bashtey v'eh cheet. 
40N||17||14||As tra v'ad er jeet gys y cheshaght, haink huggey dooinney dy row, gliooney  sheese as gra, 
40N||17||15||Hiarn, jean chymmey er my vac, son t'eh ass e cheeayl, as dy mooar seaghnit:  son t'eh dy mennick tuittym ayns yn aile, as dy mennick ayns yn ushtey. 
40N||17||16||As hug mee lhiam eh gys dty ostyllyn, as cha yarg ad eh y lheihys. 
40N||17||17||Dansoor Yeesey as dooyrt eh, O heeloghe vee-chredjuagh as roonagh, caid ta mish  dy ve meriu? caid ta mee dy hurranse diu? cur lhiat eh hym's ayns shoh. 
40N||17||18||As vaggyr Yeesey er y drogh-spyrryd, as hie eh magh ass: as va'n lhiannoo er  ny lheihys veih'n oor shen. 
40N||17||19||Eisht haink e ostyllyn gys Yeesey er-lheh, as dooyrt ad, Cre liorish nagh voddagh  shinyn eh y lheihys? 
40N||17||20||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Kyndagh rish nyn gredjue moal: son dy firrinagh ta mee gra  riu, Dy beagh nyn gredjue wheesh grine dy rass mustard, jirragh shiu rish y slieau  shoh, Scugh veih shoh noon gys shid, as nee eh scughey: as cha bee nhee erbee ro-ghoillee  diu. 
40N||17||21||Ny-yeih cha vel y dooghys shoh dy ghrogh-spyrrydyn dy ve castit, agh liorish  padjer as trostey. 
40N||17||22||As choud as v'ad ayns Galilee, dooyrt Yeesey roo, Bee Mac y dooinney er ny  vrah gys laueyn deiney: 
40N||17||23||As ver ad eh gy-baase, as y trass laa nee eh girree reesht: as v'ad feer trimshagh.   
40N||17||24||As tra v'ad er jeet gys Capernaum, haink y vooinjer va troggal argid y cheesh  gys Peddyr, gra, Nagh vel y mainshter euish geeck y cheesh? 
40N||17||25||Dooyrt eshyn, Dy row. As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh ayns y thie, va Yeesey ro-laue  rish, gra, Cre t'ou smooinaghtyn, Simon, quoi jeh ta reeaghyn y thallooin troggal  custom ny keesh? jeh nyn gloan hene, ny jeh joarreeyn? 
40N||17||26||Dooyrt Peddyr rish, Jeh joarreeyn. Dooyrt Yeesey rishyn, Eisht ta'n chloan seyr.   
40N||17||27||Ny-yeih, son nagh bee cumys er ny chur hooin, immee uss gys y cheayn, as lhig  sheese dooan, as trog y chied eeast hig hood: as tra vees oo er vosley e veeal, yiow  peesh dy argid ayn; shen gow, as eeck eh er my hon's as er dty hon hene.
40N||18||1||Ec y traa cheddin haink e ostyllyn gys Yeesey, gra, Quoi syrjey ta ayns reeriaght  niau? 
40N||18||2||As deie Yeesey er lhiannoo beg, as hoie eh eh kiongoyrt roo 
40N||18||3||As dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Mannagh jean shiu chyndaa, as cheet  dy ve myr cloan veggey, cha jed shiu stiagh ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||18||4||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen, nee eh-hene y injillaghey myr y lhiannoo beg shoh, eh  syrjey vees ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||18||5||As quoi-erbee nee soiaghey jeh lheid y lhiannoo beg shoh ayns yn ennym aym's, t'eh  jannoo soiaghey jeem's. 
40N||18||6||Agh quoi-erbee ver oyr da unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey shoh ta credjal aynym's  dy huittym (veih'n chredjue) veagh eh ny baare da dy beagh clagh-wyllin er ve croghit  mysh e wannal, as eh dy ve baiht ayns diunid ny marrey. 
40N||18||7||Smerg da'n theihll kyndagh rish oyryn peccah: son shegin da nyn lheid 've ayn;  agh smerg da'n dooinney, liorish ta'n loght cheet. 
40N||18||8||Shen-y-fa my ta dty laue ny dty chass hene dy dty hayrn gys yn olk, giare jeed,  as tilg void ad; te ny share dhyt goll stiagh ayns bea croobagh ny baccagh, na daa  laue ny daa chass y ve ayd, as oo dy ve tilgit ayns yn aile dy bragh farraghtyn.   
40N||18||9||As my ta dty hooill dy dty hayrn gys peccah, pluck assyd, as tilg void ee: te  ny share dhyt goll stiagh ayns bea lesh un hooill, na daa hooill y ve ayd, as oo  dy ve tilgit ayns aile niurin. 
40N||18||10||Cur-jee twoaie nagh soie shiu beg jeh unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey shoh: son ta  mee gra riu, dy vel ny ainleyn ocsyn ayns niau, kinjagh cur-my-ner eddin my Ayr flaunyssagh.   
40N||18||11||Son ta Mac y dooinney er jeet dy hauail shen ny va caillit. 
40N||18||12||Cre ta shiu smooinaghtyn? My ta keead keyrrey ec dooinney, as unnane jeu v'er  n'gholl er-shaghryn, nagh vel eh faagail yn chiare-feed as yn nuy-jeig, as goll gys  ny sleityn, as shirrey yn cheyrrey chailjey? 
40N||18||13||As my she shen dy vel eh dy gheddyn ee, dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy vel eh  goaill ny smoo dy voggey jeh'n cheyrrey shen, ny jeh'n chiare-feed as yn nuy-jeig,  nagh jagh er-shaghryn. 
40N||18||14||Er yn aght cheddin, cha nee aigney nyn Ayr t'ayns niau eh, unnane jeh'n vooinjer  veggey shoh dy herraghtyn. 
40N||18||15||Myrgeddin my nee dty vraar aggair dhyt, immee as insh da e oill eddyr shiu  hene nyn-lomarcan: my eaishtys eh rhyt, t'ou er chosney dty vraar. 
40N||18||16||Agh mannagh n'eaisht eh rhyt, eisht gow mayrt fer ny jees elley, ayns beeal ghaa  ny three dy eanishyn dy vod dy chooilley ockle ve jeant mie. 
40N||18||17||As mannagh der eh geill dauesyn, insh eh da'n agglish: agh mannagh der eh geill  da'n agglish, jeeagh er myr an-chreestee as myr publican. 
40N||18||18||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cre erbee nee shiuish y chiangley er y thalloo,  bee eh kianlt ayns niau: as cre-erbee nee shiu y eaysley er y thalloo, bee eh er  ny eaysley ayns niau. 
40N||18||19||Reesht ta mee gra riu, my nee jees jiuish coardail er y thalloo 'syn un aghin  bee nyn aghin er ny chooilleeney liorish my Ayr t'ayns niau. 
40N||18||20||Son raad ta ghaa ny three er nyn jaglym cooidjagh ayns m'ennym's, shen y raad  ta mish nyn mastey. 
40N||18||21||Eisht haink Peddyr huggey, as dooyrt eh, Hiarn, cre cha mennick as ta orrym's  leih da my vraar, tra yioym aggair liorish? nee choud as shiaght keayrtyn? 
40N||18||22||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cha vel mish gra rhyt, Choud as shiaght keayrtyn: agh choud  as three-feed as jeih keayrtyn shiaght. 
40N||18||23||Shen-y-fa ta reeriaght niau er ny hoylaghey gys ree dy row, baillish coontey  rish e harvaantyn. 
40N||18||24||As tra v'eh er n'yannoo toshiaght dy choontey, haink fer huggey va lhiastyn da  jeih thousane talent. 
40N||18||25||Agh son wheesh as nagh row echey dy eeck, doardee e hiarn eh dy ve creckit as  e ven, as e chloan, as ooilley ny v'echey, as e eeaghyn dy ve eeckit. 
40N||18||26||Huitt y charvaant er-y-fa shen sheese, as ghuee eh er, gra, Cur daill dou, Hiarn,  as nee'm ooilley y eeck dhyt.
40N||18||27||Eisht va chiarn y charvaant shen er ny veiyghey lesh chymmey, as ren eh feaysley  er, as leih eh da ny v'eh dy lhiastyn. 
40N||18||28||Agh hie yn charvaant cheddin magh, as hooar eh fer jeh e heshaghyn-sharvaant  va lhiastyn keead ping da: as haare eh greme er, as ghow eh eh er y scoarnagh, gra,  Eeck shen ny t'ou dy lhiastyn. 
40N||18||29||As huitt e heshey-harvaant sheese ec e chassyn, as ghuee eh er, gra, Cur daill  dou as nee'm ooilley y eeck dhyt. 
40N||18||30||Agh cha lhiggagh eh lesh: agh hie eh, as hilg eh eh ayns pryssoon, derrey eeckagh  eh ny v'eh dy lhiastyn. 
40N||18||31||Myr shen tra honnick e heshaghyn-sharvaant kys hie eh er, ghow ad dy feer olk  rish, as haink ad, as dinsh ad da nyn jiarn ooilley ny va er daghyrt. 
40N||18||32||Eisht deie e hiarn er, as dooyrt eh rish, O ghrogh harvaant, leih mish dhyt's  yn slane lhiastynys shen, er-yn-oyr dy ren oo lheid yn aghin hym: 
40N||18||33||Nagh lhisagh uss myrgeddin as chymmey er ve ayd er dty heshey-harvaant, eer myr  va chymmey aym's ort's? 
40N||18||34||As va e hiarn jymmoosagh, as livrey eh seose eh gys laue y tidoor ny phryssoonagh,  derrey eeckagh eh ooilley ny v'eh dy lhiastyn. 
40N||18||35||Er yn aght shoh myrgeddin nee my Ayr flaunyssagh riuish, mannagh leihee shiu  veih nyn greeaghyn dy chooilley ghooinney da e vraar e loghtyn. 
40N||19||1||As haink eh gy-kione, erreish da Yeesey v'er loayrt ny goan shoh, dy jimmee eh veih  Galilee, as dy daink eh gys ardjyn Yudea, er cheu elley dy Yordan: 
40N||19||2||As deiyr earrooyn mooarey dy leih er, ren eh ad y lheihys ayns shen. 
40N||19||3||Haink ny Phariseeyn huggey myrgeddin dy phrowal eh, as dooyrt ad rish, Vel eh  lowal da dooinney e ven y chur er sooyl son dy chooilley oyr? 
40N||19||4||Dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Nagh vel shiu er lhaih, eshyn chroo ad ec y toshiaght,  dy chroo eh ad fyrrynagh as bwoirrynagh? 
40N||19||5||As dooyrt eh roo, Er-yn-oyr shoh nee dooinney faagail e ayr as e voir, as lhiannee  eh gys e ven: as bee ad ny-neesht un eill. 
40N||19||6||Shen-y-fa cha vel ad ny sodjey jees, agh yn un eill. Cre-erbee er-y-fa shen ta  Jee er chur cooidjagh, ny lhig da dooinney erbee y scarrey veih-my-cheilley. 
40N||19||7||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Cre'n-oyr eisht doardee Moses screeuyn-scarree y choyrt, as  y ven y chur ersooyl? 
40N||19||8||Dooyrt eshyn roo, kyndagh rish creoghys nyn greeaghyn, lhow Moses diu nyn mraane  y chur ersooyl: agh ec y toshiaght cha row eh myr shen. 
40N||19||9||As ta mish gra riu, Quoi-erbee scarrys rish e ven, cheu-mooie jeh son maarderys,  as phoosys ben elley, t'eh brishey-poosey: as quoi-erbee phoosys ish ta scarrit,  t'eh brishey poosey: 
40N||19||10||Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, My she shoh yn chooish eddyr dooinney as e ven, cha  vel eh mie dy phoosey. 
40N||19||11||Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Cha nee dy chooilley ghooinney oddys shen y ghoaill er,  agh adsyn ny-lomarcan daue te er ny choyrt. 
40N||19||12||Son ta deiney gennish ayn, rug myr shen veih brein nyn mayrey: as ta deiney gennish  ayn, v'er nyn yannoo gennish liorish deiney: as ta deiney gennish ayn, t'er n'yannoo  ad-hene gennish er graih reeriaght niau. Eshyn oddys shoh y ghoaill er, lhig da 'ghoaill eh. 
40N||19||13||Eisht hug ad lhieu huggey cloan veggey, dy chur e laueyn orroo, as dy vannaghey  ad: as hug e ostyllyn oghsan daue. 
40N||19||14||Agh dooyrt Yeesey, Sur-jee cloan aegey, as ny jean-jee ad y lhiettal dy heet hym's:  son jeh nyn lheid ta reeriaght niau. 
40N||19||15||As hug eh e laueyn orroo, as jimmee eh veih shen. 
40N||19||16||As cur-my-ner, haink fer huggey, as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter vie, cre'n obbyr  ne lhisins y yannoo dy chosney yn vea veayn? 
40N||19||17||As dooyrt eshyn rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou genmys mish mie? cha vel ayn ny ta mie, agh  unnane, ynrycan Jee: agh my sailts goll stiagh ayns bea, freill ny annaghyn. 
40N||19||18||Dooyrt eshyn rish, Cre ny annaghyn? Dooyrt Yeesey, Cha jean oo dunverys, Cha  brish oo poosey, Cha jean oo geid, Cha n'ymmyrk oo feanish foalsey, 
40N||19||19||Cur arrym da dty ayr as da dty voir: as, Ver oo graih da dty naboo myr dhyt hene.   
40N||19||20||Dooyrt y dooinney aeg rish, Ooilley ny annaghyn shoh ta mee er vreayll veih my  aegid: cre sodjey t'orrym dy vannoo? 
40N||19||21||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, My sailt ve dy firrinagh mie, immee, as creck, as cur ny  t'ayd da ny boghtyn, as bee berchys ayd ayns niau; as tar as eiyr orrym's. 
40N||19||22||Agh tra cheayll yn dooinney aeg yn raa shen, hie eh ersooyl dy trimshagh: son  va state mooar hallooin echey. 
40N||19||23||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish e ostyllyn, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, S'doillee  hed dooinney berchagh stiagh ayns reeriaght niau. 
40N||19||24||As reesht ta mee gra riu, Te ny sassey da camel goll trooid croae snaidey, na  da dooinney berchagh dy gholl stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee. 
40N||19||25||Tra cheayll e ostyllyn shoh, ghow ad yindys erskyn-towse, gra, Quoi eisht oddys  ve er ny hauail? 
40N||19||26||Agh yeeagh Yeesey orroo, as dooyrt eh roo, Gys deiney ta shoh neu-phossible,  agh da Jee ta dy chooilley nhee possible. 
40N||19||27||Eisht dreggyr Peddyr, as dooyrt eh rish, Cur-my-ner, ta shinyn er dreigeil  ooilley, as er n'eiyrt ort's; cre yiow mainyn er-y-fa shen. 
40N||19||28||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, 'Sy stayd noa, tra nee Mac y  dooinney soie er stoyl-reeoil e ghloyr, dy jean shiuish myrgeddin t'er n'eiyrt orrym's  soie er daa stoyl-reeoil yeig, briwnys daa heeloghe yeig Israel. 
40N||19||29||As dy chooilley unnane t'er hreigeil thieyn, ny braaraghyn, ny shayraghyn, ny  ayr, ny moir, ny ben, ny cloan, ny thalloo, er graih m'ennym's, yiow ad keead filley,  as eiraght ayns y vea veayn. 
40N||19||30||Agh bee ymmodee jeusyn ta hoshiaght, er-jerrey; as jeusyn ta er-jerrey hoshiaght.     
40N||20||1||Son ta reeriaght niau casley rish dooinney va ny er-thie, hie magh dy moghey dy ailley  labreeyn son e gharey-feeyney. 
40N||20||2||As tra v'eh er choardail rish ny labreeyn son ping 'sy laa, hug eh ad stiagh ayns  e gharey-feeyney. 
40N||20||3||As hie eh magh mysh y trass oor, as honnick eh feallagh elley shassoo nyn daaue  'syn ynnyd-margee, 
40N||20||4||As dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee shiuish myrgeddin gys y gharey-feeyney, as cre erbee  ta cair, shen yiow shiu. As hie ad rhymboo. 
40N||20||5||Reesht hie eh magh mysh y cheyoo as yn nuyoo oor, as ren eh er yn aght cheddin.   
40N||20||6||As mysh yn un oor jeig, hie eh magh, as hooar eh feallagh elley shassoo nyn daaue,  as dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu nyn shassoo ayns shoh fey ny laa nyn daaue? 
40N||20||7||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Er-yn-oyr nagh vel dooinney erbee er vailley shin. Dooyrt eshyn  roo, Immee-jee shiuish myrgeddin gys y gharey-feeyney, as yiow shiu cre-erbee ta  cair. 
40N||20||8||Myr shen tra va'n fastyr er jeet, dooyrt chiarn y gharey-feeyney rish y stiurt  echey, Eie er ny labreeyn, as cur daue nyn vaill, goaill toshiaght veih yn vooinjer  s'jerree gys y chied eallagh. 
40N||20||9||As tra haink feallagh yn un oor jeig hooar ad dagh dooinney jeu ping y pheesh.   
40N||20||10||Agh tra haink y chied eallagh, heill ad dy voghe ad ny smoo, as hooar adsyn myrgeddin  dagh dooinney e phing. 
40N||20||11||As tra v'ad er ghoaill eh, ren ad tallagh noi yn er-thie. 
40N||20||12||Gra, Cha vel yn vooinjer s'jerree shoh er n'obbraghey agh un oor, as t'ou er  n'yannoo ad corrym rooinyn ta er n'ymmyrkey yn errey as chiass y laa. 
40N||20||13||Agh dreggyr eshyn fer jeu, gra, Heshey vie, cha vel mish jannoo aggair dhyt:  nagh choard uss rhym's son ping?
40N||20||14||Trog shen ny ta lhiat, as immee royd: m'aigney's eh dy choyrt da'n fer s'jerree  shoh, myr ta mee er chur dhyt's. 
40N||20||15||Nagh vel eh lowal dou dy yannoo cre saillym rish my chooid hene? vel dty hooill's  olk, er-yn-oyr dy vel mish mie? 
40N||20||16||Myr shen bee adsyn ta er-jerrey hoshiaght, as adsyn ta hoshiaght er-jerrey: son  shimmey t'er nyn eam, agh s'tiark t'er nyn reih. 
40N||20||17||As myr va Yeesey goll seose gys Jerusalem, ghow eh yn daa ostyl yeig dy lhiattee  er y raad, as dooyrt eh roo, 
40N||20||18||Cur-my-ner ta shin goll seose gys Jerusalem, as bee Mac y dooinney er ny vrah  gys ny ard-saggyrtyn, as gys ny scrudeyryn, as deyree ad eh gy-baase. 
40N||20||19||As livreyee ad seose eh gys ny Ashoonee, as nee ad faghid er, as eh y scuitchal,  as y chrossey: as er y trass laa nee eh girree reesht (veih ny merriu). 
40N||20||20||Eisht haink huggey moir cloan Zebedee, as e mec maree, cur ooashley da, as  shirrey aghin er. 
40N||20||21||As dooyrt eh r'ee, Cre ta dty yeearree? Dooyrt ish rish, Giall daue shoh my ghaa  vac dy hoie, yn derrey yeh er dty laue yesh, as y jeh elley er dty laue hoshtal ayns  dty reeriaght. 
40N||20||22||Agh dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh, Cha vel fys eu hene cre ta shiu dy yeearree.  Vod shiu giu jeh'n cappan ta mish giu jeh, as v'er nyn mashtey lesh y bashtey ta  mish dy ve bashtit lesh? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Foddee mayd. 
40N||20||23||As dooyrt eh roo, Iuee shiu dy jarroo jeh my chappan, as bee shiu er nyn mashtey  lesh y bashtey ta mish dy ve bashtit lesh: agh dy hoie er my laue yesh, as er my  laue hoshtal, cha vel shen lhiam's dy-choyrt, agh ny-lomarcan dauesyn er nyn son  te kiarit liorish my Ayr. 
40N||20||24||As tra cheayll yn jeih shoh, v'ad feer jymmoosagh rish y daa vraar. 
40N||20||25||Agh deie Yeesey orroo huggey, as dooyrt eh, Ta fys eu dy vel princeyn ny Hashoonee  gymmyrkey chiarnys harrystoo, as ta ny ard-gheiney gymmyrkey reill orroo. 
40N||20||26||Agh cha bee shillish myr shen: agh quoi-erbee jiuish baillish ve ooasle, lhig  da ve nyn shirveishagh. 
40N||20||27||As quoi-erbee baillish ve yn ard-ghooinney nyn mast' eu, lhig da ve yn charvaant  eu. 
40N||20||28||Myr nagh daink yn Mac dooinney dy ve shirveishit er, agh dy hirveish, as dy chur  e vioys ny lhiassaghey son ymmodee. 
40N||20||29||As tra v'ad er n'immeeaght veih Jericho deiyr earrooyn mooarey dy leih er. 
40N||20||30||As cur-my-ner, va daa ghooinney doal nyn soie rish oirr yn raad, as tra cheayll  ad dy row Yeesey goll shaghey, deie ad, gra, Jean myghin orrin, O Hiarn, vac Ghavid.   
40N||20||31||As hooar yn pobble foill daue, ad dy ve nyn-dhost: agh deie adsyn wheesh shen  smoo, gra, Jean myghin orrin, O Hiarn, vac Ghavid. 
40N||20||32||As hass Yeesey, as deie eh orroo, as dooyrt eh, Cre bailliu mee dy yannoo er  ny son eu? 
40N||20||33||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Hiarn, dy vod ny sooillyn ain v'er nyn vosley. 
40N||20||34||Myr shen va chymmey ec Yeesey orroo, as venn eh rish ny sooillyn oc: as chelleeragh  hooar ny sooillyn oc nyn soilshey, as deiyr ad er. 
40N||21||1||As tra v'ad tayrn er-gerrey da Jerusalem, as dy row ad er jeet gys Bethphage, gys  cronk ny Oliveyn, hug Yeesey jees jeh e ostyllyn er chaghteraght, 
40N||21||2||As dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee gys y balley-cheerey ta shiu dy akin, as chelleeragh  yiow shiu assyl kianlt as lhiy maree: feayshil-jee as cur-jee lhieu ad hym's.
40N||21||3||As my loayrys dooinney erbee veg riu, abbyr-jee shiuish, Ta feme ec y Chiarn orroo;  as chelleeragh lhiggee eh yn raad daue. 
40N||21||4||Va ooilley shoh jeant, dy voddagh shen ve cooilleenit va loayrit liorish y phadeyr  gra, 
40N||21||5||Insh-jee da inneen Sion, Cur-my-ner, ta dty ree cheet hood dy imlee, as ny hoie  er assyl, as er lhiy sharragh assyl. 
40N||21||6||As hie adsyn rhymboo, as ren ad myr va Yeesey er n'oardaghey daue. 
40N||21||7||As hug ad lhieu yn assyl as y lhiy, as hug ad orroo nyn eaddeeyn, as hug ad eshyn  ny hoie orroo. 
40N||21||8||As ren earrooyn mooarey dy leih skeayley nyn gharmadyn er y raad; yiare feallagh  elley banglaneyn jeh ny biljyn, as skeayl ad ad er y raad. 
40N||21||9||As deie yn pobble hie roish, as adsyn haink ny yei, gra, Hosanna gys mac Ghavid:  bannit t'eshyn ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn, Hosanna ayns yn yrjid. 
40N||21||10||As tra v'eh er jeet gys Jerusalem, va ooilley yn ard-valley ayns anvea, gra, Quoi  eh shoh? 
40N||21||11||Dooyrt y pobble, Shoh Yeesey yn phadeyr, ta veih Nazareth ayns Galilee. 
40N||21||12||As hie Yeesey stiagh ayns chiamble Yee, as deiyr eh magh ooilley adsyn va creck  as kionnaghey ayns y chiamble, as hilg eh harrish ny buird ocsyn va caghlaa argid,  as ny stuill ocsyn va creck calmaneyn. 
40N||21||13||As dooyrt eh roo, Te scruit, Bee my hie's enmyssit thie yn phadjer, agh ta shiuish  er n'yannoo eh ny ooig dy vaarlee. 
40N||21||14||As haink ny doail as ny croobee huggey gys y chiamble, as ren eh ad y lheihys.   
40N||21||15||As tra honnick ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scruderyn ny reddyn yindyssagh v'eh dy  yannoo, as ny paitchyn geamagh ayns y chiamble, as gra, Hosanna gys mac Ghavid, v'ad  feer chorree. 
40N||21||16||As dooyrt ad rish, Vel oo clashtyn cre t'ad shoh dy ghra? Dooyrt Yeesey roo,  Ta mee; nagh lhaih shiuish rieau, Magh ass beill oikanyn as cloan er y cheeagh t'ou  er gheddyn moylley firrinagh? 
40N||21||17||As daag eh ad, as hie eh magh ass yn ard-valley gys Bethany, as ghow eh aaght  ayns shen. 
40N||21||18||Nish ayns y voghrey, myr v'eh goll reesht gys yn ard-valley, v'eh accryssagh.   
40N||21||19||As tra honnick eh billey-figgagh er y raad, haink eh huggey, as cha dooar eh  monney er, agh ynrycan duillagyn, as dooyrt eh rish, Nar aase mess erbee ort's veih  shoh magh er son dy bragh. As chelleeragh ren y billey-figgagh fioghey ersooyl. 
40N||21||20||As tra honnick e ostyllyn shoh, ghow ad yindys, gra, Cre cha leah as ta'n billey  figgagh er chreenagh roish? 
40N||21||21||Dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, My vees shiu credjuagh,  as gyn ve fo mee-ourys erbee, nee shiu cha nee ynrycan shoh ta jeant rish y villey-figggagh,  agh my jir shiu rish y slieau shoh, Bee er dty scughey, as er dty hilgey ayns y cheayn; bee eh er ny yannoo. 
40N||21||22||As cre-erbee nee shiu geearree ayns padjer, lesh credjue, yiow shiu eh. 
40N||21||23||As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh ayns y chiamble, haink ny ard-saggyrtyn as shanstyr  yn phobble huggey myr v'eh gynsaghey, gra, Cre'n phooar t'ayd's dy yannoo ny reddyn  shoh? as quoi hug yn phooar shoh dhyt? 
40N||21||24||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Fenym's jiuish un red; as my inshys shiu  dou eh, inshym's myrgeddin diuish, cre'n phooar t'aym dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh. 
40N||21||25||Bashtey Ean, cre voish ve? veih niau, ny veih deiney? As loayr ad nyn mast' oc  hene, gra, My jir mayd, Veih niau; jir eshyn rooin, Cre'n-fa eisht nagh chred shiu  eh? 
40N||21||26||Agh my jir mayd, Veih deiney; ta aggle orrin roish y pobble; son ta dy chooilley  ghooinney goaill Ean son phadeyr. 
40N||21||27||As dreggyr ad Yeesey, as dooyrt ad, Cha vod mayd ginsh. As dooyrt eh roo, Chamoo  ta mish ginsh diuish, cre'n phooar t'aym, dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh. 
40N||21||28||Agh cre ta shiu dy smooinaghtyn? Va dooinney dy row as daa vac echey, as haink  eh gys yn er-shinney, as dooyrt eh, Vac, Immee as obbree jiu ayns my gharey-feeyney.   
40N||21||29||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Cha jem: agh ny lurg shen ghow eh arrys, as hie eh.   
40N||21||30||As haink eh gys e vac saa, as loayr eh rish myrgeddin. As dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt  eh, Hem, vainshter; as cha jagh eh. 
40N||21||31||Quoi jeu shoh ny-neesht ren aigney e ayrey? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Yn mac shinney.  Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy jed ny publicanee as ny drogh.  vraane stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee reue-ish. 
40N||21||32||Son haink Ean hiuish ayns raad y chairys, as cha chred shiu eh: agh chred ny  publicanee as ny drogh-vraane eh. As ga dy vaik shiu shoh, cha ghow shiu arrys ny  lurg shen, dy chredjal ayn. 
40N||21||33||Eaisht-jee rish coraa-dorraghey elley: Va fer-thie dy row ren garey-feeyney  y hoiaghey, as ren eh cleigh y yannoo mysh, as chleiy eh press-feeyney ayn, as hrog  eh toor, as hoie eh eh rish tannys, as hie eh gys cheer foddey. 
40N||21||34||As tra va earish ny mess tayrn er-gerrey, hug eh e ir-vooinjerey gys y tannys,  dy gheddyn jeh'n mess echey. 
40N||21||35||As ghow yn tannys e ir-vooinjerey, as woaill ad fer, as varr ad fer elley, as  chlagh ad fer elley. 
40N||21||36||Reesht hug eh magh sharvaantyn elley ny s'lhee na'n chied eallagh: as ghell ad  roosyn er yn aght cheddin. 
40N||21||37||Agh er-jerrey ooilley hug eh huc e vac, gra, Bee ad arrymagh da my vac. 
40N||21||38||Agh tra honnick y tannys yn mac dooyrt ad nyn mast' oc hene, Shoh'n eirey, tar-jee,  lhig dooin eh y varroo, as bee'n eiraght echey lhien hene. 
40N||21||39||As ghow ad eh, as hilg ad eh magh ass y gharey-feeyney, as varr ad eh. 
40N||21||40||Tra hig er-y-fa shen Chiarn y gharey-feeyney, Cre nee eh rish yn tannys shen?
40N||21||41||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Stroie-ee eh fegooish myghin ny drogh-gheiney shen, as nee  eh soiaghey yn garey-feeyney rish tannys elley, livrey-ys ny messyn da ayns nyn imbagh  cooie. 
40N||21||42||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Nagh lhaih shiu rieau ayns goo Yee, Yn chlagh ren ny masoonee  y vee-lowal, ta'n chlagh cheddin er jeet dy ve yn ard-chlagh chorneilagh: shoh jannoo  yn Chiarn, as te yindyssagh ayns ny sooillyn ainyn? 
40N||21||43||Shen-y-fa ta mish gra riu, Dy bee reeriaght Yee er ny ghoaill veue-ish, as er  ny choyrt da ashoon ymmyrkys magh yn mess echey. 
40N||21||44||As quoi-erbee huittys er y chlagh shen bee eh er ny vroo: agh er quoi-erbee huittys  y chlagh shen, nee ee cha meen as joan jeh. 
40N||21||45||As tra va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn erreish ny coraaghyn-dorraghey echey  y chlashtyn, dennee ad dy nee jeusyn v'eh loayrt. 
40N||21||46||Agh tra v'ad shleeuit er goaill eh v'ad ayns aggle roish y pobble, er-yn-oyr  dy row ad jeeaghyn er dy ve ny adeyr.
40N||22||1||As dreggyr Yeesey, as loayr eh roo reesht liorish coraaghyn-dorraghey, gra, 
40N||22||2||Ta reeriaght Yee er ny hoylaghey gys ree dy row, ren bannish son e vac 
40N||22||3||As hug eh magh e harvaantyn dy eamagh orroosyn va cuirt gys y vannish: as cha  balliu cheet. 
40N||22||4||Reesht hug eh magh sharvaantyn elley, gra, Abbyr-jee roosyn ta cuirt, Cur-my-ner  ta mee er n'aarlaghey my yinnair: ta my ghew as my veiyn beiyht marroo, as dy chooilley  nhee ullee; tar-jee gys y vannish. 
40N||22||5||Agh hoie adsyn beg jeh as hie ad rhymboo, fer gys e state-hallooin, as fer elley  gys e varchantys 
40N||22||6||As ghow yn chooid elley ny sharvaantyn echey, as ghell ad dy elgyssagh roo, as  varr ad ad. 
40N||22||7||Agh tra cheayll y ree jeh v'eh feer chorree: as hug eh magh e heshaghtyn caggee,  as stroie eh ny dunveryn shen, as losht eh yn ard-valley oc. 
40N||22||8||Eisht dooyrt eh rish e harvaantyn, Ta'n vannish aarloo, agh y vooinjer va cuirt  cha row ad feeu. 
40N||22||9||Gow-jee magh er-y-fa shen gys ny raaidyn mooarey, as whilleen as yiow shiu, cuir-jee  gys y vannish. 
40N||22||10||As hie ny sharvaantyn shen magh gys ny raaidyn-mooarey, as ren ad whilleen as  haink nyn raad y haglym cooidjagh, chammah sie as mie: as va thie ny banshey er ny  lhieeney lesh goaldee. 
40N||22||11||As tra haink y ree stiagh dy akin ny goaldee, honnick eh dooinney ayns shen  nagh row garmad-banshey er: 
40N||22||12||As dooyrt eh rish, Heshey vie, kys haink uss stiagh ayns shoh, fegooish garmad-banshey?  As cha row fockle echey dy ghra. 
40N||22||13||Eisht dooyrt y ree rish ny sharvaantyn, Kiangle-jee eh laue as cass, as gow-jee  eh ersooyl, as tilg-jee eh ayns y dorraghys sodjey-mooie: shen-y-raad vees keayney  as snaggeraght feeacklyn.
40N||22||14||Son shimmey t'er nyn eam, agh s'tiark t'er nyn reih. 
40N||22||15||Eisht hie ny Phariseeyn, as hug ad nyn goyrle dy cheilley, kys dy ghoaill vondeish  er ayns e ghoan. 
40N||22||16||As hug ad magh huggey shiartanse jeusyn v'ad hene er n'ynsaghey marish ny Herodianee,  gra, Vainshter, ta fys ain dy vel oo firrinagh, as dy vel oo gynsaghey raad Yee syn  ynrickys, chamoo t'ou ayns aggle roish dooinney erbee: son cha vel oo soiaghey jeh persoon deiney. 
40N||22||17||Insh dooin er-y-fa shen, Cre t'ou uss smooinaghtyn, Vel eh lowal keesh y eeck  da Cesar mannagh vel? 
40N||22||18||Agh dennee Yeesey yn foalsaght oc, as dooyrt eh, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey vondeish  y ghoaill orrym, shiuish chrauee-oalsey? 
40N||22||19||Jeeagh-jee dou argid y cheesh: as yeeagh ad ping da. 
40N||22||20||As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi ta'n jalloo as y screeu shoh cowraghey? 
40N||22||21||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Cesar. Eisht dooyrt eh roo, Eeck-jee er-y-fa shen da Cesar  shen ny ta lesh Cesar: as da Jee, shen ny ta lesh Jee. 
40N||22||22||Tra cheayll ad shoh ghow ad yindys as daag ad eh, as hie ad rhymboo. 
40N||22||23||Yn laa cheddin haink huggey ny Sadduceeyn, ta gra, Nagh vel irree-seose reesht  veih ny merriu dy ve ayn, as denee ad jeh 
40N||22||24||Gra, Vainshter, ta Moses er ghra, My ta dooinney geddyn baase gyn cloan, dy vel  e vraar dy phoosey yn ven echey, as dy hroggal seose sluight gys e vraar. 
40N||22||25||Nish va ny mast' ain shiaght braaraghyn, as phoose y braar shinney, as geddyn  baase gyn cloan, daag eh e ven da e nah vraar. 
40N||22||26||As hooar y nah vraar myrgeddin baase as y trass, gys y chiaghtoo. 
40N||22||27||As er-jerrey ooilley hooar y ven baase myrgeddin. 
40N||22||28||Shen-y-fa ec yn irree-reesht, quoi jeh'n chiaght vees ee echey son ben, son v'ee  poost roo ooilley. 
40N||22||29||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ta shiu fo marranys, as cha vel toiggal eu jeh  goo ny jeh pooar Yee. 
40N||22||30||Son ec yn irree-reesht, cha vel ad poosey, ny er nyn goyrt ayns poosey; agh t'ad  myr ainleyn Yee t'ayns niau. 
40N||22||31||Agh mychione irree-reesht ny merriu, nagh vel shiu er lhaih shen va loayrit riu  liorish Jee, gra, 
40N||22||32||Mish Jee Abraham, as Jee Isaac, as Jee Yacob? cha vel Jee Jee ny merriu, agh  Jee ny bioee. 
40N||22||33||As tra cheayll y pobble shoh, ghow ad yindys jeh'n ynsaghey echey. 
40N||22||34||Agh tra va ny Phariseeyn er chlashtyn dy row eh er chur ny Sadduceeyn nyn dhost,  v'ad er nyn jaglym cooidjagh. 
40N||22||35||As denee fer jeu ard-ynsit 'sy leigh, question jeh, dy phrowal eh, gra,
40N||22||36||Vainshter, cre yn ard-anney ayns y leigh?
40N||22||37||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Ver oo graih da'n Chiarn dty Yee lesh ooilley dty chree as  lesh ooilley dty annym, as lesh ooilley dt'aigney. 
40N||22||38||Shoh yn chied as yn ard-anney. 
40N||22||39||As ta'n nah anney casley rish, Ver oo graih da dty nahoo myr dhyt hene. 
40N||22||40||Yn daa anney shoh bun y leigh as ny phadeyryn. 
40N||22||41||Choud as va ny Phariseeyn er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, denee Yeesey jeu, 
40N||22||42||Gra, Cre ta nyn smooinaghtyn my chione Creest? quoi da mac eh? Dooyrt adsyn rish,  Mac Ghavid. 
40N||22||43||Dooyrt eshyn roo, Kys eisht dy vel David liorish yn spyrryd genmys eh ny Hiarn,  gra, 
40N||22||44||Dooyrt y Chiarn rish my Hiarn's, Soie uss er my laue yesh, derrey neem's dty  noidyn stoyl dty choshey? 
40N||22||45||My ta David eisht genmys eh ny Hiarn, kys t'eh yn mac echey? 
40N||22||46||As cha row dooinney ny vod oc son ansoor y chur da, chamoo by-lhoys da fer erbee  jeu (veih'n laa shen magh) question erbee sodjey y chur huggey. 
40N||23||1||Eisht loayr Yeesey rish y pobble, as rish e ostyllyn, 
40N||23||2||Gra, Ta ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn nyn soie ayns stoyl Voses. 
40N||23||3||Ooilley er-y-fa shen cre-er-bee nee ad y oardaghey diu dy reayll, freill-jee,  as jean-jee eh; agh ny jean-jee lurg ny obbraghyn oc: son t'ad gra, agh cha vel ad  jannoo. 
40N||23||4||Son t'ad kiangley erraghyn tromey as doillee dy ve er nyn ymmyrkey, as dyn goyrt  ad er geayltyn deiney, agh cha lhie ad hene wheesh mair roo dy hroggal ad. 
40N||23||5||Agh ooilley nyn obbraghyn t'ad dy yannoo dy ve cronnit liorish deiney: t'ad jannoo  lhean ny phylactereeyn oc, as ceau chemmallyn mooarey er nyn gharmadyn, 
40N||23||6||As shynney lhieu ny ard ynnydyn-soie ec cuirraghyn, as ny ard-stuill ayns ny synagogueyn,   
40N||23||7||As sleih dy vannaghey daue ayns ny margaghyn, as dy ve enmyssit liorish deiney,  Rabbi, Rabbi. 
40N||23||8||Agh ny bee-jee shiuish enmyssit Rabbi: son ta un vainshter eu, ta shen dy ghra,  Creest, as ta shiuish ooilley nyn mraaraghyn. 
40N||23||9||As ny enmys-jee dooinney erbee ny mast' eu, Yn ayr: son ta un er ynrycan nyn Ayr,  eer eh t'ayns niau. 
40N||23||10||Chamoo gow-jee erriu dy ve mainshteryn, son ta un er nyn Mainshter, eer Creest.   
40N||23||11||Agh eshyn syrjey ta nyn mast' eu, bee eh nyn shirveishagh. 
40N||23||12||Son quoi-erbee ta dy mooaralagh soiaghey seose eh-hene, bee eh er ny injillaghey,  agh eshyn ta dy injillaghey eh-hene, bee eh er ny hoiaghey seose.
40N||23||13||Agh smerg diuish scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee oalsey; son ta shiu dooney  seose reeriaght niau noi deiney: cha vel shiu goll stiagh shiu hene, as ta shiu dyn  lhiettal adsyn ta aggindagh er goll stiagh. 
40N||23||14||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey; son ta shiu cleiy fo thieyn  mraane-treoghe, as son scaa dy chraueeaght lhiggey erriu dy ve kinjagh ayns padjer:  shen-y-fa ta kerraghey strimmey nyn gour. 
40N||23||15||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey; son ta shiu goll mygeayrt  keayn as thalloo, dy hayrn agh un yoarree gys y chredjue eu hene, as tra t'eh er  jyndaa hiu, ta shiu dy yannoo eh ny lhiannoo dy niurin ghaa wheesh smessey na shiu  hene. 
40N||23||16||Smerg diu leeideilee doal, ta gra, Quoi-erbee looys liorish y chiamble, nagh  vel eh veg: agh quoi-erbee looys liorish airh y chiamble, t'eh kianlt gys e vreearrey.   
40N||23||17||O shiuish vee-cheeayllee as doail: son quoi s'ooasle ta, yn airh, ny'n chiamble  ta casherickey yn airh. 
40N||23||18||As quoi-erbee looys liorish yn altar, nagh vel eh veg: agh quoi-erbee looys liorish  y gioot t'er yn altar, t'eh kianlt gys e vreearrey. 
40N||23||19||O shiuish vee-cheayllee as doail: son quoi s'ooasle ta yn gioot, ny'n altar ta  casherickey'n gioot? 
40N||23||20||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen looys liorish yn altar, t'eh loo liorish yn altar hene,  as liorish dy chooilley nhee ta chebbit er. 
40N||23||21||As quoi-erbee looys liorish y chiamble, t'eh loo liorish y chiamble, as liorishyn  ta cummal ayn. 
40N||23||22||As eshyn looys liorish niau, t'eh loo liorish stoyl-reeoil Yee, as liorishyn  ta ny hoie er. 
40N||23||23||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey; son ta shiu geeck jaghee  jeh mynthey, anise as cummin, agh cha vel shiu er chooilleeney currymyn s'ymmyrchee  yn leigh, cairys, myghin as firrinys: ad shoh lhisagh shiu v'er n'yannoo, fegooish  y chooid elley y aagail gyn jannoo. 
40N||23||24||Shiuish leeideilee doal, ta sheeley veue yn char-chuilag, agh sluggee shiu camel.   
40N||23||25||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey: son ta shiu glenney yn cappan  as y claare er cheu-mooie, agh cheu sthie t'ad lane dy hranlaase as dy neu-heeltys.   
40N||23||26||Pharisee ghoal, glen hoshiaght cheu-sthie yn chappan as y chlaare, dy vod y cheu-mooie  ve glen myrgeddin 
40N||23||27||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey; son ta shiu goll-rish oaiagh  yn t'er nyn ghiallaghey, ta dy jarroo jeeaghyn aalin er cheu-mooie, agh cheu-sthie  t'ad lane dy chraueyn ny merriu, as jeh dy chooilley eajeeys. 
40N||23||28||Shen myr ta shiuish neesht er cheu-mooie cairagh ayns shilley deiney, agh cheu-sthie  ta shiu lane dy chraueeaght-oalsey as dy vee-chairys. 
40N||23||29||Smerg diu scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee oalsey, son dy vel shiu troggal oaiaghyn  ny phadeyryn, as soiaghey magh lhiaghtyn ny deiney cairagh. 
40N||23||30||As gra, Dy beagh shinyn er ve ayns laghyn nyn ayraghyn, cha beagh shin er ve  nyn baarteeasyn maroosyn ayns fuill ny phadeyryn. 
40N||23||31||Shen-y-fa ta shiu nyn veanishyn noi eu hene, ny nee shiuish yn sluight ocsyn  hug ny phadeyryn dy baase. 
40N||23||32||Lhieen-jee seose eisht towse nyn ayraghyn. 
40N||23||33||Shiuish ard-nieughyn, sheeloghe dy ard-nieughyn, kys oddys shiu kerraghey niurin  y scapail? 
40N||23||34||Shen-y-fa, cur-my-ner, ta mish coyrt hiu phadeyryn, as deiney creeney, as scrudeyryn;  as paart jeu nee shiu y varroo, as y chrossey, as paart jeu nee shiu y scuitchal  ayns nyn guaiylyn, as geiyrt ad veih ard-valley gys ard-valley: 
40N||23||35||Dy vod ooilley yn uill chairagh hie er deayrtey er y thalloo tuittym erriu, veih  fuilt Abel cairagh, gys fuill Zecharias, mac Varachias, eh ren shiu y varroo eddyr  y chiamble as yn altar. 
40N||23||36||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy jig dy-chooilley nhee jeu shoh er y cheeloghe  shoh. 
40N||23||37||O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, uss ta cur dy baase ny phadeyryn, as claghey adsyn t'er  nyn goyrt er chaghteraght hood, cre cha mennick as va mish aggindagh v'er haglym  dty chloan cooidjagh, myr ta kiark goaill stiagh e hein, fo my skianyn, as cha jinnagh  shiu! 
40N||23||38||Cur-my-ner, ta'n thie eu faagit diu follym-faase. 
40N||23||39||Son ta mee gra riu, Nagh vaik shiu mish maghey shoh, derrey jirrys shiu, Bannit  ta eshyn ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn. 
40N||24||1||As hie Yeesey magh as jimmee eh veih'n  chiamble; as haink e ostyllyn huggey dy ghoaill  baght marish jeh aalid y chiamble. 
40N||24||2||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Nagh vaik shiu ooilley ny reddyn shoh? dy firrinagh ta mee  gra riu, Nagh bee faagit un chlagh er clagh elley, nagh bee er ny lhieggal. 
40N||24||3||As myr v'eh ny hoie er cronk ny Oliveyn, haink e ostyllyn huggey er-lheh, gra,  Insh dooin, cuin vees ny reddyn shoh? as cre'n cowrey vees jeh'n cheet ayd, as jeh  jerrey yn theihll? 
40N||24||4||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-jee twoaie nagh moll dooinney erbee shiu.   
40N||24||5||Son hig ymmodee ayns my ennym's, gra, Mish yn Creest: as nee ad ymmodee y volley.   
40N||24||6||As cluinnee shiu jeh caggaghyn, as jeh imraaghyn dy chaggaghyn: jeeagh nagh bee  shiu seaghnit: son shegin da dy chooilley nhee jeu shoh cheet gys kione, agh cha  bee yn jerrey foast. 
40N||24||7||Son nee ashoon girree-magh noi ashoon, as reeriaght noi reeriaght: as bee gennaghyn  as crampyn, as craaghyn-thallooin ayns ymmodee ynnydyn. 
40N||24||8||Bee ooilley shoh toshiaght seaghyn diu. 
40N||24||9||Eisht livreyee ad shiu seose dy ve seaghnit, as marree ad shiu: as bee dy chooilley  ashoon dwoaiagh erriu er coontey yn ennym aym's. 
40N||24||10||As eisht nee ymmodee scarrey rish nyn gredjue, as brahee ad, as ver ad feoh yn  derrey yeh da'n jeh elley.
40N||24||11||As nee ymmodee phadeyryn-foalsey girree seose, as mooarane y volley. 
40N||24||12||As er-yn-oyr dy jean olkys bishaghey, nee graih-ghiastyllagh ymmodee feayraghey.   
40N||24||13||Agh bee eshyn, nee tannaghtyn firrinagh gys y jerrey, er ny hauail. 
40N||24||14||As bee sushtal yn reeriaght er ny phreacheil ayns ooilley yn seihll, son feanish  da dy chooilley ashoon, as eisht nee yn jerrey cheet. 
40N||24||15||Tra hee shiu er-y-fa shen eajeeys yn traartys, ta loayrit jeh liorish Daniel  y phadeyr, ny hassoo ayns yn ynnyd casherick, (eshyn ta lhaih, lhig da tastey 'ghoaill).   
40N||24||16||Eisht lhig dauesyn t'ayns Judea chea gys ny sleityn. 
40N||24||17||Eshyn t'er mullagh y thie, ny lhig da cheet neose dy ghoaill marish nhee erbee  ass e hie: 
40N||24||18||As ny lhig dasyn t'ayns y vagher chyndaa back, dy chur lesh e eaddagh. 
40N||24||19||As smerg dauesyn ta torragh, as dauesyn ta cur keeagh ayns ny laghyn shen. 
40N||24||20||Agh guee-jee shiuish nagh bee shiu eginit dy hea ayns y gheurey, ny er y doonaght.   
40N||24||21||Son bee seaghyn mooar ec y traa shen, lheid as nagh row er-dy hoshiaght y theihll  gys y traa t'ayn nish, as lheid as nagh bee dy bragh arragh. 
40N||24||22||As mannagh beagh ny laghyn shen dy leah harrish, cha beagh dooinney bio er ny  hauail: agh er graih yn chloan reiht, bee ny laghyn shen dy leah harrish. 
40N||24||23||Eisht my jir dooinney erbee riu, Cur my-ner, ta Creest ayns shoh, ny ayns shid;  ny cred-jee eh. 
40N||24||24||Son nee Creestyn foalsey, as phadeyryn foalsey girree, as cowraghyn mooarey as  yindyssyn y hoilshaghey, ayns wheesh (my oddagh eh ve) dy jinnagh ad molley yn eer  chloan reiht. 
40N||24||25||Cur-my-ner, ta mish er n'insh diu ro laue. 
40N||24||26||Shen-y-fa my jir ad riu, T'eh ayns yn aasagh, ny gow-jee magh: cur-my-ner, t'eh  ayns ny shamyryn follit, ny cred-jee eh. 
40N||24||27||Son myr ta'n tendreil cheet ass y shiar, as cur soilshey choud as gys y sheear:  myr shen neesht vees cheet Mac y dooinney. 
40N||24||28||Son cre-erbee yn raad vees yn convayrt, shen y raad bee ny urlee er nyn jaglym  cooidjagh.
40N||24||29||Chelleeragh lurg seaghyn ny laghyn shen, hig dorraghys er y ghrian, as cha  der yn eayst e soilshey, as tuittee rollageyn yn aer, as bee pooaraghyn yn aer er  nyn graa. 
40N||24||30||As eisht bee cowrey Mac y dooinney er ny akin ayns yn aer as ec y traa shen nee  ooilley sheelogheyn y thallooin dobberan, as hee ad yn Mac dooinney cheet ayns bodjallyn  yn aer, lesh pooar as gloyr vooar. 
40N||24||31||As ver eh magh e ainleyn lesh yn trumpet dy ard-choraa, as nee ad e chloan reiht  y haglym cooidjagh veih ny kiare geayghyn, veih'n derrey ard fo'n aer gys yn ard  elley. 
40N||24||32||Ynsee-jee eisht coraa-dorraghey veih'n villey-figgagh: tra ta'n banglane echey  foast oor, as cur magh duillagyn, ta fys eu dy vel y sourey er-gerrey. 
40N||24||33||Er yn aght cheddin shiuish, tra hee shiu ooilley ny reddyn shoh, toig-jee dy  vel eh er-gerrey, dy jarroo ec ny dorryssyn. 
40N||24||34||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha bee yn cheeloghe shoh harrish, derrey vees dy  chooilley nhee jeu shoh cooilleenit. 
40N||24||35||Nee yn aer as yn ooir cherraghtyn, agh my ghoan's cha jean cherraghtyn. 
40N||24||36||Agh er y laa as yn oor shen, cha vel fys ec dooinney erbee, cha vel ec ainleyn  niau, agh ec my Ayr ny-lomarcan. 
40N||24||37||Agh myr va laghyn Noe, myr shen myrgeddin vees cheet Mac y dooinney. 
40N||24||38||Son myr ayns ny laghyn va roish y thooilley, v'ad gee as giu, poosey as coyrt  ayns poosey, derrey yn laa hie Noe stiagh ayns yn arg, 
40N||24||39||As cha dug ad tastey, derrey haink y thooilley as ghow eh ad ooilley ersooyl;  myr shen myrgeddin vees cheet Mac y dooinney. 
40N||24||40||Shen y traa vees daa ghooinney ayns y vagher, bee fer goit as fer faagit. 
40N||24||41||Bee daa ven blieh ec y wyllin, yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit. 
40N||24||42||Shen-y-fa bee-jee er nyn arrey, son cha vel fys eu er yn oor tra hig nyn Jiarn.   
40N||24||43||Agh shoh toig-jee, dy beagh fys er ve ec mainshter y thie cre'n oor veagh y maarliagh  er jeet, veagh eh er e arrey, as cha beagh eh er lhiggey da brishey stiagh er hie.   
40N||24||44||Shen-y-fa bee-jee shiuish myrgeddin ullee: son ec lheid yn oor as nagh vel shiu  smooinaghtyn er, hig yn Mac dooinney. 
40N||24||45||Quoi eisht yn charvaant firrinagh as creeney shen, ta e Hiarn er n'yannoo ny  er reill er e vooinjer, dy chur daue nyn meaghey ayns traa cooie? 
40N||24||46||Bannit ta'n charvaant cheddin. yiow e Hiarn, tra hig eh, jannoo myr shen. 
40N||24||47||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy livreyee eh gys y churrym echeysyn ooilley e  chooid. 
40N||24||48||Agh my jir y drogh-harvaant shen ayns e chree, Ta my Hiarn lhiggey shaghey yn  cheet echey, 
40N||24||49||As toshiaght y yannoo dy woalley e heshaghyn-sharvaant, as dy ee as dy iu marish  ny meshtallee. 
40N||24||50||Hig Chiarn y charvaant shen ec laa nagh bee eh jeeaghyn er e hon, as ayns oor  nagh bee eh twoaiagh jeh;
40N||24||51||As giaree eh eh veih-my-cheilley, as pointee eh e chronney marish ny crauee oalsey:  ayns shen vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn.
