40N||25||1||Eisht bee reeriaght niau er ny hoylaghey gys jeih moidynyn, ghow ny lampyn oc, as  hie magh quail y dooinney poosee. 
40N||25||2||As va queig jeu creeney, as queig ommijagh. 
40N||25||3||Hug adsyn va ommijagh lhieu ny lampyn oc, agh cha dug ad lhieu ooil maroo: 
40N||25||4||Agh hug y vooinjer chreeney lhieu ooil ayns ny siyn oc marish nyn lampyn. 
40N||25||5||Choud as v'ad fieau er y dooinney poosee, huitt ad ooilley er saveenagh as cadley.   
40N||25||6||As ec main-oie va eam er ny choyrt, Cur-my-ner ta'n dooinney-poosee cheet, gow-jee  magh ny whail. 
40N||25||7||Eisht dirree ooilley ny moidynyn shen, as hooar ad aarloo nyn lampyn. 
40N||25||8||As dooyrt y vooinjer ommijagh rish y vooinjer chreeney, Cur-jee dooinyn jeh'n  ooil euish, son ta ny lampyn ain goll ass.  
40N||25||9||Agh dreggyr y vooinjer chreeney, gra, Cha der; er-aggle nagh bee dy liooar ain  dooin hene as diuish neesht: share diu roie hucsyn ta creck, as kionnaghey diu hene.   
40N||25||10||As choud as v'ad goll dy chionnaghey haink y dooinney-poosee, as hie yn vooinjer  va aarloo stiagh marish gys y vannish, as va'n dorrys jeight. 
40N||25||11||Ny lurg shen haink ny moidynyn elley gra, Hiarn, Hiarn, foshil dooin. 
40N||25||12||Agh dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, nagh voddym goaill  riu. 
40N||25||13||Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie er-y-fa shen son cha vel fys eu er y laa ny'n oor, nee  Mac y dooinney cheet. 
40N||25||14||Son ta reeriaght niau myr dooinney va mysh goaill jurnah gys cheer foddey,  deie er e harvaantyn hene, as livrey eh daue e chooid: 
40N||25||15||As da fer hug eh queig talentyn, da fer elley jees, as da fer elley unnane, da  dy chooilley ghooinney rere roshtyn e hushtey, as chelleeragh ghow eh e yurnah. 
40N||25||16||Eisht hie yn fer v'er gheddyn ny queig talentyn, as ren eh dellal lhieu, as chossyn  eh queig talentyn elley. 
40N||25||17||As myrgeddin eshyn v'er gheddyn jees, chossyn eh neesht jees elley. 
40N||25||18||Agh eshyn va lesh yn un talent, hie eh as chleiy eh ayns y thalloo, as dollee  eh argid e hiarn. 
40N||25||19||Agh lurg foddey dy hraa haink chiarn ny sharvaantyn shen, as ren eh coontey roo.   
40N||25||20||As haink eshyn v'er gheddyn ny queig talentyn, as hug eh lesh queig talentyn  elley, gra, Hiarn, livrey uss dooys queig talentyn: cur-my-ner, ta mee er chosney  queig talentyn elley lhieu. 
40N||25||21||Dooyrt e hiarn rish, S'mie t'ou er n'yannoo, harvaant vie as firrinagh; t'ou  er ny ve firrinagh ayns y veggan, livrey-yms mooarane gys dty churrym: immee uss  stiagh gys boggey dty hiarn. 
40N||25||22||Haink eshyn myrgeddin v'er gheddyn yn daa halent, as dooyrt eh, Hiarn, livrey  uss dooys daa halent: cur-my-ner, ta mee er chosney daa halent elley lhieu. 
40N||25||23||Dooyrt e hiarn rish, S'mie t'ou er n'yannoo, harvaant vie as firrinagh: t'ou  er ny ve firrinagh ayns y veggan, livrey-yms mooarane gys dty churrym: immee uss  stiagh gys boggey dty hiarn. 
40N||25||24||Agh y fer v'er gheddyn yn un talent haink eh, as dooyrt eh, Hiarn, va fys aym's  dy nee dooinney creoi oo; buinn raad nagh ren oo cuirr, as chaglym raad nagh ren  oo skeayley. 
40N||25||25||As ghow mee aggle, as hie mee as dollee mee dty halent ayns y thalloo: jeeagh,  shoh dhyt dty chooid hene. 
40N||25||26||Dreggyr e hiarn, as dooyrt eh rish, Harvaant vee-chairagh as neu-harroogh, va  fys ayd's dy row mish buinn raad nagh ren mee cuirr, as chaglym raad nagh ren mee  skeayley. 
40N||25||27||Lhisagh oo er-y-fa shen v'er chur my argid magh er-use, as eisht tra harrin,  oddin v'er gheddyn my chooid hene lesh bishaghey. 
40N||25||28||Gow-jee er-y-fa shen yn talent veihsyn, as cur-jee eh dasyn ta jeih talentyn  echey. 
40N||25||29||Son da dy chooilley ghooinney ta kuse echey vees er ny choyrt, as yiow eh ny  smoo: agh veihsyn nagh vel echey vees er ny ghoaill ersooyl eer shen ny ta echey.   
40N||25||30||As tilg-jee yn charvaant neu-harroogh ayns y dorraghys sodjey-mooie: ayns shen  vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn. 
40N||25||31||Tra hig Mac y dooinney ayns e ghloyr, as ooilley e ainleyn casherick marish,  shen y traa hoie-ys eh er stoyl-reeoil e ghloyr. 
40N||25||32||As kiongoyrt rish vees dy chooilley ashoon er nyn jaglym; as scarree eh ad veih-my-cheilley,  myr ta bochilley scarrey eddyr e chirree as ny goair: 
40N||25||33||As soie-ee eh ny kirree er e laue-yesh, agh ny goair er e laue-chiare. 
40N||25||34||Eisht jir y ree roosyn er e laue-yesh, Tar-jee chloan vannit my Ayrey, gow-jee  eiraght 'sy reeriaght ta kiarit diu er-dy hoshiaght y theihll. 
40N||25||35||Son va mee accryssagh, as hug shiu beaghey dou: va mee paagh, as hug shiu jough  dou: va mee my yoarree, as ghow shiu stiagh mee: 
40N||25||36||Rooisht, as ren shiu m'y choamrey: va mee ching, as haink shiu dy my yeeaghyn:  va mee ayns pryssoon, as haink shiu hym. 
40N||25||37||Eisht nee'n chloan chairagh eh y reggyrt, gra, Hiarn, cuin honnick shin oo accryssagh,  as dy dug shin beaghey dhyt? ny paagh, as dy dug shin jough dhyt? 
40N||25||38||Cuin honnick shin oo dty yoarree, as dy-ghow shin stiagh oo? ny rooisht, as dy  ren shin dty choamrey? 
40N||25||39||Ny cuin honnick shin oo ching, ny ayns pryssoon, as dy daink shin dy dty yeeaghyn?   
40N||25||40||As freggyree yn Ree, as jir eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ayns wheesh  as dy vel shiu er n'yannoo eh son y fer sloo jeu shoh my vraaraghyn, ta shiu er n'yannoo  eh er my hon's. 
40N||25||41||Eisht jir eh roosyn myrgeddin er y laue-chiare, Immee-jee voym, chloan churstey  gys yn aile dy bragh farraghtyn, kiarit son y drogh-spyrryd as e ainleyn. 
40N||25||42||Son va mee accryssagh, as cha dug shiu beaghey dou: va mee paagh, as cha dug  shiu jough dou: 
40N||25||43||Va mee my yoarree, as cha ghow shiu stiagh mee: rooisht, as cha ren shiu m'y  choamrey: ching, as ayns pryssoon, as cha daink shiu dy my yeeaghyn. 
40N||25||44||Eisht nee adsyn myrgeddin eh y reggyrt, gra, Hiarn, cuin honnick shin oo accryssagh,  ny paagh, ny dty yoarree, ny rooisht, ny ching, ny ayns pryssoon, as nagh chooin  shin lhiat? 
40N||25||45||Eisht nee eh nyn reggyrt, gra, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ayns wheesh as nagh  ren shiu eh son unnane jeh'n vooinjer sloo jeu shoh, cha ren shiu eh er my hon's.   
40N||25||46||As hed ad shoh ersooyl gys y kerraghey dy bragh farraghtyn: agh y chloan chairagh  gys y vea veayn.
40N||26||1||As haink eh gy-kione erreish da Yeesey ve er loayrt ooilley ny goan shoh, dy dooyrt  eh rish e ostyllyn, 
40N||26||2||Ta fys eu lurg daa laa dy bee feailley ny caisht, as dy bee yn Mac dooinney er  ny vrah dy ve er ny chrossey. 
40N||26||3||Eisht va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scrudeyryn as shanstyr y phobble er nyn jaglym  cooidjagh gys thie yn ard-saggyrt va enmyssit Caiaphas. 
40N||26||4||As hug ad nyn goyrle dy cheilley, my chione Yeesey y ghoaill dy follit, as dy  choyrt eh gy-baase. 
40N||26||5||Agh dooyrt ad, Cha nee er laa ny feailley, er-aggle dy bee irree-magh ayn mastey'n  pobble. 
40N||26||6||Nish tra va Yeesey ayns Bethany, ayns thie Simon yn lourane, 
40N||26||7||Haink huggey ben lesh box alabaster dy ooil feer chostal, as gheayrt ee eh er  e chione, myr v'eh ny hoie ec bee. 
40N||26||8||Agh tra honnick e ostyllyn shoh, v'ad jymmoosagh, gra, Cre'n-fa va'n jummal shoh  jeant?
40N||26||9||Son oddagh yn ooil shoh v'er ny ve creckit son mooarane, as er ny choyrt da ny  boghtyn. 
40N||26||10||Tra hoig Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh roo, Kys dy vel shiu boirey yn ven? son t'ee er  n'yannoo obbyr vie orrym's. 
40N||26||11||Son ta ny boghtyn eu kinjagh meriu, agh mish cha vel eu kinjagh. 
40N||26||12||Son liorish dy vel ee er gheayrtey yn ooil shoh er n y chorp, t'ee er n'yannoo  eh cour my oanluckey. 
40N||26||13||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cre theihll y raad vees yn sushtal shoh er ny phreacheil,  dy bee shoh myrgeddin ta'n ven shoh er n'yannoo, er ny imraa ayns cooinaghtyn j'ee.   
40N||26||14||Eisht hie fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig, va enmyssit Yuaase Iscariot, gys ny ard-saggyrtyn.   
40N||26||15||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre ver shiu dooys, as livrey-ym diuish eh? As choard ad rish  son jeih peeshyn as feed dy argid. 
40N||26||16||As veih'n traa shen v'eh shirrey caa dy vrah eh. 
40N||26||17||Nish er y chied laa jeh feailley yn arran-caisht, haink e ostyllyn gys Yeesey  as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n raad sailt shin dy yannoo aarloo er dty hon dy ee yn eayn  caisht? 
40N||26||18||As dooyrt eh, Gow-jee gys yn ard-valley gys lheid y dooinney shen, as abbyr-jee  rish, Ta'n mainshter gra, Ta my hraa er gerrey, freill-ym y chaisht ec dty hie's  marish my ostyllyn. 
40N||26||19||As ren adsyn myr va Yeesey er n'oardaghey daue, as daarlee ad yn eayn-caisht.   
40N||26||20||Nish tra va'n fastyr er-jeet, hoie eh sheese marish yn daa ostyl yeig. 
40N||26||21||As myr v'ad gee, dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy jean fer jiuish mish  y vrah. 
40N||26||22||As v'ad dy mooar seaghnit, as ren ad toshiaght dagh fer jeu dy ghra rish, Hiarn,  nee orrym's t'ou cheet? 
40N||26||23||As dansoor eshyn, gra, eshyn ta thummey e laue marym ayns y chlaare, eh shen  nee mish y vrah. 
40N||26||24||Ta Mac y dooinney goll, myr te scruit jeh: agh smerg da'n dooinney shen liorish  vees Mac y dooinney er ny vrah: s'mie veagh eh son y dooinney shen mannagh row eh  rieau er jeet er y theihll. 
40N||26||25||Eisht dansoor Yuaase, ren y vrah eh, as dooyrt eh, Vainshter, nee mish eh? Dooyrt  eshyn rish, T'ou er ghra eh. 
40N||26||26||As myr v'ad gee, ghow Yeesey arran as vannee eh  as vrish eh eh, as hug eh  eh da ny ostyllyn, gra, Gow-jee, ee-jee, shoh my chorp's. 
40N||26||27||As ghow eh yn cappan, as hug eh booise, as hug eh eh daue, gra, iu-jee ooilley  jeh shoh. 
40N||26||28||Son shoh my uill's jeh'n conaant noa, t'er ny gheayrtey son ymmodee son leih  peccaghyn. 
40N||26||29||Agh ta mee gra riu, Nagh n'iu-ym maghey shoh jeh mess y villey-feeyney, derrey'n  laa iu-ym eh ass-y-noa meriu ayns reeriaght my Ayrey. 
40N||26||30||As tra v'ad er ghoaill arrane-moyllee hie ad magh gys cronk ny Oliveyn. 
40N||26||31||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Failee yn credjue euish ooilley noght kyndagh rhym's:  son te scruit, Bwoaill-ym's yn bochilley, as bee kirree yn chioltane er nyn skeayley.   
40N||26||32||Agh erreish dou v'er n'irree reesht, hem reu gys Galilee. 
40N||26||33||Dansoor Peddyr as dooyrt eh rish, Ga dy vaill credjue dy chooilley ghooinney  kyndagh rhyt's, cha vaill my chredjue's dy bragh. 
40N||26||34||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt , Noght hene roish gerrym chellee,  dy nob uss mish three keayrtyn.
40N||26||35||Dooyrt Peddyr rish, Dy beign dou goll dy baase mayrt, cha nobbin oo. As er yn  aght cheddin loayr ooilley ny ostyllyn. 
40N||26||36||Eisht haink Yeesey maroo gys ynnyd va enmyssit Gethsemane, as dooyrt eh rish  ny ostyllyn, Soie-jee shiuish ayns shoh, choud as hem's gys padjer 'sy voayl shid.   
40N||26||37||As ghow eh marish Peddyr, as daa vac Zebedee, as ren eh toshiaght dy ve trimshagh  as trome-chreeagh.
40N||26||38||Eisht dooyrt eh roo, Ta my annym feer trimshagh, dy jarroo gys y baase: fuirree-jee  ayns shoh as freill-jee arrey marym. 
40N||26||39||As hie eh red beg sodjey, as huitt eh sheese er e eddin, as ghow eh padjer, as  dooyrt eh, O my Ayr, my oddys eh 've, lhig da'n cappan shoh goll shagh-ym: ny-yeih  cha nee m'aigney's, agh dty aigney's dy row jeant. 
40N||26||40||As haink eh gys ny ostyllyn, as hooar eh ad nyn gadley, as dooyrt eh rish Peddyr,  Kys ta shoh, nagh voddagh shiu arrey y reayll marym un oor? 
40N||26||41||Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie as gow-jee padjer, nagh duitt shiu ayns miolagh: ta'n spyrryd  dy jarroo arryltagh, agh ta'n eill annoon. 
40N||26||42||Hie eh roish reesht yn nah cheayrt, as ghow eh padjer, gra, O my Ayr, mannagh  vod yn cappan shoh goll shagh-ym, fegooish mee dy iu eh, dty aigney's dy row jeant.   
40N||26||43||As haink eh as hooar eh ad nyn gadley reesht: son va ny sooillyn oc trome. 
40N||26||44||As daag eh ad, as hie eh roish reesht as ghow eh padjer yn trass cheayrt, gra  ny goan cheddin. 
40N||26||45||Eisht haink eh gys e ostyllyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Caddil-jee nish, as gow-jee  nyn vea; cur-my-ner ta'n oor tayrn er-gerrey, as ta'n Mac dooinney er ny vrah gys  laueyn peccee.
40N||26||46||Irree-jee, as lhig dooin goll: cur-my-ner t'eshyn er-gerrey dooin ta dy my vrah.   
40N||26||47||As choud as v'eh foast loayrt, cur my-ner, haink Yuaase, fer jeh'n daa ostyl  yeig, as va sheshaght vooar marish lesh cliwenyn as luirg veih ny ard-saggyrtyn as  shanstyr y phobble 
40N||26||48||Nish hug eshyn v'er vrah eh, cowrey daue, gra, Quoi-erbee ver-yms paag da, shen  eh, cum-jee eh dy shickyr. 
40N||26||49||As chelleeragh haink eh gys Yeesey, as dooyrt eh, Dy vannee dhyt, Vainshter;  as phaag eh eh. 
40N||26||50||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, My heshey, cre'n-fa t'ou er jeet? Eisht haink ad, as ghreimm  ad er Yeesey, as ghow ad eh. 
40N||26||51||As cur-my-ner heeyn fer jeusyn va marish Yeesey magh e laue, as hayrn eh e chliwe,  as woaill eh fer-mooinjerey yn ard saggyrt, as ghiare eh yn chleaysh jeh. 
40N||26||52||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cur seose dty chliwe reesht 'sy fine: son nee adsyn  ooilley ta goaill y cliwe, cherraghtyn liorish y chliwe.
40N||26||53||Vel uss smooinaghtyn nagh voddym's nish guee gys my Ayr, as yinnagh eh chelleeragh  hym erskyn daa legion jeig dy ainleyn? 
40N||26||54||Agh kys eisht vees ny scriptyryn er nyn gooilleeney, dy nee shoh myr te dy ve?   
40N||26||55||Ayns yn oor cheddin dooyrt Yeesey rish y pobble, Vel shiu er jeet magh myr noi  maarliagh, lesh cliwenyn as luirg dy my ghoaill? hoie mee meriu gagh-laa gynsaghey  ayns y chiamble, as cha ren shiu my ghoaill. 
40N||26||56||Agh va ooilley shoh jeant, dy voddagh scriptyryn ny phadeyryn ve cooilleenit.  Eisht ren ooilley ny ostyllyn treigeil eh, as cosney roue. 
40N||26||57||As leeid y vooinjer v'er ghoaill Yeesey eh ersooyl gys Caiaphas yn ard saggyrt,  raad va ny scrudeyryn as y chanstyr er nyn jaglym cooidjagh. 
40N||26||58||Agh deiyr Peddyr er foddey ny yei, gys thie yn ard-saggyrt, as hie eh stiagh,  as hoie eh marish y vooinjer dy yeeaghyn cre'n erree harragh er. 
40N||26||59||Nish yn ny ard-saggyrtyn as y chanstyr as ooilley yn choonceil, shirrey feanishyn  foalsey noi Yeesey dy choyrt eh gy-baase. 
40N||26||60||Agh cha dooar ad veg: ga dy daink ymmodee feanishyn foalsey, foast cha dooar  ad veg. Ec y jerrey haink daa eanish foalsey, 
40N||26||61||As dooyrt ad, T'eh shoh er ghra, Ta'n phooar aym's dy lhieggal chiamble Yee,  as dy hroggal eh reesht ayns three laa. 
40N||26||62||As hass yn ard-saggyrt seose, as dooyrt eh rish, Nagh vel oo cur ansoor? cre  shoh t'ad dy lhiassaghey dt'oi? 
40N||26||63||Agh va Yeesey ny-host. As dreggyr yn ard-saggyrt as dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee cur  currym ort liorish y Jee bio, oo dy insh  dooin, nee oo yn Creest mac Yee?
40N||26||64||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, T'ou uss er ghra eh: ny-yeih ta mish gra riu, Ny lurg shoh  hee shiu Mac y dooinney ny hoie er laue yesh yn phooar, as cheet ayns bodjallyn yn  aer. 
40N||26||65||Eisht raip yn ard-saggyrt e choamrey, gra, ren er loayrt goan mollaghtagh, cre'n  feme sodjey t'ain er feanishyn? cur-my-ner, nish ta shiu er chlashtyn e ghoan mollaghtagh.   
40N||26||66||Cre ta shiu smooinaghtyn jeh? Dansoor ad, as dooyrt ad, T'eh toilchin dy ve er  ny choyrt gy-baase. 
40N||26||67||Eisht cheau ad shellaghyn ayns e eddin, as woaill ad eh, as woaill feallagh elley  eh lesh bassyn nyn laueyn. 
40N||26||68||Gra, Jean phadeyrys dooin, uss yn Creest, quoi ta dy dty woalley? 
40N||26||69||Nish va Peddyr ny hoie cheu-mooie jeh'n cheshaght ayns y halley: as haink ben  aeg huggey, gra, V'ou uss myrgeddin marish Yeesey dy Ghalilee. 
40N||26||70||Agh dob eh kiongoyrt roo ooilley, gra, Cha s'aym cre t'ou dy ghra. 
40N||26||71||As tra v'eh er gholl magh ayns y phorch, honnick ben-aeg elley eh, as dooyrt  ee roosyn v'ayns shen, V'eh shoh myrgeddin marish Yeesey dy Nazareth. 
40N||26||72||As reesht dob eh lesh loo, Cha nione dou yn dooinney. 
40N||26||73||As tammylt ny lurg shen haink huggey paart jeh'n cheshaght, as dooyrt ad rish  Peddyr, Shickyr she fer jeu oo, son ta dty ghlare dy dty vrah. 
40N||26||74||Eisht ren eh toshiaght dy ghweeaghyn as dy loo, gra, Cha nione dou yn dooinney.  As chelleeragh ren y kellagh gerrym. 
40N||26||75||As chooinee Peddyr er ny goan va Yeesey er ghra rish, Roish gerrym y chellee,  obbee uss mish three keayrtyn. As hie eh magh as cheayn eh dy sharroo. 
40N||27||1||Tra va'n moghrey er jeet rish, hug ooilley ny ard-saggyrtyn as shanstyr yn phobble  nyn goyrle dy cheilley, dy choyrt eh gy-baase. 
40N||27||2||As erreish daue v'er chiangley eh, leeid ad eh ersooyl, as livrey ad eh gys Pontius  Pilate yn kiannoort, 
40N||27||3||Tra honnick eisht Yuaase ren y vrah eh, dy row eh er ny gheyrey, ghow eh arrys,  as hug eh lesh reesht ny jeih peeshyn as feed dy argid gys ny ard-saggyrtyn as y  chanstyr, 
40N||27||4||Gra, Ta mee er n'yannoo peccah, ayns dy vel mee er vrah yn uill neu-chyndagh.  As dooyrt adsyn, Cre ta shen dooinyn? jeeagh uss da shen. 
40N||27||5||As hilg eh sheese ny peeshyn argid ayns y chiamble, as jimmee eh roish, as hie  eh as ren eh eh-hene y chroghey. 
40N||27||6||As ghow ny ard-Saggyrtyn ny peeshyn argid, as dooyrt ad, Cha vel eh lowal dy choyrt  ad mastey tashtaghyn y chiamble er-yn-oyr dy nee leagh foalley t'ayn.
40N||27||7||As ghow ad coyrle, as chionnee ad lhieu magher yn phasheyder, dy oanluckey joarreeyn  ayn. 
40N||27||8||Shen-y-fa va'n magher shen enmyssit, Yn magher-foalley, gys y laa t'ayn jiu. 
40N||27||9||(Shen y traa va cooilleenit ny va loayrit liorish Jeremy yn phadeyr, gra, As ghow  ad ny jeih peeshyn as feed dy argid, yn phrice echeysyn v'er ny phriceil, eshyn hug  cloan Isra price er: 
40N||27||10||As hug ad ad son magher yn phasheyder, myr va'n Chiarn er n'oardaghey dou). 
40N||27||11||As hass Yeesey fenish y chiannoort, as denee yn kiannoort jeh, gra, Nee uss ree  ny Hewnyn? As dooyrt Yeesey rish, T'ou uss dy ghra eh. 
40N||27||12||As tra v'eh er ny chassid liorish ny ard-saggyrtyn as y chanstyr, cha dug eh  ansoor erbee daue. 
40N||27||13||Eisht dooyrt Pilate rish, Nagh vel oo clashtyn cre whilleen red t'ad shoh cur  stiagh 
40N||27||14||As cha dug eh un ockle dy ansoor da, ayns wheesh as dy ghow yn kiannoort yindys  mooar. 
40N||27||15||Nish ec y feailley shen va'n kiannoort cliaghtey feaysley daue pryssoonagh erbee  dy bailloo. 
40N||27||16||As va oc ec y traa shen ard-phryssoon agh va enmyssit Barabbas. 
40N||27||17||Shen-y-fa tra v'ad er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, dooyrt Pilate roo, Quoi sailliu mee  dy eaysley diu? Barabbas, ny Yeesey, ta enmyssit Creest?  
40N||27||18||Son va fys echey dy nee ayns goanlys v'ad er chur stiagh eh. 
40N||27||19||Erreish da soie er stoyl y vriwnys, hug e ven fys huggey, gra, Ny bee veg ayd's  dy yannoo rish y dooinney cairagh shen: son s'mooar ta mee er hurranse jiu ayns my  chadley, er y choontey echeysyn. 
40N||27||20||Agh choyrlee ny ard-saggyrtyn as shanstyr y phobble ad dy yannoo aghin son Barabbas,  as Yeesey y choyrt gy-baase. 
40N||27||21||Dansoor y kiannoort as dooyrt eh roo, Quoi jeh'n jees sailliu mee dy eaysley  diu? Dooyrt adsyn, Barabbas. 
40N||27||22||Dooyrt Pilate roo, Cre nee'm eisht rish Yeesey, ta enmyssit Creest? Dooyrt ad  ooilley rish, Lhig da v'er ny chrossey. 
40N||27||23||As dooyrt y kiannoort, Cre'n-oyr, cre'n olk t'eh er n'yannoo? Agh deie adsyn  ny smoo, gra, Lhig da v'er ny chrossey. 
40N||27||24||Tra honnick Pilate nagh dug ad geill da e choyrle, agh dy row ad aarloo dy  irree-magh, ghow eh ushtey, as niee eh e laueyn kiongoyrt rish y pobble, gra, Ta  mish neu-chyndagh jeh fuill yn phersoon cairagh shen, jeeagh-jee shiuish da. 
40N||27||25||Eisht dansoor ooilley yn pobble, gra, Yn uill echey dy row orrinyn, as er nyn  gloan. 
40N||27||26||Eisht deayshil eh Barabbas daue; as erreish da Yeesey ve scuitchit, hug eh  briwnys er dy v'er ny chrossey. 
40N||27||27||Eisht hug sidooryn y chiannoort lhieu Yeesey gys halley ny briwnys, as deie ad  er slane sheshaght ny sidooryn. 
40N||27||28||As rooisht ad eh, as hug ad er coamrey scarleod. 
40N||27||29||As fee attey dy ghrineyn hug ad eh mysh e chione, as cuirtlagh ayns e laue-yesh:  as gliooney kiongoyrt rish dooyrt ad ayns craid, Dy vannee dhyt, Ree ny Hewnyn. 
40N||27||30||As cheau ad shellaghyn er, as ghow ad y chuirtlagh, as woaill ad eh er y chione   
40N||27||31||As erreish daue v'er n'yannoo (nyn saie) craid er, ghow ad yn coamrey reeoil  jeh as hug ad e gharmad hene er, as leeid ad eh ersooyl dy chrossey eh. 
40N||27||32||As myr haink ad magh, hooar ad dooinney jeh Cyrene, enmyssit Simon: eshyn ren  ad y eaginaghey dy ymmyrkey e chrosh. 
40N||27||33||As tra v'ad er jeet gys ynnyd ta enmyssit Golgotha, ta shen dy ghra, Ynnyd bollag.   
40N||27||34||Hug ad da vinegar dy iu, as gall ny-chione: as tra v'eh er vlashtyn eh, cha baillish  giu. 
40N||27||35||As ren ad eh y chrossey, as rheynn ad e gharmadyn, tilgey lottyn: as shoh myr  va cooilleenit shen loayr y phadeyr, Rheynn ad my gharmadyn nyn mast' oc, as er my  chooat ren ad lottyn y hilgey. 
40N||27||36||As hoie ad sheese as dreill ad arrey er ayns shen. 
40N||27||37||As hoie ad erskyn e chione oyr e vaaish scruit, SHOH YEESEY REE NY HEWNYN. 
40N||27||38||Eisht va daa vaarliagh er ny chrossey marish: yn derrey yeh er y laue-yesh, as  y jeh elley er y laue-chiare. 
40N||27||39||As doltooan y vooinjer va goll shaghey eh, craa nyn ghing. 
40N||27||40||As gra, Uss ta lhieggal y chiamble, as dy hroggal eh reesht ayns three laa, saue  oo hene: my she mac Yee oo, tar neose jeh'n chrosh. 
40N||27||41||Myr shen neesht ren ny ard saggyrtyn craidey mysh, marish ny scrudeyryn as y  chanstyr, as dooyrt ad, 
40N||27||42||Haue eh feallagh elley, eh-hene cha vod eh sauail: my she ree Israel eh, lhig  da cheet neose jeh'n chrosh, as nee mayd credjal ayn. 
40N||27||43||Hreisht eh ayns Jee; lhig da eh y livrey nish my saillish eh: son dooyrt eh,  She mac Yee mee. 
40N||27||44||Hilg ny maarlee myrgeddin v'er nyn grossey marish yn lheid cheddin er. 
40N||27||45||Nish veih yn cheyoo oor, va dorraghys harrish ooilley yn cheer, gys yn nuyoo  oor. 
40N||27||46||As mygeayrt yn nuyoo oor, deie Yeesey lesh ard-choraa, gra, ELI, ELI, LAMA SABACTHANI?  ta shen dy ghra, My Yee, My Yee, cre'n-fa t'ou er my hreigeil? 
40N||27||47||Dooyrt paart jeusyn va nyn shassoo ayns shen, tra cheayll ad shen, Ta'n dooinney  shoh geamagh er Elias. 
40N||27||48||As chelleeragh roie fer jeu, as ghow eh sponge as lhieen eh eh lesh vinegar,  as hug eh eh er cuirtlagh, as heeyn eh eh huggey dy iu. 
40N||27||49||Dooyrt y vooinjer elley, Faag-jee veue eh, hee mayd jig Elias dy hauail eh. 
40N||27||50||Tra va Yeesey er n'eamagh reesht lesh ard-choraa, phaart eh.. 
40N||27||51||As cur-my-ner, va'n coodaghey va eddyr, y chiamble as yn ynnyd casherick raipit  veih-my-cheilley, veih'n vullagh gys y laare; as ren y thalloo craa, as ny creggyn  scoltey. 
40N||27||52||As va ny oaiaghyn er nyn vosley, as ren ymmodee jeh kirp ny nooghyn va nyn gadley,  girree seose, 
40N||27||53||As cheet ass ny oaiaghyn oc lurg yn irree-seose-reesht echey, hie ad stiagh ayns  yn ard-valley casherick, as hoilshee ad ad hene da ymmodee. 
40N||27||54||Nish tra honnick yn captan, as adsyn va marish freayll arrey er Yeesey, yn craa  thallooin, as ny reddyn v'er jeet gy-kione, ghow ad aggle mooar, gra, Dy firrinagh  shoh va Mac Yee. 
40N||27||55||As va ymmodee mraane ayns shen (va jeeaghyn er tammylt voue) va er n'eiyrt er  Yeesey veih Galilee dy hirveish er. 
40N||27||56||Nyn mast' oc va Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey moir Yamys as Voses, as moir cloan  Zebedee.
40N||27||57||Tra va'n fastyr er jeet, haink dooinney berchagh ass Arimathea, va enmyssit Joseph  va myrgeddin eh-hene credjal ayns Yeesey. 
40N||27||58||Hie eh shoh gys Pilate, as ren eh aghin son corp Yeesey: eisht doardee Pilate  yn corp dy ve er ny livrey. 
40N||27||59||As tra va Joseph er n'ghoaill y corp hoill eh eh ayns aanrit glen, 
40N||27||60||As doanluck eh eh ayns yn oaie noa echey hene, v'eh er chleiy ass y chreg: as  rowl eh clagh vooar er beeal yn oaie, as jimmee eh roish. 
40N||27||61||As va Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey elley, nyn soie jeeragh er yn oaie. 
40N||27||62||Nish yn nah laa lurg laa yn aarlaghey haink ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn  cooidjagh gys Pilate, 
40N||27||63||Gra, Vainshter, ta cooinaghtyn ain dy dooyrt yn molteyr shen, choud as v'eh foast  bio, Lurg three laa neem's girree reesht. 
40N||27||64||Cur sarey er-y-fa shen yn oaie dy ve jeant shickyr, derrey yn trass laa, er-aggle  dy jig e ostyllyn ayns yn oie, as dy geid ad eh ersooyl, as dy jir ad rish yn pobble,  T'eh er n'irree veih ny merriu: myr shen bee yn molteyrys s'jerree ny smessey na'n  chied volteyrys. 
40N||27||65||Dooyrt Pilate roo, Ta watch eu immee-jee reue, jean-jee cha shickyr jeh as oddys  shiu. 
40N||27||66||Myr shen hie ad, as ren ad yn oaie shickyr, sealal y chlagh, as soiaghey watch.     
40N||28||1||Tra va'n doonaght harrish, as y vadran cheet rish er y chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin,  haink Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey elley dy voddagh ad yn oaie y akin. 
40N||28||2||As cur-my-ner va craa thallooin mooar ayn; son va ainle y Chiarn er jeet neose  veih niau, as er jeet as er rowlal back yn chlagh jeh beeal yn oaie, as er hoie urree.   
40N||28||3||Va'n eddin echey goll-rish y tendreil, as e choamrey gial myr y sniaghtey. 
40N||28||4||As ayns aggle roish va ny arreyderyn er creau, as haink ad dy ve myr deiney marroo.   
40N||28||5||As dreggyr yn ainle, as dooyrt eh rish ny mraane, Ny gow-jee aggle: son ta fys  aym's dy vel shiu shirrey Yeesey, v'er ny chrossey. 
40N||28||6||Cha vel eh ayns shoh, son t'eh er n'irree myr dooyrt eh-hene: tar-jee, jeeagh-jee  er yn ynnyd raad va'n Chiarn oanluckit. 
40N||28||7||As immee-jee dy tappee, as insh-jee da e ostyllyn, dy vel eh er n'irree veih ny  merriu; as cur-my-ner, t'eh goll reue gys Galilee, ayns shen hee shiu eh, cur-my-ner,  ta mish er n'insh diu. 
40N||28||8||As jimmee ad dy tappee veih'n oaie lesh aggle as boggey mooar, as roie ad dy chur  lhieu yn naight gys e ostyllyn. 
40N||28||9||As myr v'ad goll dy insh eh da e ostyllyn, cur-my-ner haink Yeesey nyn guail,  gra, Dy vannee diu. As haink ad, as huitt ad sheese ec e chassyn, lesh nyn laueyn  orroo, cur ooashley da. 
40N||28||10||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Ny gow-jee aggle: immee-jee, as abbyr-jee rish my vraaraghyn  ad dy gholl gys Galilee, as ayns shen hee ad mee. 
40N||28||11||Nish myr v'ad goll, cur-my-ner, haink shiartanse jeh'n arrey gys yn ard-valley,  as dinsh ad da ny ard-saggyrtyn ooilley ny va er daghyrt. 
40N||28||12||As tra v'adsyn as y chanstyr er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, as er chur nyn goyrle dy  cheilley hug ad sym mooar dy argid da ny sidooryn, 
40N||28||13||Gra, Abbyr-jee shiuish, Haink e ostyllyn ayns yn oie, as gheid ad eh ersooyl  choud as va shin nyn gadley. 
40N||28||14||As my chlinnys y kiannoort jeh, nee mayd eshyn y vreagey as shiuish y heyrey.   
40N||28||15||Myr shen ghow ad yn argid, as ren ad myr va currit roue: as ta'n raa shoh dy  cadjin er ny insh magh mastey ny Hewnyn gys y laa t'ayn jiu. 
40N||28||16||Eisht hie yn un ostyl yeig roue gys Galilee, gys slieau raad va Yeesey er n'oardaghey  daue. 
40N||28||17||As tra honnick ad eh, hug ad ooashley da: agh va paart jeu fo mee-ourys. 
40N||28||18||As haink Yeesey, as loayr eh roo, gra, Ta dy chooilley phooar er ny chur dou  ayns niau as er y thalloo. 
40N||28||19||Immee-jee er-y-fa shen, as ynsee-jee dy chooilley ashoon, as bashtee-jee ad  ayns ennym yn Ayr, as y Vac, as y spyrryd Noo: 
40N||28||20||Gynsaghey daue dy reayll dy chooilley nhee cre-erbee ta mish er chur ayns sarey  diu: as cur-my-ner, ta mish meriu kinjagh, eer gys jerrey yn theihll. 
41N||1||1||Toshiaght sushtal Yeesey Creest, Mac Yee; 
41N||1||2||Myr te  scruit ayns ny phadeyryn; Cur-my-ner, ta mee cur my haghter roish dty eddin, dy  chiartaghey dty raad kiongoyrt rhyt. 
41N||1||3||Coraa fer geamagh ayns yn aasagh,  Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, jean-jee ny cassanyn echey jeeragh. 
41N||1||4||Ren Ean  bashtey ayns yn aassagh, as preacheil bashtey arrys, son leih peccaghyn. 
41N||1||5||As hie magh huggey ooilley cheer Yudea as cummaltee Yerusalem, as v'ad ooilley  er nyn mashtey liorish ayns awin Yordan, goaill rish nyn beccaghyn. 
41N||1||6||As  va Ean coamrit lesh garmad jeh fynney chamel, as lesh cryss liare mysh e  veeghyn: as v'eh beaghey er locustyn as mill feie: 
41N||1||7||As ren eh preacheil,  gra, Ta fer s'pooaral na mish cheet my-yei, kiangley ny braagyn echey cha vel  mee feeu dy chroymmey sheese as dy eaysley. 
41N||1||8||Ta mish dy jarroo er vashtey  shiu lesh ushtey: agh bashtee eshyn shiu lesh y Spyrryd Noo. 
41N||1||9||As haink eh  gy-kione ayns ny laghyn shen, dy daink Yeesey veih Nazareth dy Ghalilee, as v'eh  er ny vashtey liorish Ean ayns Jordan. 
41N||1||10||As jeeragh myr haink eh seose  ass yn ushtey, honnick eh ny niaughyn foshlit, as y spyrryd myr calmane cheet  neose er. 
41N||1||11||As haink coraa veih niau, gra, Oo my vac ennoil, jeed ta mee  dy mooar soiaghey. 
41N||1||12||As chelleeragh hug yn spyrryd lesh eh gys yn aasagh.  
41N||1||13||As v'eh ayns shen 'syn aasagh da-eed laa er ny violaghey liorish y  drogh-spyrryd, as v'eh marish ny beiyn feie, as ren ny ainleyn shirveish er.  
41N||1||14||Nish erreish da Ean ve currit ayns pryssoon, haink Yeesey gys Galilee,  preacheil sushtal reeriaght Yee, 
41N||1||15||As gra, Ta'n traa cooilleenit, as ta  reeriaght Yee er-gerrey: gow-jee arrys, as credjee yn sushtal. 
41N||1||16||Nish myr  v'eh shooyl liorish faarkey ghalilee, honnick eh Simon as Andreays e vraar cuirr  magh lieen ayns y cheayn: (son v'ad nyn eeasteyryn) 
41N||1||17||As dooyrt Yeesey  roo, Tar-jee as eiyr-jee orrym's, as neem's shiu nyn eeasteyryn dy gheiney.  
41N||1||18||As chelleeragh hreig ad nyn lieenteenyn, as deiyr ad er. 
41N||1||19||As  tra v'eh er n'gholl red beg sodjey veih shen, honnick eh Jamys mac Zebedee, as  Ean e vraar, va myrgeddin ayns y lhong kerraghey nyn lieen. 
41N||1||20||As  chelleeragh deie eh orroo as daag ad nyn ayr Zebedee ayns y lhong marish ny  sharvaantyn failt, as hie ad geiyrt er. 
41N||1||21||As hie ad stiagh ayns  Capernaum, as chelleeragh er laa yn doonaght, hie eh stiagh ayns y synagogue, as  dynsee eh. 
41N||1||22||As ghow ad yindys mooar jeh'n ynsaghey echey: son dynsee eh  ad myr fer ayns pooar, as cha nee myr ny scrudeyryn. 
41N||1||23||As va ayns y  synagogue oc dooinney Iesh spyrryd neu-ghlen, as dyllee eh, 
41N||1||24||Gra, Faag  void shin, cre'n eie t'ayd orrin, Yeesey dy Nazareth? vel oo er jeet dy nyn  stroie? ta fys aym quoi oo hene, eer fer casherick Yee. 
41N||1||25||As hug Yeesey  oghsan da, gra, Bee dty host, as tar magh ass. 
41N||1||26||As tra va'n spyrryd  neu-ghlen er n'eiyrt eh noon as noal, as er n'eamagh lesh ard choraa, haink eh  magh ass. 
41N||1||27||As v'ad ooilley fo atchim, ayns wheesh as dy row ad resooney  nyn mast' oc hene, gra, Cre'n red shoh? cre'n ynsagh noa shoh? son ta ny eer  spyrrydyn neu-ghlen dy pooaral echey fo smaght, as t'ad beasagh da. 
41N||1||28||As  chelleeragh hie goo jeh magh trooid ooilley yn cheer mygeayrt Galilee. 
41N||1||29||As cha leah as v'ad er jeet magh ass y synagogue, hie ad stiagh ayns thie Simon  as Andreays, marish Jamys as Ean. 
41N||1||30||Agh va moir ben Simon ny lhie ching  'sy chiassaghey, as chelleeragh dinsh ad da mychione eck. 
41N||1||31||As haink eh  as ghow eh ee er y laue, as hrog eh seose ee; as chelleeragh daag y chiassaghey  ee, as ren ee shirveish orroo. 
41N||1||32||As ayns yn astyr mysh lhie ny greiney  hug ad lhieu huggey dy chooilley unnane va doghanit, as adsyn va drogh-spyrrydyn  ayndoo. 
41N||1||33||As va ooilley yn ard-valley er nyn jaglym cooidjagh ec y  dorrys. 
41N||1||34||As ren eh ymmodee y lheihys va seaghnit lesh mooarane doghanyn,  as ymmodee drogh-spyrrydyn y chastey, as cha lhig eh da ny drogh-spyrrydyn dy  loayrt, ny dy ghra dy row enney oc er. 
41N||1||35||As moghrey laa-ny-vairagh dirree  eh foddey roish y laa, as hie eh magh, as jimmee eh gys boayl faasagh, as ayns  shen ghow eh padjer. 
41N||1||36||As deiyr Simon er, as adsyn va marish. 
41N||1||37||As  tra v'ad er gheddyn eh, dooyrt ad rish, Ta dy chooilley ghooinney briaght dty  yei. 
41N||1||38||As dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dooin goll gys baljyn sniessey dooin, dy  voddym preacheil ayndoo shen myrgeddin: son er-yn-oyr shen haink mee gys y  theihll. 
41N||1||39||As ren eh preacheil ayns ny synagogueyn oc trooid ooilley  Galilee, as chast eh drogh spyrrydyn. 
41N||1||40||As haink lourane huggey, guee er,  as gliooney sheese huggey, as gra rish, My she dty aigney eh, foddee oo mish y  yannoo glen. 
41N||1||41||As va Yeesey er ny veiyghey lesh chymmey, as heeyn eh magh  e laue, as venn eh rish, as dooyrt eh, M'aigney's eh, bee er dty ghlenney.  
41N||1||42||As cha row eh ny s'leah er loayrt, agh chelleeragh daag y louraanys eh,  as v'eh er ny ghlenney. 
41N||1||43||As hug eh currym geyre er, as chelleeragh hug  eh ersooyl eh. 
41N||1||44||As dooyrt eh rish, Jeeagh nagh loayr oo veg rish  dooinney erbee: agh immee royd, jeeagh oo hene da'n taggyrt, as cheb son dty  ghlenney shen doardee Moses son cowrey daue. 
41N||1||45||Agh hie eh roish, as ren  eh toshiaght dy hoilshaghey magh as dy skeayley mygeayrt yn chooish, ayns wheesh  as nagh dod Yeesey goll ny smoo dy foshlit gys yn ard-valley, agh v'eh mooie  ayns ynnydyn faasagh: as haink ad huggey veih dy chooilley ard.   
41N||2||1||As laghyn ny lurg shen, hie eh reesht gys Capernaum, as ve er ny  insh magh dy row eh ayns y thie. 
41N||2||2||As chelleeragh va ymmodee er nyn jaglym  cooidjagh, ayns wheesh as nagh row room dy ghoaill ad, wheesh as mygeayrt y  dorrys: as ren eh yn goo y phreacheil daue. 
41N||2||3||As haink ad huggey, cur  lhieu fer va seaghnit lesh y chingys-craaee, v'er ny hroggal stiagh liorish  kiare dy leih. 
41N||2||4||As tra nagh dod ad cheet er-gerrey da kyndagh rish y  chennid, rooisht ad kione y thie raad v'eh: as erreish daue v'er vosley stiagh  ny hrooid, lhig ad sheese y lhiabbee ayn va'n palsee-doghanit ny lhie. 
41N||2||5||Tra hug Yeesey tastey da'n chredjue oc, dooyrt eh rish y dooinney ching, Vac, ta  dty pheccaghyn er nyn leih dhyt. 
41N||2||6||Agh va shiartanse jeh ny scrudeyryn nyn  soie ayns shen, as v'ad resooney ayns nyn greeaghyn, 
41N||2||7||Cre'n-fa ta'n  dooinney shoh loayrt goan mollaghtagh? quoi oddys peccaghyn y leih, agh Jee  ny-lomarcan? 
41N||2||8||As chelleeragh tra dennee Yeesey ayns e spyrryd dy row ad  myr shoh resooney cheu-sthie jeu hene, dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu  smooinaghtyn lheid ny reddyn shoh ayns nyn greeaghyn? 
41N||2||9||Cre sassey dy  ghra, rish y palsee-doghanit, Ta dty pheccaghyn er nyn leih dhyt: ny dy ghra,  Irree, as trog seose dty lhiabbee, as jean shooyl. 
41N||2||10||Agh dy vod fys y ve  eu dy vel pooar ec Mac y dooinney er y thalloo dy leih peccaghyn (dooyrt eh rish  y palsee-doghanit) 
41N||2||11||Ta mee gra rhyt, Irree, as trog seose dty lhiabbee,  as immee royd gys dty hie. 
41N||2||12||As chelleeragh dirree eh, hrog eh e  lhiabbee, as hie eh magh kiongoyrt roo ooilley, ayns wheesh as dy row ad ooilley  lhieent lesh atchim, as dy ren ad Jee y ghloyraghey, gra, Cha vaik shin eh rieau  er yn aght shoh. 
41N||2||13||As hie eh magh reesht rish oirr ny marrey, as haink  ooilley yn pobble huggey, as dynsee eh ad. 
41N||2||14||As myr v'eh goll shaghey,  honnick eh Levi mac Alpheus ny hoie ec boayrd y cheesh, as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr  orrym's. As dirree eh seose as deiyr eh er. 
41N||2||15||As haink eh gy-kione, myr  va Yeesey ny hoie ec bee ayns y thie echey, dy ren myrgeddin ymmodee publicanee  as peccee soie sheese marish Yeesey as e heshaght: son va ymmodee er n'eiyrt er.  
41N||2||16||As tra honnick ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn eh gee marish publicanee  as peccee, dooyrt ad rish e ynseydee, Kys dy vel eh gee as giu marish publicanee  as peccee? 
41N||2||17||Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel feme ocsyn  ta slane er yn er-lhee, agh ec sleih chingey: cha daink mish dy eamagh er y  vooinjer chairagh, agh er peccee gys arrys. 
41N||2||18||As ve cliaghtey ynseydee  Ean as ny Phariseeyn dy reayll trostey; as haink ad as dooyrt ad rish, Kys te dy  vel ynseydee Ean as ny Phariseeyn trostey, agh cha vel adsyn t'ou uss er  n'ynsaghey trostey? 
41N||2||19||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Vod cloan y chamyr-phoosee  trostey, choud as ta'n dooinney-poosee maroo? choud as ta'n dooinney-poosee  maroo, cha vod ad trostey. 
41N||2||20||Agh hig ny laghyn, tra vees y  dooinney-poosee er ny ghoaill ersooyl voue, as eisht nee ad trostey ayns ny  laghyn shen. 
41N||2||21||As cha vel dooinney erbee whaaley peesh dy eaddagh noa er  shenn gharmad: er-nonney ta'n pheesh goaill y laane ass y chenn gharmad, as bee  yn raipey ny smessey na ve. 
41N||2||22||Chamoo ta dooinney erbee cur feeyn noa ayns  shenn voteilyn, er-nonney ta'n feeyn noa scoltey ny boteilyn, as ta'n feeyn  deayrtit, as bee ny boteilyn dy choayl orroo: agh shegin da feeyn noa v'er ny  chur ayns boteilyn noa. 
41N||2||23||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh shooyl trooid ny  magheryn arroo er laa'n doonaght, dy ren e ynseydee toshiaght, myr v'ad goll dy  phluckey jeeassyn jeh'n arroo. 
41N||2||24||As dooyrt ny Phariseeyn rish,  Cur-my-ner, cre'n-fa t'ad shoh er laa'n doonaght jannoo shen nagh vel lowit?  
41N||2||25||As dooyrt eshyn roo, Nagh lhaih shiuish rieau, cre ren David, tra v'eh  ayns feme as accryssagh, eh-hene as y vooinjer va marish? 
41N||2||26||Kys hie eh  stiagh ayns thie Yee, rish lhing Abiathar yn ard-saggyrt, as d'ee eh yn  arran-casherick, nagh row lowit dy ve eeit, agh liorish ny saggyrtyn, as hug eh  eh myrgeddin dauesyn va marish? 
41N||2||27||As dooyrt eh roo, Va'n doonaght er ny  yannoo son dooinney, as cha nee dooinney son y doonaght: 
41N||2||28||Shen-y-fa ta'n  Mac dooinney ny Hiarn myrgeddin er y doonaght.  
41N||3||1||As hie  eh reesht stiagh ayns y synagogue, as va dooinney ayns shen lesh laue shyrgit.  
41N||3||2||As va sooill oc er, dy yeeaghyn jinnagh eh eh y lheihys er laa yn  doonaght, dy voddagh oyr y ve oc dy phlaiynt noi. 
41N||3||3||As dooyrt eh rish y  dooinney lesh y laue shyrgit, Shass magh. 
41N||3||4||As dooyrt eh roo, Vel eh lowal  dy yannoo mie er laghyn y doonaght, ny dy yannoo olk? dy hauail bioys, ny dy  stroie eh? Agh v'adsyn nyn-dhost. 
41N||3||5||As tra v'eh er yeeaghyn mygeayrt orroo  lesh corree, v'eh seaghnit son creoghys nyn greeaghyn, as dooyrt eh rish y  dooinney, Sheeyn magh dty laue: as heeyn eh magh ee; as va e laue er ny  laanaghey myr y laue elley. 
41N||3||6||As hie ny Phariseeyn magh, as chelleeragh  ghow ad-hene, as ny Herodianee coyrle n'oi, kys oddagh ad eh y stroie. 
41N||3||7||Agh hie Yeesey dy lhiattee marish e ynseydee gys oirr ny marrey: as deiyr  earrooyn mooarey dy leih er veih Galilee, as veih Judea, 
41N||3||8||As veih  Jerusalem, as veih Idumea, as veih'n cheu elley dy Yordan, as adsyn mygeayrt  Tyre as Sidon, earroo mooar, tra cheayll ad cre ny reddyn yindyssagh v'eh er  n'yannoo, haink ad huggey. 
41N||3||9||As loayr eh rish e ynseydee, lhong veg dy ve  aarloo er e hon, kyndagh rish y pobble, son nagh jinnagh ad chionney stiagh er.  
41N||3||10||Son v'eh er laanaghey ymmodee, ayns wheesh as dy row ad chionney stiagh  huggey, dy ventyn rish, whilleen as va dourinagh. 
41N||3||11||As ny spyrrydyn  neughlen tra honnick ad eh, huitt ad sheese kiongoyrt rish, as dyllee ad, gra,  She Mac Yee oo. 
41N||3||12||As hug eh currym gyere orroo, gyn ad dy insh magh quoi  v'eh. 
41N||3||13||As hie eh seose er slieau, as deie eh er y vooinjer baillish: as  haink ad huggey. 
41N||3||14||As doardee eh ghaa-yeig dy ve marish, dy voddagh eh  coyrt ad magh dy phreacheil: 
41N||3||15||As dy voddagh pooar y ve oc dy lheihys  aslayntyn, as dy hilgey magh drogh-spyrrydyn. 
41N||3||16||As Simon lhiennoo eh  Peddyr. 
41N||3||17||As Jamys mac Zebedee, as Ean braar Yamys (as lhiennoo eh adsyn  Boanerges, ta shen dy ghra, Cloan ny taarnee) 
41N||3||18||As Andreays, as Philip,  as Bartholomew, as Mian, as Thomase, as Jamys mac Alpheus, as Thaddeus, as Simon  yn Canaanite. 
41N||3||19||As Yuaase Iscariot, ren myrgeddin eh y vrah: as hie ad  stiagh ayns thie. 
41N||3||20||As va'n pobble er nyn jaglym cooidjagh reesht, myr  shen nagh row wheesh caa oc dy ghoaill beaghey. 
41N||3||21||As tra cheayll e  gheiney-mooinjerey jeh, hie ad magh dy ghoaill eh: son dooyrt ad, T'eh ass e  cheeayl. 
41N||3||22||As dooyrt ny scrudeyryn haink neose veih Jerusalem, Ta  Beelzebub echey, as liorish prince ny drogh-spyrrydyn t'eh tilgey magh  drogh-spyrrydyn. 
41N||3||23||As deie eh orroo huggey, as dooyrt eh roo ayns  coraaghyn-dorraghey, kys oddys Satan Satan y chastey? 
41N||3||24||As my ta  reeriaght girree-magh n'oi hene, cha vod y reeriaght shen shassoo. 
41N||3||25||As  my ta thie girree-magh n'oi hene, cha vod y thie shen shassoo. 
41N||3||26||As my ta  Satan girree-magh, as my t'eh n'oi hene, cha vod eh shassoo, agh ta e phooar ec  kione. 
41N||3||27||Cha vod dooinney erbee goll stiagh ayns thie yn treanagh, as  cragh y yannoo jeh e chooid, mannagh giangle eh hoshiaght yn treanagh, as eisht  nee eh cragh y yannoo er e hie. 
41N||3||28||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Bee dy  chooilley pheccah er ny leih da mec gheiney, as ny goan mollaghtagh lioroo nee  ad loayrt dy mollaghtagh: 
41N||3||29||Agh eshyn loayrys dy mollaghtagh noi yn  Spyrryd Noo, cha bee dy bragh leih ny chour, agh t'eh ayns dangeyr coayl-anmey  dy baagh farraghtyn. 
41N||3||30||Er-yn-oyr dy dooyrt ad, Ta spyrryd neu-ghlen  echey. 
41N||3||31||Eisht haink e vraaraghyn as e voir as shassoo cheu-mooie (jeh'n  dorrys) hug ad fys huggey dy heet dy loayrt roo. 
41N||3||32||As va'n pobble nyn  soie mygeayrt-y-mysh, as dooyrt ad rish, Cur-my-ner, ta dty voir as dty  vraaraghyn mooie fenaght er dty hon. 
41N||3||33||As dreggyr eh ad, gra, Quoi my  voir, ny my vraaraghyn? 
41N||3||34||As yeeagh eh mygeayrt orroosyn va nyn soie  mygeayrt-y-mysh, as dooyrt eh, Cur-jee my-ner my voir as my vraaraghyn. 
41N||3||35||Son quoi-erbee nee aigney Yee, she eshyn my vraar, as my huyr, as my voir.   
41N||4||1||As ren eh toshiaght reesht dy ynsaghey rish oirr ny  marrey: as va earroo mooar dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh huggey, myr shen dy  jagh eh er-board lhong, as hoie eh er y cheayn, as va ooilley yn pobble liorish  y cheayn, er y thalloo. 
41N||4||2||As dynsee eh daue ymmodee nheeghyn ayns  coraaghyn-dorraghey, as dooyrt eh roo ayns e ynsagh, 
41N||4||3||Clasht-jee,  cur-my-ner hie correyder agh dy chuirr: 
41N||4||4||As haink eh gy-kione myr v'eh  cuirr, dy huitt paart jeh'n rass rish oirr y raad, as haink eeanlee yn aer, as  d'ee ad seose eh. 
41N||4||5||As huitt paart er thalloo claghagh, raad nagh row  mooarane ooir echey, as chelleeragh daase eh, er-yn-oyr nagh row diunid  thallooin echey. 
41N||4||6||As tra ghow yn ghrian niart ve fiojit, as er-yn-oyr  nagh row eh er n'ghoaill fraue, ren eh shyrgaghey ersooyl. 
41N||4||7||As huitt  paart mastey drineyn, as daase ny drineyn seose marish, as phloogh ad eh, as cha  dymmyrk eh mess. 
41N||4||8||Agh huitt cooid elley jeh ayns thalloo mie, as hug eh  magh mess ren gaase seose as bishaghey, as dymmyrk eh, paart jeih fillaghyn as  feed, as paart three-feed, as paart keead filley. 
41N||4||9||As dooyrt eh roo,  Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn. 
41N||4||10||As tra v'eh  ny-lomarcan, denee yn vooinjer va mygeayrt-y-mysh marish y daa ostyl yeig jeh  mychione y coraa-dorraghey. 
41N||4||11||As dooyrt eh roo, Diuish te er ny choyrt dy  hoiggal folliaght reeriaght Yee: agh dauesyn ta mooie, ta dy chooilley nhee  jeant ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: 
41N||4||12||Son fakin hee ad, agh cha der ad tastey  as clashtyn cluinnee ad, agh cha gow ad tushtey; er-aggle ec traa erbee dy beagh  ad er nyn jyndaa, as dy beagh nyn beccaghyn er nyn leih daue. 
41N||4||13||As dooyrt  eh roo, Nagh vel toiggal eu jeh'n choraa-dorraghey shoh? as kys eisht nee shiu  dy chooilley choraa-dorraghey y hoiggal? 
41N||4||14||Ta'n correyder cuirr yn goo.  
41N||4||15||As ad shoh adsyn ta rish oirr y raad, ayn ta'n goo er ny chuirr, agh  tra t'ad er chlashtyn, ta'n drogh-spyrryd cheet jeeragh, as goaill ersooyl yn  goo va cuirt ayns nyn greeaghyn. 
41N||4||16||As ad shoh neesht yn vooinjer ta cuirt  ayns thalloo claghagh, ta, erreish daue v'er chlashtyn y goo, chelleeragh dy  ghoaill eh dy aggindagh: 
41N||4||17||Agh cha vel fraue oc ayndoo hene, as myr shen  cha vel ad cummal rish agh son earish: ny lurg shen tra ta seaghyn ny tranlaase  cheet orroo er coontey yn ghoo, chelleeragh ta nyn gredjue failleil. 
41N||4||18||As  ad shoh yn vooinjer ta cuirt mastey drineyn: lheid as ta clashtyn y goo 
41N||4||19||As ta kiarail y theihll shoh, as molteyraght berchys, as saynt reddyn elley goll  stiagh, as plooghey yn goo, as te cheet dy ve neu-vessoil. 
41N||4||20||As ad shoh  yn vooinjer ta cuirt ayns thalloo mie, lheid as ta clashtyn y goo, as ta dy  ghoaill eh, as gymmyrkey magh mess, paart jeih fillaghyn as feed, paart  three-feed, as paart keead-filley. 
41N||4||21||As dooyrt eh roo, Vel cainle dy ve  er ny choyrt fo saagh, ny fo lhiabbee? as nagh vel ee dy v'er ny choyrt ayns  cainleyr? 
41N||4||22||Son cha vel nhee erbee keillit, nagh bee er ny hoilshaghey:  ny nhee erbee freilt follit, nagh jig er-ash? 
41N||4||23||My ta cleayshyn ec  dooinney erbee dy chlashtyn lhig da clashtyn. 
41N||4||24||As dooyrt eh roo, Cur-jee  tastey da ny ta shiu dy chlashtyn: lesh y towse ta shiu towse, bee eh er ny  howse diu: as diuish ta clashtyn, bee ny smoo er ny choyrt. 
41N||4||25||Son eshyn  ta echey, dasyn vees er ny choyrt: as eshyn nagh vel echey, veihsyn vees er ny  ghoaill eer shen hene ny ta echey. 
41N||4||26||As dooyrt eh, Shoh myr ta reeriaght  Yee, myr dy dilgagh dooinney rass ayns y thalloo 
41N||4||27||As eh dy chadley, as  dy irree oie as laa; as y rass dy heet er y hoshiaght, as dy aase seose, gyn-yss  da. 
41N||4||28||Son ta'n thalloo cur magh mess j'ee hene, hoshiaght yn chass, eisht  yn jeeas, ny lurg shen, yn arroo creen ayns y jeeas. 
41N||4||29||Agh tra ta'n mess  er greenaghey, chelleeragh t'eh cur yn corran fo, er-yn-oyr dy vel y fouyr er  jeet. 
41N||4||30||As dooyrt eh, Cre gys nee mayd reeriaght Yee y hoyllaghey? ny  lesh cre'n co-chaslys nee mayd y hoiaghey magh eh? 
41N||4||31||Te goll-rish grine  dy rass mustard, ta ny sloo, tra te cuirt ayns y thalloo, na dy chooilley rass  ta ayns y thalloo. 
41N||4||32||Agh tra te cuirt, te gaase seose, as cheet dy ve ny  smoo na ooilley ny lossreeyn, as cur magh banglaneyn mooarey, myr shen dy vod  eeanlee yn aer fastee y ghoaill fo'n scadoo echey. 
41N||4||33||As lesh ymmodee dy  lheid ny coraaghyn dorraghey loayr eh yn goo roo, myr v'adsyn son goaill rish.  
41N||4||34||Agh fegooish coraa-dorraghey cha loayr eh roo: as tra v'ad nyn-lomarcan  hoilshee eh dy chooilley nhee da e ostyllyn.
41N||4||35||As yn laa cheddin tra va'n  fastyr er, dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dooin goll harrish gys y cheu elley. 
41N||4||36||As  tra v'ad er chur ersooyl yn pobble, hug ad lhieu eh myr v'eh ayns y lhong, as va  myrgeddin lhongyn beggey elley marish. 
41N||4||37||As dirree sterrym mooar dy  gheay, as va ny tonnyn brishey stiagh ayns y lhong, myr shen dy row ee nish er  lhieeney. 
41N||4||38||As v'eshyn ayns jerrey ny lhuingey ny chadley er clooisag: as  ghooisht ad eh, as dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter, nagh vel geill ayd dy bee mayd  caillit? 
41N||4||39||As dirree eh, as smaghtee eh yn gheay, as dooyrt eh rish y  faarkey, Gow fea, bee kiune: as ghow yn gheay fea, as va kiuney vooar ayn.  
41N||4||40||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu cha agglagh? kys te nagh vel credjue  eu? 
41N||4||41||As v'ad feer agglagh, as dooyrt ad yn derrey yeh rish y jeh elley,  cre'n monney dy ghooinney eh shoh, dy vel y gheay hene as faarkey cur biallys  da? 
41N||5||1||. As haink ad harrish gys y cheu elley jeh'n  cheayn, gys cheer ny Gadarenee.
41N||5||2||As tra v'eh er jeet ass y lhong,  chelleeragh haink ny whail veih mastey ny oaiaghyn, dooinney lesh spyrryd  neu-ghlen.
41N||5||3||Va cummal mastey ny oaiaghyn, as cha voddagh dooinney erbee y  chiangley eh, eer lesh geulaghyn:
41N||5||4||Er-y-fa dy row eh dy mennick er ny ve  kianlt lesh yiarnyn as geulaghyn, as va ny geulaghyn er ny ve tayrnit  veih-my-cheilley liorish, as ny yiarnyn brisht ayns peeshyn: as cha dod dooinney  erbee eh y veeinaghey.
41N||5||5||As kinjagh oie as laa v'eh ayns ny sleityn, as  mastey ny oaiaghyn, gyllagh, as dy ghiarey eh-hene lesh claghyn.
41N||5||6||Agh tra  honnick eh Yeesey foddey jeh, roie eh, as hug eh ooashley da,
41N||5||7||As deie eh  lesh ard-choraa, as dooyrt eh, Cre'n eie t'ayd orrym, Yeesey, Vac yn Jee smoo  ard? ta mee guee ort, ayns ennym Yee, gyn oo dy my horchaghey.
41N||5||8||(Son v'eh  er ghra rish, Tar magh ass y dooinney, uss spyrryd neu-ghlen) 
41N||5||9||As denee  eh jeh, Cre'n ennym t'ort? As dreggyr eh, gra, Ta m'ennym Legion Son ta shin  ymmodee.
41N||5||10||As ren eh aghin jeean huggey, gyn eh dy chur ad ersooyl ass y  cheer.
41N||5||11||Nish va ayns shen, er-gerrey da ny sleityn, griagh mooar dy vucyn  fo bochillyn.
41N||5||12||As ghuee ooilley ny drogh-spyrrydyn er, gra, Eiyr shin gys  ny mucyn, dy vod mayd goll stiagh ayndoo.
41N||5||13||As chelleeragh hug Yeesey kied  daue. As hie ny spyrrydyn neu-ghlen roue, as hie ad stiagh ayns ny mucyn, as  roie yn ghriagh gour nyn mullee lesh yn eaynee gys y cheayn (v'ad mysh daa  housane) as v'ad plooghit ayns y cheayn.
41N||5||14||As roie bochillyn ny mucyn  roue, as dinsh ad eh ayns yn ard-valley, as er y cheer. As hie ad magh dy akin  cre va jeant.
41N||5||15||As haink ad gys Yeesey, as honnick ad eshyn va'n  drogh-spyrryd as y legion er ny ve ayn, ny hoie, as e eaddagh er, as dy mie ayns  e cheeayl, as ghow ad aggle.
41N||5||16||As diush y vooinjer honnick eh daue, kys ve  er daghyrt dasyn va'n drogh-spyrryd er ve ayn, as myrgeddin mychione ny  mucyn.
41N||5||17||As ren ad toshiaght dy ghuee er, eh dy gholl roish ass ny ardjyn  oc.
41N||5||18||As tra v'eh er jeet gys y lhong, ren eshyn va'n drogh spyrryd er ve  ayn guee er kied y chur da goll marish.
41N||5||19||Agh cha lhiggagh Yeesey da, agh  dooyrt e rish, Immee thie gys dty vooinjer hene, as insh daue cre ny reddyn  mooarey ta'n Chiarn er n'yannoo er dty hon, as dy vel chymmey er ve echey  ort.
41N||5||20||As jimmee eh roish, as ren eh toshiaght dy hoilshaghey magh ayns  Decapolis, cre dy reddyn mooarey va Yeesey er n'yannoo er e hon: as ghow dy  chooilley ghooinney yindys.
41N||5||21||As tra va Yeesey er n'gholl harrish reesht  ayns y lhong gys y cheu elley, va earroo mooar dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh  huggey, as v'eh er-gerrey da'n cheayn. 
41N||5||22||As cur-my-ner, haink fer jeh  reiltee yn synagogue va enmyssit Jairus, as tra honnick eh eh, huitt eh sheese  ec e chassyn, 
41N||5||23||As ghuee eh er dy jeean, gra, Ta my inneen veg ny lhie  raad y vaaish, tar as cur dty laueyn urree, dy vod ee v'er ny lheihys, as bee ee  bio. 
41N||5||24||As hie Yeesey marish, as deiyr ymmodee dy leih, as ren ad chionney  stiagh er. 
41N||5||25||(As va ben dy row va seaghnit lesh roie-foalley rish daa  vlein jeig. 
41N||5||26||As v'ee er hurranse mooarane liorish ymmodee fir-lhee, as  er vaarail ooilley ny v'eck, as cha row ee veg share, agh goll ny smessey,  
41N||5||27||Tra cheayll ee jeh Yeesey, haink ee ayns y chennid cheu e chooylloo, as  venn ee rish e gharmad. 
41N||5||28||Son dooyrt ee, My oddym agh bentyn rish e  eaddagh, bee'm er my laanaghey. 
41N||5||29||As chelleeragh va'n roie-foalley eck er  ny hyrmaghey: as dennee ee ayns e corp dy row ee er ny lheihys jeh'n doghan  shen. 
41N||5||30||As chelleeragh va fys ec Yeesey cheu sthie jeh hene, dy row bree  er n'gholl ass, as hyndaa eh mygeayrt ayns y chennid, as dooyrt eh, Quoi venn  rish my eaddagh?
41N||5||31||As dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, T'ou fakin y pobble chionney  stiagh ort, as vel oo gra, Quoi venn rhym? 
41N||5||32||As yeeagh eh mygeayrt dy  akin ish v'er n'yannoo shoh. 
41N||5||33||Agh va'n ven agglagh as er-creau,  gennaghtyn ny va jeant aynjee, as haink ee as huitt ee sheese kiongoyrt rish, as  dinsh ee da ooilley yn irriney. 
41N||5||34||As dooyrt eh r'ee, Inneen, ta dty  chredjue, er dty laanaghey; immee ayns shee, as bee slane jeh dty ghoghan).  
41N||5||35||Choud as v'eh foast loayrt, haink feallagh veih thie fer-reill y  synagogue dooyrt rish, ta dty inneen marroo, cre s'lhiass dhyt trubbyl sodjey y  chur er y vainshter?
41N||5||36||Tra va Yeesey er chlashtyn yn fockle va loayrit,  dooyrt eh rish fer-reill yn synagogue, Ny gow aggle ynrycan jean credjal.  
41N||5||37||As cha lhig eh da dooinney erbee cheet geiyrt er, cheu-mooie jeh  Peddyr, as Jamys, as Ean braar Yamys 
41N||5||38||As haink eh gys thie fer-reill yn  synagogue, as hug eh my-ner yn boirey, as adsyn va keayney as dobberan dy  trimshagh. 
41N||5||39||As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh, dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta  ooilley yn anvea as y cheayney shoh? cha vel y ven-aeg marroo agh ny cadley.  
41N||5||40||As hie ad son craidey mysh, agh tra v'eh er chur ad ooilley magh, ghow  eh ayr as moir y ven-aeg, as adsyn va marish, as hie eh stiagh raad va'n ven-aeg  ny lhie. 
41N||5||41||As ghow eh yn ven-aeg er laue, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Talitha  cumi, ta shen dy ghra, Ven-aeg (ta mee gra rhyt) irree. 
41N||5||42||As chelleeragh  dirree yn ven-aeg, as huill ee; son v'ee daa vlein jeig dy eash: as v'ad  erskyn-towse atchimagh. 
41N||5||43||As hug eh currym gyere orroo, nagh voghe  dooinney erbee fys er shoh: as doardee eh red ennagh dy ve er ny choyrt j'ee dy  ee.  
41N||6||1||.As hie eh magh veih shen, as haink eh gys e heer  hene, as deir e ostyllyn er. 
41N||6||2||As tra va'n doonaght er jeet ren eh  toshiaght dy ynsaghey ayns y synagogue: as ghow ymmodee jeusyn va dy chlashtyn  eh yindys mooar, gra, Cre voish ta ny reddyn shoh ec y dooinney shoh? as cre'n  chreenaght shoh t'er ny choyrt da, dy vel lheid ny obbraghyn niartal er nyn  obbraghey liorish ny laueyn echey? 
41N||6||3||Nagh nee shoh yn seyir mac Voirrey  braar Yamys as Yoses as Juda as Simon, as nagh vel ny shayraghyn echey ayns shoh  marin? as ghow ad comys rish. 
41N||6||4||Agh dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cha vel phadeyr  fegooish ooashley, agh ayns e heer hene, as mastey e chynney hene, as ayns e hie  hene. 
41N||6||5||As cha dod eh mirril erbee y obbraghey ayns shen, cheu-mooie jeh  dy dug eh e laueyn er reggryn dy leih chingey, as dy ren eh ad y lheihys.  
41N||6||6||As ghow eh yindys jeh'n vee-chredjue oc. As hie eh mygeayrt ny  baljyn-cheerey oc gynsaghey. 
41N||6||7||As deie eh er y daa ostyl yeig huggey, as  ren eh toshiaght dy chur ad magh jees as jees, as hug eh daue pooar harrish  spyrrydyn neu-ghlen,
41N||6||8||As sarey gyn ad dy ghoaill red erbee cour nyn  yurnah, agh ynrycan lorg: gyn ad dy ghoaill spaagey, ny arran, ny argid ayns nyn  sporran: 
41N||6||9||Agh dy gholl ayns nyn mraagyn, as gyn ad dy chur orroo daa  chooat. 
41N||6||10||As dooyrt eh roo, Raad erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayns thie,  fuirree jee ayn derrey aagys shiu yn ynnyd shen. 
41N||6||11||As quoi-erbee nagh  jean goaill riu, ny geill y choyrt da ny goan eu, tra vees shiu goll reue,  crie-jee yn Joan ta fo ny cassyn eu, son feanish nyn 'oi. Dy firrinagh ta mee  gra riu, Dy bee eh ny sassey son Sodom as Gomorrah ec laa ny briwnys, na son yn  ard valley shen. 
41N||6||12||As hie ad magh, as ren ad preacheil, sleih dy ghoaill  arrys. 
41N||6||13||As deiyr ad magh ymmodee drogh-spyrrydyn, as d'ooilee ad lesh  ooil ymmodee sleih chingey, as ren ad ad y laanaghey. 
41N||6||14||As cheayll ree  Herod jeh (son va'n goo echey er n'gholl magh) as dooyrt eh, Dy row Ean Bashtey  er n'irree veih ny merriu, as er-yn-oyr shen dy row mirrillyn er nyn obbraghey  liorish. 
41N||6||15||Dooyrt paart dy leih, dy nee Elias v'ayn: dooyrt feallagh  elley, Dy nee phadeyr v'eh, ny myr fer jeh ny phadeyryn. 
41N||6||16||Agh tra  cheayll Herod jeh, dooyrt eh, She Ean Bashtey t'ayn, hug mish y kione jeh, t'eh  er n'irree veih ny merriu. 
41N||6||17||Son va Herod hene er chur fys magh, as er  ghoaill Ean, as er choyrt eh ayns geulaghyn 'sy phryssoon, kyndagh rish Herodias  ben e vraar Philip son v'eh er phoosey ee. 
41N||6||18||Son va Ean er ghra rish  Herod, Te noi yn leigh dhyt ben dty vraarey y ve ayd son ben. 
41N||6||19||Shen-y-fa  va Herodias ayns goanlys da, as v'ee shleeuit er cur dy baase eh, agh cha daink  eh lh'ee. 
41N||6||20||Son va Herod ayns ammys Ean, toiggal dy row eh ny ghooinney  cairagh as crauee as hug eh geill da, as er y choyrle echey v'eh er n'yannoo  ymmodee reddyn, as deaisht eh rish dy arryltagh. 
41N||6||21||Agh tra va laa jesh er  y hon er jeet, dy ren Herod corrym rish y laa ruggyr eh, shibber y yannoo, son e  hiarnyn, ard-chaptanyn, as deiney ooasle Ghalilee: 
41N||6||22||As haink inneen  Herodias cheddin stiagh, as ghaunse ee, as ghow Herod as e ghoaldee va marish  ard-voghey j'ee, as dooyrt y ree rish y ven-aeg, Shir orrym's aghin erbee dy  nailt, as giall-ym dhyt eh. 
41N||6||23||As loo eh jee, Cre-erbee hirrys oo orrym,  ver-ym dhyt eh, gys y derrey lieh jeh my reeriaght. 
41N||6||24||As hie ee magh, as  dooyrt ee rish e moir, Cre hirrym? As dooyrt ish, Kione Ean Bashtey. 
41N||6||25||As  haink ee stiagh er-y-chooyl ayns siyr gys y ree, as hir ee, gra, Saillym oo dy  chur dou nish hene er claare kione Ean Bashtey. 
41N||6||26||As va'n ree trome  trimshagh, ny yeih er coontey e loo, as y vooinjer va nyn soie marish, cha row  eh booiagh cur obbal jee. 
41N||6||27||As chelleeragh hug y ree magh marrooder, as  doardee eh cur lesh e chione: as hie eh, as hug eh yn kione jeh Ean ayns y  phryssoon, 
41N||6||28||As hug eh lesh yn kione er claare, as livrey eh eh gys y  ven-aeg as livrey ish eh gys e moir. 
41N||6||29||As tra cheayll e ynseydee jeh  shoh, haink ad as hrog ad e chorp, as doanluck ad eh ayns lhiaght 
41N||6||30||As  haink ny ostyllyn cooidjagh gys Yeesey, as dinsh ad da dy chooilley nhee,  chammah cre v'ad er n'yannoo, as cre v'ad er n'ynsaghey.
41N||6||31||As dooyrt eh  roo, Tar-jee shiuish er-lheh gys boayl faasagh, as gow-jee tammylt dy nyn aash:  son va ymmodee cheet as goll, as cha row caa oc wheesh as dy ee. 
41N||6||32||As  jimmee ad ayns lhong gys ynnyd faasagh er-lheh. 
41N||6||33||Agh honnick y pobble ad  goll roue, as hug ymmodee jeu enney er, as roie ad gys shen rish nyn gosh veih  dy chooilley ard-valley, as haink ad gys shen rhymboo, as chruinnee ad huggey.  
41N||6||34||As tra va Yeesey er jeet er thalloo honnick eh earroo mooar dy leih, as  v'eh er ny veiyghey lesh chymmey orroo, er-yn-oyr dy row ad myr kirree fegooish  bochilley: as ren eh toshiaght dy ynsaghey ad ayns ymmodee reddyn. 
41N||6||35||As  tra va'n laa nish foddey baarit, haink e ostyllyn huggey, as dooyrt ad, Shoh  boayl faasagh, as ta'n traa nish er n'gholl foddey shaghey: 
41N||6||36||Lhig y raad  daue, dy vod ad goll er y cheer mygeayrt, as gys ny baljyn cheerey, dy  chionnaghey arran daue hene: son cha vel veg y veaghey oc. 
41N||6||37||As dreggyr  eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-jee shiuish bee daue. As dooyrt ad rish, Nailt shin  goll dy chionnaghey feeagh daa cheead ping dy arran, as beaghey 'chur  daue?
41N||6||38||Dooyrt eh roo, Cre-woad bwilleen t'eu? immee-jee as jeeagh-jee. As  tra va fys oc, dooyrt ad, Queig, as daa eeast. 
41N||6||39||As doardee eh daue ad dy  chur orroo ooilley soie sheese ayns sheshaghtyn er yn aiyr ghlass. 
41N||6||40||As  hoie ad sheese ayns roaghyn, keead as lieh-cheead ayns roa. 
41N||6||41||As tra v'eh  er ghoaill ny queig bwilleenyn as y daa eeast, yeeagh eh seose gys niau, as  vannee eh, as vrish eh ny bwilleenyn, as hug eh ad da e ostyllyn dy hoiaghey  rhymboo; as y daa eeast rheynn eh ny mast' oc ooilley. 
41N||6||42||As ren ad  ooilley gee, as v'ad er nyn n'yannoo magh. 
41N||6||43||As hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh  as jeh ny eeastyn lane daa vaskad jeig. 
41N||6||44||As v'adsyn v'er n'ee jeh ny  bwilleenyn mysh queig thousane dooinney. 
41N||6||45||As chelleeragh hug eh er e  ostyllyn lhuingys y ghoaill, as ad dy gholl roish gys y cheu elley gys  Bethsaida, choud as v'eh cur y pobble ersooyl. 
41N||6||46||As tra v'eh er chur ad  ersooyl, hie eh seose er slieau dy ghoaill padjer. 
41N||6||47||As tra va'n fastyr  er jeet, va'n lhong ayns mean ny marrey, as eshyn ny-lomarcan er y thalloo.  
41N||6||48||As honnick eh ad tooilleil ayns gymmyrt (son va'n gheay nyn 'oi oc) as  mygeayrt y chiarroo arrey jeh'n oie, haink eh huc shooyll er y cheayn, as ren eh  myr dy ragh eh shaghey ad. 
41N||6||49||Agh tra honnick ad eh shooyll er y cheayn,  heill ad dy nee scaan v'ayn, as dyllee ad. 
41N||6||50||(Son honnick ad ooilley eh,  as v'ad seaghnit.) As chelleeragh loayr eh roo, as dooyrt eh roo, Bee-jee dy  yien mie, she mish t'ayn, ny gow-jee aggle. 
41N||6||51||As hie eh seose 'sy lhong  huc, as ghow yn gheay fea: as v'ad feer atchimagh ayndoo hene erskyn towse, as  goaill yindys. 
41N||6||52||Son cha chooinee ad er (mirril) ny bwilleenyn, son va'n  cree oc er ny chreoghey. 
41N||6||53||As tra v'ad er n'gholl harrish, haink ad gys  cheer Ghennesaret, as hayrn ad gys thalloo. 
41N||6||54||As tra v'ad er jeet ass y  lhong, chelleeragh hug y sleih enney er, 
41N||6||55||As roie ad trooid ooilley yn  cheer mygeayrt, as hug ad lhieu er lhiabbaghyn adsyn va ching, raad v'ad  clashtyn v'eh. 
41N||6||56||As raad erbee dy jagh eh, gys baljyn-cheerey, ny  ard-valjyn, ny er y cheer, lhie ad yn vooinjer hingey ayns ny raaidyn, as ghuee  ad er agh dy ventyn rish oirr e gharmad: as whilleen as venn rish, v'ad er nyn  lheihys.  
41N||7||1||.Eisht haink cooidjagh huggey ny Phariseeyn  as shiartanse jeh ny scrudeyryn, haink veih Jerusalem. 
41N||7||2||As tra honnick ad  paart jeh e ostyllyn gee arran lesh laueyn neu-ghlen (ta shen dy ghra gyn-niee)  hooar ad foill. 
41N||7||3||Son cha vel ny Phariseeyn, ny veg jeh ny Hewnyn goaill  beaghey mannagh vel ad dy kiaralagh niee nyn laueyn, freayll oardaghyn y  chanstyr. 
41N||7||4||As tra t'ad cheet thie veih'n vargey, cha vel ad gee, derrey  t'ad niee. As ta ymmodee dy reddyn elley, t'ad er ghoaill orroo dy reayll, niee  cappanyn as siyn crayee, siyn prashey as buird. 
41N||7||5||Eisht denee ny  Phariseeyn as ny scrudeyryn jeh, Cre'n-fa nagh vel dty ostyllyn freayll  oardaghyn y chanstyr, agh t'ad gee arran lesh laueyn nagh vel nieet? 
41N||7||6||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, S'mie ren Esaias phadeyrys jiuish,  chrauee-oalsey, myr te scruit, Ta'n pobble shoh cur ooashley dou lesh nyn  meillyn, agh ta'n cree oc foddey voym. 
41N||7||7||Ny-yeih ayns fardail t'ad cur  ooashley dooys, gynsaghey son y goo aym's, oardaghyn deiney. 
41N||7||8||Son  treigeil annaghyn Yee ta shiu freayll oardaghyn deiney, niee siyn crayee as  cappanyn: as ymmodee lheid ny reddyn shen ta shiu dy yannoo. 
41N||7||9||As dooyrt  eh roo, S'mie ta shiu jannoo anney Yee gyn vree, dy hoiaghey seose ny oardaghyn  eu hene. 
41N||7||10||Son ta Moses er ghra, Cur arrym da dty ayr as da dty voir: as,  Eshyn ta gweeaghyn da ayr ny moir, lhig da ve deyrit gy baase. 
41N||7||11||Agh ta  shiuish gra, My jir dooinney rish e ayr ny e voir, She Corban eh, ta shen dy  ghra, Yn chooid-choonee shen oddagh uss jerkal rish voym's, te gioot er ny  chasherickey gys Jee: 
41N||7||12||As cha vel shiu lhiggey da red erbee sodjey y  yannoo son e ayr ny e voir: 
41N||7||13||Jannoo goo Yee gyn vree trooid ny oardaghyn  eu, ta shiu er harey: as ymmodee lheid ny reddyn shoh ta shiu dy yannoo.  
41N||7||14||As tra v'eh er n'eamagh er ooilley yn pobble huggey, dooyrt eh roo,  Eaisht-jee ooilley rhym's, as toig-jee. 
41N||7||15||Cha vel nhee erbee veih  cheu-mooie jeh dooinney, oddys goll stiagh ayn, as jannoo neu-ghlen jeh: agh ny  reddyn ta cheet veih cheu-sthie jeh, ad shen ta jannoo neu-ghlen jeh'n dooinney.  
41N||7||16||My ta dooinney erbee as cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn.  
41N||7||17||As tra v'eh er n'gholl stiagh ayns y thie veih'n pobble, denee e  ostyllyn jeh my chione y coraa-dorraghey.
41N||7||18||As dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiuish  myrgeddin lesh cha beg dy hushtey? nagh vel shiu foast cur tastey, cre-erbee  veih cheu-mooie ta goll stiagh ayns y dooinney, nagh vod eh jannoo neu-ghlen  jeh, 
41N||7||19||Er-y-fa nagh vel eh goll stiagh ayns y chree; agh ayns y volg, as  goll magh trooid y chorp, glenney dy chooilley veaghey? 
41N||7||20||As dooyrt eh,  Shen ta cheet magh ass y dooinney, ta jannoo yn dooinney neu-ghlen. 
41N||7||21||Son  veih cheu-sthie, magh veih creeaghyn deiney, ta cheet drogh-smooinaghtyn,  brishey-poosey, maarderys, dunverys, 
41N||7||22||Maarlys, saynt, olkys, molteyrys,  rouanys, drogh-hooill, goan mollaghtagh, moyrn, ommijys: 
41N||7||23||Ta ooilley ny  drogh reddyn shoh cheet veih cheu-sthie, as jannoo yn dooinney neu-ghlen.  
41N||7||24||As hrog eh er veih shen, as jimmee eh gys ardjyn Tyre as Sidon, as hie  eh stiagh ayns thie, as cha baillish fys y ve ec dooinney erbee er, agh cha dod  eh ve keillit. 
41N||7||25||Son va ben dy row, va'n inneen aeg eck as spyrryd  neu-ghlen aynjee, tra cheayll ee jeh, haink ee as huitt ee sheese ec e chassyn:  
41N||7||26||(Va'n ven ny Greek, jeh cheer Syrophenicia) as ghuee ee er, eh dy  hilgey magh yn drogh-spyrryd ass e hinneen. 
41N||7||27||Agh dooyrt Yeesey r'ee,  Lhig da'n chloan ve hoshiaght jeant magh: son cha vel eh cooie arran ny clienney  y ghoaill as y hilgey eh gys moddee. 
41N||7||28||As dreggyr ish as dooyrt ee,  S'feer shen Hiarn: foast ta ny moddee fo yn voayrd as ad gee brooillagh ny  clienney. 
41N||7||29||As dooyrt eh r'ee, Son y raa shoh, immee royd, ta'n  drogh-spyrryd er gholl ass dty inneen. 
41N||7||30||As tra v'ee er jeet thie, hooar  ee e hinneen ny lhie er y lhiabbee, as y drogh spyrryd er gholl ass-jee.  
41N||7||31||As hie eh reesht veih ardjyn Tyre as Sidon, as haink eh gys faarkey  Ghalilee, trooid mean ardjyn Decapolis. 
41N||7||32||As hug ad lhieu huggey dooinney  bouyr, balloo: as ghuee ad er eh dy chur e laue er. 
41N||7||33||As ghow eh dy  lhiattee eh veih'n pobble, as hug eh e veir ayns e chleayshyn, as hug eh magh  shelley, as venn eh rish e hengey. 
41N||7||34||As yeeagh eh seose gys niau, as lhig  eh osney, as dooyrt eh rish, Ephphatha, ta shen, Bee foshlit. 
41N||7||35||As  chelleeragh va ny cleayshyn echey er nyn vosley, as streng e hengey er ny  eaysley, as haink e ghlare lesh. 
41N||7||36||As hug eh currym orroo gyn ad dy insh  shoh da dooinney erbee: agh myr smoo hug eh currym orroo, wheesh shen foddey  smoo ren adsyn y hoilshaghey eh. 
41N||7||37||As v'ad erskyn towse atchimagh, gra,  T'eh er n'yannoo dy chooilley nhee dy mie: t'eh cur chammah er ny beuyr dy  chlashtyn, as ny balloo dy loayrt.  
41N||8||1||.Ayns ny laghyn  shen va earroo yn phobble feer vooar, as gyn veg y veaghey oc dy ghoaill, deie  Yeesey er e ostyllyn huggey, as dooyrt eh roo: 
41N||8||2||Ta chymmey aym's er y  pobble, er-yn-oyr dy vel ad er ny ve marym nish three laa, as nagh vel monney oc  dy ee: 
41N||8||3||As my ver-ym ad ersooyl nyn drostey gys nyn dhieyn hene, nee ad  gannooinaghey er y raad: son ta paart jeu er jeet veih foddey. 
41N||8||4||As  dreggyr e ostyllyn eh, Cre voish oddys dooinney ad shoh y yannoo magh lesh arran  ayns shoh ayns yn aasagh? 
41N||8||5||As denee eh jeu, Cre-woad bwilleen t'eu? As  dooyrt adsyn, Shiaght. 
41N||8||6||As doardee eh da'n pobble dy hoie sheese er y  thalloo: as ghow eh ny shiaght bwilleenyn, as hug eh booise, as vrish eh, as hug  eh ad da e ostyllyn dy hoiaghey rhymboo; as ren adsyn shirveish ad er y pobble.  
41N||8||7||As va kuse dy eeastyn beggey oc: as vannee eh, as doardee eh dy hoiaghey  ad shen myrgeddin er nyn meealloo. 
41N||8||8||Myr shen ren ad gee, as v'ad er nyn  n'yannoo magh, as hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh va er-mayrn, lane shiaght baskadyn.  
41N||8||9||As v'adsyn ren gee mysh kiare thousaneyn, as hug eh ad ersooyl. 
41N||8||10||As jeeragh ghow eh lhuingys marish e ostyllyn, as haink eh gys ardjyn  Dalmanutha. 
41N||8||11||As haink ny Phariseeyn magh, as ren ad toshiaght dy enaght  questionyn jeh, as dy hirrey er cowrey veih niau, er-chee dy phrowal eh.  
41N||8||12||As ren eh osnaghey dy trome ayns e spyrryd, as dooyrt eh, Cre'n-fa ta'n  chee oghe shoh shirrey cowrey? dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh bee cowrey er  ny choyrt da'n cheeloghe shoh. 
41N||8||13||As daag eh ad, as ghow eh lhuingys  reesht, as haink eh gys y cheu elley.
41N||8||14||Nish va e ostyllyn er yarrood dy  ghoaill arran maroo, as cha row oc ayns y lhong agh un willeen. 
41N||8||15||As hug  eh currym orroo, gra, Bee-jee er nyn arrey, cur-jee twoaie jeh soorid ny  Phariseeyn, as jeh soorid Herod. 
41N||8||16||As v'ad pleadeil ry-cheilley, gra, Ta  shoh er-yn-oyr nagh vel arran ain. 
41N||8||17||As tra va fys ec Yeesey er, dooyrt  eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu arganey ny-vud eu hene, son nagh vel arran eu? nagh vel  shiu foast cur tastey, ny toiggal? vel y cree eu foast moal ayns tushtey?  
41N||8||18||Shiuish ta sooillyn eu, nagh vel shiu fakin? as cleayshyn, nagh vel  shiu clashtyn? as nagh vel eh eu ayns cooinaghtyn? 
41N||8||19||Tra vrish mish ny  queig bwilleenyn mastey queig thousaneyn, cre whilleen baskad d'ooilliagh hrog  shiu? Dooyrt ad rish, Daa vaskad jeig. 
41N||8||20||As tra vrish mee ny shiaght  mastey kiare thousaneyn, cre whilleen baskad d'ooilliagh hrog shiu? As dooyrt  adsyn, shiaght. 
41N||8||21||As dooyrt eh roo, Kys te nagh vel shiu goaill tushtey?  
41N||8||22||As haink eh gys Bethsaida, as hug ad lhieu dooinney doal huggey, as  ghuee ad er eh dy ventyn rish. 
41N||8||23||As ghow eh yn dooinney doal er laue as  leeid eh eh magh ass y valley; as tra v'eh er chur shelley er e hooillyn, as er  chur e laueyn er, denee eh jeh row eh fakin nhee erbee. 
41N||8||24||As yeeagh eh  seose, as dooyrt eh, Hee-ym deiney myr biljyn, shooyll. 
41N||8||25||Ny lurg shen,  hug eh e laueyn reesht er e hooillyn, as hug eh er jeeaghyn seose: as hooar eh e  hoilshey, as honnick eh dy chooilley ghooinney dy cronnal. 
41N||8||26||As hug eh eh  ersooyl gys e hie, gra, Ny gow stiagh ayns y valley, chamoo inshys oo eh da  unnane erbee ayns y valley. 
41N||8||27||As hie Yeesey as e ostyllyn magh gys baljyn  Cesarea Philippi: as er y raad denee eh jeu, gra, Cre ta deiney dy ghra  my-mychione's, quoi mee? 
41N||8||28||As dreggyr ad, Ean Bashtey: agh ta paart gra,  Elias; as feallagh elley, Fer jeh ny phadeyryn. 
41N||8||29||As dooyrt eh roo, Agh  quoi ta shiuish dy ghra dy vel mee? As dreggyr Peddyr as dooyrt eh rish, Oo yn  Creest. 
41N||8||30||As hug eh currym orroo gyn ad dy insh da doinney erbee quoi  v'eh. 
41N||8||31||As ren eh toshiaght dy hoilshaghey daue, dy row yn Mac dooinney  dy hurranse ymmodee reddyn, as dy ve mee-lowit liorish y chanstyr, as ny  ard-saggyrtyn as ny scrudeyryn, as dy ve er ny choyrt gy-baase, as er y trass  laa dy irree reesht. 
41N||8||32||As loayr eh yn raa shoh dy foshlit. As ghow Peddyr  eh dy lhiattee, as ren eh toshiaght dy choyrlaghey eh. 
41N||8||33||Agh tra v'eh er  jyndaa mygeayrt, as er yeeaghyn er e ostyllyn, hug eshyn oghsan da Peddyr, gra,  Ass my enish, y violeyder: son cha vel ennaghtyn ayd jeh ny reddyn ta bentyn  rish Jee, agh jeh ny reddyn ta bentyn rish deiney. 
41N||8||34||As tra v'eh er  n'eamagh er y pobble huggey, marish e ostyllyn, dooyrt eh roo, Quoi-erbee ta  aggindagh geiyrt orrym's, lhig da eh-hene y obbal, as e chrosh y hroggal, as  geiyrt orrym. 
41N||8||35||Son quoi-erbee baillish e vioys y hauail, caillee eh eh;  agh quoi-erbee chailIys e vioys er my ghraih's as graih yn tushtal, sauee eh eh.  
41N||8||36||Son cre'n vondeish vees ec dooinney my chosnys eh yn seihll ooilley, as  e annym hene y choayl? 
41N||8||37||Ny cre nee dooinney y choyrt ayns coonrey son e  annym? 
41N||8||38||Quoi-erbee er-y-fa shen ghoys nearey roym's, as roish my ghoan,  ayns y cheeloghe foalsey as peccoil shoh, roishyn myrgeddin ghoys Mac y dooinney  nearey, tra hig eh ayns gloyr e Ayrey, as ny ainleyn casherick marish.  
41N||9||1||As dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy vel  paart jeusyn ta nyn shassoo ayns shoh, nagh jean blashtyn er y baase, derrey  vees ad er vakin reeriaght Yee er jeet lesh pooar. 
41N||9||2||As ec kione shey laa,  ghow Yeesey marish Peddyr as Jamys, as Ean, as hug eh lesh ad seose gys slieau  ard ad-hene er-lheh: as va'n cummey echey er ny chaghlaa kiongoyrt roo. 
41N||9||3||As haink y coamrey echey dy ve sollys, erskyn towse gial myr y sniaghtey; nagh  row walker er y thalloo oddagh jannoo cha gial roo. 
41N||9||4||As hug ad my-ner  Elias, as Moses: as ad taggloo rish Yeesey. 
41N||9||5||As dreggyr Peddyr as dooyrt  eh rish Yeesey, Vainshter, s'maynrey dooinyn dy hannaghtyn ayns shoh: as lhig  dooin three cabbaneyn y hroggal, cabbane er dty hon's, as cabbane son Moses, as  cabbane son Elias. 
41N||9||6||Son cha row fys echey cre dy ghra, son s'mooar yn  aggle v'orroo. 
41N||9||7||As ren bodjal scadoo y hilgey harrystoo: as haink coraa  ass y vodjal, gra, Shoh my vac ennoil; eaisht-jee rish. 
41N||9||8||As chelleeragh  jeeaghyn mygeayrt, cha vaik ad dooinney erbee agh Yeesey ynrycan maroo hene.  
41N||9||9||As myr v'ad cheet neose jeh'n clieau, hug eh currym orroo, gyn ad dy  insh da dooinney erbee cre v'ad er vakin, derrey veagh Mac y dooinney er n'irree  veih ny merriu.
41N||9||10||As dreill ad y raa shen oc hene, resooney yn derrey yeh  rish y jeh elley cre v'er ny hoiggal liorish yn irree seose-reesht veih ny  merriu. 
41N||9||11||As denee ad jeh, gra, Cre'n-oyr ta ny scrudeyryn gra, dy vel  Elias dy heet hoshiaght? 
41N||9||12||As dreggyr eshyn as dinsh eh daue, Dy row  Elias dy firrinagh dy heet hoshiaght, as dy lhiassaghey dy chooilley nhee, as  kys te scruit mychione Mac y dooinney dy nhegin da goll trooid mooarane  surranse, as beg dy ve soit jeh. 
41N||9||13||Agh ta mish gra riu, dy vel Elias dy  jarroo er jeet, myr te scruit jeh, as dy vel ad er n'yannoo rish myr bailloo.  
41N||9||14||As tra v'eh er jeet gys e ostyllyn honnick eh chaglym mooar dy leih my  geayrt-y-moo, as ny scrudeyryn arganey roo. 
41N||9||15||As chelleeragh tra honnick  yn pobble eh, ghow ad ooilley lane boggey jeh, as roie ad huggey goltaghey da.  
41N||9||16||As denee eh jeh ny scrudeyryn, Cre ny questionyn va shiu dy enaght jeu?  
41N||9||17||As dreggyr fer jeh'n cheshaght, as dooyrt eh, Vainshter, Ta mee er chur  lhiam my vac hood, ayn ta spyrryd balloo: 
41N||9||18||As raad erbee dy vel eh dy  ghoaill eh, t'eh dy eiyrt eh noon as noal; as t'eh keshal as snaggeraght Iesh e  eeacklyn, as shymley ersooyl: as loayr mee rish dty ostyllyn, ad dy chastey eh;  agh cha daink eh lhieu. 
41N||9||19||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, O heeloghe  vee-chredjuagh, caid ta mish dy ve meriu? caid ta mee dy hurranse diu? cur lhiat  eh hym's. 
41N||9||20||As hug ad lhieu eh huggey: as tra honnick eh eh, chelleeragh  deiyr y spyrryd eh noon as noal, as huitt eh er y thalloo, rowlal as keshal ec y  veeal. 
41N||9||21||As denee eh jeh'n ayr echey, Caid neayr as haink shoh er? As  dooyrt eh, T'eh er ve myr shoh neayr as v'eh ny lhiannoo. 
41N||9||22||As dy mennick  t'eh er hilgey eh ayns yn aile, as ayns ny ushtaghyn, dy stroie eh: agh my oddys  oo nhee erbee y yannoo, jean chymmey orrin, as cooin lhien. 
41N||9||23||Dooyrt  Yeesey rish, My oddys oo credjal, ta dy chooilley nhee cheet leshyn ta credjal.  
41N||9||24||As chelleeragh deie ayr y lhiennoo, as dooyrt eh lesh jeir, Hiarn, ta  mee credjal; niartee lesh my chredjue faase. 
41N||9||25||Tra honnick Yeesey dy row  yn pobble ayns preis chionney dy cheilley, vaggyr eh er y spyrryd neu-ghlen, as  dooyrt eh rish, Uss spyrryd balloo as bouyr, ta mee dy dty harey, Oo dy heet  magh ass, as gyn arragh dy gholl stiagh ayn. 
41N||9||26||As dyllee yn spyrryd, as  deiyr eh noon as noal eh, as haink eh magh ass; as v'eh myr dy beagh eh marroo,  ayns wheesh as dy dooyrt ymmodee, T'eh marroo. 
41N||9||27||Agh ghow Yeesey eh er  laue, as hrog eh eh seose, as dirree eh. 
41N||9||28||As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh  ayns y thie, denee e ostyllyn jeh er-lheh, Cre'n-oyr nagh voddagh shin y chastey  eh? 
41N||9||29||As dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel y keint shoh cheet magh er aght erbee,  agh liorish padjer as trostey.
41N||9||30||As jimmee eh veih shen, as hie ad trooid  Galilee; as cha baillish fys y ve ec dooinney erbee er. 
41N||9||31||Son dynsee eh e  ostyllyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Ta Mac y dooinney dy ve livreit gys laueyn deiney,  as marree ad eh, as erreish da v'er ny varroo, nee eh girree reesht yn trass  laa. 
41N||9||32||Agh cha hoig ad yn raa shen, as cha by-lhoys daue fenaghtyn jeh.  
41N||9||33||As haink eh gys Capernaum, as ayns y thie denee eh jeu, Cre'n taggloo  shen va eu ny mast' eu hene er y raad? 
41N||9||34||Agh v'ad nyn-dhost: Son er y  raad v'ad pleadeil nyn mast' oc hene, quoi syrjey veagh. 
41N||9||35||As hoie eh  sheese, as deie eh er y ghaa-yeig, as dooyrt eh roo, My ta dooinney erbee  geearree dy ve hoshiaght, bee eh er-jerrey ooilley, as ny harvaant da ooilley.  
41N||9||36||As ghow eh lhiannoo, as hoie eh eh kiongoyrt roo: as tra v'eh er  ghoaill eh ayns e roihaghyn, dooyrt eh roo, 
41N||9||37||Quoi-erbee nee soiaghey jeh  unnane dy lheid y chloan shoh, t'eh soiaghey jeem's: as quoi-erbee nee soiaghey  jeem's, cha nee jeem's t'eh soiaghey, agh jehsyn t'er my choyrt. 
41N||9||38||As  dreggyr Ean eh, gra, Vainshter, honnick shin fer castey drogh-spyrrydyn ayns dty  ennym's, as cha vel eh geiyrt orrinyn, as ren shin eh y lhiettal, er-yn-oyr nagh  vel eh geiyrt orrinyn. 
41N||9||39||Agh dooyrt Yeesey, Ny jean-jee eh y lhiettal:  son cha vel dooinney erbee nee mirril y yannoo ayns m'ennym's, oddys dy eddrym  loayrt olk jee'm. 
41N||9||40||Son eshyn nagh vel nyn 'oi, t'eh er nyn baart.  
41N||9||41||Son quoi-erbee ver diu cappan dy ushtey dy iu, ayns m'ennym's,  er-yn-oyr dy vel shiu bentyn gys Creest, dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, nagh gaill  eh e leagh. 
41N||9||42||As quoi-erbee ver oyr da unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey shoh  ta credjal aynym's dy huittym ( veih'n chredjue ) bare da clagh wyllin dy ve  croghit mysh e wannal, as eh dy ve tilgit ayns y cheayn. 
41N||9||43||As my ta dty  laue dy dty hayrn gys yn olk, giare jeed ee: te ny share dhyt goll stiagh ayns y  vea veayn, baccagh, na daa laue y ve ayd, as oo dy gholl gys niurin, gys yn aile  nagh bee dy bragh er ny vooghey. 
41N||9||44||Raad nagh vel y veishteig oc geddyn  baase, as cha vel yn aile er ny vooghey. 
41N||9||45||As my ta dty chass dy dty  hayrn gys peccah, giare jeed ee: te ny share dhyt goll croobagh stiagh ayns y  vea veayn, na daa chass y ve ayd, as oo dy ve tilgit ayns niurin, ayns yn aile  nagh bee dy bragh er ny vooghey:
41N||9||46||Raad nagh vel y veishteig oc geddyn  baase, as cha vel yn aile er ny vooghey. 
41N||9||47||As my ta dty hooill dy dty  hayrn gys peccah, pluck assyd ee: te ny share dhyt goll stiagh ayns reeriaght  Yee lesh un hooill, na daa hooill y ve ayd, as oo dy ve tilgit ayns aile niurin:  
41N||9||48||Raad nagh vel y veishteig oc geddym baase, as cha vel yn aile er ny  vooghey. 
41N||9||49||Son bee dy chooilley unnane jeh nyn lheid oc shoh er nyn  sailley lesh aile, as dy chooilley oural er ny hailley lesh sollan. 
41N||9||50||Ta'n sollan mie: agh my ta'n sollan er choayl e hailjys, kys hig e vree ayn  reesht? Freill-jee sollan ayndiu hene, as bee-jee ayns shee yn derrey yeh rish y  jeh elley. 
41N||10||1||As hrog eh er veih shen, as haink eh gys  ardjyn Yudea, trooid y cheer v'er cheu elley dy Yordan: as haink y pobble huggey  reesht; as myr v'eh cliaghtey, dynsee eh ad reesht. 
41N||10||2||As haink ny  Phariseeyn huggey, as denee ad jeh, er-chee prowal eh, Vel eh lowal da dooinney  scarrey rish e ven? 
41N||10||3||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n sarey hug  Moses diu? 
41N||10||4||As dooyrt adsyn, Lhow Moses screeuyn scarree y yannoo, as dy  choyrt ee ersooyl. 
41N||10||5||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, Son creoghys ny  creeaghyn eu scrieu eh diu yn sarey shoh, 
41N||10||6||Agh er-dy hoshiaght y theihll,  chroo Jee ad fyrrynagh as bwoirrynagh. 
41N||10||7||Er-yn-oyr shoh nee dooinney  faagail e ayr as e voir, as lhiannee eh gys e ven. 
41N||10||8||As bee ad ny-neesht  un eill: myr shen cha vel ad ny-sodjey jees, agh yn un eill. 
41N||10||9||Cre-erbee  er-y-fa shen ta Jee er chur cooidjagh, ny lhig da dooinney erbee y scarrey  veih-my-cheilley.
