41N||10||10||As ayns y thie denee e ostyllyn jeh reesht, mychione  y chooish cheddin. 
41N||10||11||As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi-erbee scarrys rish e ven, as  phoosys ben elley, t'eh brishey poosey n'oi eck. 
41N||10||12||As my scarrys ben rish  e sheshey, as ee dy ve poost rish dooinney elley, t'ee brishey poosey. 
41N||10||13||As hug ad lhieu cloan aegey gys Creest, dy jinnagh eh bentyn roo; as hug e  ostyllyn oghsan dauesyn hug lhieu ad. 
41N||10||14||Agh tra honnick Yeesey eh, v'eh  feer jymmoosagh, as dooyrt eh roo, Sur-jee cloan aegey dy heet hym's, as ny  jean-jee ad y lhiettal: son jeh nyn lheid ta reeriaght Yee. 
41N||10||15||Dy  firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Quoi erbee nagh jean goaill reeriaght Yee myr lhiannoo  beg, cha jed eh stiagh ayn. 
41N||10||16||As ghow eh ad seose ayns e roihaghyn, hug  eh e laueyn orroo, as vannee eh ad. 
41N||10||17||As tra v'eh er n'gholl magh er y  raad, haink fer roie ny whuail, as gliooney huggey, denee eh jeh, Vainshter vie,  cre neem's dy voddym eiraght y choshey ayns y vea veayn? 
41N||10||18||As dooyrt  Yeesey rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou genmys mish mie? cha vel ayn ny ta mie, agh unnane,  ynrycan Jee. 
41N||10||19||Shione dhyt ny annaghyn, Ny jean poosey y vrishey, Ny jean  dunverys, Ny jean geid, Ny jean feanish foalsey y ymmyrkey, Ny Jean molteyraght,  Cur arrym da dty ayr, as da dty voir. 
41N||10||20||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh  rish, Vainshter, ooilley ny annaghyn shoh ta mee er reayll veih my aegid.  
41N||10||21||Eisht Yeesey, jeeaghyn dy ennoil er dooyrt rish, Ta un red ort foast dy  yannoo immee royd, as creck ny t'ayd, as cur eh da ny boghtyn, as bee berchys  ayd ayns niau; as tar, trog y chrosh, as eiyr orrym's. 
41N||10||22||As v'eh  trimshagh ec y raa shen, as hie eh ersooyl: son va cummallyn mooarey echey.  
41N||10||23||As yeeagh Yeesey mygeayrt, as dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Cre cha  doillee as vees eh dauesyn ta berchys oc dy gholl stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee!  
41N||10||24||As ghow adsyn yindys jeh ny goan echey. Agh dreggyr Yeesey reesht, as  dooyrt eh roo, Chloan, cre cha doillee as te dauesyn ta treishteil ayns berchys,  dy gholl stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee! 
41N||10||25||Te ny sassey da camel goll trooid  croae snaidey, na da lheid y dooinney berchagh shoh dy gholl stiagh ayns  reeriaght Yee. 
41N||10||26||As v'ad atchimagh erskyn towse, gra nyn mast' oc hene,  Quoi eisht oddys v'er ny auail. 
41N||10||27||As yeeagh Yeesey orroo, as dooyrt eh,  Da deiney ta shoh neu-phossible, agh cha vel eh da Jee: son da Jee ta dy  chooilley nhee possible. 
41N||10||28||Eisht ren Peddyr toshiaght dy ghra rish,  Cur-my-ner ta shinyn er dreigeil ooilley, as er n'eiyrt ort's. 
41N||10||29||As  dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh vel dooinney  erbee, t'er dreigeil thie, ny braaraghyn, ny shayraghyn, ny ayr, ny moir, ny  ben, ny cloan, ny thalloo, er my ghraih's as graih yn tushtal, 
41N||10||30||Nagh vow  keead-filley nish ayns y traa shoh, thieyn, as braaraghyn, as shayraghyn, as  moiraghyn, as cloan, as thalloo, lesh seaghyn; as ayns y theihll ta ry-heet yn  vea veayn. 
41N||10||31||Agh bee ymmodee jeusyn ta hoshiaght er-jerrey: as jeusyn ta  er-jerrey, hoshiaght. 
41N||10||32||As v'ad er y raad goll seose gys Jerusalem: as  hie Yeesey rhymboo; as v'ad atchimagh, as myr vad geiyrt er, va aggle orroo. As  ghow eh yn daa ostyl yeig reesht, as ren eh toshiaght dy insh daue, cre ny  reddyn harragh er, 
41N||10||33||Gra, Cur-my-ner, ta shin goll seose gys Jerusalem,  as bee Mac y dooinney er ny livrey gys ny ard-saggyrtyn, as gys ny scrudeyryn:  as nee ad eh y gheyrey dy baase, as livreyee ad eh gys ny Ashoonee. 
41N||10||34||As  craidee ad mysh, as custee ad eh, as tilgee ad shellaghyn er, as marree ad eh:  as y trass laa nee eh girree reesht. 
41N||10||35||As haink Jamys as Ean mec Zebedee  huggey, gra, Vainshter; Ta shin guee ort, dy chur dooin yn aghin shen, nee mayd  y yeearree ort. 
41N||10||36||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre bailliu mee dy yannoo er nyn son?  
41N||10||37||Dooyrt adsyn rish, Giall dooinyn dy hoie, yn derrey yeh er dty laue  yesh, as y jeh elley er dty laue chiare, ayns dty ghloyr. 
41N||10||38||Agh dooyrt  Yeesey roo, Cha s'eu cre ta shiu dy yeearree: vod shiu giu jeh'n cappan ta mish  giu jeh? as v'er nyn mashtey lesh y bashtey ta mish bashtit lesh? 
41N||10||39||As  dooyrt ad rish, Foddee mayd. As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Iu-ee shiu dy jarroo jeh'n  cappan ta mish giu jeh; as bee shiu er nyn mashtey lesh y bashtey ta mish  bashtit lesh: 
41N||10||40||Agh dy hoie er my laue-yesh as er my laue-chiare, cha vel  shen lhiam's dy choyrt, agh bee eh er ny choyrt ynrycan dauesyn er nyn son te  kiarit. 
41N||10||41||As tra cheayll yn jeih shoh, ren ad toshiaght dy ve feer  jymmoosagh rish Jamys as Ean. 
41N||10||42||Agh deie Yeesey orroo huggey, as dooyrt  eh roo, Ta fys eu dy vel fir-reill ny Hashoonee gymmyrkey chiarnys orroo, as ta  ny ard-gheiney oc reill dy mooaralagh harrystoo. 
41N||10||43||Agh cha bee shiuish  myr shen: agh quoi-erbee jiuish baillish ve ooasle, lhig da ve nyn shirveishagh:  
41N||10||44||As quoi-erbee baillish ve yn ard ghooinney nyn mast' eu, lhig da ve ny  harvaant da ooilley. 
41N||10||45||Son cha daink yn eer Mac dooinney dy ve  shirveishit, agh dy hirveish, as dy chur e vioys ny lhiassaghey son ymmodee.  
41N||10||46||As haink ad gys Jericho: as myr v'eh goll magh ass Jericho marish e  ostyllyn, as marish earroo mooar dy leih, va Bartimeus doal mac Timeus, ny hoie  rish oirr yn raad, shirrey jeirk. 
41N||10||47||As tra cheayll eh dy nee Yeesey dy  Nazareth v'ayn, ren eh toshiaght dy eamagh as dy ghra, Yeesey Vac Ghavid, jean  myghin orrym. 
41N||10||48||As hooar ymmodee foill da eh dy ve ny-host: agh dyllee  eshyn wheesh shen foddey smoo, Vac Ghavid, jean myghin orrym. 
41N||10||49||As hass  Yeesey, as doardee eh eh dy ve eit: as deie ad er y dooinney doal, gra rish, Bee  dy yien mie, irree; t'eh geamagh ort. 
41N||10||50||As hilg eh ersooyl e gharmad, as  dirree eh, as haink eh-gys Yeesey. 
41N||10||51||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh  rish, Cre bailt mee dy yannoo er dty hon? Dooyrt y dooinney doal rish, Hiarn, dy  voddym my hoilshey y gheddyn. 
41N||10||52||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Immee royd; ta dty  chredjue er dty laanaghey. As chelleeragh hooar eh e hoilshey, as jimmee eh  marish Yeesey er y raad.
41N||11||1||As tra v'ad er jeet  er-gerrey da Jerusalem, gys Bethphage as Bethany ec cronk ny Oliveyn, hug eh  magh jees jeh e ostyllyn, 
41N||11||2||As dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee reue gys y  balley-cheerey ta jeeragh erriu; as cha leah as vees shiu er n'gholl stiagh ayn,  yiow shiu lhiy kainlt, urree nagh varkee rieau dooinney; feayshil-jee as cur-jee  lhieu ee. 
41N||11||3||As my jir dooinney erbee riu, Cre'n-fa ta shiu jannoo shoh?  abbyr-jee dy vel feme ec y Chiarn urree; as chelleeragh nee eh yn raad y lhiggey  jee, 
41N||11||4||As hie ad rhymboo, as hooar ad y lhiy kianlt cheu-mooie jeh'n  dorrys, ayns boayl va daa raad cheet dy cheilley: as deayshil ad ee. 
41N||11||5||As  dooyrt shiartanse jeusyn va nyn shassoo ayns shen, Kys dy vel shiu feaysley yn  lhiy? 
41N||11||6||As dooyrt ad roo myr va Yeesey er n'oardaghey daue, as lhig ad y  raad daue. 
41N||11||7||As hug ad lhieu yn lhiy gys Yeesey, as hilg ad ny garmadyn oc  urree; as hoie eshyn er y lhiy. 
41N||11||8||As ren ymmodee jeu nyn gharmadyn y  skeayleyery raad: as ghiare feallagh elley banglaneyn jeh ny biljyn as skeayl ad  ad er y raad. 
41N||11||9||As adsyn hie roish, as y vooinjer haink ny yei, deie ad,  gra, Hosanna, bannit ta eshyn ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn. 
41N||11||10||Bannit dy  row reeriaght yn ayr ain David, ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn; Hosanna ayns yn  yrjid. 
41N||11||11||As hie Yeesey gys Jerusalem, as hie eh stiagh ayns y chiamble;  as tra v'eh er yeeaghyn mygeayrt er dy chooilley nhee, as nish dy row yn fastyr  er jeet, hie eh magh gys Bethany marish y daa ostyl yeig. 
41N||11||12||As laa ny  vairagh, tra v'ad er jeet veih Bethany, v'eh accryssagh. 
41N||11||13||As honnick eh  billey-figgagh er y raad, as duillagyn er, as haink eh, dy yeeaghyn voghe eh  mess erbee er: as tra v'eh er jeet huggey, cha dooar eh nhee erbee er, agh  duillagyn; son cha row imbagh ny figgyn ayn foast. 
41N||11||14||As dreggyr Yeesey,  as dooyrt eh rish, Nar ee dooinney erbee mess jeeds veih shoh magh er son dy  bragh. As cheayll e ostyllyn eh. 
41N||11||15||As haink ad gys Jerusalem: as hie  Yeesey stiagh ayns y chiamble, as ren eh toshiaght dy eiyrt magh adsyn va creck  as kionnaghey ayns y chiamble, as hilg eh harrish ny buird ocsyn va caghlaa  argid, as ny stuill ocsyn va creck calmaneyn 
41N||11||16||As cha lhowagh eh da  dooinney erbee saagh erbee y chur lesh trooid y chiamble. 
41N||11||17||As dynsee eh  ad, gra, Nagh vel eh scruit, Bee my hie's enmyssit liorish dy chooilley ashoon,  thie yn phadjer? agh ta shiuish er n'yannoo eh ny ooig dy vaarlee. 
41N||11||18||As  cheayll ny scrudeyryn as ny ard-saggyrtyn jeh, as v'ad shirrey kys oddagh ad eh  y stroie: son v'ad ayns aggle roish, er-yn-oyr dy row ooilley yn pobble goaill  yindys jeh'n ynsagh echey. 
41N||11||19||As tra va'n fastyr er jeet, hie eh magh ass  yn ard-valley. 
41N||11||20||As ayns y voghrey, myr v'ad goll shaghey, honnick ad y  billey-figgagh dy row eh er greenaghey seose veih ny fraueyn. 
41N||11||21||As  by-chooinee lesh Peddyr, as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, cur-my-ner, ta'n billey  figgagh hug uss fo mollaght er fioghey ersooyl. 
41N||11||22||As dreggyr Yeesey as  dooyrt eh roo, Soie-jee nyn gredjue ayns Jee. 
41N||11||23||Son dy firrinagh ta mee  gra riu, Quoi erbee jir rish y slieau shoh, Bee er dty scughey, as er dty hilgey  ayns y cheayn, as nagh jean mee-ourys ayns e chree, agh ta credjal dy jig ny  reddyn t'eh dy ghra gy kione, bee shen ny jir eh er ny chooilleeney. 
41N||11||24||Shen-y-fa ta mee gra riu, Cre-erbee ta shiu dy yeearree ayns padjer, cred-jee dy  vow shiu ad, as bee ad eu. 
41N||11||25||As tra vees shiu shassoo dy ghoaill padjer,  leih-jee, my ta nhee erbee eu noi dooinney erbee: dy vod nyn Ayr myrgeddin  t'ayns niau nyn loghtyn y leih diuish. 
41N||11||26||Son mannagh jean shiuish leih,  cha jean nyn Ayr t'ayns nian nyn loghtyn y leih diuish. 
41N||11||27||As haink ad  reesht gys Jerusalem: as myr v'eh walkal ayns y chiamble, haink huggey ny  ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn, as y chanstyr. 
41N||11||28||As dooyrt ad rish,  Cre'n phooar t'ayd's dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh, as quoi hug y phooar shoh dhyt dy  yannoo ny reddyn shoh? 
41N||11||29||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Fenyms  jiuish myrgeddin un red, as freggyr-jee mee, as insh-yms diuish cre'n phooar  t'aym dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh. 
41N||11||30||Bashtey Ean, nee veih niau ve, ny veih  deiney? cur-jee ansoor dou. 
41N||11||31||As ren ad resooney roo hene, gra, My jir  mayd, Veih niau, jir eshyn, Cre'n-oyr eisht nagh ren shiu eh y chredjal?  
41N||11||32||Agh my jir mayd, Veih deiney, v'ad ayns aggle roish y pobble, son va dy  chooilley ghooinney jeeaghyn er Ean dy ve dy jarroo ny adeyr. 
41N||11||33||As  dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad rish Yeesey, Cha nod mayd ginsh. As dreggyr Yeesey as  dooyrt eh roosyn, Chamoo insh-yms diuish liorish cre'n phooar ta mee dy yannoo  ny reddyn shoh. 
41N||12||1||As ren eh toshiaght dy loayrt roo  liorish coraaghyn-dorraghey. Va dooinney dy row ren garey-feeyney y hoiaghey, as  ren eh cleigh mygeayrt-y-mysh, as chleiy eh ynnyd son y press-feeyney, as hrog  eh toor, as hoie eh eh rish eirrinnee, as hie eh gys cheer foddey. 
41N||12||2||As ec  yn imbagh cooie hug eh sharvaant gys ny eirinnee, dy gheddyn veih ny eirinnee  jeh mess y gharey feeyney. 
41N||12||3||As ghow ad as woaill ad eh, as hug ad eh  ersooyl follym. 
41N||12||4||As reesht hug eh huc sharvaant elley as ersyn cheau ad  claghyn, as vrish ad y kione er, as hug ad eh ersooyl lesh dellal feer  scammyltagh. 
41N||12||5||As reesht hug eh huc sharvaant elley; as eshyn ren ad y  varroo: as ymmodee elley, bwoalley paart, as marroo paart. 
41N||12||6||As va echey  foast un vac, er v'eh feer ghraihagh, as hug eh eshyn myrgeddin ec y jerrey huc,  gra, Ver ad arrym da my vac. 
41N||12||7||Agh dooyrt ny eirinnee shen ny mast' oc  hene, Shoh'n eirey: tar-jee as lhig dooin eh y varroo, as bee yn eiraght lhien  hene. 
41N||12||8||As ghow ad, as varr ad eh, as hilg ad eh magh ass y  gharey-feeyney. 
41N||12||9||Cre nee Chiarn y gharey-feeyney er-y-fa shen y yannoo?  hig eh as stroie-ee eh ny eirinnee, as ver eh yn garey-feeyney da eirinnee  elley. 
41N||12||10||Nagh vel shiuish er lhaih ayns goo Yee? Ta'n chlagh ren ny  masoonee y vee-lowal, er jeet dy ve yn ard chlagh chorneilagh. 
41N||12||11||Shoh va  jannoo yn Chiarn, as te yindyssagh ayns ny sooillyn ainyn. 
41N||12||12||As v'ad  shegin er goaill eh, agh v'ad ayns aggle roish y pobble; son va fys oc dy row eh  er loayrt yn coraa-dorraghey noi ad-hene: as daag ad eh, as hie ad rhymboo.  
41N||12||13||As hug ad huggey shiartanse jeh ny Phariseeyn, as ny Herodianee, dy  ghoaill vondeish jeh ayns e ghoan. 
41N||12||14||As tra v'ad er jeet, dooyrt ad rish  Vainshter, ta fys ain dy vel oo firrinagh, as nagh vel oo ayns imnea roish  dooinney erbee; son cha vel oo soiaghey jeh persoon deiney, agh gynsaghey raad  Yee ayns firrinys: vel eh lowal keesh y choyrt da Cesar, mannagh vel? 
41N||12||15||Jean mayd coyrt, ny dyn coyrt? Agh va fys echeysyn er y chialgeyrys oc, as  dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey dy my ghoaill ayns ribbey? cur-jee lhieu  ping hym, dy vaik-ym eh. 
41N||12||16||As hug ad lhieu eh: as dooyrt eh roo, Quoi gys  ta'n cowrey as y screeu shoh bentyn? As dooyrt adsyn rish, Gys Cesar. 
41N||12||17||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh roo, Eeck-jee da Cesar, shen ny ta lesh Cesar,  as da Jee, ny reddyn ta lesh Jee. As ghow ad yindys jeh. 
41N||12||18||Eisht haink  huggey ny Sadduceeyn, ta gra nagh vel irree-seose-reesht dy ve ayn; as denee ad  jeh, gra, 
41N||12||19||Vainshter, ta Moses er scrieu dooin, My ta braar dooinney  geddyn baase, as faagail e ven ny yei, gyn cloan echey r'ee, dy vel e vraar dy  phoosey yn ven echey, as dy hroggal seose sluight da e vraar. 
41N||12||20||Nish va  shiaght braaraghyn: as ghow yn braar shinney ben, agh geddyn baase cha daag eh  sluight. 
41N||12||21||As ghow yn nah vraar ee, as hooar eh baase, as cha daag eh  sluight: as y trass myrgeddin. 
41N||12||22||As v'ee ec y chiaght, as cha daag ad  sluight: er-jerrey ooilley hooar y ven baase myrgeddin. 
41N||12||23||Shen-y-fa ec yn  irree-seose-reesht veih ny merriu, tra nee ad girree, quoi jeu vees ee echey son  ben? son v'ee ny ben da'n chiaght. 
41N||12||24||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo,  Nagh vel shiu er-y-fa shen fo marranys, er yn-oyr nagh vel toiggal eu jeh goo ny  jeh pooar Yee? 
41N||12||25||Son ec yn irree-seose-reesht veih ny merriu, cha vel ad  poosey, ny er nyn goyrt ayns poosey: agh t'ad myr ny ainleyn t'ayns niau.  
41N||12||26||As mychione ny merriu, dy nirree ad; nagh vel shiu er lhaih ayns lioar  Voses, kys loayr Jee rish ass y thammag, gra, Mish Jee Abraham, as Jee Isaac, as  Jee Yacob? 
41N||12||27||Cha nee Jee ny merriu eh, agh Jee ny bioee: ta shiu er-y-fa  shen fo marranys vooar. 
41N||12||28||As haink fer jeh ny scrudeyryn cheayll ad  resooney cooidjagh, as cur tastey dy row eh er n'ansoor ad dy mie, denee eh jeh,  Cre'n ard-anney jeh ny annaghyn ooilley? 
41N||12||29||As dreggyr Yeesey eh, Yn chied  anney jeh ooilley ny annaghyn, Clasht, O Israel, Ta'n Chiarn yn Jee ain yn  ynrycan Chiarn; 
41N||12||30||As ver oo graih da'n Chiarn dty Yee lesh ooilley dty  chree, as lesh ooilley dty annym, as lesh ooilley dty aigney, as lesh ooilley  dty niart: shoh'n chied anney. 
41N||12||31||As ta'n nah anney casley rish, ta shen  dy ghra, Ver oo graih da dty naboo, myr dhyt hene: cha vel anney erbee elley  smoo na ad shoh. 
41N||12||32||As dooyrt y scrudeyr rish, S'mie shen Vainshter, t'ou  er loayrt yn irriney: son ta un Jee ayn, as cha vel Jee erbee elley agh eh-hene.  
41N||12||33||As dy ve graihagh er lesh ooilley yn chree, as lesh ooilley yn tushtey,  as lesh ooilley yn annym, as lesh ooilley yn niart, as dy ve graihagh er e naboo  myr er hene ta shen ny smoo na ooilley ny slane chebballyn losht as ourallyn.  
41N||12||34||As tra honnick Yeesey dy dansoor eh dy tushtagh, dooyrt eh rish, Cha  vel oo foddey veih reeriaght Yee. As cha by-lhoys da dooinney erbee maghey shen  question erbee sodjey y chur huggey. 
41N||12||35||As dreggyr Yeesey myr v'eh  gynsaghey ayns y chiamble, as dooyrt eh, Kys ta ny scurudeyryn gra dy nee Creest  mac Ghavid? 
41N||12||36||Son ta David eh-hene er ghra liorish y Spyrryd Noo, Dooyrt  y Chiarn rish my Hiarn's, Soie uss er my laue yesh, derrey ver-ym dty noidyn son  stoyl dty choshey. 
41N||12||37||Ta David er-y-fa shen eh-hene genmys eh ny Hiarn; as  kys t'eh eisht yn mac echey? As deaisht yn pobble v'er nyn jaglym cooidjagh rish  dy arryltagh. 
41N||12||38||As dooyrt eh roo, myr v'eh gynsagh, Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie  jeh ny scrudeyryn, ta geearree shooyll ayns coamraghyn liauyrey, as sleih dy  vannaghey daue ayns ny margaghyn, 
41N||12||39||As ny ard-stuill y ve oc ayns ny  synagogueyn, as ny ard ynnydyn-soie ec cuirraghyn: 
41N||12||40||T'ad cur mow thieyn  mraane treoghe, as son scaa dy chraueeaght lhiggey orroo dy ve mennick ec  padjer: ta briwnys strimmey ny chour oc shoh. 
41N||12||41||As myr va Yeesey ny hoie  liorish kishtey yn stoyr, ghow eh tastey kys va'n pobble cur argid ayns y stoyr:  as ren ymmodee va berchagh cur ayn dy palchey. 
41N||12||42||As haink ben voght  treoghe dy row, as hilg ee ayn daa vite ta jannoo farling. 
41N||12||43||As deie eh  er e ostyllyn huggey, as dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy vel y  ven-treoghe voght shoh er chur ny smoo ayns kishtey yn stoyr, na dy chooilley  unnane t'er choyrt ayn. 
41N||12||44||Son t'adsyn ooilley er chur ayn ass nyn  balchey: as t'eeish myr s'boght ee, er choyrt ayn ooilley ny v'eck, dy jarroo  ooilley e cooid-seihlt. 
41N||13||1||As myr v'eh goll magh ass y  chiamble, dooyrt fer jeh e ostyllyn rish, Jeeagh, Vainshter, cre ny claghyn! as  cre'n vuildal t'ayns shoh! 
41N||13||2||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Vel oo  fakin y vuildal vooar shoh? cha bee faagit un chlagh er clagh elley nagh bee er  ny lhieggal. 
41N||13||3||As myr v'eh ny hoie er cronk ny Oliveyn, jeeragh er y  chiamble, denee Peddyr as Jamys, as Ean, as Andreays jeh er-lheh 
41N||13||4||Insh  dooin, cuin vees ny reddyn shoh? as cre vees y cowrey tra vees dy chooilley nhee  jeu shoh er nyn gooilleeney? 
41N||13||5||As dreggyr Yeesey ad, as ren eh toshiaght  dy ghra, Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie nagh jean dooinney erbee shiu y volley. 
41N||13||6||Son hig ymmodee ayns m'ennym's, gra, Mish Creest: as nee ad ymmodee y volley.  
41N||13||7||As tra chluinnys shiu jeh caggaghyn as jeh imraaghyn dy bee-jee  seaghnit: son shegin da lheid y ve ayn, agh cha vel yn jerrey foast. 
41N||13||8||Son  nee ashoon girree-magh noi ashoon as reeriaght noi reeriaght: as bee craaghyn  thallooin ayns ymmodee ynnydyn, as gennaghyn as seaghyn: ad shoh toshiaght  trimshaghyn. 
41N||13||9||Agh jeeagh-jee shiuish diu hene: son livreyee ad shiu seose  gys coonceilyn; as ayns ny quaiyllyn vees shiu er nyn mwoalley, as ver ad lhieu  shiu kiongoyrt rish fir-reill as reeaghyn er y choontey aym's, dy ve son  feanishyn jeem's. 
41N||13||10||As shegin da'n sushtal ve hoshiaght er ny phreacheil  mastey dy chooilley ashoon. 
41N||13||11||Agh tra ver ad lhieu shiu dy ve currit  stiagh, ny smooinee-jee ro-laue cre nee shiu loayrt, chamoo bee-jee imneagh cre  dy ghra: agh cre-erbee vees er ny choyrt diu ayns yn oor cheddin, shen  loayr-jee; son cha nee shiuish ta loayrt, agh y Spyrryd Noo. 
41N||13||12||Eisht nee  braar e vraar y vrah gys baase, as yn ayr e vac: as nee cloan girree seose noi  nyn ayr as nyn moir, as bee ad feanishyn baaish daue. 
41N||13||13||As ver yn ymmodee  feoh diu er coontey yn ennym aym's: agh bee eshyn nee tannaghtyn firrinagh gys y  jerrey er ny hauail. 
41N||13||14||Agh traa hee shiu eajeeid y traartys ta loayrit  jeh liorish Daniel y phadeyr, ny hassoo raad nagh lhisagh eh, (eshyn ta lhaih  lhig da tastey ghoaill) eisht lhig dauesyn t'ayns Judea chea gys ny sleityn.  
41N||13||15||As eshyn t'er mullagh y thie, ny lhig da cheet neose, ny goll stiagh,  dy ghoaill marish nhee erbee ass e hie. 
41N||13||16||As ny lhig dasyn t'ayns y  vagher chyndaa back, dy chur lesh e gharmad. 
41N||13||17||Agh smerg dauesyn ta  torragh, as dauesyn ta cur keeagh ayns ny laghyn shen. 
41N||13||18||As guee-jee nagh  bee shiu eginit dy roie er-chea 'sy gheurey. 
41N||13||19||Son bee seaghyn ayns ny  laghyn shen, lheid as nagh row er-dy hoshiaght y theihll ta Jee er chroo, gys yn  earish shen, as lheid, as nagh bee arragh dy bragh. 
41N||13||20||As mannagh beagh y  Chiarn dy leah er n'ghoaill ny laghyn shen giare, cha beagh dooinney bio er ny  hauail: agh er graih e chloan reiht t'eh er n'yannoo giare ny laghyn: 
41N||13||21||As eisht my jir dooinney erbee riu, Cur-my-ner, ta Creest ayns shoh, ny  cur-my-ner, t'eh ayns shid; ny credjee eh. 
41N||13||22||Son nee Creestyn foalsey, as  phadeyr yn foalsey girree, as cowraghyn as yindyssyn y hoilshaghey, dy volley,  my oddagh eh ve, yn eer chloan reiht. 
41N||13||23||Agh gow-jee tastey: cur-jee  my-ner, ta mish er n'insh diu dy chooilley nhee ro-laue. 
41N||13||24||Agh ayns ny  laghyn cheddin, lurg y seaghyn shen, aasee yn ghrian dorraghey, as cha der yn  eayst e soilshey: 
41N||13||25||As tuittee ny rollageyn veih niau, as bee pooaraghyn  yn aer er nyn graa. 
41N||13||26||As eisht hee ad Mac y dooinney cheet ayns ny  bodjallyn, lesh pooar as ard-ghloyr. 
41N||13||27||As eisht ver eh magh e ainleyn, as  nee eh e chloan reiht y haglym cooidjagh veih ny kiare geayghyn, veih ny ardjyn  sodjey magh jeh'n ooir, gys ny ardjyn sodjey magh jeh'n aer. 
41N||13||28||Nish  ynsee-jee coraa-dorraghey jeh'n billey-figgagh: Tra ta'n banglane echey foast  oor, as cur magh duillagyn, ta fys eu dy vel y sourey er-gerrey: 
41N||13||29||Myr  shen myrgeddin shiuish, tra hee shiu ny reddyn shoh cheet gy kione, toig-jee dy  vel eh er-gerrey, dy jarroo ec ny dorryssyn. 
41N||13||30||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra  riu, roish my vees yn cheeloghe shoh harrish, dy bee dy chooilley nhee jeu shoh  er nyn gooilleeney 
41N||13||31||Nee yn aer as yn ooir cherraghtyn: agh my ghoan's  cha jean cherraghtyn. 
41N||13||32||Agh jeh'n laa as yn oor shen, cha vel fys ec dooinney  erbee, ny ec ny ainleyn t'ayns niau, ny ec y Mac, agh yn Ayr. 
41N||13||33||Gow-jee  tastey, bee-jee er nyn dwoaie as gow-jee padjer: son cha nione diu cuin ta'n  traa. 
41N||13||34||Son ta'n Mac dooinney myr fer va goll er jurnah foddey, as daag e  hie, as hug currym er e vooinjer, as da dy chooilley ghooinney e obbyr hene, as  doardee eh da'n porter dy reayll arrey. 
41N||13||35||Bee-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen er  nyn arrey (son cha vel fys eu cuin hig mainshter y thie; ayns yn astyr, ny ec  mean-oie, ny ec gerrym y chellee, ny ayns y voghrey). 
41N||13||36||Er-aggle dy jig  eh doaltattym, as dy vow eh shiu nyn gadley. 
41N||13||37||As ny ta mee dy ghra  riuish, ta mee dy ghra rish ooilley, Bee-jee er nyn arrey.  
41N||14||1||Lurg daa laa va feailley ny Caisht as yn arran gyn  soorid: as va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scruderyn shegin er goaill eh dy follit, as  dy choyrt eh gy-baase. 
41N||14||2||Agh dooyrt ad, Cha nee er laa ny feailley,  er-aggle dy bee irree-magh ayn mastey'n pobble. 
41N||14||3||As myr v'eh ny hoie ec  bee, ayns Bethany, ayns thie Simon yn lourane, haink ben as box alabaster dy  ooil eck, jeh spikenard, feer chostal; as doshil ee yn box, as gheayrt ee eh er  y chione echey. 
41N||14||4||As va paart va mooaraghey shoh ayns nyn greeaghyn, gra,  Cre'n-fa va'n jummal shoh jeant er yn ooil? 
41N||14||5||Son oddagh eh v'er ny ve  creckit son ny smoo na three cheead ping, as shen baarit er ny boghtyn. As v'ad  jymmoosagh r'ee. 
41N||14||6||As dooyrt Yeesey, Faag-jee veue ee, cre'n eie t'eu  urree? t'ee er n'yannoo obbyr vie orrym's. 
41N||14||7||Son ta ny boghtyn eu kinjagh  meriu, as tra erbee dy nailliu, foddee shiu ve mie roo: agh mish cha vel eu dy  kinjagh. 
41N||14||8||T'ee er n'yannoo gys rere e pooar; t'ee er jeet ro-laue dy  ooillaghey my chorp cour my oanluckey.
41N||14||9||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cre  theihll yn raad bee yn sushtal shoh er ny phreacheil, dy bee shoh t'eesh er  n'yannoo, er ny imraa ayns cooinaghtyn jeeish. 
41N||14||10||As hie Yuaase Iscariot,  fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig, gys ny ard-saggyrtyn, dy vrah eh huc. 
41N||14||11||As tra  cheayll ad shoh, ghow ad boggey jeh, as ghiall ad argid da. As v'eh fieau er caa  dy vrah eh. 
41N||14||12||As er yn chied laa jeh'n arran caisht, tra v'ad marroo yn  Eayn-caisht, dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Cre'n raad sailt shin dy gholl, as dy  yannoo aarloo dhyts, dy ee yn Eayn 
41N||14||13||As hug eh magh jees jeh e ostyllyn,  as dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee gys yn ard-valley, as hig nyn guail dooinney cur  lesh saagh craie dy ushtey: eiyr-jee ersyn. 
41N||14||14||As raad erbee dy jed eh  stiagh, abbyr-jee rish y fer-thie, Ta'n Mainshter gra, Cre vel shamyr ny  goaldee, raad nee'm yn Eayn-caisht y ee marish my ostyllyn? 
41N||14||15||As jeeaghee  eh diu ard-shamyr mooar soit magh as jeant aarloo: ayns shen aarlee-jee er nyn  son.
41N||14||16||As jimmee ny ostyllyn rhymboo, as tra v'ad er jeet gys yn  ard-valley, hooar ad myr v'eh er ghra roo: as daarlee ad yn Eayn-caisht.  
41N||14||17||As ec yn astyr haink eh marish yn daa ostyl yeig. 
41N||14||18||As myr v'ad  nyn soie ec bee, dooyrt Yeesey, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy jean fer jiuish  ta gee marym mish y vrah. 
41N||14||19||As ren ad toshiaght dy ve trimshagh as dy  ghra rish, fer lurg fer, Nee mish eh? as dooyrt fer elley, Nee orrym's t'ou  cheet? 
41N||14||20||As dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh roo, She fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig  eh, ta cur e laue marym ayns y chlaare. 
41N||14||21||Ta Mac y dooinney dy jarroo  goll myr te scruit jeh: agh smerg da'n dooinney shen, liorish ta Mac y dooinney  er ny vrah; s'mie veagh eh er ve son y dooinney shen nagh beagh eh rieau er jeet  er y theihll. 
41N||14||22||As myr v'ad gee, ghow Yeesey arran, as vannee eh, as  vrish eh eh, as hug eh eh daue, gra, Gow-jee, ee-jee, shoh my chorp. 
41N||14||23||As  ghow eh yn cappan, as tra v'eh er chur booise, hug eh eh daue: as diu ad ooilley  jeh 
41N||14||24||As dooyrt eh roo, Shoh my uill's jeh'n conaant noa, t'er ny  gheayrtey son ymmodee. 
41N||14||25||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh n'iuym arragh  jeh mess y villey-feeyney, derrey'n laa iu-ym eh ass-y-noa ayns reeriaght Yee.  
41N||14||26||As tra v'ad er ghoaill arrane-moyllee, hie ad magh gys cronk ny  Oliveyn. 
41N||14||27||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Failee yn credjue euish ooilley noght  kyndagh rhym's: son t'eh scruit, Bwoaill-yms yn bochilley, as bee ny kirree er  nyn skeayley. 
41N||14||28||Agh erreish dou v'er n'irree reesht, hem reue gys  Galilee. 
41N||14||29||Agh dooyrt Peddyr rish, Ga dy vaill credjue dy chooilley  unnane, foast cha vaill my chredjue's. 
41N||14||30||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Dy  firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Yn laa jiu, eer yn oie noght roish my gerr y kellagh  daa cheayrt, dy nob uss mish three keayrtyn. 
41N||14||31||Agh loayr eshyn ny  s'jeeanney, Dy beign dy gholl gy-baase mayrt, cha nobbin oo er coontey erbee. As  er yn aght cheddin loayr ad ooilley. 
41N||14||32||As haink ad gys ynnyd va enmyssit  Gethsemane: as dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Soie-jee shiuish ayns shoh, choud as  hem's gys padjer. 
41N||14||33||As ghow eh marish Peddyr as Jamys as Ean, as ren eh  toshiaght dy ve mooar seaghnit as trome-chreeagh, 
41N||14||34||As dooyrt eh roo, Ta  my annym feer trimshagh eer gys y baase: fuirree-jee ayns shoh, as freill-jee  arrey. 
41N||14||35||As hie eh red beg er e hoshiaght, as huitt eh er y thalloo, as  ghow eh padjer, my oddys eh ve yn oor shen dy gholl shaghey. 
41N||14||36||As dooyrt  eh, Abba, Ayr, ta dy chooilley nhee ayns dty phooar, gow ersooyl yn cappan shoh  voym: ny-yeih cha nee my aigney's, agh dty aigney's dy row jeant. 
41N||14||37||As  haink eh as hooar eh ad nyn gadley as dooyrt eh rish Peddyr, Simon, vel uss dty  chadley? nagh voddagh oo arrey y reayll marym un oor? 
41N||14||38||Bee-jee er nyn  arrey, as gow-jee padjer nagh duitt shiu ayns miolagh: ta'n spyrryd eu dy jarroo  arryltagh, agh ta'n eill annoon.
41N||14||39||As hie eh roish reesht, as ghow eh  padjer, as loayr eh ny goan cheddin. 
41N||14||40||As tra haink eh reesht, hooar eh  ad nyn gadley reesht, (son va ny sooillyn oc trome) as cha row fys oc cre'n  ansoor dy chor da. 
41N||14||41||As haink eh yn trass cheayrt, as dooyrt eh roo,  Caddil-jee nish, as gow-jee nyn vea: s'liooar eh, ta'n oor er jeet; cur-my-ner  ta Mac y dooinney er ny vrah gys laueyn peccee. 
41N||14||42||Trog-jee erriu, lhig  dooin goll: cur-my-ner, ta eshyn er-gerrey dooin ta dy my vrah. 
41N||14||43||As  chelleeragh choud as v'eh foast loayrt, haink Yuaase, fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig,  as marish va sheshaght vooar lesh cliwenyn as luirg, veih ny ard-saggyrtyn, as  ny scrudeyryn, as y chanstyr. 
41N||14||44||As hug eshyn v'er vrah eh cowrey daue,  gra, Quoi-erbee ver-yms paag da, shen eh; gow-jee eh, as leeid-jee e ersooyl dy  sauchey. 
41N||14||45||As cha leah as v'eh er jeet, hie eh chelleeragh huggey, as  dooyrt eh, Vainshter, vainshter; as phaag eh eh. 
41N||14||46||As hug ad nyn laueyn  er, as ghow ad eh. 
41N||14||47||As hayrn fer jeusyn va nyn shassoo marish cliwe, as  woaill eh fer-mooinjerey yn ard-saggyrt, as ghiare eh e chleaysh jeh. 
41N||14||48||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiu er jeet magh myr noi marliagh,  lesh cliwenyn as luirg dy my ghoaill? 
41N||14||49||Va mee meriu gagh laa ayns y  chiamble, gynsaghey, as cha ghow shiu mee: agh shegin da ny scriptyryn v'er nyn  gooilleeney. 
41N||14||50||As ren ny ostyllyn ooilley treigeil eh as cosney roue.  
41N||14||51||As deiyr er dooinney aeg dy row, nagh row monney agh brilleen mysh e  chorp; as haare ny deiney aegey greme er. 
41N||14||52||As daag eh yn vrilleen, as  chossyn eh voue rooisht. 
41N||14||53||As hug ad lhieu Yeesey ersooyl gys yn  ard-saggyrt: as marishyn v'er nyn jaglym cooidjagh ooilley ny ard-saggyrtyn as y  chanstyr, as ny scrudeyryn. 
41N||14||54||As deiyr Peddyr er foddey ny yei, gys eer  plaase yn ard-saggyrt: as hoie eh marish yn vooinjer, as hiow eh eh-hene ec yn  aile. 
41N||14||55||As va ny ard saggyrtyn as ooilley'n choonceil shirrey feanishyn  noi Yeesey dy chur eh gy-baase; as cha dooar ad veg. 
41N||14||56||Son dymmyrk  ymmodee feanish foalsey n'oi, agh cha row yn eanish oc coardail ry-cheilley.  
41N||14||57||As dirree shiartanse, as dymmyrk ad feanish foalsey n'oi, gra, 
41N||14||58||Cheayll shin eh gra, Lhieg-yms y chiamble shoh ta jeant lesh laueyn, as cheu  sthie jeh three laa, trog-ym chiamble elley vees jeant fegooish laueyn. 
41N||14||59||Agh myr shen hene cha row yn eanish oc coardail ry-cheilley. 
41N||14||60||As hass yn  ard-saggyrt seose ayns mean y cheshaght, as denee eh jeh Yeesey gra, Nagh vel oo  cur ansoor erbee? cre ta ny feanishyn shoh dy lhiassaghey dt'oi? 
41N||14||61||Agh  v'eh ny-host, as cha dug eh ansoor erbee, Reesht denee yn ard-saggyrt jeh, as  dooyrt eh rish, Nee uss yn Creest, Mac yn Er-vannit? 
41N||14||62||As dooyrt Yeesey,  She shen mee: as hee shiuish Mac y dooinney ny hoie er laue yesh y phooar, as  cheet ayns bodjallyn yn aer. 
41N||14||63||Eisht raip yn ard-saggyrt e eaddagh, as  dooyrt eh, Cre'n feme t'ain er feanishyn erbee sodjey? 
41N||14||64||Ta shiu er  chlashtyn ny goan-mollaghtagh. cre ta shiu smooinaghtyn? As hug ad ooilley  briwnys er, dy row eh toilchin baase. 
41N||14||65||As ren paart toshiaght dy cheau  shellaghyn er, as dy choodaghey yn eddin echey, as dy woalley eh, as dy ghra  rish, Jean phadeyrys: as woaill ny sidooryn e lesh nyn massyn 
41N||14||66||As myr va  Peddyr heese ayns halley yn ard-saggyrt, haink unnane jeh ny sharvaantyn,  
41N||14||67||As tra honnick ee Peddyr dy hiow eh-hene, yeeagh ee er, as dooyrt ee,  As v'ou uss neesht marish Yeesey dy Nazareth. 
41N||14||68||Agh dob eh, gra, Cha vel  fys ny toiggal aym, cre t'ou dy ghra. As hie eh magh ayns y phorch; as gherr y  kellagh. 
41N||14||69||As honnick ben-aeg elley eh reesht, as ren ee toshiaght dy  ghra rish y cheshaght, T'eh shoh fer jeu. 
41N||14||70||As dob eh reesht. As tammylt  ny lurg shen, dooyrt paart jeh'n cheshaght reesht rish Peddyr, Son shickyrys  t'ou uss fer jeu: son she Galilean oo, as ta dty ghlare dy hoilshaghey eh.  
41N||14||71||Agh ren eh toshiaght dy ghweeaghyn as dy loo, gra, Cha nione dou yn  dooinney shoh mychione ta shiu loayrt. 
41N||14||72||As ren y kellagh gerrym yn nah  cheayrt. As chooinee Peddyr er ny goan va Yeesey er loayrt rish, Roish my gerr y  kellagh daa cheayrt, nee uss mish y obbal three keayrtyn. As tra smooinee eh er  shen, ren eh keayney. 
41N||15||1||As chelleeragh ayns y voghrey  hug ny ard-saggyrtyn, as y chanstyr, as ny scrudeyryn, as y slane coonceil, nyn  goyrle dy cheilley, as chiangle ad Yeesey, as leeid ad eh ersooyl, as livrey ad  eh gys Pilate. 
41N||15||2||As denee Pilate jeh, Nee uss ree ny Hewnyn? As dreggyr  eshyn as dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee ny t'ou uss dy ghra. 
41N||15||3||As ren ny  ard-saggyrtyn ymmodee reddyn y lhiassaghey n'oi, agh cha dreggyr eh gys nhee  erbee. 
41N||15||4||As denee Pilate jeh reesht, gra, Nagh vel oo cur ansoor erbee?  cur-my-ner cre whilleen red as t'ad shoh dy lhiassaghey dt'oi. 
41N||15||5||As cha  dug Yeesey ansoor erbee da myr shen dy ghow Pilate yindys. 
41N||15||6||Nish ec y  feailley shen ve (yn cliaghtey dy) eaysley daue un phryssoonagh ec yeearree yn  phobble. 
41N||15||7||As va fer va enmyssit Barabbas, va ny phryssoonagh maroosyn  v'er n'irree magh marish, as v'er n'yannoo dunverys ayns nyn irree-magh. 
41N||15||8||As dyllee yn pobble dy ard, as ren ad toshiaght dy ghuee er, Eh dy yannoo er nyn  son, myr v'eh rieau cliaghtey. 
41N||15||9||Agh dreggyr Pilate ad, gra, Nailliu mee  dy eaysley diu ree ny Hewnyn? 
41N||15||10||(Son va fys echey dy nee trooid goanlys  va ny ard-saggyrtyn er chur stiagh eh.) 
41N||15||11||Agh ghreinnee ny ard-saggyrtyn  y pobble, ad dy yeearree er my reih, eh dy eaysley daue Barabbas. 
41N||15||12||As  dreggyr Pilate, as dooyrt eh reesht roo, Cre bailliu mee eisht dy yannoo rishyn  ta shiu dy enmys ree ny Hewnyn? 
41N||15||13||As dyllee ad dy ard reesht, Jean y  chrossey eh. 
41N||15||14||Eisht dooyrt Pilate roo, Cre'n oyr, cre'n olk t'eh er  n'yannoo? as dyllee ad wheesh shen s'elgyssee, Jean y chrossey eh. 
41N||15||15||As  er shoh va Pilate booiagh nyn aigney y choyrt da'n pobble, as deayshil eh  Barabbas daue, agh livrey eh Yeesey, erreish da ve scuitchit, dy ve er ny  chrossey. 
41N||15||16||As hug ny sidooryn lhieu ersooyl eh gys yn halley va enmyssit  Pretorium; as deie ad er y slane sheshaght dy cheilley. 
41N||15||17||As hug ad er  coamrey gorrym-jiarg, as fee ad attey dy ghrineyn, as hug ad eh mysh y chione  echey. 
41N||15||18||As ren ad toshiaght dy oltaghey da, Dy vannee dhyt, Ree ny  Hewnyn. 
41N||15||19||As woaill ad eh er y chione lesh cuirtliagh, as cheau ad  shellaghyn er, as chroym ad nyn ghlioonyn kiongoyrt rish, as hug ad ooashley da.  
41N||15||20||As tra v'ad (myr shoh) er chraidey mysh, ghow ad yn coamrey purple jeh,  as hug ad e eaddagh hene er, as chur ad lhieu magh eh dy chrossey eh. 
41N||15||21||As d'eginee ad fer va enmyssit Simon Cyrenian va goll shaghey, cheet ass y  cheer, ayr Alexander as Rufus, dy ymmyrkey e chrosh. 
41N||15||22||As hug ad lhieu eh  gys yn ynnyd Golgotha, ta shen dy ghra 'sy ghlare ainyn, ynnyd bollag. 
41N||15||23||As hug ad da dy iu, feeyn as myrrh ny chione: agh cha ghow eh eh. 
41N||15||24||As  tra v'ad er chrossey eh, reynn ad e gharmadyn, tilgey lottyn orroo, son ayrn  dagh dooinney. 
41N||15||25||As ve yn trass oor tra ren ad y chrossey eh. 
41N||15||26||As  er-e-skyn va scruit oyr e vaaish, REE NY HEWNYN. 
41N||15||27||As marish ren ad daa  vaarliagh y chrossey; fer er e laue-yesh, as fer elley er e laue-chlare.  
41N||15||28||As shoh myr va'n scriptyr cooilleenit, ta dy ghra, As v'eh er ny earroo  marish ny drogh-yantee. 
41N||15||29||As loayr yn vooinjer va goll shaghey dy lunagh  n'oi, craa nyn ghing, as gra, Ah, uss ta lhieggal y chiamble, as dy hroggal eh  reesht ayns three laa, 
41N||15||30||Saue oo hene, as tar neose jeh'n chrosh.  
41N||15||31||Er yn aght cheddin neesht ren ny ard-saggyrtyn craidey mysh, gra ny  mast'oc hene marish ny scrudeyryn, Haue eh feallagh elley, agh eh-hene cha vod  eh sauail. 
41N||15||32||Lhig da Creest Ree Israel cheet neose nish jeh'n chrosh, dy  vod mayd fakin as credjal. As ren adsyn v'er nyn grossey marish, eh y oltooan,  
41N||15||33||As tra va'n cheyoo oor er jeet, va dorraghys harrish ooilley yn cheer,  gys yn nuyoo oor. 
41N||15||34||As ec yn nuyoo oor deie Yeesey lesh ard-choraa, gra,  ELOI, ELOI, LAMASABACH THANI? ta shen dy ghra 'sy ghlare ainyn, My Yee, My Yee,  cre'n-fa t'ou er my hreigeil 
41N||15||35||As dooyrt paart jeusyn va nyn shassoo ayns  shen, tra cheayll ad shoh, Cur-my-ner t'eh geamagh er Elias. 
41N||15||36||As roie  fer, as lhieen eh spunge lesh vinegar, as hug eh eh er cuirtliagh, as heeyn eh  huggey dy iu, gra, Faag-jee eh; hee mayd jig Elias dy ghoaill neose eh. 
41N||15||37||As deie Yeesey lesh ard-choraa, as ren eh paartail. 
41N||15||38||As va'n coodaghey  va eddyr y chiamble as yn ynnyd casherick raipit veih-my-cheilley, veih'n  vullagh gys y laare. 
41N||15||39||As tra honnick yn captan-keead va ny hassoo  kiongoyrt rish, dy row eh myr shen er n'eamagh, as er phaartail, dooyrt eh, Dy  firrinagh she Mac Yee va'n dooinney shoh. 
41N||15||40||Va myrgeddin ymmodee mraane  cur-my-ner veih foddey: nyn mast' oc va Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey moir Yamys  by-loo as Joses as Salome; 
41N||15||41||Va myrgeddin er n'eiyrt er, as v'ad  shirveishagh da choud's v'eh ayns Galilee as maroosyn ymmodee mraane elley v'er  jeet seose marish gys Jerusalem. 
41N||15||42||As nish tra va'n fastyr er jeet (er-yn  oyr dy nee traa yn aarlaghey ve, ta shen, yn laa roish yn doonaght.) 
41N||15||43||Haink Joseph dy Arimathea, fer coyrlee ooasle, va myrgeddin eh-hene farkiaght  son reeriaght Yee, as cha ghow eh aggle, agh hie eh stiagh dy dunnal gys Pilate,  as ren eh aghin son corp Yeesey. 
41N||15||44||As ghow Pilate yindys my v'eh hannah  marroo: as deie eh er y centurion huggey, as denee eh jeh, row eh er ve foddey  marroo? 
41N||15||45||As tra hooar eh fys er veih'n centurion, hug eh yn corp da  Joseph. 
41N||15||46||As chionnee eh aanrit-keyl as ghow eh neose eh, as hoill eh eh  ayns yn aanrit, ass doanluck eh eh ayns oaie va cleight ayns creg, as rowll eh  clagh er beeal yn oaie. 
41N||15||47||As honnick Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey moir  Voses, cre raad v'eh er ny oanluckey. 
41N||16||1||As tra va'n  doonaght ec kione, va Moirrey Malaine, as Moirrey moir Yamys as Salome, er  chionnaghey spisyn millish, dy voddagh ad cheet dy ooillaghey eh. 
41N||16||2||As  feer voghey ayns y vadran, er y chied laa jeh'n chaghtin, haink ad gys yn oaie  ec irree ny greiney. 
41N||16||3||As dooyrt ad nyn mast'oc hene. Quoi rowlys ersooyl  yn chlagh jeh beeal yn oaie? 
41N||16||4||(As tra v'ad er yeeaghyn, honnick ad y  chlagh rowlit ersooyl) son v'ee feer vooar. 
41N||16||5||As hie ad stiagh ayns yn  oaie, as honnick ad dooinney aeg ny hoie er y cheu yesh, coamrit ayns coamrey  liauyr gial: as v'ad agglagh. 
41N||16||6||As dooyrt eh roo, Ny bee aggle erriu: ta  shiu shirrey Yeesey dy Nazareth, v'er ny chrossey: t'eh er n'irree; cha vel eh  ayns shoh: cur-jee my-ner shoh'n boayl v'eh oanluckit ayn. 
41N||16||7||Agh immee-jee  reue, insh-jee da e ostyllyn as da Peddyr, dy vel eh goll reue gys Galilee:  shen-y-raad hee shiu eh, myr dooyrt eh riu.
41N||16||8||As hie ad magh ayns siyr, as  roie ad roue veih'n oaie, son v'ad er-creau as atchimagh: chamoo loayr ad veg  rish dooinney erbee; son v'ad agglit. 
41N||16||9||Nish tra va Yeesey er n'irree er  moghrey yn chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, hoilshee eh eh hene hoshiaght da Moirrey  Malaine, ass-jee v'eh er hilgey shiaght drogh-spyrrydyn.
41N||16||10||As hie ish as  dinsh ee yn naight dauesyn b'oallagh ve sheer marish, myr v'ad dobberan as  keayney. 
41N||16||11||As tra cheayll ad dy row eh bio, as dy row ish er vakin eh,  foast cha ren ad credjal. 
41N||16||12||Ny lurg shen hoilshee eh eh-hene ayns cummey  elley da jees jeu, myr v'ad shooyl er y raad, as goll er y cheer. 
41N||16||13||As  hie ad as dinsh ad eh da'n chooid elley jeh'n cheshaght: chamoo chred ad ad  shoh. 
41N||16||14||Ny lurg shen hoilshee eh eh-hene da'n un ostyl yeig, myr v'ad nyn  soie ec bee, as hooar eh foill daue son y vee-chredjue as y chreoghys cree oc,  er-yn-oyr nagh ren ad credjal adsyn v'er vakin eh, erreish da v'er n'irree.  
41N||16||15||As dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee magh trooid ooilley yn seihll, as jean-jee  yn sushtal y phreacheil da dy chooilley chretoor. 
41N||16||16||Bee eshyn ta credjal  as ta bashtit, er ny hauail; agh bee eshyn nagh jean credjal er ny gheyrey.  
41N||16||17||As eiyree ny cowraghyn shoh orroosyn ta credjal; Ayns my ennym's nee ad  drogh spyrrydyn y chastey, loayree ad lesh chengaghyn noa, 
41N||16||18||Nee ad  loaghtey ard-nieughyn, as my iu-ys ad nhee erbee pushoonagh, cha jean eh  skielley daue; ver ad nyn laueyn er sleih chingey, as nee ad coural. 
41N||16||19||Myr shen erreish da'n Chiarn v'er loayrt roo, v'eh er ny ghoaill seose gys niau,  as hoie eh er laue yesh Yee. 
41N||16||20||As hie ad magh, as ren ad preacheil dy  chooilley raad, yn Chiarn gobbraghey maroo; as jannoo yn goo breeoil liorish ny  mirrillyn va goll lesh. Amen. </BODY></HTML>
42N||1||1||Son wheesh as dy vel ymmodee er ghoaill ayns laue dy chur coontey cairagh jeh ny reddyn  ta dy firrinagh er nyn gredjal nyn mast'ain.  
42N||1||2||Eer myr hoilshee ad dooinyn ad, va er-dyn toshiaght nyn veanishyn sooilley as nyn  shirveishee jeh'n ghoo.  
42N||1||3||Ta mish myrgeddin er vakin eh mie, myr ta slane toiggal aym jeh dy chooilley nhee  er-dyn eer toshiaght, dy scrieu hoods ayns order, Theophilus smoo ooasle,  
42N||1||4||Dy vod tushtey share y ve ayd jeh firrinys ny reddyn shen, t'ou er ny ve ynsit ayndoo.   
42N||1||5||Rish lhing Heron ree Yudea, va saggyrt dy row enmyssit Zacharias, jeh coorse Abia;  as va'n ven echey jeh inneenyn Aaron, as yn ennym eck Elizabeth.  
42N||1||6||As v'ad ny-neesht cairagh kiongoyrt rish Jee, gimmeeaght ayns ooilley annaghyn as  oardaghyn y Chiarn gyn loght.  
42N||1||7||As cha row sluight oc, er-yn-oyr dy row Elizabeth gennish, as v'ad ny-neesht er  roie dy mie ayns eash.  
42N||1||8||As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'eh cooilleeney oik y taggyrt kiongoyrt rish Jee,  myr va e choorse er jeet magh,   
42N||1||9||Cordail rish cliaghtey oik y taggyrt, dy haghyr eh dy ve yn currym echey dy lostey  oural-millish, tra v'eh goll stiagh ayns chiamble y Chiarn. 
42N||1||10||As va'n slane chaglym jeh'n pobble cheu-mooie ec padjer rish traa yn oural-millish.   
42N||1||11||As haink ainle y Chiarn, as hass eh er cheu yesh altar yn oural-millish.  
42N||1||12||As tra honnick Zacharias eh, v'eh seaghnit, as huitt aggle er.  
42N||1||13||Agh dooyrt yn ainle rish, Ny gow aggle Zacharias: son ta dty phadjer er ny chlashtyn,  as nee yn ven ayd Elizabeth mac y ymmyrkey dhyt, as nee oo genmys eh Ean.  
42N||1||14||As bee boggey as gerjagh ayd, as nee ymmodee boggey y ghoaill tra hig eh er y theihll.
42N||1||15||Son bee eh ooasle ayns shilley yn Chiarn, as cha n'iu eh feeyn ny jough lajer,  as bee eh er ny lhieeney lesh y Spyrryd Noo, veih eer brein e vayrey.  
42N||1||16||As ymmodee jeh cloan Israel nee eh y hyndaa gys y Chiarn y Jee oc.  
42N||1||17||As hed eh roishyn ayns spyrryd as pooar Elias, dy hyndaa creeaghyn ny ayragh yn  gys y chloan, as ny mee-viallee gys creenaght yn vooinjer chairal, dy yannoo aarloo  pobble kiarit son y Chiarn.  
42N||1||18||As dooyrt Zacharias rish yn ainle, Cre liorish vees fys aym's er shoh  son ta mee  shenn, as ta'n ven er roie dy mie ayns eash.                
42N||1||19||As dreggyr yn aile as dooyrt e rish, Mish Gabriel ta shirveish fenish Yee: as ta  mee-er my choyrt dy loayrt rhyt, as dy hoilshaghey dhyt ny naightyn mie shoh.  
42N||1||20||As cur-my-ner bee oo balloo, as cha jig dty ghlare lhiat, derrey yn laa vees ny  reddyn shoh cooilleenit, er-y-fa nagh vel oo er chredjal my ghoan's vees er nyn gooilleeney  ayns nyn imbagh cooie.  
42N||1||21||As va'n pobble fieau son Zacharias, as yindys orroo dy row eh cumrail choud ayns  y chiamble.  
42N||1||22||As tra haink eh magh, cha voddagh eh loayrt roo; as hoig ad dy row eh er vakin  ashlish ayns y chiamble: son v'eh jannoo signyn daue, as hannee eh balloo.
42N||1||23||As shen myr ve, tra v'eh er chooilleeney laghyn e hirveish, dy jimmee eh gys e  hie hene.  
42N||1||24||As lurg ny laghyn shen ren e ven Elizabeth giennaghtyn, as dollee ee ee-hene queig  meeghyn, gra,  
42N||1||25||Shoh myr ta'n Chiarn er n'yannoo er my hon tra yeeagh eh orrym, dy ghoaill ersooyl  my oltooan mastey deiney.  
42N||1||26||As ayns y cheyoo vee, va'n ainle Gabriel er ny choyrt veih Jee, gys ard-valley  dy Ghalilee, va enmyssit Nazareth,  
42N||1||27||Gys moidyn nasht rish dooinney enmyssit Joseph, jeh thie Ghavid; as va ennym y  voidyn Moirrey.  
42N||1||28||As haink yn ainle stiagh as dooyrt eh r'ee, Dy vannee dhyt's ta ayns ard-foayr  ta'n Chiarn mayrt; bannit t'ou uss mastey mraane.  
42N||1||29||As tra honnick ee eh, v'ee seaghnit ec y raa echey, as smooinee ee r'ee hene cre'n  monney dy vannaghey va shoh.   
42N||1||30||As dooyrt yn ainle r'ee, Ny bee aggle ort, O Voirrey; son t'ou er gheddyn foayr  veih Jee.  
42N||1||31||As cur-my-ner, nee oo giennaghtyn, as mac y ymmyrkey, as enmyssee oo yn ennym echey  Yeesey.  
42N||1||32||Bee eshyn cronnal, as enmyssit Mac yn Er-syrjey; as ver y Chiarn Jee dasyn stoyl-reeoil  e ayr David.
42N||1||33||As nee eh reill harrish thie Yacob gys earishyn foddey beayn, as er e reeriaght  cha bee jerrey erbee.   
42N||1||34||Eisht dooyrt Moirrey rish yn ainle, Kys oddys shoh y ve, fakin nagh nione dou dooinney?    
42N||1||35||As dreggyr yn ainle as dooyrt eh r'ee, Hig yn Spyrryd Noo neose ort, as bee  pooar  yn Er-syrjey er ny skeayley harryd: shen-y-fa bee yn sluight chasherick shen ver  oo son y theihll, enmyssit Mac Yee.  
42N||1||36||As cur-my-ner, dty ven-vooinjerey Elizabeth, t'eeish myrgeddin er ghiennaght yn  mac ayns ny shenn laghyn eck: as shoh yn cheyoo vee jeeish va raait dy ve gennish.   
42N||1||37||Son da Jee cha bee nhee erbee neu-phossible.  
42N||1||38||As dooyrt Moirrey, Cur-my-ner sharvaant y Chiarn, dy jig eh lhiam cordail rish  dty ghoo. As jimmee yn ainle voee.   
42N||1||39||As mysh ny laghyn shen hrog Moirrey urree lesh siyr dy gholl gys cheer ny liargagh,  gys ard-valley dy Yudah,   
42N||1||40||As hie ee stiagh ayns thie Zacharias as vannee ee da Elizabeth.   
42N||1||41||As haink eh gy-kione, tra cheayll Elizabeth bannaghey Moirrey, dy lheim yn oikan  ayns e brein, as va Elizabeth lhieent lesh y Spyrryd Noo.   
42N||1||42||As loayr ee lesh ard-choraa as dooyrt ee, Bannit t'ou uss mastey mraane, as bannit  ta sluight dty vre&iuml;n.   
42N||1||43||As kys ta'n (ooashley) aym, dy vel moir my Hiarn er jeet dy my yeeaghyn?   
42N||1||44||Son cur-my-ner, cha leah as ren coraa dty vannaghey bingys ayns my chleayshyn,  lheim yn oikan ayns my vrein son boggey.   
42N||1||45||As bannit t'eeish ta er chredjal: son bee slane cooilleeney ny reddyn shen v'er  ny hoilshaghey jee liorish y Chiarn.   
42N||1||46||As dooyrt Moirrey, Ta m'annym cur ard-voylley da'n Chiarn.   
42N||1||47||As ta my spyrryd er ghoaill boggey ayns Jee my Haualtagh.   
42N||1||48||Son t'eh er chur tastey da stayd injil e harvaant: son cur-my-ner, maghey shoh  nee dy chooilley heeloghe mish y enmys bannit.   
42N||1||49||Son s'mooar ta'n Ooilley-niartal er n'yannoo er my hon, as s'casherick ta e ennym.    
42N||1||50||As ta e vyghin orroosyn ta goaill aggle roish, veih sheeloghe gys sheeloghe.    
42N||1||51||T'eh er hoilshaghey niart lesh e roih t'eh er skeayley ny moyrnee ayns mooaralys  nyn greeaghyn.   
42N||1||52||T'eh er lhieggal sheese ny treanee veih nyn stuill-reeoil, as er hoiaghey seose  ny imlee.   
42N||1||53||T'eh er lhieeney ny accryssee lesh reddyn mie, as ny berchee t'eh er chur follym  ersooyl.   
42N||1||54||T'eh er chooney lesh e harvaant Israel ayns cooinaghtyn jeh e vyghin.   
42N||1||55||(Myr loayr eh rish nyn shenn-ayryn, rish Abraham as e luight) er son dy bragh.    
42N||1||56||As duirree Moirrey m&acirc;ree mysh three meeghyn, as haink ee reesht gys e thie hene.    
42N||1||57||Nish va slane traa Elizabeth er jeet dy ve livreit, as hug ee mac son y theihll.    
42N||1||58||As cheayll ny naboonyn as y sleih mooinjerey eck, kys va'n Chiarn er hoilshaghey  ard-vyghin jee; as ghow ad boggey m&acirc;ree.   
42N||1||59||As haink eh gy-kione er yn hoghtoo laa dy daink ad dy ghiarey-chymmylt yn lhiannoo;  as denmys ad eh Zacharias, lurg ennym e ayrey.   
42N||1||60||As dreggyr e voir, as dooyrt ee, Cha nee; agh bee eh enmyssit Ean.   
42N||1||61||As dooyrt ad r'ee, Cha vel veg jeh dty chynney jeh'n ennym shen.   
42N||1||62||As ren ad signyn gys e ayr, cre'n ennym bailIishyn y ve er. 
42N||1||63||As hir eh boayrd-screeuee, as scrieu eh, gra, Ta'n ennym echey Ean. As ghow ad  ooilley yindys.   
42N||1||64||As er-y-chooyl va e veeal er ny osley, as e hengey er ny eaysley, as loayr eh,  as hug eh moylley da Jee.   
42N||1||65||As huitt aggle (arrymagh) er ooilley nyn naboonyn: as hie goo jeh ooilley ny reddyn  shoh magh trooid ooilley cheer sleitagh Yudea.   
42N||1||66||As adsyn ooilley cheayll shoh, hasht ad ayns nyn greeaghyn ad, gra, Cren monney  dy ghooinney vees eh shoh? as va laue yn Chiarn m&acirc;rish.   
42N||1||67||As va'n ayr echey Zacharias lhieent lesh y Spyrryd Noo, as ren eh phadeyrys, gra,    
42N||1||68||Bannit dy row yn Chiarn Jee Israel, son t'eh er yeeaghyn er, as er livrey e phobble,    
42N||1||69||As t'eh er hroggal seose saualtys niartal er nyn son, ayns thie e harvaant David;    
42N||1||70||Myr loayr eh liorish beeal e adeyryn crauee, t'er ny ve er-dy hoshiaght y theihll;    
42N||1||71||Dy hauail shin veih nyn noidyn, as veih'n lane ocsyn ooilley ta dwoaie oc orrin.    
42N||1||72||Dy chooilleeney yn vyghin va giallit da ny ayraghyn ain, as dy chooinaghtyn er  e chonaant casherick:   
42N||1||73||Eer yn breearrey ren eh gys yn ayr ain Abraham,   
42N||1||74||Dy giallagh eh dooinyn, dy beagh shin er nyn livrey veih laueyn nyn noidyn, as  shirveish eh fegooish aggle.   
42N||1||75||Ayns craueeaght as cairys kiongoyrt rish, ooilley laghyn nyn mea. 
42N||1||76||As bee uss lhiannoo enmyssit phadeyr yn Er-syrjey; son hed oo roish eddin y Chiarn,  dy yannoo aarloo e raaidyn;    
42N||1||77||Dy chur tushtey dy haualtys da e phobble, liorish leih nyn beccaghyn,   
42N||1||78||Trooid myghin meiygh yn Jee ain; liorish ta irree-ny-greiney veih yn yrjid er hoilshean  orrin   
42N||1||79||Dy chur soilshey dauesyn ta nyn soie ayns dorraghys as ayns scadoo yn vaaish, dy  leeideil ny cassyn ain ayns raad y chee.   
42N||1||80||As daase y lhiannoo, as v'eh er ny niartaghey 'sy spyrryd, as v'eh ayns ny faasaghyn,  derrey'n laa v'eh er ny hoilshaghey da Israel. 
42N||2||1||As haink eh gy-kione ayns ny laghyn shen, dy jagh sarey magh veih Cesar Augustus,  dy beagh coontey er ny ghoaill jeh'n slane rheam.  
42N||2||2||(As va'n recortys shoh jeant magh roish my va Cyremus ny chiannoort er Syria.)   
42N||2||3||As hie ad ooilley dy chur stiagh nyn enmyn, dagh unnane gys e ard-valley hene.   
42N||2||4||As hie Joseph myrgeddin seose veih Galilee, veih ard-valley Nazareth, gys Judea,  gys ard-valley Ghavid, ta enmyssit Bethlehem (son dy row eh jeh thie as kynney Ghavid.)    
42N||2||5||Dy chur stiagh e ennym hene as ennym Moirrey yn ven va nasht rish, va trome torragh.    
42N||2||6||As shen myr ve, choud as v'ad ayns shen, dy row yn traa er jeet jeeish dy ve livreit.    
42N||2||7||As hug ee son y theihll yn chied mac rug jee, as hoill ee eh ayns aanrityn so&iuml;llee,  as hug ee eh ny lhie ayns manjoor, er-y-fa nagh row room er nyn son ayns y thie-oast.    
42N||2||8||Nish v'ayns y cheer cheddin bochilley mooie er y vagher freayll arrey er nyn shioltaneyn  'syn oie.    
42N||2||9||As cur-my-ner haink ainle y Chiarn neose orroo, as ren gloyr y Chiarn soilshean  mygeayrt-y-moo; as v'ad fo aggle feer atchimagh.    
42N||2||10||As dooyrt yn ainle roo, Ny bee aggle erriu: son cur-my-ner, ta mish coyrt lhiam  hiu naightyn mie dy voggey mooar vees gys dy chooilley phobble.   
42N||2||11||Son diuish t'er ny ruggey jiu ayns ard valley Ghavid, Saualtagh, ta shen Creest  yn Chiarn.   
42N||2||12||As bee shoh son cowrey diu; Yiow shiu yn oikan ayns aanrityn soillee, as ny lhie  ayns manjoor.   
42N||2||13||As ayns y tullogh va marish yn ainle ymmodee jeh'n cheshaght flaunyssagh cur moylley  da Jee, as gra,   
42N||2||14||Gloyr dy row gys Jee ayns yn yrjid, as er y thalloo shee, aigney-mie gys deiney.    
42N||2||15||As haink eh gy-kione, cha leah as va ny ainleyn er n'gholl ersooyl voue gys niau,  dy dooyrt ny bochillyn yn derrey yeh rish y jeh elley, Lhig dooin goll nish derrey  Bethlehem, dy akin yn red shoh t'er jeet gy-kione, ta'n Chiarn er hoilshaghey dooin.    
42N||2||16||As haink ad lesh siyr, as hooar ad Moirrey as Joseph, as yn oikan ny lhie ayns  manjoor.   
42N||2||17||As tra honnick ad eh, hoilshee ad magh yn raa va er ny insh daue mychione y lhiannoo  shoh.   
42N||2||18||As ghow dy chooilley unnane cheayll eh, yindys jeh ny reddyn va inshit daue liorish  ny bochillyn.   
42N||2||19||Agh hasht Moirrey ooilley ny raaghyn shoh (ayns e haigney) as smooinee ee orroo  dy dowin ayns e cree.   
42N||2||20||As haink ny bochillyn roue, cur gloyr as moylley da Jee son dy chooilley nhee v'ad  er chlashtyn as er vakin, myr ve inshit daue.   
42N||2||21||As tra va hoght laa ec kione son giarey-chymmylt y lhiannoo, v'eh enmyssit YEESEY,  son shen yn ennym hug yn ainle er, roish my row eh er ny ghiennaghtyn 'sy vrein.     
42N||2||22||As tra va laghyn nyn ghlenney, cordail rish leigh Voses, er jeet, hug ad lhieu  eh gys Jerusalem, dy hebbal eh gys y Chiarn,   
42N||2||23||(Myr te scruit ayns leih yn Chiarn, Bee dy chooilley chied-ruggit yrrynagh er ny  chasherickey gys y Chiarn.)   
42N||2||24||As dy hebbal yn oural t'er ny harey ayns leigh yn Chiarn, Piyr dy chalmaneyn turtle,  ny daa chalmane aegey.   
42N||2||25||As cur-my-ner va dooinney ayns Jerusalem va enmyssit Simeon; as va'n dooinney cheddin  cairagh as crauee, farkiaght son gerjagh Israel: as va'n Spyrryd Noo ersyn.   
42N||2||26||As ve er ny hoilshaghey da liorish y Spyrryd Noo, nagh noghe eh baase, roish da  v'er vakin Creest yn Chiarn.   
42N||2||27||As haink eh liorish y Spyrryd stiagh ayns y chiamble: as tra va'n ayr as y voir  er chur lhieu yn lhiannoo Yeesey stiagh, dy yannoo er e hon, lurg cliaghtey yn leigh;    
42N||2||28||Eisht ghow eh seose eh ayns e roihaghyn, as hug eh moylley da Jee, as dooyrt eh,    
42N||2||29||Hiarn nish t'ou cur kied da dty harvaant paartail ayns she, cordail rish dty ghoo.    
42N||2||30||Son ta my hooillyn er vakin dty haualtys;   
42N||2||31||T'ou er chiarail dy ve er ny hoilshaghey fenish dy chooilley phobble;   
42N||2||32||Soilshey dy hoilshean er ny Ashoonee as gloyr dty phobble Israel.   
42N||2||33||As ghow Joseph as e voir yindys jeh ny reddyn va loayrit my-e-chione,   
42N||2||34||As vannee Simeon ad, as dooyrt eh rish Moirrey e voir, Cur-my-ner ta'n lhiannoo  shoh soit dy chur sheese as dy hoiaghey seose ymmodee ayns Israel; as son cowrey  dy oltooan.   
42N||2||35||(As dy jarroo hed cliwe trooid dty annym hene neesht) dy vod smooinaghtyn ymmodee  creeaghyn v'er ny chronnaghey.   
42N||2||36||As va myrgeddin phadeyrben enmyssit Anna, inneen Phanuel, jeh kynney Aser: v'ee  dy eash vooar, as v'ee er veaghey marish e sheshey shiaght bleeaney neayr as v'ee  ny moidyn.   
42N||2||37||As v'ee ny ben-treoghe mysh kiare feed as kiare bleeaney dy eash, as v'ee dy kinjagh  taaghey yn chiamble, shirveish Jee lesh trostey as padjeryn oie as laa.   
42N||2||38||As haink ish stiagh ec y traa cheddin, as hug ee booise myrgeddin da'n Chiarn,  as loayr ee jeh roosyn ooilley va jeeaghyn son livrey-ys ayns Jerusalem.   
42N||2||39||As tra v'ad er chooilleeney dy chooilley nhee cordail rish leigh yn Chiarn, haink  ad reesht gys Galilee, gys yn ard-valley oc hene Nazareth.   
42N||2||40||As daase y lhiannoo, as v'eh er ny niartaghey 'sy spyrryd, as lhieent lesh creenaght,  as va grayse Yee m&acirc;rish.   
42N||2||41||Nish va e ayr as e voir goll seose gys Jerusalem dy chooilley vlein ec feailley  ny caisht.   
42N||2||42||As tra v'eh daa vlein jeig dy eash, hie ad seose gys Jerusalem lurg cliaghtey ny  feailley. 
42N||2||43||As tra va ny laghyn harrish, as ad goll thie reesht, duirree yn lhiannoo Yeesey  nyn yei ayns Jerusalem, gyn-yss da Joseph as e voir.  
42N||2||44||Agh smooinaghtgn dy row eh ayns y cheshaght, hie ad jurnah laa; as v'ad briaght  er e hon mastey nyn gheiney mooinjerey as nyn ainjys.
42N||2||45||As tra nagh dooar ad eh, hie ad reesht gys Jerusalem shirrey er e hon.  
42N||2||46||As haink eh gy-kione, lurg three laa dy dooar ad eh ayns y chiamble, ny hoie mastey  ny fir-ynsee, chammah geaishtagh roo, as cur feyshtyn orroo.  
42N||2||47||As ghow ooilley ny va geaishtagh rish yindys jeh'n toiggal as jeh ny ansooryn echey.   
42N||2||48||As tra honnick ad eh, v'ad fo mooarane atchim; as dooyrt e voir rish, Vac, cre'n-fa  t'ou er n'yannoo myr shoh rooin? cur-my-ner, ta dty ayr as mish er ve briaght dy  trimshagh er dty hon.  
42N||2||49||As dooyrt eh roo, Kys dy row shiu briaght er my hon's? nagh row fys eu dy beign  dou ve mysh obbyr my Ayrey ?  
42N||2||50||As cha row toiggyl oc jeh'n raa loayr eh roo.  
42N||2||51||As hie eh sheese m&acirc;roo, as haink eh gys Nazareth, as v'eh biallagh daue: as hasht  e voir ooilley ny raaghyn shoh ayns e cree.  
42N||2||52||As ren Yeesey bishaghey ayns creenaght as aase, as ayns foayr rish Jee as dooinney.  
42N||3||1||NISH ayns y wheiggoo vlein jeig jeh reill, Tiberius Cesar, tra va Pontius Pilate ny  chiannoort er Judea, as Herod ny hetrarch er Galilee, as e vraar Philip reill ayns  Iturea as cheer Trachonitis, as Lysanias reill ayns Abilene.  
42N||3||2||Tra va Annas as Caiaphas nyn ard-saggyrtyn, haink goo Yee gys Ean mac Zacharias  ayns yn aasagh.  
42N||3||3||As haink eh gys ooilley yn cheer my geayrt Jordan, preacheil bashtey arrys son leih  peccaghyn.  
42N||3||4||Myr te scruit ayns lioar goan Esaias yn phadeyr, gra, Coraa fer geamagh ayns yn  aasagh, Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, jean-jee ny cassanyn echey jeeragh.  
42N||3||5||Bee dy chooilley choan er ny lhieeney as dy chooilley slieau as cronk er nyn injillaghey,  as ny ynnydyn cammey er nyn yannoo jeeragh, as ny raaidyn garroo er nyn yannoo rea.   
42N||3||6||As hee dy chooilley eill saualtys Yee.  
42N||3||7||Eisht dooyrt eh rish y pobble v'er jeet magh huggey dy ve er nyn mashtey, O shiuish  heeloghe dy ard-nieughyn, quoi t'er chur raaue diu dy hea veih yn jymmoose ta ry-heet?
42N||3||8||Cur-jee magh nish er-y-fa shen messyn cooie dy arrys, as ny jean-jee toshiaght  dy ghra riu hene, Ta Abraham ain son nyn ayr: son ta mee gra riu, dy vel pooar ec  Jee eer jeh ny claghyn shoh cloan y hroggal seose da Abraham. 
42N||3||9||As nish hannah ta'n teigh er ny choyrt gys fraue ny biljyn: shen-y-fa ta dy chooilley  villey nagh vel gymmyrkey mess mie, dy ve giarit sheese as tilgit ayns yn aile.
42N||3||10||As denee yn pobble jeh, gra, Cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo?
42N||3||11||Dreggyr eh as dooyrt eh roo, Eshyn ta daa chooat echey, lhig da y choyrt dasyn  nagh vel cooat eddyr echey  as eshyn ta beaghey echey, lhig da jannoo er yn aght  cheddin.
42N||3||12||Eisht haink myrgeddin ny publicanee dy ve er nyn mashtey, as dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter,  cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo?
42N||3||13||As dooyrt eh roo, Ny trog-jee ny smoo na ta er nyn gurrym.
42N||3||14||As d&ecirc;nee ny sidooryn myrgeddin, jeh, gra, As cre ta orrinyn dy yannoo? As dooyrt  eh roo, Ny jean-jee tranlaase er dooinney erbee, ny jean-jee cassid vreagagh er dooinney  erbee, as bee-jee booiagh lesh nyn vaill.
42N||3||15||As myr va'n pobble ayns imnea, as dy chooilley ghooinney smooinaghtyn ayns nyn  greeaghyn mychione Ean, nee eh va'n Creest mannagh nee;
42N||3||16||Dreggyr Ean as dooyrt eh roo ooilley, Ta mish dy jarroo bashtey shiu lesh ushtey;  agh ta fer s'pooaral na mish cheet kiangley ny braagyn echey cha vel mee feeu dy  eaysley: nee eshyn shiu y vashtey lesh y Spyrryd Noo, as lesh aile.
42N||3||17||Ta'n cleayst echey ayns e laue, as fasnee eh dy bollagh e laare-vooie, as gowee  eh yn churnaght stiagh ayns e hie tashtee; agh yn coau nee eh y lostey lesh aile  nagh bee er ny vooghey.
42N||3||18||As ymmodee dy reddyn elley ren eh y choyrlaghey as y phreacheil gys y pobble.
42N||3||19||Agh tra v'eh er choyrt oghsan da Herod yn Tetrarch kyndagh rish Herodias ben e  vraar Philip, as ooilley ny huilk va Herod er n'yannoo,
42N||3||20||Ren eh shoh marish y chooid elley, dy dug eh Ean ayns pryssoon.
42N||3||21||Nish tra va ooilley'n pobble er nyn mashtey, haink eh gy-kione dy row Yeesey myrgeddin  er ny vashtey, as ghow eh padjer, as va niau er ny osley; 
42N||3||22||As haink y Spyrryd Noo neose er, myr ayns cummey dooghyssagh calmane, as haink  coraa veih niau, gra, Oo my vac ennoil, jeed ta mee dy mooar soiaghey.
42N||3||23||As ghow Yeesey eh-hene toshiaght dy ve mysh jeih bleeaney as feed dy eash, as (goit  dy ve) mac Yoseph, mac Heli,
42N||3||24||Mac Matthat, mac Leyi, mac Melchi, mac Janna, mac Joseph,
42N||3||25||Mac Mattathias, mac Amos,mac Naum, mac Esli, mac Nagge,
42N||3||26||Mac Maath, mac Mattathias, mac Semei, mac Joseph, mac Juda,
42N||3||27||Mac Joanna, mac Rhesa, mac Zorobabel, mac Salathiel, mac Neri,
42N||3||28||Mac Melchi, mac Addi, mac Cosam, mac Elmodam, mac Er,
42N||3||29||Mac Jose, mac Eliezer, mac Jorim, mac Matthat, mac Levi,
42N||3||30||Mac Simeon, mac Juda, mac Joseph, mac Jonan, mac Eliakim,  
42N||3||31||Mac Melea, mac Menan, mac Mattatha, mac Nathan, mac David,   
42N||3||32||Mac Jesse, mac Obed, mac Booz, mac Salmon, mac Naasson,  
42N||3||33||Mac Aminadab, mac Aram, mac Esrom, mac Phares, mac Juda   
42N||3||34||Mac Jacob, mac Isaac, mac Abraham, mac Thara, mac Nachor,  
42N||3||35||Mac Saruch, mac Ragan, mac Phalec, mac Heber, mac Sala.  
42N||3||36||Mac Cainan, mac Arphaxad, mac Sem, mac Noe, mac Lamech,  
42N||3||37||Mac Mathusala. mac Enoch, mac Ja red, mac Maleleel, mac Cainan,  
42N||3||38||Mac Enos, mac Seth, mac Adam, mac Yee. 
42N||4||1||As va Yeesey lane jeh'n Spyrryd Noo, as hyndaa eh veih Jordan, as v'eh er ny leeideil  liorish y Spyrryd gys yn aasagh,  
42N||4||2||As v'eh da-eed laa er ny violaghey liorish y drogh-spyrryd, as ayns ny laghyn shen  cha d'ee eh veg; as tra v'ad harrish, v'eh ny lurg shen accryssagh.  
42N||4||3||As dooyrt y drogh-spyrryd rish, My she Mac Yee oo, abbyr rish yn chlagh shoh dy  ve jeant ny arran.  
42N||4||4||As dreggyr Yeesey eh, gra, Te scruit, Nagh nee er arran ny-lomarcan nee dooinney  beaghey, agh liorish ooilley goan Yee.  
42N||4||5||As hug y drogh-spyrryd lesh seose eh gys mullagh slieau ard, as ayns y tullogh hug  eh shilley da jeh ooilley reeriaghtyn y theihll.  
42N||4||6||As dooyrt y drogh-spyrryd rish, Ooilley yn phooar shoh ver-ym dhyt's, as y ghloyr  oc; son ta shen er ny livrey dou, as da quoi-erbee saillym, ta mee dy choyrt eh.   
42N||4||7||My ver oo er-y-fa shen ooashley dou bee ooilley lhiat hene.  
42N||4||8||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Ass my enish oo, Noid-ny-hanmey: son te scruit,  Ver oo ooashley da'n Chiarn dty Yee, as eshyn ynrycan nee oo y hirveish.   
42N||4||9||As hug eh lesh eh gys Jerusalem, as hoie eh eh er beinn toor syrjey yn chiamble,  as dooyrt eh rish, My she Mac Yee oo, tilg oo hene sheese veih shoh.  
42N||4||10||Son te scruit, Ver eh currym da e ainleyn harryd, dy dty reayll:  
42N||4||11||As ayns nyn laueyn nee ad oo y ymmyrkey, er-aggle ec traa erbee dy bwoaill oo dty  chass noi clagh.  
42N||4||12||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Te er ny ghra, Cha jean oo daanys er y Chiarn  dty Yee.  
42N||4||13||As erreish da'n drogh-spyrryd v'er n'yannoo jerrey er ooilley yn violagh, daag  eh eh son earish.  
42N||4||14||As haink Yeesey reesht ayns pooar y spyrryd gys Galilee: as hie goo magh jeh  trooid ooilley yn cheer mygeayrt. 
42N||4||15||As dynsee eh ayns ny kialteenyn oc, as v'eh ayns ard-voylley rish y theay.  
42N||4||16||As haink eh gys Nazareth, raad v'eh er ny ve troggit: as hie eh, myr v'eh cliaghtey,  stiagh ayns y synagogue er laa yn doonaght, as hass eh seose dy lhaih.  
42N||4||17||As va lioar y phadeyr Esaias er ny livrey da, as tra v'eh er vosley yn lioar, hooar  eh yn ynnyd raad v'eh scruit,  
42N||4||18||Ta spyrryd y Chiarn orrym's, er-y-fa dy vel eh er my ooillaghey dy phreacheil y  sushtal gys ny boghtyn, t'eh er my choyrt dy laanaghey yn vooinjer hrome-chreeagh,  dy phreacheil livrey-ys gys ny cappeeyn, dy chur soilshey da ny doail, as reamys  dauesyn ta broojit, 
42N||4||19||Dy phreacheil blein eunyssagh y Chiarn.  
42N||4||20||As yeigh eh yn lioar, as hug eh ee reesht da'n chirveishagh, as hoie eh sheese:  as va sooillyn dy chooilley unnane v'ayns y synagogue dy jeean soit er.  
42N||4||21||As ren eh toshiaght dy ghra roo, Jiu ta'n scriptyr shoh cooilleenit ayns y chlashtyn  euish.  
42N||4||22||As dymmyrk ad ooilley feanish lesh, as ghow ad yindys jeh ny goan graysoil haink  ass y veeal echey. As dooyrt ad, Nagh nee shoh mac Yoseph?   
42N||4||23||As dooyrt eh roo, Jir shiu ayns shickyrys yn chenn raa shoh rhym, Er-lhee, jean  oo hene y lheihys: cre-erbee ta shin er chlashtyn va jeant ayns Capernaum, jean myrgeddin  ayns shoh ayns dty heer hene.  
42N||4||24||As dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh vel soiagh jeant jeh phadeyr erbee  ayns e heer hene.  
42N||4||25||Agh ta mee ginsh diu ayns firrinys, dy row ymmodee mraane treoghe ayns Israel rish  hing Elias, tra va'n aer jeight seose three bleeaney as shey meeghyn, tra va genney  vooar trooid ooilley yn cheer:  
42N||4||26||Agh gys unnane oc cha row Elias er ny choyrt, cheu mooie jeh gys Sarepta ard-valley  dy Sidon, gys ben-treoghe v'ayns shen.  
42N||4||27||As va ymmodee louranee ayns Israel rish traa Eliseus yn phadeyr, as cha row fer  jeu er ny ghlenney, cheu-mooie jeh Naaman yn Syrian.  
42N||4||28||As va ooilley ny v'ayns y synagogue tra cheayll ad ny goan shoh, lhieent lesh jymmoose,   
42N||4||29||As dirree ad, as deiyr ad eh magh ass yn ard-valley, as hug ad lhieu eh gys broogh  yn chronk (er va'n ard-valley oc troggit) ry-hoi tilgey sheese eh gour e vullee.   
42N||4||30||Agh hie eh magh trooid mean y cheshaght, as jimmee eh roish:  
42N||4||31||As haink eh neose gys Capernaum, ard-valley dy Ghalilee, as dynsee eh ad er laghyn  y doonaght.  
42N||4||32||As ghow ad yindys mooar jeh'n ynsaghey echey: son va e ghoo lesh pooar.  
42N||4||33||As ayns y synagogue va dooinney seaghnit lesh spyrryd neu-ghlen, as dyllee eh  lesh ard-choraa. 
42N||4||34||Gra, Faag shin; cre'n eie t'ayd orrin uss Yeesey dy Nazareth? vel oo er jeet dy  nyn stroie? ta fys aym quoi oo hene; Fer-casherick Yee.  
42N||4||35||As hug Yeesey oghsan da, gra Bee dty-host, as tar magh ass. As tra va'n drogh spyrryd  er hilgey neeal eh, haink eh magh ass, gyn assee da.  
42N||4||36||As v'ad ooilley fo atchim, as loayr ad ny mast' oc hene, gra, Cre'n fockle (vreeoil)  shoh? son lesh pooar as niart t'eh cur ny spyrrydyn neu ghlen fo harey, as t'ad cheet  magh.  
42N||4||37||As hie goo magh jeh trooid dy chooilley ard jeh'n cheer mygeayrt.  
42N||4||38||As hrog eh magh ass y synagogoe, as hie eh stiagh ayns thie Simon: as va moir  ben Simon feer ching ayns y chiassaghey; as ren ad aghin huggey er e son.  
42N||4||39||As hass eh er-e-skyn, as hug eh oghsan da'n chiassaghey, as daag eh ee. As chelleeragh  dirree ee seose, as ren ee shirveish orroo.  
42N||4||40||Nish ec lhie ny greiney, whilleen as va sleih chingey oc fo mooarane doghanyn  hug ad lhieu ad huggey; as hug eh e laueyn er dy chooilley unnane oc, as ren eh ad  y lheihys.  
42N||4||41||As haink drogh-spyrrydyn myrgeddin magh ass ymmodee, gyllagh as gra, Oo yn Creest  Mac Yee. As hug eh oghsan daue, as cha lhig eh daue loayrt; son va fys oc dy nee  eh va'n Creest.  
42N||4||42||As 'sy vadran, jimmee eh roish, as hie eh gys boayl er-lheh: as va'n pobble briaght  er e hon, as cheet huggey, as chionney er, eh dy uirriaght m&acirc;roo.            
42N||4||43||As dooyrt eh roo, Shegin dooys reeriaght Yee y phreacheil gys ard-valjyn elley  myrgeddin: son er yn oyr shen ta mee er my choyrt.  
42N||4||44||As ren eh preacheil ayns kialteenyn Ghalilee. 
42N||5||1||As haink eh gy-kione myr va'n pobble chionney stiagh er dy chlashtyn goo Yee, as eh  ny hassoo liorish faarkey Ghennesareth,  
42N||5||2||As honnick eh daa lhong rish oirr y traie: agh va ny eeasteyryn er n'gholl assdoo,  as v'ad niee yn lieen.  
42N||5||3||As hie eh er-board unnane jeh ny lhongyn va lesh Simon, as ghuee eh er, eh dy heiy  magh tammylt veih yn thalloo: as hoie eh sheese, as dynsee eh yn pobble ass y lhong.   
42N||5||4||Nish tra v'eh erreish loayrt, dooyrt eh rish Simon, Ymmyrt-jee magh gys y diunid,  as cuir-jee yn lieen son tayrn.  
42N||5||5||As dreggyr Simon as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, ta shin er hooilleil fud ny hoie,  as cha vel shin er ghoaill monney: ny-yeih er dty ockle's cuir-yms yn lieen.
42N||5||6||As tra v'ad er n'yannoo shoh chruinnee ad dy cheilley lheid yn earroo mooar dy eeastyn;  dy row yn lieen oc brishey.  
42N||5||7||As chrie ad er ny parteeassyn oc v'ayns y lhong elley, ad dy heet dy chooney lhieu.  As haink ad, as lhieen ad y daa lhong, myr shen dy row ad ayns gaue goll fo.  
42N||5||8||Tra honnick Simon Peddyr shoh, huitt eh sheese ec glioonyn Yeesey, gra, Immee voym,  son ta mee my ghooinney peccoil, O Hiarn.   
42N||5||9||Son ghow eshyn, as ooilley ny va m&acirc;rish, yindys mooar jeh'n lught dy eeastyn v'ad  er ghoaill:   
42N||5||10||Myr ren neesht Jamys as Ean mec Zebedee, va nyn barteeassyn marish Simon. As dooyrt  Yeesey rish Simon, Ny bee aggle ort, veih shoh magh nee oo goaill deiney.
42N||5||11||As tra v'ad er chur lhieu nyn lhongyn gys thalloo, hreig ad ooilley, as deiyr ad  er. 
42N||5||12||As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh ayns ard-valley dy row, cur-my-ner, dooinney lane  jeh'n louraneys: as tra honnick eh Yeesey, huitt eh sheese er e eddin, jannoo aghin  huggey as gra, Hiarn, my she dty aigney eh, foddee oo mish y yannoo glen.   
42N||5||13||As heeyn eh magh e laue, as venn eh rish, gra, M'aigney's eh; bee er dty ghlenney.  As chelleeragh daag y louraneys eh.   
42N||5||14||As hug eh currym er gyn eh dy insh shoh da dooinney erbee: agh immee, as jeeagh  oo hene da'n taggyrt, as cheb son dty ghlenney, myr ta Moses er harey, dy ve son  feanish daue.   
42N||5||15||Agh wheesh shen smoo hie goo magh jeh: as haink earrooyn mooarey dy leih cooidjagh  dy chlashtyn, as dy ve er nyn lheihys liorish jeh nyn aslayntyn.   
42N||5||16||Agh hie eshyn eh-hene roish gys yn aasagh, dy ghoaill padjer.   
42N||5||17||As haink eh gy-kione laa dy row, myr v'eh gynsaghey, dy row Phariseeyn as fir-ynsee  yn leigh nyn soie liorish, v'er jeet magh ass ooilley baljyn Ghalilee, as Judea as  Jerusalem: as va pooar y Chiarn feer vreeoil m&acirc;rish ayns lheihys doghanyn.   
42N||5||18||As cur-my-ner, hug sleih lhieu ayns lhiabbee dooinney va ching jeh'n palsee:  as v'ad shirrey y chur lhieu stiagh eh, dy hoiaghey eh kiongoyrt rish   
42N||5||19||As tra nagh row saase erbee oc dy chur lhieu stiagh eh kyndagh rish chennid y phobble,  hie ad seose er mullagh y thie, as lhig ad sheese ny hrooid, eh-hene as e lhaibbee,  er y laare kiongoyrt rish Yeesey.   
42N||5||20||As tra hug eh tastey da'n chredjue oc, dooyrt eh rish, Ghooinney, ta dty pheccaghyn  er nyn leih dhyt.   
42N||5||21||As ren ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn toshiaght dy phleadeil ry-cheilley, gra,  Quoi eh shoh ta loayrt goan mollaghtagh? Quoi oddys peccaghyn y leih, agh Jee ny  lomarcan?
42N||5||22||Agh va fys ec Yeesey er ny smooinaghtyn oc, as dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre  er ta shiu resooney ayns nyn greeaghyn?
42N||5||23||Quoi sassey dy ghra, Ta dty pheccagh yn er nyn leih dhyt, ny dy ghra, Irree seose  as shooill?   
42N||5||24||Agh dy vod fys y ve eu, dy vel pooar ec Mac y dooinney er y thalloo dy leih peccaghyn  (dooyrt eh rishyn va ching jeh'n chingys craa-ee.) Ta mee gra rhtt, Irree, as trog  seose dty lhiabbee, as gow royd gys dty hie.    
42N||5||25||As chelleeragh dirree eh seose kiongoyrt roo, as hrog eh shen v'eh ny lhie er,  as jimmee eh gys e hie, cur moylley da Jee.   
42N||5||26||As ghow ad ooilley lane yindys, as ren ad Jee y ghloyraghey, as v'ad lhieent lesh  aggle, gra, Ta shin er vakin reddyn yindyssagh jiu.   
42N||5||27||As ny lurg shoh hie eh magh, as honnick eh publican va enmyssit Levi, ny hoie ec  boayrd y cheesh: as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym's.   
42N||5||28||As daag eh ooilley as dirree eh seose, as deiyr eh er.   
42N||5||29||As ren Levi aarlaghey mooar er e hon ayns e hie hene: as va sheshaght vooar dy  phublicanee as dy eallagh elley nyn soie ec y voayrd m&acirc;roo.   
42N||5||30||Agh va ny scrudeyryn oc as ny Phariseeyn jymmoosagh rish e ynseydee, gra, Cre'n-fa  ta shiu gee as giu marish publicanee as peccee?   
42N||5||31||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel feme ocsyn ta slane er yn er-lhee:  agh ec sleih chingey.   
42N||5||32||Cha daink mish dy eamagh er yn vooinjer chairagh, agh er peccee gys arrys.   
42N||5||33||As dooyrt ad roo, Cre'n-fa ta ynseydee Ean trostey dy mennick, as jannoo padjeryn,  as myrgeddin ynseydee ny Phariseeyn; agh ta'n vooinjer ayd's gee as giu?   
42N||5||34||As dooyrt eh roo, Bailliu mooinjer y chamyr-phoosee dy hrostey, choud as ta dooinney  yn phoosee m&acirc;roo?   
42N||5||35||Agh hig ny laghyn, tra vees dooinney yn phoosee er ny ghoaill ersooyl voue, as  eisht nee ad trostey ayns ny laghyn shen.   
42N||5||36||As loayr eh myrgeddin coraa-dorraghey roo, Cha vel dooinney erbee cur peesh dy  eaddagh noa er shenn gharmad: er-nonney, ta chammah yn noa raipey yn laane lesh,  as cha vel yn pheesh va goit ass yn noa coardail rish y chenn   
42N||5||37||As cha vel dooinney erbee cur feeyn noa ayns shenn voteilyn er-nonney scoltee yn  feeyn noa ny boteilyn, as bee eh deayrit, as bee ny boteilyn dy choayl er.   
42N||5||38||Agh shegin da feeyn noa v'er ny chur ayns boteilyn noa; as t'ad ny-neesht sauchey.    
42N||5||39||Chamoo ta dooinney erbee, erreish da v'er n'iu shenn feeyn, chelleeragh shirrey  feeyn noa: son t'eh gra, Ta'n shenn ny share. 
42N||6||1||AS haink eh gy-kione er y chied doonaght lurg yn nah laa jeh'n chaisht, myr v'eh  goll trooid ny magheryn-arrooo dy ren e ynseydee ny jeeassyn y phluckey, as rubbey  yn arroo assdoo ayns nyn laueyn ren ad gee jeh.  
42N||6||2||As dooyrt shiartanse jeh ny Phariseeyn roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu jannoo shen nagh vel  lowal dy ve jeant er laghyn y doonaght?  
42N||6||3||As dreggyr Yeesey ad, gra, Nagh vel shiu er lhaih wheesh shoh, cre ren David tra  v'eh hene as e heshaght accryssagh:  
42N||6||4||Kys hie eh stiagh ayns thie Yee, as ghow eh as d'ee eh yn arran casherick, as hug  eh eh myrgeddin dauesyn va marish, ga nagh row eh lowit dy ve eeit, agh liorish ny  sag gyrtyn ny-lomarcan?   
42N||6||5||As dooyrt eh roo, Dy row yn Mac dooinney ny Hiarn myrgeddin er y doonaght.  
42N||6||6||As haink eh gy-kione er doonaght elley, dy jagh eh stiagh ayns y synagogne, as dy  dynsee eh: as va dooinney ayns shen va'n laue yesh echey er shyrgaghey.  
42N||6||7||As va sooill gheyre ec ny scruderyn as ny Phariseeyn er, dy yeeaghyn jinnag eh eh  y lheihys er laa yn doonaght: dy voddagh cooish chassid 've oc n'oi.  
42N||6||8||Agh va fys echeysyn er ny smooinaghtyn oc, as dooyrt eh rish y dooinney lesh y laue  shyrgit, Irree seose as shass magh er y laare. As dirree eh, as hass eh magh.  
42N||6||9||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, F&ecirc;nyms un red jiuish, Vel eh lowal er laghyn y doonaght  dy yannoo mie, ny dy yannoo olk? dy hauail bioys, ny dy stroie eh?   
42N||6||10||As yeeagh eh mygeayrt orroo ooilley, as dooyrt eh rish y dooinney, Sheeyn magh  dty laue. As ren eh shen; as va'n laue echey er ny lheihys myr y laue elley.  
42N||6||11||As v'adsyn myr deiney baanrit; as hug ad nyn goyrle dy cheilley, cre dy yannoo  rish Yeesey.  
42N||6||12||As haink eh gy-kione ayns ny laghyn shen, dy jagh eh seose er slieau dy ghoaill  padjer, as dy ren eh tannaghtyn fud ny hoie ayns padjer gys Jee.   
42N||6||13||As tra va'n laa er hoilshagh, de&iuml;e eh er e ynseydee huggey: as jeusyn reih eh  ghhaa-yeig, denmys eh myrgeddin nyn os tyllyn:  
42N||6||14||Simon (denmys eh myrgeddin Peddyr) as Andreays e vraar, Jamys as Ean, Philip as  Parlane,  
42N||6||15||Mian as Thomase, Jamys mac Alpheus, as Simon va enmyssit Zelotes  
42N||6||16||As Judas braar Yamys, as Yuaase Iscariot, va myrgeddin yn traitoor.  
42N||6||17||As haink eh neose maroo gys y cheer-rea, as haggil huggey sheshaght e eiyrtee,  as earroo mooar dy leih veih ooilley Judea as Jerusalem, as veih ardjyn ny marrey  Tyre as Sidon, haink dy eaishtagh rish, as dy ve er nyn lheihys jeh nyn ghoghanyn;    
42N||6||18||As adsyn va seaghnit lesh spyrrydyn neu-ghlen; as v'ad er nyn lheihys.   
42N||6||19||As va'n slane chaglym shirrey bentyn rish: son va bree goll magh ass, va dyn lheihys  ad ooilley.   
42N||6||20||As hrog eh seose e hooillyn er e eiyrtee, as dooyrt eh, Bannit ta shiuish voghtyn:  son lhieuish reeriaght Yee.   
42N||6||21||Bannit ta shiuish ta accryssagh nish: son bee shiu er nyn yannoo magh. Bannit ta  shiuish ta nish dobberan: son nee shiu garaghtee.   
42N||6||22||Bannit ta shiuish, tra ta deiney cur feoh diu, as tra nee ad nyn scarrey shiu voue,  as nyn oltooaney shiu, as nyn ennym y ghiarey magh myr olk, er coontey Mac y dooinney.    
42N||6||23||Bee-jee dy ghien mie ayns y laa shen, as lheim-jee son boggey son cur-my-ner, s'mooar  ta nyn leagh ayns niau: son er yn aght cheddin ren ny shenn-ayryn oc rish ny phadeyryn.    
42N||6||24||Agh smerg diuish verchee: son ta shiu er gheddyn nyn gherjagh.   
42N||6||25||Smerg diuish ta lane: son bee shiu accryssagh. Smerg diuish ta garaghtee nish:  son nee shiu dobberan as keayney.   
42N||6||26||Smerg diuish tra nee dy chooilley ghooinney loayrt dy mie jiu: son shen myr ren  ny ayraghyn oc jeh ny phadeyryn foalsey.   
42N||6||27||Agh ta mish gra riuish ta clashtyn, Bee-jee graihagh er nyn noidyn, bee-jee dooie  roosyn ta cur feoh diu:   
42N||6||28||Bannee-jee adsyn ta gwee mollaght diu, as gow-jee padjer er nyn son ocsyn ta cur  seaghyn erriu.   
42N||6||29||As huggeysyn woaillys oo er y derrey lieckan, chyndaa myrgeddin yn lieckan elley:  as eshyn ghoys ersooyl dty chloagey, ny bee noi dty chooat y lhiggey lesh myrgeddin.    
42N||6||30||Cur da dy chooilley ghooinney ta jannoo aghin hood; as jehsyn ta goaill ersooyl  dty chooid vo&iuml;d, ny shir ad reesht.   
42N||6||31||As myr bailliuish deiney dy yannoo riuish, jean-jee shiuish myrgeddin roosyn.    
42N||6||32||Son my ta shiu dooie dauesyn ta dooie riu, s'beg ta nyn mooise; son ta eer drogh-yantee  dooie dauesyn ta dooie roo.   
42N||6||33||As my ta shiu jannoo mie dauesyn ta jannoo mie diuish, cre'n booise ta nyn gour?  son ta ny eer drogh-yantee jannoo yn lheid cheddin.   
42N||6||34||As my ta shiu geeasaght dauesyn voue ta shiu jeeaghyn son cooilleeney, cre ta nyn  mooise? son ta eer drogh-sleih geeasaght da drogh-sleih; dy gheddyn wheesh cheddin  reesht.   
42N||6||35||Agh cur-jee graih da nyn noidyn, as jean-jee mie, as eeasee-jee, fegooish jerkal  rish veg y gheddyn reesht: as s'mooar vees nyn leagh! as bee shiu cloan yn Er-syrjey:  son t'eh dooie da'n vooinjer neu-wooisal as ny mee-chrauee.
42N||6||36||Bee-jee er-y-fa shen myghinagh, myr ta'n Ayr eu myrgeddin myghinagh.  
42N||6||37||Ny jean-jee briwnys, as cha bee shiu er nyn mriwnys: ny jean-jee deyrey, as cha  bee shiu er nyn gheyrey: leih-jee, as yiow shiu leih:
