42N||6||38||Jean-jee coyrt, as bee eh er ny choyrt diu; towse mie, jingit sheese, as criht  cooidjagh, as roie harrish, ver deiney diu ayns nyn oghrish. Son lesh y towse cheddin  ta shiu towse, bee eh er ny howse diu reesht.  
42N||6||39||As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, Vod y doal shooyll kione y doal? as nagh duitt  ad ny-neesht ayns y jeeg?  
42N||6||40||Cha vel y schoillar erskyn e vainshter: agh bee dy chooilley unnane ta slane-ynsit,  corrym rish e vainshter.  
42N||6||41||As cre'n-fa t'ou cronnaghey yn brenneein t'ayns sooill dty vraarey, agh cha vel  oo gennaghtyn yn darrag t'ayns dty hooill hene?  
42N||6||42||Ny kys oddys oo gra rish dty vraar, Vraar, lhig dou yn brenneein y ghoaill ass  dty hooill's, tra nagh vel oo goaill tastey dy vel darrag ayns dty hooill hene? Er-crauee-oalsey,  tilg hoshiaght yn darrag ass dty hooill hene, eisht bee soilshey ayd dy ghoaill yn brenneein ass sooill dty vraarey.  
42N||6||43||Son cha vel billey mie tilgey drogh vess: ny drogh villey tilgey mess mie.  
42N||6||44||Son ta dy chooilley villey er ny chronnaghey liorish e vess: son cha vel mess y  villey figgagh er ny heiy jeh drineyn, ny mess y villey-feeyney jeh thammag-ghress.   
42N||6||45||Ta dooinney mie ass stoyr mie e chree, cur magh shen ny ta mie: as drogh-ghooinney  ass drogh stoyr e chree, gymmyrkey shen ny ta olk: son magh ass stoyr y chree ta'n  beeal loayrt.  
42N||6||46||As cre'n-fa ta shiu dy my enmys Hiarn, Hiarn, fegooish jannoo ny reddyn ta mee  dy ghra? 
42N||6||47||Quoi-erbee ta cheet hym's, as clashtyn my ghoan, as jannoo ymmyd mie jeu, jeeaghym's  diu quoi rish t'eh er ny hoylaghey.
42N||6||48||T'eh er ny hoylaghey rish dooinney ren thie y hroggal, as chleiy dy dowin, as hoie  yn undin er creg: as tra dhatt yn ushtey, vrish yn thooilley stiagh dy trome er y  thie shen, agh cha yiarg eh er y chraa eh; er-yn-oyr dy row yn undin echey er creg.    
42N||6||49||Agh eshyn ta clashtyn as nagh vel jannoo ymmyd mie jeh, t'eh goll-rish dooinney,  ren fegooish undin thie y hroggal er yn ooir, as ren y thooilley brishey stiagh dy  trome, as chelleeragh huitt eh, as s'mooar va toyrt-mow yn thie shen. 
42N||7||1||NISH tra v'eh erreish ooilley ny goan shoh y loayrt ayns clashtyn y phobble, hie eh  stiagh ayns Calpernaum. 
42N||7||2||As va centurion dy row va fer-mooinjerey echey, v'eh dy mooar soiaghey jeh, as v'eh  ching, as raad y vaaish.   
42N||7||3||As tra cheayll eh jeh Yeesey, hug eh shanstyr ny Hewnyn huggey, guee er eh dy heet  dy laanaghey e er-mooinjerey.   
42N||7||4||As tra v'ad er jeet gys Yeesey, ren ad aghin huggey dy jeean, gra, Dy row eshyn  feeu v'eh dy yannoo shoh er y hon:   
42N||7||5||Son t'eh ny charrey da'n ashoon ain, as t'eh er hroggal synagogue dooin.   
42N||7||6||Eisht hie Yeesey m&acirc;roo. As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey da'n thie, hug y centurion  caarjyn huggey, gra rish, Hiarn, ny boir oo hene, son cha vel mish feeu oo dy heet  stiagh fo my chlea.   
42N||7||7||As er-yn-oyr shen cha yeeagh mee orrym pene dy ve feeu dy heet hood: agh loayr y  fockle, as nee my er-mooinjerey coural.   
42N||7||8||Son ta mish mee hene my ghooinney ayns pooar, as ta sidooryn aym foym, as ta mee  gra rish shoh, Immee, as t'eh goll: as rish fer elley, Tar, as t'eh cheet: as rish  my harvaant, Jean shoh, as t'eh dy yannoo eh.   
42N||7||9||Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, ghow eh yindys, as hyndaa eh mygeayrt, as dooyrt eh rish  y pobble va geiyrt er, Ta mee gra riu, Lheid y credjue lajer shoh, cha vel mee er  gheddyn ayns Israel hene.    
42N||7||10||As tra haink ny chaghteryn reesht gys y thie, hooar ad dy row yn fer-mooinjerey  va ching dy slane er choural.   
42N||7||11||As haink eh gy-kione yn laa er-giyn dy jagh eh gys ard-valley va enmyssit Nain,  as hie ymmodee jeh e ynseydee marish, as mooarrane sleih.   
42N||7||12||Nish tra haink eh er-gerrey da giat yn ard-valley, cur-my-ner, va sleih cur lhieu  magh dooinney marroo, va ny ynrycan mac da e voir, as v'eeish ny ben-treoghe: as  va ymmodee jeh sleih yn ard-valley m&acirc;ree.    
42N||7||13||As tra honnick y Chiarn ee, va chymmey  echey urree, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Ny jean keayney.   
42N||7||14||As haink eh, as venn eh rish y carbyd (as hass adsyn va fo) as dooyrt eh, Ghooinney  aeg, ta mee gra rhyt, Irree.   
42N||7||15||As hoie yn dooinney marroo seose, as ren eh toshiaght dy loayrt: as livrey eh eh  gys e vo1r.   
42N||7||16||As haink aggle orroo ooilley: as hug ad moylley da Jee, gra, Ta phadeyr mooar er  n'irree seose ny mast' ain; as, Ta Jee er yeeaghyn er e phobble.   
42N||7||17||As hie yn goo shoh magh my-e-chione trooid ooilley Judea, as trooid ooilley yn  cheer mygeayrt.   
42N||7||18||As hug ynseydee Ean coontey da jeh ooilley ny reddyn shoh.   
42N||7||19||As deie Ean er jees jeh e ynseydee as hug eh ad er chaghteraght gys Yeesey, gra,  Nee uss Eh va ry-hoi cheet, ny vel shin dy yeeaghyn son fer elley? 
42N||7||20||Tra va ny deiney er jeet huggey, dooyrt ad, Ta Ean Bastey er nyn goyrt shin dy  &ecirc;naght jeed, Nee uss Eh va ry-hoi cheet, ny vel shin dy yeeaghyn son fer elley?    
42N||7||21||As ayns yn oor cheddin v'eh lheihys ymmodee jeh ny aslayntyn as ny doghanyn, as  ny drogh-spyrrydyn oc, as da ymmodee va doal v'eh coyrt soilshey.   
42N||7||22||Eisht dregyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee reue, as insh-jee da Ean cre y  reddyn ta shiu er vakin as er chlashtyn kys dy vel ny doail geddyn nyn soilshey,  ny croobee shooyll, ny louraanee er nyn ghlenney, ny beuyr clashtyn, ny merriu er  nyn mioghey, as y sushtal er ny phreacheil da ny boghtyn.   
42N||7||23||As bannit ta eshyn nagh jean beg y hoiaghey jeem's.    
42N||7||24||As tra va chaghteryn Ean er n'immeeaght, ren eh toshiaght dy ghra rish y pobble  mychione Ean, Cre hie shiu magh gys yn aasagh dy akin? Nee cuirtliagh criht lesh  y gheay.
42N||7||25||Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Dooinney soit magh ayns coamrey moyrnagh! Cur-my-ner  t'adsyn ta ceau coamrey costal, as farrail dy seyr, ayns plaaseyn reeoil.   
42N||7||26||Agh cre hie shiu magh dy akin? Phadeyr? dy jarroo, ta mee gra riu, as fer s'ooasle  na phadeyr.   
42N||7||27||Shoh eh jeh te scruit, Cur-my-ner, ta mee cur my haghter magh royd, dy chiartaghey  yn raad kiongoyrt rhyt.   
42N||7||28||Son ta mee gra riu, Ny mast' oc syn t'er nyn ruggey jeh mraane, cha vel phadeyr  syrjey na Ean Bashtey: agh ta'n fer sloo t'ayns reeriaght Yee ny syrjey na eshyn.     
42N||7||29||As ren ooilley yn pobble cheayll eh as ny publicanee Jee y heyrey, as v'ad er nyn  mashtey lesh bashtey Ean.   
42N||7||30||Agh ren ny Phariseeyn as fir-ynsee yn leigh soiaghey beg jeh coyrle Yee nyn 'o&iuml;  oc hene, as cha row ad er nyn mashtey liorish.   
42N||7||31||As dooyrt y Chiarn, Cre gys nee'm deiney yn cheeloghe shoh y hoylaghey? as cre  rish t'ad goll?   
42N||7||32||T'ad goll-rish cloan, ta nyn soie ayns ny margaghyn, geamagh yn derrey yeh gys  y jeh elley, as gra, Ta shin er n'yannoo bingys diu, as cha vel shiu er ghaunsin:  ta shin er hroggal bardoon diu, as cha vel shiu er ghobberan.   
42N||7||33||Son cha daink Ean Bashtey gee arran, ny giu feeyn; as ta shiu gra, Ta drogh spyrryd  echey.   
42N||7||34||Ta'n Mac dooinney er jeet gee as giu; as ta shiu gra, Cur-my-ner dooinney jollyssagh,  as iuder-feeyney, carrey dy phublicanee as dy pheccee.   
42N||7||35||Agh ta creenaght er ny heyrey liorish ooilley e cloan. 
42N||7||36||As chuir fer jeh ny Phariseeyn eh gys bee marish. As hie eh stiagh ayns thie  yn Pharisee, as hoie eh sheese gys bee.   
42N||7||37||As cur-my-ner va ben ayns yn ard-valley, va ny drogh yantagh, tra va fys eck dy  row Yeesey ny hoie ec bee ayns thie yn Pharisee, hug ee lh'ee box alabaster dy ooil  chostal.   
42N||7||38||As hass ee ec e chassyn cheu e chooylloo keayney, as ren ee toshiaght dy niee e  chassyn lesh jeir, as rub ee ad lesh folt e king, as phaag ee e chassyn, as ren ee  ad y ooillaghey lesh yn ooil.   
42N||7||39||Nish yn Pharisee ren y chuirrey eh, tra honnick eh shoh, loayr eh cheu-sthie jeh  hene, gra, Veagh fys er ve ec y dooinney shoh, dy beagh eh ny adeyr, quoi, as cre'n  monney dy ven ee shoh, ta bentyn rish: son t'ee ny ben pheccoil.   
42N||7||40||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Simon, ta red aym's dy ghra rhyt, As dooyrt  eh, Abbyr eh, vainshter.   
42N||7||41||Va dooinney dy row, as jees ayns lhiastynys da: va'n derrey yeh lhiastyn queig  cheead ping, as y jeh elley jeih pingyn as da-eed.   
42N||7||42||As tra nagh row oc dy eeck, leih eh daue ny-neesht dy arryltagh. Insh dou eisht,  quoi jeu s'booisal vees da?   
42N||7||43||Dreggyr Simon as dooyrt eh, Er-lhiam dy nee eshyn, da smoo ren eh leih. As dooyrt  eh rish, T'ou er vriwnys dy cairagh.   
42N||7||44||As hyndaa eh gys y ven, as dooyrt eh rish Simon, Vel oo cur-my-ner yn ven shoh?  Haink mee stiagh ayns dty hie's, as cha dug oo dou ushtey son my chassyn: agh t'eeish  er niee my chassyn lesh jeir, as er jyrmagh ad lesh folt e king.   
42N||7||45||Cha dug uss paag dou: agh ta'n ven shoh, er-dyn traa haink mee stiagh, er ve kinjagh  paagey my chassyn.   
42N||7||46||My chione lesh ooil cha ren oo y ooillaghey: agh ta'n ven shoh er n'ooillaghey  my chassyn lesh ooil.   
42N||7||47||Shen-y-fa ta mee gra rhyt, Ta ny peccaghyn eck ta ymmodee, er nyn leih jee: shen-y-fa  wheesh shen smoo ta yn ghraih eck: agh dasyn ta beggan er ny leih, cha vel e ghraih  agh beggan.   
42N||7||48||As dooyrt eh r'ee, Ta dty pheccaghyn er nyn leih dhyt.   
42N||7||49||As ren y vooinjer va nyn soie ec bee m&acirc;rish, toshiaght dy ghra cheu-sthie jeu hene,  Quoi eh shoh ta myrgeddin leih peccaghyn?   
42N||7||50||As dooyrt eh rish y ven, Ta dty chredjue er dty hauail; immee ayns shee. 
42N||8||1||As haink eh gy-kione ny lurg shen, dy jagh eh trooid dy chooilley valley, mooar as  beg preacheil as soilshaghey sushtal gerjoilagh reeriaght Yee: as va'n daa ostyl  yeig marish:  
42N||8||2||As shiartanse dy vraane, v'er nyn lheihys jeh drogh-spyrrydyn, as aslayntyn, Moirrey  va enmyssit Malaine, ass-jee hie shiaght drogh-spyrrydyn,   
42N||8||3||As Joanna ben Chusa stiurt Herod, as Susanna, as ymmodee elley, v'er hirveish er  Jeh nyn gooid.   
42N||8||4||As tra va earroo mooar dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, as er jeet huggey ass dy  chooilley ard-valley; loayr eh liorish coraa dorraghey:   
42N||8||5||Hie correyder magh dy chuir e rass: as myr v'eh cuir, huitt paart rish oirr y raad,  as ve stampit sheese, as d'ee eeanlee yn aer eh.   
42N||8||6||As huitt paart er creg, as cha leah as ve er n'aase seose, hie eh naardey, er-yn-oyr  dy row eh laccal soo.   
42N||8||7||As huitt paart mastey drineyn, as daase ny drineyn seose m&acirc;rish, as phloogh ad eh.    
42N||8||8||As huitt cooid elley jeh ayns thalloo mie, as daase eh seose, as dymmyrk eh mess  keead-filley. As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, de&iuml;e eh, Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn,  lhig da clashtyn.    
42N||8||9||As d&ecirc;nee e ostyllyn jeh, gra, Cre ta er ny hoiggal liorish y coraa-dorraghey shoh?     
42N||8||10||As dooyrt eh, Diuish te er ny choyrt dy hoiggal folliaghtyn reeriaght Yee; agh  da feallagh elley ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: ga t'ad fakin cha vel ad cur-my-ner,  as clashtyn cha vel ad toiggal.   
42N||8||11||Nish shoh bun y choraa-dorraghey: Yn rass goo Yee.    
42N||8||12||Shen rish oirr y raad, yn vooinjer ta clashtyn: eisht ta'n drogh-spyrryd cheet,  as goaill ersooyl yn goo ass ny creeaghyn oc, er-aggle dy jinnagh ad credjal, as  dy beagh ad er nyn sauail.   
42N||8||13||Adsyn er y chreg, yn vooinjer, tra t'ad er chlashtyn, ta goaill y goo dy arryltagh;  as cha vel fraue oc shoh, son tammylt t'ad credjal, agh ayns earish miolagh ta nyn  gredjue failleil.   
42N||8||14||As shen huitt mastey drineyn, yn vooinjer, tra t'ad er chlashtyn, ta goll magh  as ta plooghit lesh kiarail as berchys, as eunyssyn y vea shoh, as cha vel ad gymmyrkey  magh mess gys lhieeney vie.   
42N||8||15||Agh shen er y thalloo mie, yn vooinjer ta lesh creeaghyn onneragh as mie, er chlashtyn  yn goo, as ta dy reayll oc eh, as cur magh mess lesh meenid.   
42N||8||16||Cha vel doooinney erbee, tra t'eh er voaddey cainle, dy choodaghey ee lesh saagh  ny dy choyrt ee fo lhiabbee: agh soiaghey ee ayns cainleyr, dy vod adsyn ta cheet  stiagh yn soilshey y akin.   
42N||8||17||Son cha vel nhee erbee follit, nagh jig gys soilshey: ny nhee erbee kiellit, nagh  bee fys er, as nagh jig magh.   
42N||8||18||Cur-jee twoaee er-y-fa shen kys ta shiu clashtyn: son quoi-erbee ta echey, dasyn  vees er ny choyrt; as quoi-erbee nagh vel echey, veihsyn vees er ny ghoaill eer shen  hene er-lesh dy vel echey.
42N||8||19||Eisht haink huggey e voir as e vraaraghyn, as cha voddagh ad cheet n'aare, kyndagh  rish y chennid.  
42N||8||20||As va shoh er ny insh da, lioroosyn dooyrt, Ta dty voir as dty vraaraghyn nyn shassoo  mooie, geearee dy dty akin.  
42N||8||21||Agh dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh roo, My voir as my vraaraghyn ad shoh ta clashtyn  goo Yee, as ta dy yannoo eh.  
42N||8||22||Nish haink eh gy-kione, er laa dy row, dy jagh eh er-board lhong marish e ostyllyn:  as dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dooin goll harrish gys y cheu elley jeh'n logh. As hie ad  magh son y cheayn.  
42N||8||23||Agh myr v'ad shiaulley, huitt eh ny chadley: as dirree sterrym mooar dy gheay er  y cheayn, as lhieen yn ushtey stiagh orroo, dy row ad ayns gaue.  
42N||8||24||As haink ad huggey as ghooisht ad eh, gra, Vainshter, vainshter, bee mayd caillit.  Eisht dirree eh, as smaghtee eh yn gheay as freaney ny tonnyn: as ghow ad fea, as  va kiuney ayn.  
42N||8||25||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre vel y credjue eu? As va aggle orroo, goaill yindys as gra  ry-cheilley, Cre'n monney dy ghooinney eh shoh? son t'eh cur ny eer geayghyn as yn  ushtey fo harey, as t'ad ayns biallys da.  
42N||8||26||As haink ad gys cheer ny Gadarenee ta harrish noi Galilee.  
42N||8||27||As tra v'eh er n'gholl er thalloo, haink ny whail ass yn ard-valley, dooinney dy  row va ry-foddey seaghnit lesh drogh-spyrrydyn, as cha row eh ceau eaddagh, chamoo  duirree eh ayns thie erbee, agh mastey ny hoaiaghyn.  
42N||8||28||Tra honnick eh Yeesey, dyllee eh, as huitt eh sheese kiongoyrt rish, as dooyrt  eh lesh ard-choraa, Cre'n eie t'ayd orrym Yeesey, Vac yn Jee smoo ard? Guee-ym ort  nagh jean oo my horchaghey.  
42N||8||29||(Son v'eh er harey yn spyrryd neu ghlen dy heet magh ass y dooinney. Son v'eh dy  mennick er hoiaghey er: as v'eh freilt kianlt lesh geulaghyn, as ayns yiarnyn; as  vrish eh ny geulaghyn, as v'eh er ny ve eiyrit liorish y drogh-spyrryd gys yn aasagh.)   
42N||8||30||As d&ecirc;nee Yeesey jeh, gra, Cre'n ennym t'ort? As dooyrt eh, Legion: er-yn oyr dy  row ymmodee drogh-spyrrydyn er n'gholl stiagh ayn.  
42N||8||31||As ghuee ad er gyn eh dy oardaghey daue goll sheese gys y diunid.  
42N||8||32||As va griagh mooar dy vuckyn fo bochillyn er y clieau: as ghuee ad er, eh dy chur  kied daue goll stiagh ayndoo. As hug eh kied daue.  
42N||8||33||Eisht hie ny drogh-spyrrydyn ass y dooinney, as hie ad stiagh ayns ny muckyn: as  roie yn ghriagh gour nyn mullee lesh yn eaynee gys y cheayn, as v'ad plooghit.  
42N||8||34||Tra honnick ny bochillyn cre va jeant, roie ad roue, as hie ad as dinsh ad eh ayns  yn ard-valley, as trooid y cheer. 
42N||8||35||Eisht hie ad magh dy yeeaghyn cre va jeant; as haink ad gys Yeesey, as hooar ad  y dooinney, ass va ny drogh spyrrydyn er n'gholl, ny hoie ec cassyn Yeesey, as e  eaddagh er, as v'eh dy mie ayns e cheeayl: as ghow ad aggle.  
42N||8||36||Dinsh myrgeddin yn vooinjer honnick eh daue, kys va fer ny drogh-spyrrydyn er ny  lheihys. 
42N||8||37||Eisht ren y slane chaglym jeh cheer y Gadalenee mygeayrt, guee er eh dy gholl roish:  son va aggle mooar er duittym orroo: as hie eh er-board yn lhong, as hyndaa eh back  reesht.  
42N||8||38||Nish va'n dooinney ass va ny drogh spyrrydyn er n'immeeaght geearree dy ve marish:  agh hug Yeesey ersooyl eh, gra,  
42N||8||39||Gow royd gys dty hie hene, as soilshee cre ny reddyn mooarey ta Jee er n'yannoo  er dty hon. As hie eh roish, as dinsh eh magh trooid ooilley yn ard-valley, cre ny  reddyn mooarey va Yeesey er n'yannoo er e hon.  
42N||8||40||As haink eh gy-kione, tra va Yeesey er jeet back, dy ghow yn pobble lane boggey  jeh: son v'ad ooilley fieau er.  
42N||8||41||As cur-my-ner, haink dooinney va enmyssit Jairus, as v'eh fer jeh reiltee yn  synagogue: as huitt eh sheese ec cassyn Yeesey, as ghuee eh er, eh dy heet stiagh  ayns e hie:  
42N||8||42||Son va un ynrycan inneen echey, va mysh daa vlein jeig dy eash, as v'ee raad y  vaaish. (Agh myr v'eh goll, va'n pobble chionney er.  
42N||8||43||As va ben va roie foalley er ve eck rish daa vlein jeig, v'er vaarail ooilley  e cooid-seihlt er fir-lhee, as cha daink eh lesh veg jeu ee y lheihys,  
42N||8||44||Haink ee shoh cheu e chooylloo, as venn ee rish oirr e gharmad: as chelleeragh  hyrmee yn roie-foalley eck.
42N||8||45||As dooyrt Yeesey, Quoi venn rhym? Tra ren ooilley gobbal, dooyrt Peddyr, as adsyn  va marish, Vainshter, ta'n pohble chionney ort, as dy dty yingey, as t'ou uss gra,  Quoi venn rhym?  
42N||8||46||As dooyrt Yeesey, Ta peccagh ennagh er ventyn rhym: son ta mee gennaghtyn dy vel  bree er n'gholl ass-ym.  
42N||8||47||As tra honnick yn ven dy row ee cronnit, haink ee er-creau, as huitt ee sheese  ec e chassyn, as hoilshee ee da kiongoyrt rish ooilley yn pobble, cre'n oyr v'eck  dy ventyn rish, as er-y-chooyl kys v'ee er ny lheihys  
42N||8||48||As dooyrt eh r'ee, Inneen, bee dy ghien mie; ta dty chredjue er dty laanaghey:  immee ayns shee.)  
42N||8||49||Choud as v'eh foast loayrt, haink fer veih thie fer-reill yn synagogue, gra rish,  Ta dty inneen marroo; ny cur trubbyl sodjey da'n Vainshter.  
42N||8||50||Agh tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dreggyr eh eh, gra, Ny bee aggle ort: cha vel ort  agh dy chredjal, as bee ee er ny lheihys. 
42N||8||51||As tra v'eh er jeet stiagh 'sy thie, cha lhig eh da dooinney erbee goll stiagh  marish, agh Peddyr, as Jamys, as Ean, as ayr as moir y ven-aeg.  
42N||8||52||As v'ad ooilley keayney, as jannoo dobberan er e son: agh dooyrt eshyn, Ny jean-jee  keayney; cha vel ee marroo, agh ny cadley.  
42N||8||53||Agh s'beg hoie ad jeh e raa, as fys oc son shickyrys dy row ee marroo.  
42N||8||54||As hug eh ad ooilley magh, as ghow eh ee er laue, as deie eh, gra, Ven-aeg, irree  seose.  
42N||8||55||As haink y spyrryd eck reesht, as dirree ee jeeragh: as doardee eh bee y chur jee.   
42N||8||56||As ghow yn ayr as y voir eck yindys mooar: agh hug eh currym daue gyn ad dy insh  da dooinney erbee cre va jeant. 
42N||9||1||Eisht deie eh er y daa ostyl yeig cooidjagh, as hug eh daue pooar as eaghtyrys harrish  dy chooilley ghrogh-spyrryd, as dy lheihys doghanyn.   
42N||9||2||As hug eh ad magh dy phreacheil reeriaght Yee, as dy laanaghey sleih chingey.    
42N||9||3||As dooyrt eh roo, Ny cur-jee lhieu nhee erbee son nyn yurnah, chamoo luirg, ny spagey,  ny arran, ny argid; as ny lhig da daa chooat y pheesh y ve eu.   
42N||9||4||As thie erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, gow-jee aaght ayns shen, derrey hed shiu reue.    
42N||9||5||As quoi-erbee nagh jean goaill riu, tra aagys shiu yn ard-valley shen, crie-jee  yn eer joan jeh ny cassyn eu, son feanish nyn 'oi    
42N||9||6||As hie ad magh, as jimmee ad trooid ny baljyn, preacheil yn sushtal, as lheihys  dy chooilley raad.   
42N||9||7||Nish va Herod yn tetrarch er chlasht yn jeh ooilley e yannoo: as v'eh seaghnit,  er-y-fa dy row paart gra, dy row Ean er n'irree veih ny merriu:   
42N||9||8||As paart, dy row Elias er jeet kionfenish: as feallagh elley, dy row fer jeh ny  sbenn adeyryn er n'irree reesht.    
42N||9||9||As dooyrt Herod, Jeh Ean ren mish yn kione y ghoaill; agh quoi eh shoh jeh ta mee  clashtyn lheid ny reddyn? As v'eh aggindagh dy akin eh.   
42N||9||10||As tra va ny ostyllyn er jeet reesht, dinsh ad da [Yeesey] ooilley ny v'ad er  n'yannoo. As ghow eh ad, as hie eh dy lhiattee gys boayl er-lheh ayns yn aasagh,  bentyn gys ard-valley enmyssit Bethsaida    
42N||9||11||As tra hooar y pobble fys er, deiyr ad er: as hug eh oltaghey daue, as loayr eh  roo jeh reeriaght Yee, as laanee eh adsyn va feme slaanaghey.   
42N||9||12||As tra va'n laa faggys ceaut, haink yn daa ostyl yeig as dooyrt ad rish, Lhig y  raad da'n pobble, dy vod ad goll roue gys ny baljyn as er y cheer mygeayrt, dy gheddyn  aaght as beaghey: son ta shin ayns shoh ayns boayl faasagh. 
42N||9||13||Agh dooyrt eh roo, Cur-jee shiuish bee daue. As dooyrt ad, Cha vel ain agh queig  bwilleenyn as daa eeast; mannagh jem mayd dy chionnaghey bee son ooilley yn pobble  shoh.   
42N||9||14||Son v'ad mysh queig thousane dooinney. As dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Cur-jee orroo  soie sheese, jeih as da-eed ayns sheshaght.   
42N||9||15||As ren ad shen, as hug ad orroo ooilley soie sheese.   
42N||9||16||Eisht ghow eh ny queig bwilleenyn as y daa eeast, as yeeagh eh seose gys niau,  as vannee eh, as vrish eh, as hug eh ad da e ostyllyn dy hoiaghey roish y pobble.    
42N||9||17||As ren ad ooilley gee, as v'ad er nyn yannoo magh: as hrog ad jeh'n fooilliagh  daag ad, lane daa vaskad jeig.   
42N||9||18||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh ec padjer ayns ynnyd er-lheh, as e ostyllyn marish:  dy denee eh jeu, gra, Cre ta'n pobble dy ghra my-mychione's, quoi mee?   
42N||9||19||Dreggyr adsyn, as dooyrt ad, Ean Bashtey: agh ta paart gra, Elias: as paart elley,  dy vel fer jeh ny shenn adeyryn er n'irree reesht.   
42N||9||20||Dooyrt eshyn roo, Agh quoi ta shiuish gra dy vel mee? Dreggyr Peddyr as dooyrt  eh, Yn Creest dy Yee.   
42N||9||21||As hug eh currym gyere orroo, gyn ad dy insh shen da dooinney erbee,  
42N||9||22||Gra, Shegin da Mac y dooinney ymmodee reddyn y hurranse, as ve beg soit jeh liorish  y chanstyr, as ny ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn, as ve er ny varroo, as girree  reesht yn trass laa.   
42N||9||23||As dooyrt eh roo ooilley, My ta dooinney erbee aggindagh geiyrt orrym's lhig  da eh-hene y obbal, as e chrosh y hroggal gagh laa, as geiyrt orrym.   
42N||9||24||Son quoi-erbee baillish e vioys y hauail, caillee eh eh: agh quoi-erbee chaillys  e vioys er my ghraih's, sauee eh shoh eh.   
42N||9||25||Son cre'n vondeish t'ec dooinney, my chosnys eh yn seihll ooilley, as eh-hene dy  ve caillit, ny ceaut ersooyl?   
42N||9||26||Son quoi-erbee ghoys nearey jeem's as jeh my ghoan, jehsyn ghoys yn Mac dooinney  nearey, tra hig eh ayns e ghloyr hene, as gloyr e Ayrey, as ny ainleyn casherick.    
42N||9||27||Agh ta mee ginsh diu ayns firrinys, dy vel paart nyn shassoo ayns shoh nagh jean  blashtyn er y baase, derrey hee ad reeriaght 
42N||9||28||As haink eh gy-kione mygeayrt hoght laa lurg ny raaghyn shoh, dy ghow eh marish,  Peddyr as Ean as Jamys, as dy jagh eh seose er slieau dy ghoaill padjer.   
42N||9||29||As myr v'eh ayns padjer, va cummey yn eddin echey er ny chaghlaa, as va'n coamrey  echey gial as follys.   
42N||9||30||As cur-my-ner va daa ghooinney taggloo rish, ta shen dy ghra Moses as Elias: 
42N||9||31||Haink kionfenish ayns gloyr, as loayr ad heh e vaase, v'eh dy hurranse ec Jerusalem.    
42N||9||32||Agh haink cadley trome er Peddyr as orroosyn va marish: as tra v'ad er ghoostey,  honnick ad yn ghloyr echey, as y daa ghooinney va nyn shassoo marish.  
42N||9||33||As haink eh gy-kione myr v'ad goll dy aagail eh, dy dooyrt Peddyr rish Yeesey,  Vainshter, s'mie dooin dy ve ayns shoh; as lhig dooin three cabbaneyn y yannoo, cabbane  er dty hon's, as cabbane son Moses, as cabbane son Elias: s'coan toiggal cre v'eh  dy ghra.  
42N||9||34||Choud as v'eh loayrt shoh, haink bodjal lesh scadoo harrystoo: as ghow ad aggle  myr va'n bodjal cheet moo.   
42N||9||35||As haink coraa ass y vodjal, gra, Shoh my vac graihagh; eaisht-jee rishyn.  
42N||9||36||As lurg y choraa, hooar ad Yeesey ny lomarcan: as dreill ad shoh oc hene, as cha  dinsh ad da dooinney erbee ayns ny laghyn shen, veg jeh ny reddyn v'ad er vakin.   
42N||9||37||As haink eh gy-kione yn nah laa tra v'ad er jeet neose jeh'n clieau, dy daink  ymmodee ny whail.  
42N||9||38||As cur-my-ner, deie dooinney jeh'n cheshaght, gra, Vainshter, ta mee guee ort jeeagh  er my vac, son she my ynrycan lhiannoo eh.  
42N||9||39||As cur-my-ner, ta spyrryd dy ghoaill eh, as doaltattym t'eh gyllagh; as tuittym  neeal, t'eh keshal, as s'coan t'eh cheet huggey hene, erreish da ve dy mooar broojit.   
42N||9||40||As ghuee mee er dty ostyllyn ad dy hilgey magh eh, agh cha daink eh lhieu.  
42N||9||41||As dreggyr Yeesey, gra, 0 heeloghe vee-chredjuagh as roonagh, caid ta mish dy ve  meriu, as dy hurranse diu? Cur lhiat dty vac ayns shoh.  
42N||9||42||As myr v'eh foast cheet, cheau yn drogh-spyrryd sheese eh ayns strepyn: agh vaggyr  Yeesey er y spyrryd neu-ghlen, as laanee eh yn lhiannoo, as livrey eh eh reesht gys  e ayr.  
42N||9||43||As v'ad ooilley ayns ard-yindys jeh pooar niartal Yee: Agh choud as va dy chooilley  unnane ayns ard-imnea mychione dagh nhee va Yeesey er n'yannoo, dooyrt eh rish e  ostyllyn,  
42N||9||44||Lhig da ny raaghyn shoh goll dowin ayns nyn glashtyn: son bee yn Mac dooinney er  ny livrey gys laueyn deiney.
42N||9||45||Agh cha hoig ad y raa shoh, as ve gyn yss daue, nagh row toiggal oc jeh: as va  aggle orroo fenaght jeh mychione y raa cheddin.   
42N||9||46||Eisht hie ad son argane ry-cheilley, quoi jeu syrjey veagh.  
42N||9||47||As Yeesey toiggal smooinaghtyn y chree oc, ghow eh lhiannoo, as hoie eh eh liorish,   
42N||9||48||As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi-erbee nee soiaghey jeh'n lhiannoo shoh ayns m'ennynn's,  t'eh jannoo soiaghey jeem's: as quoi-erbee nee soiaghey jeem's, t'eh soiaghey jehsyn  t'er my choyrt: son eshyn sloo ta nyn mast' eu ooilley, eshyn syrjey vees.  
42N||9||49||As dreggyr Ean as dooyrt eh, Vainshter, honnick shin fer castey drogh spyrrydyn  ayns dty ennym's; as liett shin eh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel eh geiyrt ort's marinyn.   
42N||9||50||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Ny jean-jee eh y lhiettal: son, eshyn nagh vel nyn 'oi,  t'eh lhien.  
42N||9||51||As haink eh gy-kione, myr va'n traa tayrn er-gerrey dasyn dy ve goit seose, dy  row eh dy shickyr kiarit er soiaghey e eddin dy gholl gys Jerusalem.  
42N||9||52||As hug eh chaghteryn roish: as jimmee ad, as haink ad gys balley jeh ny Samaritanee  dy aarlaghey er e hon.  
42N||9||53||Agh cha dug adsyn oltaghey-bea da, er-yn-oyr dy dug ad my-ner dy row eh goll gys  Jerusalem.  
42N||9||54||As tra honnick e ostyllyn Jamys as Ean shoh, dooyrt ad, Hiarn, nailt shin dy harey  aile orroo veih niau, dy stroie ad, eer myr ren Elias?  
42N||9||55||Agh hyndaa eh, as hug eh oghsan daue, gra, Cha s'eu cre'n monney dy spyrryd ta  shiu jeh.  
42N||9||56||Son cha vel Mac yn dooinney er jeet dy stroie bioys deiney, agh dy nyn sauail.  As hie ad roue gys balley elley. 
42N||9||57||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'ad goll er y raad, dy dooyrt dooinney dy row rish,  Hiarn, eiyr-yms ort raad erbee dy jed oo.  
42N||9||58||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Ta tuill ec ny shynnee, as idd ec eeanlee yn aer, agh ec  Mac yn dooimley cha vel boayl, ayn dy chur e chione fo.  
42N||9||59||As dooyrt eh rish fer elley, Eiyr orrym: Agh dooyrt eshyn, Hiarn, cur kied dou  hoshiaeht goll thie dy oanluckey my ayr.  
42N||9||60||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Lhig da ny me riu nyn merriu y oanluckey; agh gow uss royd  as jean reeriaght Yee y phreacheil.  
42N||9||61||As dooyrt fer elley myrgeddin rish Hiarn, eiyr-yms ort-agh lhig dou hoshiaght bannaght  y aagail ec y vooinjer t'ec my hie.  
42N||9||62||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Dooinney erbee t'er chur e laue gys y cheeaght, as ta jeeaghyn  back, t'eh an-chooid son reeriaght Yee.         
42N||10||1||Ny lurg shoh, doardee yn Chiarn three-feed as jeih elley, as hug eh ad magh jees as  jees roish hene, gys dy chooilley ard valley as ynnyd, raad v'eh hene ry-hoi cheet.    
42N||10||2||Shen-y-fa dooyrt eh roo, Ta'n fouyr dy jarroo mooar, agh ta ny labreeyn beggan:  guee-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen er Chiarn y fouyr, eh dy chur magh labreeyn gys y fouyr  echey.    
42N||10||3||Immee-jee eisht: cur-jee my-ner, ta mish dyn goyrt shiu magh myr eayin mastey moddee-oaldey.  
42N||10||4||Ny cur-jee lhieu sporran, ny spagey, ny braagyn: as ny jean-jee cumrail ayns goltaghey  dooinney erbee er y raad.  
42N||10||5||As thie erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, abbyr-jee hoshiaght, Shee dy row gys y thie  shoh. 
42N||10||6||As my vees mac ny shee ayns shen, nee yn chee eu tannaghtyn er: mannagh vel, chyndaa-ee  eh hiu hene reesht.  
42N||10||7||As ayns y thie cheddin fuirree-jee, gee as giu lheid as ver ad reue: son ta'n labree  toilliu e aill. Ny gow-jee veih thie dy thie.  
42N||10||8||As ard-valley erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, as ad dy oltaghey nyn mea, ee-jee lheid  as vees soit reue.   
42N||10||9||As slaanee-jee yn sleih chingey t'ayn, as abbyr-jee roo, Ta reeriaght Yee er jeet  er-gerrey diu.  
42N||10||10||Agh ard-valley erbee dy jed shiu stiagh ayn, as nagh jean goaill riu, gow-jee reue  magh ayns ny straidyn oc, as abbyr-jee,  
42N||10||11||Eer joan yn ard-valley eu, ta lhiantyn hooin, ta shin dy chraa j'in nyn 'oi eu:  ny yeih, bee-jee shickyr jeh shoh, dy vel reeriaght Yee er jeet er-gerrey diu.  
42N||10||12||Agh ta mish gra riu, dy bee eh ny sassey da Sodom ec y laa shen, na da'n ard valley  shen.  
42N||10||13||Smerg dhyt's Chorazin, smerg dhyt's Vethsaida: son dy beagh ny obbraghyn yindyssagh  er ve jeant ayns Tyre as Sidon, t'er ny ve jeant ayndiuish, veagh ad er ghoaill arrys  foddey er dy henney ayns aanrit-sack as leoie.  
42N||10||14||Agh bee kerraghey s'eddrym er ny choyrt er Tyre as Sidon ec y vriwnys, na vees  er ny choyrt erriuish.  
42N||10||15||As uss Chapernaum, ta dty ooash]ey roshtyn gys niau, bee oo er dty hilgey sheese  eys niurin.  
42N||10||16||Eshyn eaishtys riuish, t'eh geaishtagh rhym's: as eshyn ta soiaghey beg jiuish,  t'eh soiaghey beg jeem's: as eshyn ta soiaghey beg jeem's, t'eh soiaghey beg jehsyn  ta er mychoyrt.  
42N||10||17||As haink y three-feed as jeih huggey reesht lesh boggey, gra, Hiarn, ta ny eer  drogh-spyrrydyn biallagh dooin, trooid dty ennym's.  
42N||10||18||As dooyrt eh roo, Honnick mee Noid ny hanmey, myr tendreil, tuittym veih niau.   
42N||10||19||Cur-my-ner, ta mish coyrt diu pooar dy chur fo-chosh ard-nieughyn as scorpionee,  as ooilley pooar y noid; as cha jean nhee 'sy theihll, er aght erbee, skielley diu.   
42N||10||20||Ny-yeih ayns shoh ny gow-jee boggey, dy vel ny spyrrydyn biallagh diu: agh gow-jee  boggey smoo, dy vel ny enmyn eu scruit ayns niau.  
42N||10||21||Ayns yn oor cheddin ghow Yeesey boggey ayns e spyrryd, as dooyrt eh, Ta mee cur  booise dhyt, O Ayr Hiarn niau as thalloo, dy vel oo er cheiltyn ny reddyn shoh vouesyn  ta creeney as tushtagh, as dy vel oo er hoilshaghey ad da oikanyn: shen dy  jarroo  myr te, Ayr, sonshen myr ve mie ayns dty hilley's.  
42N||10||22||Ta dy chooilley nhee er ny livrey dooys liorish my Ayr: as cha vel fys ec unnane  erbee quoi yn Mac, agh yn Ayr; ny quoi yn Ayr, agh yn Mac, as eshyn da nee yn Mac  eh y hoilshaghey.  
42N||10||23||As hyndaa eh gys e ostyllyn, as dooyrt eh er-lheh, Bannit ta ny sooillyn ta fakin  ny reddyn ta shiuish dy akin.  
42N||10||24||Son ta mee ginsh diu, dy vel ymmodee phadeyryn as reeaghyn er ve aignagh dy akin  ny reddyn shen ta shiuish er vakin, as cha vel ad er vakin ad; as dy chlashtyn ny  reddyn ta shiuish dy chlashtyn, as cha vel ad er chlashtyn ad.  
42N||10||25||As cur-my-ner, hass fer-ynsee dy row jeh'n leigh seose, erchee y phrowal eh,  gra, Vainshter, cre t'orrym's dy yannoo dy vod eiraght y ve aym ayns y vea veayn?   
42N||10||26||Dooyrt eshyn rish, Cre ta scruit ayns y leigh? kys t'ou lhaih?  
42N||10||27||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Ver oo graih da'n Chiarn dty Yee lesh ooilley dty  chree, as lesh ooilley dty annym, as lesh ooilley dty niart, as lesh ooilley dty  aigney  as da dty naboo myr dhyt hene.  
42N||10||28||As dooyrt eh rish, T'ou er n'ansoor dy mie: jean shoh, as yiow yn vea.  
42N||10||29||Agh v'eshyn booiagh eh-hene y heyrey, as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, As quoi my naboo?  
42N||10||30||As dreggyr Yeesey, gra, Hie dooinney dy row sheese veih Jerusalem gys Jericho,  as huitt eh mastey maarlee, rooisht eh jeh e choamrey, as lhott ad eh, as hie ad  rhymboo, erreish daue y er vaagail eh lieh-varroo.  
42N||10||31||As haghyr eh da saggyrt dy row goll sheese y raad shen; as tra honnick eh eh, hie  eh shaghey er y derrey heu jeh.  
42N||10||32||As myrgeddin Levite, tra v'eh ec yn ynnyd, haink eh as yeeagh eh er, as hie eh  shaghey er y cheu elley. 
42N||10||33||Agh haink Samaritan dy row, myr v'eh er e yurnah, raad v'eh: as tra honnick eh  eh, va chymmey echey er.  
42N||10||34||As hie eh huggey, as chiangle eh seose ny lhottyn echey, niee ad lesh ooil as feeyn,  as hoie eh eh er e vaagh hene, as hug eh lesh eh gys thie-oast, as ghow eh kiarail  jeh.   
42N||10||35||As laa ny vairagh tra v'eh goll roish ghow eh daa pheesh dy argid as hug eh ad  da mainshter y thie-oast as dooyrt eh rish, Gow kiarail jeh; as cre-erbee smoo vaarys  oo er, eeck-ym dhyt eh, tra hig-ym reesht.
42N||10||36||Quoi nish jeu shoh nyn droor, t'ou  uss dy smooinaghtyn, va ny naboo dasyn huitt mastey ny maarlee?  
42N||10||37||As dooyrt eh rish, Eshyn ren myghin y hoilshaghey er, Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish,  Immee, as jean uss er yn aght cheddin.  
42N||10||38||Nish haink eh gy-kione, myr vad goll, dy jagh ad stiagh ayns balley beg dy row:  as ren ben v'ayns shen enmyssit Martha, eh y chuirrey gys y thie eck. 
42N||10||39||As va shuyr eck enmyssit Moirrey hoie myrgeddin ec cassyn Yeesey, clashtyn e ghoo.   
42N||10||40||Agh va Martha tooillit lesh y phreish vooar vurree, as haink ee huggey, as dooyrt  ee, Hiarn, nee dty aighey's eh dy vel my huyr er n'aagail y currym orryms my lomarcan  dy hirveish er y cheshaght? abbyr r'ee er-y-fa shen, ee dy chooney lhiam.  
42N||10||41||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh ree, Martha, Martha, t'ou ro-imneagh as seaghnit  mysh ymmodee nheeghyn:  
42N||10||42||Agh un red ta ymmyrchagh. As ta Moirrey er reih yn ayrn vie shen, nagh bee er ny  ghoaill ersooyl vo'ee.
42N||11||1||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh ec padjer ayns ynnyd dy row, tra daag eh jeh, dy dooyrt  fer jeh e ostyllyn rish, Hiarn ynsee dooinyn dy ghoaill padjer, myr dynsee Ean myrgeddin  da ny ynseydee echeysyn.  
42N||11||2||As dooyrt eh, Tra ghoys shiu padjer, abbyr-jee, Ayr ain t'ayns niau, Casherick dy  row dty ennym. Dy jig dty reeriaght. Dty aigney dy row jeant er y thalloo, myr te  ayns niau.
42N||11||3||Cur dooin laa Iurg laa nyn arran gagh laa.   
42N||11||4||As leih dooin nyn beccaghyn; son ta shinyn myrgeddin leih da dy chooilley unnane  ta ayns lhiastynys dooin. As ny leeid shin ayns miolagh, agh livrey shin veih olk.    
42N||11||5||As dooyrt eh roo, Quoi jiuish vees carrey echey, as hed huggey ec main-oie, as jir  rish, Charrey, eeasee dou three bwilleenyn;   
42N||11||6||Son ta dooinney-mooinjerey dou, va er e yurnah, er jeet hym, as cha vel monney aym  dy hoiaghey roish:   
42N||11||7||As freggyr-ee eshyn veih cheu-sthie gra, Ny boir mee: ta'n dorrys nish jeight, as  ta my chloan 'sy lhiabbee marym; cha voddym girree dy chur dhyt.   
42N||11||8||Ta mee gra riu, Ga nagh n'irree eh dy chur da, er-coontey dy nee e charrey eh: ny-yeih  kyndagh rish yn jeeanid echey, irree eh, as ver eh da whilleen as vees eh ny eme.    
42N||11||9||As ta mish gra riuish, Yeearree-jee, as yiow shiu: shir-jee, as nee shiu feddyn:  bee-jee aignagh fosley y gheddyn, as bee eh er ny osley diu.
42N||11||10||Son ta dy chooilley  unnane ta geearree, geddyn: as y fer ta shirrey, feddyn: as eshyn ta aignagh fosley  y gheddyn, bee eh er ny osley da.   
42N||11||11||My nee mac arran y hirrey er fer jiuish ta ny ayr, nee clagh ver eh da? ny my hirrys  eh eeast, jean eh ayns ynnyd eeast ard-nieu y chur da?   
42N||11||12||Ny my hirrys eh ooh, jeb eh scorpion da?   
42N||11||13||My ta toiggal er-y-fa shen euish, ta olk, kys dy choyrt giootyn mie da nyn gloan;  cre-woad smoo nee yn Ayr flaunyssagh eu yn Spyrryd Noo y choyrt dauesyn ta jannoo  aghin huggey?  
42N||11||14||As v'eh tilgey magh drogh-spyrryd, as v'eh balloo. As haink eh gy-kione, tra  va'n drogh-spyrryd er gholl ass dy loayr y balloo: as ghow yn pobble yindys.  
42N||11||15||Agh dooyrt paart jeu, She liorish Beelzebub, yn ard drogh-spyrryd, t'eh castey  drogh-spyrrydyn.  
42N||11||16||As va feallagh elley er-chee prowal eh shirrey er cowrey veih niau.  
42N||11||17||Agh eshyn toiggal ny smooinaghtyn oc dooyrt roo, Ta dy chooilley reeriaght ta girree-magh  n'oi hene, er ny choyrt mow: as thie ta n'oi hene goll naardey.  
42N||11||18||As my ta'n jouyl girree-magh n'oi hene, kys nee yn reeriaght echey shassoo? er-y-fa  dy vel shiu gra, dy nee liorish Beelzebub ta mish castey drogh-spyrrydyn.  
42N||11||19||As my ta mish liorish Beelzebub castey drogh-spyrrydyn, quoi liorish ta ny mec  eu hene dy chastey ad? bee adsyn er-y-fa shen ny briwnyn eu.  
42N||11||20||Agh my ta mish liorish mair Yee tilgey magh drogh-spyrrydyn, fegooish dooyt ta  reeriaght Yee er jeet erriuish.  
42N||11||21||Tra ta dooinney-caggee eillit freayll arrey er e hie, ta e chooid sauchey.  
42N||11||22||Agh tra ta fer stroshey na eh soiaghey er, as geddyn yn varriaght, t'eh goaill  veih ooilley e eilley, huggey v'eh treishteil, as t'eh rheynn e chooid.  
42N||11||23||Eshyn nagh vel lhiam, t'eh m'oi; as eshyn nagh vel chymsaghey marym, t'eh skeayley.   
42N||11||24||Tra ta'n spyrryd neu-ghlen er gholl ass dooinney, t'eh shooyll trooid faasaghyn  fadaneagh, chee aash, agh ayns fardail, eisht t'eh gra, Hem reesht gys my hie, veih  haink mee.  
42N||11||25||As tra t'eh cheet, t'eh dy gheddyn eh sceabit as soit magh dy stooamey.  
42N||11||26||Eisht t'eh goll as goaill marish shiaght spyrrydyn elley, ny smessey na eh-hene,  as t'ad goll stiagh as cummal ayns shen: as ta stayd yerrinagh yn dooinney shen ny  s'doogh na'n toshiaght.  
42N||11||27||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh loayrt ny goan shoh, dy hrog ben dy row jeh'n  cheshaght seose e coraa, as dooyrt ee rish, Bannit ta'n vrein ren oo y ymmyrkey,  as ny keeaghyn t'ou er yiole.  
42N||11||28||Agh dooyrt eshyn, Dy jarroo foddey s'bannee t'adsyn ta clashtyn goo Yee, as freayll  eh.  
42N||11||29||As tra va'n pobble er nyn jaglym chion dy cheilley, ghow eh toshiaght dy ghra,  s'drogh y cheeloghe shoh: t'ad shirrey cowrey, as cha bee cowrey er ny choyrt daue,  agh cowrey yn phadeyr Jonas.  
42N||11||30||Son myr va Jonas ny chowrey da ny Nineviteyn, er yn aght cheddin neesht vees Mac  y dooinney da'n cheeloghe shoh.  
42N||11||31||Nee ben-rein y jiass girree seose ayns briwnys noi deiney yn cheeloghe shoh, as  ad y gheyrey: son haink ish veih ardjyn sodjey magh y thallooin dy chlashtyn creenaght  Solomon; as cur-my-ner, ta fer syrjey na Solomon ayns shoh.  
42N||11||32||Nee deiney Nineveh girree seose ayns briwnys, as y cheeloghe shoh y gheyrey: son  ghow adsyn arrys ec preacheil Yonas; as cur-my-ner, ta fer syrjey na Jonas ayns shoh.   
42N||11||33||Cha vel dooinney erbee, tra t'eh er voaddey cainle, dy choyrt ee ayns ynnyd follit,  ny fo saagh; agh ayns cainleyr, dy vod adsyn ta cheet stiagh yn soilshey y akin.   
42N||11||34||Yn tooill ta cur soilshey da'n chorp: shen-y-fa tra ta dty hooill glen, bee dty  chorp ooilley ayns slane soilshey: agh tra ta lheamys er dty hooill, bee dty chorp  myrgeddin ayns slane dorraghys.   
42N||11||35||Cur twoaie er-y-fa shen nagh bee yn soilshey ta aynyd ny ghorraghys.  
42N||11||36||My ta ooilley dty chorp er-y-fa shen ayns slane soilshey, gyn dorraghys ayns ayrn  erbee, bee yn clane sollys, myr t'ou, tra ta soilshey sollys ayd veih cainle,  
42N||11||37||As myr v'eh loayrt, chuir Pharisee dy row eh gys jinnair marish: as hie eh stiagh,  as hoie eh sheese gys bee.  
42N||11||38||As tra honnick yn Pharisee shoh, ghow eh yindys nagh niee eh (e laueyn) roish jinnair.   
42N||11||39||As dooyrt y Chiarn rish, Nish ta shiuish Phariseeyn glenney yn cappan as y claare  er cheu-mooie: agh ta'n cheu-sthie eu lane dy hranlaase as dy olkys.  
42N||11||40||Gheiney vee-cheaylagh, nagh nee eshyn ren y cheu-mooie, ren y cheu-sthie myrgeddin?   
42N||11||41||Agh cur-jee lheid as t'eu da ny boghtyn: as cur-my-ner, bee dy chooilley nhee glen  diu.  
42N||11||42||Agh smerg diuish Phariseeyn: son ta shiu jagheenys mynthey, rue, as dy chooilley  horch dy lossreeyn, agh s'beg ta shiu soiaghey jeh briwnys as graih Yee: ad shoh  lhisagh shiu v'er n'yannoo, gyn faagail y chooid elley gyn jannoo.  
42N||11||43||Smerg diuish Phariseeyn: son shynney lhieu ny ard-stuill ayns ny kialteenyn, as  sleih dy vannaghey diu ayns ny margaghyn.  
42N||11||44||Smerg diuish scrudeyryn as Phariseeyn, chrauee-oalsey: son ta shiu myr oaiaghyn  nagh vel ry-akin, as ny deiney ta shooyl harrystoo, cha vel fys oc dy vel ad ayn.   
42N||11||45||Eisht dreggyr fer jeh fir-ynsee yn leigh, as dooyrt eh rish, Vainshter, liorish  shen y ghra, t'ou dy oltooan shinyn myrgeddin.  
42N||11||46||As dooyrt eh, Smerg diuish neesht fir-ynsee yn leigh son ta shiu laadey deiney  lesh erraghyn doillee dy ve er nyn ymmyrkey, as cha vel shiu hene bentyn rish ny  er raghyn lesh unnane jeh nyn meir.
42N||11||47||Smerg diuish: son ta shiu troggal lhiaghtyn ny phadeyryn, as ny ayraghyn eu ren  y varroo ad.
42N||11||48||Dy firrinagh ta shiu gymmyrkey feanish dy vel shiu lowal jeh jannoo ny ayraghyn  eu: son ren adsyn dy jarroo y varroo ad, as ta shiuish coamrey ny lhiaghtyn oc.   
42N||11||49||As shoh yn oyr ta creenaght Yee er ghra, Ver-ym huc phadeyryn, as ostyllyn, as  paart jeu nee ad y varroo, as tranlaase y yannoo orroo:  
42N||11||50||Dy vod fuill ooilley ny phadeyryn v'er ny gheayrtey er-dy hoshiaght y theihll v'er  ny chooilleeney er y cheeloghe shoh   
42N||11||51||Veih fuill Abel gys fuill Zacharias ren cherraghtyn eddyr yn altar as y chiamble:  dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy bee eh er ny chooilleeney er y cheeloghe shoh.  
42N||11||52||Smerg diu fir-ynsee yn leigh: son ta shiu er ghoaill ersooyl ogher yn ysseree:  cha jagh shiu stiagh shiu hene, as adsyn va goll stiagh, ren shiu y lhiettal.  
42N||11||53||As tra v'eh er ghra ny reddyn shoh roo, ren ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn toshiaght  dy eginaghey, as dy ghreinnaghey eh dy loayrt jeh ymmodee reddyn:  
42N||11||54||Lhie ayns farkiaght er e hon, as shegin er tayrtyn red ennagh ass e veeal son oyr  plaiynt n'oi.                
42N||12||1||Nish mysh y traa shen va ymmodee erskyn-earroo dy leih er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, ayns  wheesh as dy row ad stampey yn derrey yeh er yn jeh elley, ghow eh toshiaght dy ghra  rish e ostyllyn, Erskyn ooilley bee-jee twoaiagh jeh soorid ny Phariseeyn, ta shen  dy ghra, craueeaght oalsey.  
42N||12||2||Son cha vel nhee erbee follit nagh jig gys soilshey; ny kiellit, nagh jig er-ash.   
42N||12||3||Shen-y-fa cre-erbee ta shiuish er loayrt ayns y dorraghys, bee eh er ny chlashtyn  ayns y toilshey: as shen ta shiu er ghra myr hannish, ayns shamyryn, bee eh er ny  ockley magh er mullagh ny dhieyn.  
42N||12||4||As ta mee gra riuish, my chaarjyn, Ny gow-jee aggle rouesyn varrys y corp, as ny  lurg shen nagh vel arragh oc oddys ad y vannoo.  
42N||12||5||Agh ver-yms raaue diu quoi roish ghoys shiu aggle: Gow-jee aggle roishyn, echey  ta pooar, erreish da v'er varroo dy hilgey ayns niurin; dy jarroo ta mee dy ghra  riu, Gow jee aggle roishyn.  
42N||12||6||Nagh vel queig sperriu er nyn greck son daa farling, as cha vel unnane oc jarroodit  kiongoyrt rish Jee?  
42N||12||7||Agh ta eer renaigyn nyn ghing ooilley er nyn earroo. Ny gow-jee aggle er-y-fa shen:  ta ny smoo dy ve soit jiuish, na jeh ymmodee sperriu.  
42N||12||8||Myrgeddin ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee ghoys rhyms kiongoyrt rish deiney, nee yn Mac  dooinney myrgeddin goaill rishyn kiongoyrt rish ainleyn Yee. 
42N||12||9||Agh bee eshyn obbys mie fenish deiney, er ny obbal fenish ainleyn Yee.  
42N||12||10||As  quoi-erbee loayrys fockle noi Mac y dooinney, bee eh er ny leih da: agh dasyn ta  loayrt goan-mollaghtagh noi yn Spyrryd Noo, cha bee eh er ny leih.   
42N||12||11||As tra ver ad lhieu shiu gys ny quaiylyn, as gys fir-reill as pooaraghyn, ny bee-jee  imneagh kys ny cre nee shiu y reggyrt, ny cre nee shiu y ghra:   
42N||12||12||Son ynsee yn Spyrryd Noo diu, ayns yn oor cheddin cre lhisagh shiu y ghra.  
42N||12||13||As dooyrt fer jeh'n cheshaght rish Vainshter, loayr rish my vraar eh dy rheynn  yn eiraght rhym.  
42N||12||14||As dooyrt eh rish, Ghooinney, quoi t'er my hoiaghey's seose son briw ny rheynneyder  harrishdiu?  
42N||12||15||As dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee tastey, as cur-jee twoaie jeh saynt: son cha vel maynrys  bea yn dooinney lhie ayns mooarane e chooid-seihlt.  
42N||12||16||As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, gra, Ren thalloo dooinney berchagh dy row mess  y chur magh dy palchey.  
42N||12||17||As smooinee eh rish hene, gra, Cre share dou jannoo, tra nagh vel boayl tashtee  aym dy ghoaill my hroar?  
42N||12||18||Eisht dooyrt eh, Shoh nee'm y yannoo: Lhieg-ym my hoaltyn, as trog-ym soaltyn smoo;  as shen y raad nee'm ooilley my vess as my chooid y hashtey.  
42N||12||19||As jir-ym rish my annym, O my annym, ta mooarane cooid ayd tashtit seose cour ymmodee  bleeantyn: gow dty aash, ee, iu, as bee gennal.  
42N||12||20||Agh dooyrt Jee rish, Uss ommydan yn oie noght vees dty annym er ny ghoaill void:  quoi lesh eisht vees yn chooid shen t'ou uss er jaglym?  
42N||12||21||Myr shoh ta eshyn ta tashtey seose berchys ny chour hene, as nagh vel berchagh  ass lieh Yee.  
42N||12||22||As dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Shen y fa ta mish gra riuish, Ny bee-jee imneagh  son nyn mea, cre nee shiu y ee: ny son nyn girp, cre ver shiu miu.  
42N||12||23||Ta'n vea ny smoo dy ve soit jeh na beaghey, as y corp na coamrey.  
42N||12||24||Smooinee-jee er ny fee: son cha vel ad cuirr, ny buinn: cha vel thie stoyr ny soalt  oc, as ta Jee dyn meaghey ad: As nagh vel shiuish foddey share na ny eeanlee?  
42N||12||25||Quoi jiuish liorish smooinaghtyn dy imneagh oddys un chubit y chur gys e yrjid  hene?  
42N||12||26||Mannagh vod shiuish wheesh shen hene y yannoo, cre'n-fa ta shiu imneagh son y chooid  elley?  
42N||12||27||Gow-jee tastey jeh lileeyn ny magher agh kys t'ad gaase, cha vel ad tooilleil,  chamoo t'ad sneeu: as foast ta mee gra riu, nagh row Solomon ayns ooilley e ghloyr  er ny choamrey myr unnane jeu shoh.  
42N||12||28||My ta Jee eisht myr shoh coamrey blaa ny magheragh, ta jiu 'sy vagher, as mairagh  ceaut ayns yn oghe: nagh jean eh foddey smoo er nyn son euish, O gheiney faase-chredjuagh?   
42N||12||29||As ny bee-jee seaghnit mysh cre ee-ys, ny cre iu-ys shiu, chamoo bee-jee jeh aigney  imneagh nagh bee eh twoaiagh jeh, as giaree eh eh veih my-cheilley, as pointee eh  e chronney marish y vooinjer vee-chredjuagh. 
42N||12||30||Son er ooilley ny reddyn shoh ta ashoonyn y theihll dy jeean aggindagh: agh ta  fys ec yn Ayr eu dy vel shiu feme ny reddyn shoh.  
42N||12||31||Agh shir-jee hoshiaght reeriaght Yee, as bee shiu jeant magh lesh ooilley ny  reddyn shoh.  
42N||12||32||Ny gow-jee aggle my hioltane veg; son she aigney-mie nyn Ayr eh; dy chur diuish  yn reeriaght.  
42N||12||33||Creck-jee ny t'eu, as cur-jee da ny boghtyn: kiare-jee diu hene sporranyn nagh  naase shenn, berchys ayns ny niaughyn nagh vel failleil, raad nagh vel y maarliagh  cheet er-gerrey, ny'n lhemeen cur mow.  
42N||12||34||Son raad ta nyn merchys, shen y raad vees y cree eu myrgeddin.
42N||12||35||Lhig da ny meeghyn eu ve cryssit, as ny cainleyn eu foaddit;  
42N||12||36||As shiu hene goll-rish deiney ta farkiaght son cheet-thie nyn Jiarn veih'n vannish,  ec y cheet echey tra nee eh cronkal dy vod ad fosley da chelleeragh.  
42N||12||37||Bannit ta ny sharvaantyn shen yiow yn Chiarn er nyn arrey, tra hig eh: dy firrinagh  ta mee gra riu, dy gryss eh e gharmad mysh, as dy der eh orroo soie sheese gys bee,  as dy jig eh magh dy hirveish orroo.  
42N||12||38||As my hig eh ayns yn nah arrey, ny my hig eh ayns y trass arrey, as ad y gheddyn  myr shen, bannit ta'n vooinjer cheddin.  
42N||12||39||As shoh toig-jee, dy beagh fys er ve ec mainshter y thie cre'n oor veagh y maarliagh  er jeet, veagh eh er ve er e arrey, as cha lhiggagh eh da e hie v'er ny vrishey stiagh.   
42N||12||40||Bee-jee shiuish myrgeddin er-y-fa shen er nyn arrey: son hig Mac y dooinney ec  oor nagh vel shiu smooinaghtyn er.  
42N||12||41||Eisht dooyrt Peddyr rish, Hiarn nee orrinyn t'ou cheet 'sy choraa-dorraghey shoh,  ny myrgeddin er ooilley?  
42N||12||42||As dooyrt y Chiarn, Quoi eisht yn stiurt firrinagh as creeney shen nee e hiarn  y yannoo ny er-reill er lught e hie, dy hirveish orroo nyn meaghey ayns traa cooie?   
42N||12||43||S'maynrey yn charvaant cheddin, yiow e hiarn tra hig eh jannoo myr shen.  
42N||12||44||Ayns firrinys ta mee gra riu, dy der eh da yn stiurtys er ooilley e chooid.  
42N||12||45||Agh my jir y charvaant shen ayns e chree, Ta my hiarn lhiggey shaghey dy heet;  as goaill er dy woalley ny fir-vooinjerey, as ny inneenyn, as dy ee, as dy iu, as  dy ve er meshtey.  
42N||12||46||Hig chiarn y charvaant shen ec laa nagh bee eh jeeaghyn er e hon, as ayns oor  nagh bee eh twoaiagh jeh, as giaree ehe eh veih my-cheilley, as pointee eh e chronney  marish y vooinjer vee-chredjuagh. 
42N||12||47||As y charvaant shen va toiggal aigney e hiarn, as nagh dooar eh-hene aarloo, as  nagh ren cordail rish e aigney, s'mooar vees y kerraghey echey. 
42N||12||48||Agh eshyn nagh row toiggal, as ren foiljyn va toilliu kerraghey, cha bee yn kerraghey  echey cha trome. Son da quoi erbee ta mooarane er ny choyrt, ersyn vees mooarane  er ny hirrey: as da quoi-erbee ta lane currit er e churrym, veihsyn nee sleih jeeaghyn son ny smoo 
42N||12||49||Haink mish dy chur aile er y thalloo, as cre ta my yeearree, agh dy bee eh hannah  er ny oaddey?  
42N||12||50||Agh ta bashtey ayms dy ve er my vashtey lesh, as kys ta mee eginit, derrey vees  eh er ny chooilleeney?  
42N||12||51||Vel shiu smooinaghtyn dy daink mish dy chur shee er y thalloo? Cha nee, ta mee  gra riu, agh anvea.  
42N||12||52||Son veih shoh magh bee queig ayns un thie noi-ry-hoi, three noi jees, as jees noi  three.  
42N||12||53||Bee yn ayr noi yn mac, as y mac noi yn ayr; yn voir noi yn inneen, as yn inneen  noi yn voir yn voir-'sy-leigh noi e ben chleuin, as y ven-chleuin noi e moir-'sy-leigh.   
42N||12||54||As dooyrt eh myrgeddin rish y pobble, Tra heeys shiu bodjal troggal ass y sheear;  chelleeragh ta shiu gra, Ta frass cheet; as shen myr te.  
42N||12||55||As tra ta'n gheay-jiass sheidey, ta shiu gra, Bee chiass ayn, as te cheet gy-kione.   
42N||12||56||Chrauee-oalsey, ta shiu son baght y ghoaill jeh neeal yn aer as y thalloo: agh  kys te nagh vel shiu goaill baght jeh'n earish shoh? 
42N||12||57||As cre'n-fa myrgeddin nagh vel shiu eer j'iu hene briwnys shen ny ta cairagh?    
42N||12||58||Tra t'ou goll fenish yn er-reill marishyn ta ec streeu rhyt, jean ny oddys oo  er y raad dy gheddyn rea rish; er-aggle dy dayrn eh lesh oo gys y vriw, as dy livrey  yn briw oo da'n tidoor, as dy dilg eh shen oo ayns pryssoon.  
42N||12||59||Ta mee ginsh dhyt, nagh jig oo magh ass shen derrey t'ou er n'eeck yn farling s'jerree.
42N||13||1||Va kionfenish ec y traa shen paart dinsh  y da mychione ny Galileanee, yn uill oc  va Pilate er gheayrtey maStey (filill) ny ourallyn oc.  
42N||13||2||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiuish sheiltyn dy row ny Galileanee shoh  nyn beccee erskyn ooilley ny Galileanee, er-y-fa dy duillee ad lheid y baase?  
42N||13||3||Ta mee ginsh diu, Nagh row: agh mannagh gow shiuish arrys, nee shiu ooilley myrgeddin  cherraghtyn.  
42N||13||4||Ny yn hoght-jeig shen, orroo ren y toor nyns Siloam tuittym, as ad y varroo, vel  shiu smooinaghtyn dy row ad nyn beccee erskyn ooilley cummaltee Yerusalem?   
42N||13||5||Ta mee ginsh diu, Nagh row: agh mannagh gow shiuish arrys, nee shiu ooilley myrgeddin  cherraghtyn.   
42N||13||6||Loayr eh myrgeddin yn coraa-dorraghey shoh: va dooinoey dy row va billey-figgagh  echey soit ayns e gharey-feeyney, as haink eh dy yeeaghyn row mess er, as cha dooar  eh veg.   
42N||13||7||Eisht dooyrt eh rish y ghareyder, Cur-my-ner, ny three bleeaney shoh ta mee er jeet  dy yeeaghyn voin mess er y villey-figgagh shoh, as cha vel mee geddyn veg: giare  sheese eh, cha vel eh agh goaill seose room hallooin.   
42N||13||8||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, lhig da shassoo blein elley, derrey neem's  reurey mygeayrt y mysh as lhiassaghey eh.   
42N||13||9||As my nee eh mess y ymmyrkey, s'mie shen: as mannagh jean, foddee oo ny lurg shen  y ghiarey sheese eh.    
42N||13||10||As v'eh gynsaghey ayns unnane jeh ny synagogueyn er y doonaght.   
42N||13||11||As cur-my-ner va ben ayns shen seaghnit lesh spyrryd doghanagh rish hoght bleeaney  jeig, as v'ee crybbit dy cheilley, as cha dod ee er aght erbee ec hene y yeeraghey.    
42N||13||12||As tra honnick Yeesey ee, deie eh urree huggey, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Ven, t'ou er  dty eaysley veih dty ghoghan.   
42N||13||13||As hug eh e laueyn urree; as er-y chooyl v'ee er ny yannoo jeeragh, as ren ee Jee  y ghloyraghey.   
42N||13||14||As dreggyr fer-reill yn synagogue lesh jymmoose, er-yn-oyr dy row Yeesey er lheihys  er laa yn doonaght, as dooyrt eh rish y pobble, Ta shey laa ayn ry-hoi gobbraghey:  er ny laghyn shen er-y-fa shen tar-jee dy ve er nyn lheihys, as cha nee er laa yn  doonaght.   
42N||13||15||Eisht dreggyr y Chiarn eh, gra, Er crauee-oalsey, nagh vel dagh fer jiuish er y  doonaght feaysley e ghow ny e assyl veih'n staik, as dy chur lesh magh dy ushtaghey  eh?   
42N||13||16||As nagh lhisagh y ven shoh ta ny hinneen da Abraham, ee ta satan er chiangley,  cur-my-ner ny hoght bleeaney jeig shoh, ve er ny eaysley veih yn vondiaght shoh er  laa yn doonaght?    
42N||13||17||As tra v'eh er loayrt ny goan shoh, ghow ooilley e noidyn nearey: agh va ooilley  yn pobble ayns ard-voggey son ooilley ny reddyn gloyroil va jeant liorishyn.   
42N||13||18||Eisht dooyrt eh, Cre ta reeriaght Yee goll-rish? as cre gys nee'm y hoylaghey  eh?   
42N||13||19||Te goll-rish grine dy rass mustard, ren dooinney y ghoaill, as y hilgey ayns e  gharey, as daase eh, as haink eh dy ve ny villey vooar: as ren eeanlee yn aer fastee  y ghoaill ayns ny banglaneyn echey. 
42N||13||20||As reesht dooyrt eh, Cre gys nee'm reeriaght Yee y hoylaghey?  
42N||13||21||Te goll-rish soorid, ren ben y ghoaill as follaghey ayns three towseyn dy veinn,  derrey va'n clane soorit.  
42N||13||22||As hie eh magh trooid ny ard-valjyn as ny baljyn-cheerey, gynsaghey as goll er  e hoshiaght gys Jerusalem.  
42N||13||23||Eisht dooyrt fer rish, Hiarn, nee beggan ta er nyn sauail? As dooyrt eh roo.  
42N||13||24||Streeu-jee shiuush dy gholl stiagh er y ghiat coon: son nee ymmodee, ta mee gra  riu, shirrey goll stiagh, agh cha jig eh lhieu. 
42N||13||25||Keayrt dy vel mainshter y thie er n'irree, as y dorrys dooint, as dy jean shiuish  toshiaght dy hassoo er cheu-mooie, as dy chronkal ec y dorrys, gra, Hiarn, Hiarn,  foshil dooin; as freggyree eshyn as jir eh riu, Cha nione dou shiu, cre veih ta shiu:   
42N||13||26||Eisht gowee shiuish toshiaght dy ghra, Ta shin er n'ee as er n'iu ayns dty enish,  as t'ou er n'ynsaghey ayns ny straidyn ain.  
42N||13||27||Agh jir eshyn, Ta mee ginsh diu, nagh nione dou shiu, cre veih ta shiu: ersooyl-jee  voym ooilley shiuish ghrogh-yantee.  
42N||13||28||Shen-y-raad vees keayney as snaggeraght feeacklyn, tra hee shiu Abraham, aa Isaac  as Jacob as ooilley ny phadeyryn ayns reeriaght Yee, as shiu hene er nyn yioolaey  magh.  
42N||13||29||As hig ad veih'n niar, as veih'n neear, as veih'n twoaie as veih'n jiass, as soie-ee  ad sheese ayns reeriaght-Yee.  
42N||13||30||As cur-my-ner, ta er-jerrey vees hoshiaght, as ta hoshiaght vees er-jerrey.  
42N||13||31||Yn laa cheddin, haink shiartanse jeh ny Phariseeyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Fow ersooyl,  as immee royd veih shoh; son ta Herod sleeuit er dty rioys y ghoaill.   
42N||13||32||As dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee shiuish as insh-jee da'n shynnagh shen, Cur-my-ner,  ta mee castey drogh-spyrrydyn, as lheihys doghanyn jiu as mairagh, as y trass laa  bee'm er my ghloyraghey.  
42N||13||33||Ny yeih, Shegin dou shooyl jiu as mairagh, as y laa er-giyn: son s'coan oddys phadeyr  cherraghtyn agh ayns Jerusalem.  
42N||13||34||O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, ta cur dy baase ny phadeyryn, as dyn glaghey adsyn t'er  nyn goyrt er chaghteraght hood: cre cha mennick as va mish aggindagh v'er hagIym  dty chloan cooidjagh, myr ta kiark clussaghey e aalagh fo my skianyn, agh cha bailliu  shen!  
42N||13||35||Cur-my-ner, ta'n thie eu faagit diu follym-faase: as dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu,  nagh vaik shiu mish maghey shoh, derrey hig yn traa dy jir shiu, Bannit ta eshyn  ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn. 
42N||14||1||As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er gholl stiagh ayns thie fer jeh ny ard Phariseeyn  dy ee arran er y doonaght, dy row sooill oc er. 
42N||14||2||As cur-my-ner, va dooinney kionfenish, va'n dropsee er.  
42N||14||3||As dreggyr Yeesey, as loayr eh rish fir-ynsee yn leigh as rish ny Phariseeyn, gra,  Vel eh lowal dy lheihys er laayn doonaght? 
42N||14||4||As v'ad nyn-dhost. As ghow eh as laanee eh eh, as lhig eh yn raad da:  
42N||14||5||As dreggyr eh ad, gra, Quoi j'iu vees dow ny assyl echey er huittym ayns jeeg, nagh  jean jeeragh y hayrn ass eh er y doonaght?  
42N||14||6||As cha row ansoor erbee oc dy choyrt gys ny goan shoh.  
42N||14||7||As loayr eh coraa-dorraghey rish ny goaldee, tra hug eh tastey kys v'ad reih ny  stuill byrjey; gra roo,  
42N||14||8||Tra t'ou cuirt liorish dooinney erbee gys bannish, ny soie sheese er y stoyl syrjey;  er-aggle dy bee dooinney s'ooasle na uss er ny chuirrey liorish;   
42N||14||9||As dy jig eshyn ren shiu nyn neesht y chuirrey, as dy jir eh rhyt, Cur raad da'n  dooinney shoh; as dy jean oo toshiaght lesh nearey dy ghoaill y stoyl s'inshley.    
42N||14||10||Agh tra vees oo cuirt, immee, as soie sheese er y stoyl s'inshley; tra hig eshyn  ren dty chuirrey, dy vod eh gra rhyt, Charrey, gow seose ny syrjey: eisht bee ooashley  ayd ayns yn enish ocsyn ta nyn soie ec bee mayrt:  
42N||14||11||Son quoi-erbee ta dy hoiaghey eh-hene seose, bee eh er ny injillaghey; as eshyn  ta dy injillaghey eh-hene, bee eh er ny hoiaghey seose.  
42N||14||12||Eisht dooyrt eh rishyn ren y chuirrey eh, Tra t'ou jannoo jinnair ny shibber,  ny cuir dty chaarjyn, ny dty vraaraghyn, ny dty gheiney-mooinjerey, ny dty naboonyn  berchagh; er-aggle dy jean adsyn oo y chuirrey reesht, as dy bee lhiassaghey er ny  yannoo dhyt.   
42N||14||13||Agh tra t'ou jannoo cuirraghyn, eie er ny boghtyn, ny baccee, ny croobee, as ny  doail:  
42N||14||14||As bee oo bannit; son cha vod adsyn cooilleeney 'chur dhyt: son bee oo cooilleenit  ec irree-reesht y chloan chairagh.  
42N||14||15||As tra cheayll fer jeusyn va nyn soie ec bee marish ny goan shoh, dooyrt eh rish,  Bannit ta eshyn ee-ys arran ayns reeriaght Yee.  
42N||14||16||Eisht dooyrt eh rish, Ren dooinney dy row shibber vooar, as chuir eh ymmodee:   
42N||14||17||As hug eh magh e harvaant ec traa shibberagh dy ghra rish ny goaldee, Tar-jee,  son ta dy chooilley nhee nish aarloo.  
42N||14||18||As ren ad ooilley toshiaght lesh un aigney dy yannoo leshtalyn. Dooyrt y chied  er, Ta mee er chionnaghey peesh dy halloo, as shegin dou goll dy yeeaghyn er: guee-ym  ort, jean my leshtal.  
42N||14||19||As dooyrt fer elley, Ta mee er chionnaghey queig chubbil dy ghew, as ta mee goll  dy phowal ad: ta mee guee ort jean my leshtal. 
42N||14||20||As dooyrt fer elley, Ta mee er phoosey ben, as er-y-fa shen cha voddym cheet.   
42N||14||21||Myr shen haink y charvaant cheddin, as hoilshee eh da e hiarn ny reddyn shoh. Eisht  va mainshter y thie jymmoosagh, as dooyrt eh rish e harvaant, Gow magh dy tappee  gys straidyn as raaidyn yn ard-valley, as cur lhiat stiagh ayns shoh ny boghtyn,  as ny baccee, as ny croobee, as ny doail:  
42N||14||22||As dooyrt y charvaant, Hiarn, te jeant myr t'ou er harey, as foast ta room.  
42N||14||23||As dooyrt y chiarn rish y charvaant, Gow magh gys ny raaidyn mooarey as ny cleigh,  as guee orroo dy heet stiagh, dy vod my hie ve er ny lhieeney.  
42N||14||24||Son ta mee gra riu, nagh jean fer jeh ny deiney va cuirt, blashtyn jeh my hibber,   
42N||14||25||As hie earrooyn mooarey dy leih marish: as hyndaa eh, as dooyrt eh roo,  
42N||14||26||My hig dooinney erbee hym's, as nagh vel graih sloo echey er e ayr as e voir, as  e ven, as e chloan, as e vraaraghyn, as e hayraghyn, dy jarroo, as er e vioys hene  (na orrym's) cha vod eh dy firrinagh gynsaghey voym's.  
42N||14||27||As quoi-erbee nagh vel gymmyrkey e chrosh, as cheet geiyrt orrym's, cha vod eh  ve ny eiyrtyssagh dooys.  
42N||14||28||Quoi jiuish ta kiarail toor y hroggal, nagh vel soie sheese hoshiaght, as coontey  yn cost, vel wheesh echey as ver mullagh er?  
42N||14||29||Er-aggle erreish da yn undin y boiaghey, as nagh vel yn fort echey dy chur kione  er, dy jean ooilley nee fakin eh toshiaght dy chraidey mysh,  
42N||14||30||Gra, Ren y dooinney shoh toshiaght dy vuildal, as cha row fort echey kione y cur  er e obbyr.  
42N||14||31||Ny cre'n ree ragh dy yannoo caggey noi ree elley, nagh soiagh sheese hoshiaght  dy ghoaill coyrle, vel eh son goll magh lesh jeih thousaneyn ny whail echeysyn ta  cheet n'oi lesh feed thousane?  
42N||14||32||Er-nonney, choud as ta'n ree elley foddey veih, t'eh cur chaghteraght huggey, as  chebbal conaantyn shee.  
42N||14||33||Myr shen myrgeddin quoi-erbee jiuish, nagh vel treigeil ooilley ny t'echey, cha  vod eh ve ny eiyrtyssagh dooys.  
42N||14||34||Ta sollan mie: agh my ta'n sollan er choayl e vlass, kys hig e vree ayn reesht?   
42N||14||35||Cha vel ymmyd ayn son y thalloo, ny foast son y torran; agh ta deiney dy cheau  magh eh. Eshyn ta cleayshyn echey dy chlashtyn, lhig da clashtyn.
42N||15||1||Eisht haink er-gerrey da ooilley ny publicanee as ny peccee dy eaishtagh; rish.  
42N||15||2||As ren ny Phariseeyn as ny scrudeyryn tallagh, gra, Ta'n dooinney shoh goaill rish  peccee, as gee maroo.
42N||15||3||as loayr eh yn coraa-dorraghey shoh roo, gra,  
42N||15||4||Quoi yn dooinney ny mast' euish ta keead keyrrey echey, as coayl unnane jeu nagh  vel eh faagail yn chiare-feed as yn nuy jeig ayns yn aasagh, as goll dy hirrey yn  cheyrrey chailjey, derrey t'eh dy gheddyn ee?  
42N||15||5||As tra t'eh er gheddyn ee, t'eh dy choyrt ee er e gheayltyn, goaill boggey.  
42N||15||6||As tra t'eh cheet thie, t'eh geamagh er e chaarjyn as e naboonyn cooidjagh, as gra  roo, Gow-Jee boggey marym, son ta mee er gheddyn my cheyrrey va caillit.  
42N||15||7||Ta mee gra riu, dy bee boggey myrgeddin ayns niau, jeh un pheccagh ta goaill arrys,  ny smoo na jeh kiare-feed as nuy persoonyn jeig cairagh, nagh vel feme arrys.  
42N||15||8||Ny cre'n ven ta jeih peeshyn dy argid eck, as ee dy choayl un pheesh, nagh vel  ee foaddey cainle, as sceabey yn thie, as shirrey dy kiaralagh, derrey t'ee dy gheddyn  eh?   
42N||15||9||As tra t'ee er gheddyn eh, t'ee geamagh er e caarjyn as e naboonyn cooidjagh, gra,  Gow-jee boggey marym, son ta mee er gheddyn yn pheesh ren mee y choayl.   
42N||15||10||Myrgeddin ta mee gra riu, dy vel boggey ayns fenish ainleyn Yee jeh un pheccagh  ta goaill arrys.  
42N||15||11||As dooyrt eh, Va daa vac ec dooinney dy row:  
42N||15||12||A s dooyrt y fer saa rish e ayr, Ayr, cur dooys yn ayrn dy chooid ta my chour.   As rheynn eh e eh chooid orroo.  
42N||15||13||As laghyn ny lurg shen, hymsee yn mac saa ooilley cooidjagh as ghow eh jurnah gys  cheer foddey, as ayns shen hug eh jummal er e chooid liorish baghey rouanagh.  
42N||15||14||As tra va ooilley baarit echey, dirree genney vooar ayns y cheer shen; as ren eh  toshiaght dy ve ayns feme.  
42N||15||15||As hie eh as daill eh eh-hene rish cummaltagh jeh'n cheer shen; as hug eshyn eh  magh gys ny magheryn echey dy ve son bochilley muickey.  
42N||15||16||As by-vian lesh e volg y lhieeney lesh ny bleaystyn va ny muckyn dy ee: as cha  row dooinney erbee hug cooney da.  
42N||15||17||As tra v'eh er jeet huggey hene, dooyrt eh, Nagh nhimmey sharvaant failt t'ec my  ayr ta nyn saie arran oc, as fooilliagh, as ta mish goll mow laccal beaghey!  
42N||15||18||Trog-ym orrym, as hem roym gys my ayr, as jir-ym rish, Ayr, ta mee er n'yannoo  peccah noi niau, as kiongoyrt rhyt's,  
42N||15||19||As cha vel mee ny-sodjey feeu dy ve enmyssit dty vac: dell rhym myr
42N||15||19||rish fer jeh dty harvaantyn sailt.  
42N||15||20||As hrog eh er, as haink eh gys e ayr. Agh tra v'eh foast foddey veih, honnick e  ayr eh, as va chymmey echey er, as roie eh, as ghow eh eh ayns e roihaghyn as phaag  eh eh.
42N||15||21||As dooyrt y mac rish, Ayr, ta mee er n'yannoo peccah noi niau, as ayns dty hilley's,  as cha vel mee ny-sodjey feeu dy ve enmyssit dty vac.  
42N||15||22||Agh dooyrt yn ayr rish e harvaantyn, Cur-jee lhieu magh yn coamrey share, as cur-jee  er eh, as cur-jee fainey er e laue, as braagyn er e chassyn.  
42N||15||23||As cur-jee lhieu ayns shoh yn lheiy beiyht, as marr-jee eh; as lhig dooin gee as  ve gennal.  
42N||15||24||Son v'eh shoh my vac marroo, as t'eh bio reesht; v'eh caillit, as t'eh er ny gheddyn  reesht. As ren ad toshiaght dy yannoo gien mie.  
42N||15||25||Nish va'n mac shinney mooie 'sy vagher: as tra haink eh er-gerrey da'n thie, cheayll  eh kiaulleeaght as daunsin.  
42N||15||26||As deie eh er fer jeh'n vooinjer, as denee eh cre son va shoh.  
42N||15||27||As dooyrt eh rish, Ta dty vraar er jeet thie; as ta dty ayr er varroo yn lheiy  beiyht, er-yn-oyr dy vel eh er jeet thie huggey slane follan.  
42N||15||28||As v'eh feer chorree, as cha baillish goll stiagh: shen-y-fa haink e ayr magh,  as vreag eh eh.  
42N||15||29||As dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh rish e ayr, Cur-my-ner, ta mish rish whilleen blein  shen ayns dty hirveish, chamoo ren mee rieau noi dty aigney, as foast cha dug oo  dou rieau wheesh mannan, dy yannoo gien marish my gheiney-mooinjerey:  
42N||15||30||Agh cha leah as v'eh shoh dty vac er jeet, ta er vaarail dty chooid er streebeeyn  t'ou er varroo er e hon yn lheiy beiyht.  
42N||15||31||As dooyrt eh rish, Vac, t'ou er ny ve kinjagh marym, as lhiat's ooilley ny t'aym.   
42N||15||32||Ve cooie dooin ve gennal, as boggey y ghoaill: son v'eh shoh dty vraar marroo as  t'eh bio reesht: v'eh caillit, as t'eh er ny gheddyn.
42N||16||1||AS dooyrt eh myrgeddin rish e ostyllyn, Va dooinney berchagh dy row as stiurt echey,  va er ny chassid huggey son jummal e chooid.  
42N||16||2||As deie eh er, as dooyrt eh rish, Kys dy vel mee clashtyn shoh jeed? cur coontey  jeh dty stiurtys: son cha vod oo ve ny sodjey dty stiurt,  
42N||16||3||Eisht dooyrt y stiurt rish hene, Cre nee'm? son ta my hiarn goaill y stiurtys voym:  cha voddym reurey, as dy huill ny dhieyn ta nearey orrym.  
42N||16||4||Shoh ta mee kiarail dy yannoo tra chaill-ym y stiurtys, dy vod paart jeu goaill  mee stiagh ayns ny thieyn oc.  
42N||16||5||Er shoh deie eh orroosyn ooilley v'ayns lhiastynys da e hiarn, as dooyrt eh rish  y chied er, Cre-woad t'ou uss dy lhiastyn dy my hiarn?  
42N||16||6||As dooyrt eh, Keead towse dy ooil As dooyrt eh rish, Gow dty lioar, as soie sheese-dy  tappee, as scrieu jeih as da-eed.  
42N||16||7||As doogrt eh rish fer elley, As cre-woad t'ou uss dy lhiastyn? As dooyrt eh, Keead  owse dy churnaght. As dooyrt eh rish,Gow dty lioar as scrieu kiare-feed.
42N||16||8||As voyll y chiarn y stiurt neu-chairagh, er-y-fa dy row eh er n'yannoo  dy creeney:  son ta cloan y theihll shoh ayns nyn sheeloghe ny s'creeney na cloan y toilshey.
42N||16||9||As ta mee gra riu, Jean-jee diu hene caarjyn liorish y mammon molteyragh; tra nee  shiu failleil dy vod ad shiu y ghoaill stiagh gys ny ynnydyn vaghee dy bragh farraghtyn.
42N||16||10||Eshyn ta ynrick ayns yn nhee s'fardalee, t'eh ynrick myrgeddin ayns mooarane: as  eshyn ta neu-charragh ayns y nhee s'fadalee, t'eh neu-chairagh myrgeddin ayns mooarane.
42N||16||11||Mannagh vel shiu er-y-fa shen er ve ynrick ayns y mammon molteyragh, quoi ver yn  verchys firrinagh fo nyn gurrym?
42N||16||12||As mannagh vel shiu er ve firrinagh ayns ny ta lesh dooinney elley, quoi ver diu  ny vees lhieu hene?
42N||16||13||Cha vod sharvaant erbee daa vainshter y hirveish: son eddyr ver eh feoh da'n  derrey yeh as graih da'n jeh elley; er nonney cummee eh gys y derrey yeh, as soie-ee  eh beg jeh'n jeh elley. Cha vod shiu Jee as mammon y hirveish.
42N||16||14||As cheayll ny Phariseeyn myrgeddin va sayntoilagh, ooilley ny reddyn shoh: as ren  ad gannidys er.
42N||16||15||As dooyrt eh roo, Shiuish yn vooinjer ta dy heyrey shiu hene kiongoyrt rish deiney:  agh ta fys ec Jee er ny creeaghyn eu: son ta shen ta dy mooar soit jeh mastey deiney,  feohdoil ayns shilley Yee.
42N||16||16||Va'n leigh as ny phadeyryn derrey Ean: er-dyn traa shen, ta reeriaght Yee er ny  phreacheil, as ta dy chooilley ghooinney chionney stiagh huggey.
42N||16||17||Agh te ny sassey da'n aer as da'n thalloo dy herraghtyn, na da un floag jeh'n leigh  dy ailleil.
42N||16||18||Quoi-erbee scarrys rish e ven, as phoosys ben elley, t'eh brishey poosey: as quoi-erbee  phoosys ish ta scarrit veih e sheshey, t'eh brishey poosey.
42N||16||19||Va dooinney berchagh dy row va coamrit ayns gorrym-jiarg, as sheeidey, as farrail  dy soaillagh dy chooilley laa.
42N||16||20||As va boght dy row va enmyssit Lazarus, va ny lhie ec y ghiat echey lane dy hingyn,
42N||16||21||As geearree dy ve jeant magh lesh y vrooillagh va tuittym jeh boayrd y dooinney  berchagh: agh haink ny eer moddee as sliee ad ny chingyn echey.
42N||16||22||As haink eh gy-kione, dy dooar y dooinney boght baase, as dy dug dy ainleyn lhieu  eh gys oghrish Abraham: hooar y dooinney berchagh myrgeddin baase, as v'eh er ny  oanluckey.
42N||16||23||As ayns niurin, raad v'eh er ny horchaghey, hrog eh seose e hooillyn, as honnick  eh Abraham foddey veih, as Lazarus ayns e oghrish. 
42N||16||24||As deie eh as dooyrt eh, Ayr Abraham, jean myghin orrym, as cur Lazarus, dy vod  eh baare e vair y hummey ayns ushtey, as my hengey y eayraghey; son ta mee er my  horchaghey ayns y lossey shoh.  
42N||16||25||Agh dooyrt Abrabam, Vac, cooinee uss ayns earish dty vea dy row ayd's dy chooilley  nhee mie, as myrgeddin ec Lazarus cha row monney agh seaghyn: agh nish t'eshyn er  ny gherjaghey, as t'ou uss er dty horchaghey,  
42N||16||26||As marish shoh ooilley, ta eddyr shinyn as shiuish diunid vooar soit: myr shen  adsyn ta aignagh dy gholl yeih shoh hiuish, cha vod ad; chamoo oddys adsyn cheet  hooinyn bailliu cheet veih shen.  
42N||16||27||Eisht dooyrt eh, Ta mee guee ort er-y-fa shen, ayr, dy choyrt eh gys thie my ayrey:   
42N||16||28||Son ta queig braaraghyn aym; dy vod eh feanish y ymmyrkey daue, nagh jig adsyn  myrgeddin gys y boayl shoh dy horchagh.  
42N||16||29||Dooyrt Abraham rish, Ta Moses as ny phadeyryn oc; lhig daue clashtyn adsyn.  
42N||16||30||As dooyrt eh, Cha nee, O ayr Abraham: agh dy ragh chaghter huc veih ny merriu,  ghoghe ad arrys.  
42N||16||31||As dooyrt eh rish, Mannagh der ad geill da Moses as ny phadeyryn, cha greidjagh  ad, ga dy n'irragh fer veih ny merriu. 
42N||17||1||Eisht dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Cha  vod eh ve, agh dy bee oyryn peccah ayn: agh  smerg dasyn liorish hig ad.  
42N||17||2||Veagh eh ny bare dasyn clagh-wyllin ve croghit mysh e wannal, as eh dy ve baiht  ayns y cheayn, na eh dy hayrn gys peccah unnane jeh'n vooinjer veggey shoh.  
42N||17||3||Cur-jee twoaie diu hene: My nee dty vraar aggair dhyt, cur oghsan da; us my ghoys  eh arrys, leih da.  
42N||17||4||As my nee eh peccah dt'oi shiaght keayrtyn 'sy laa, as shiaght keayrtyn 'sy laa  chyndaa reesht hood as gra, Ta mee goaill arrys; te ort leih da.  
42N||17||5||As dooyrt ny ostyllyn rish y Chiarn, Bishee yn credjue ainyn.  
42N||17||6||As dooyrt y Chiarn, Dy beagh credjue eu myr grine dy rass mustard, oddagh shiu gra  rish y billey-sycamine shoh, Bee er dty hayrn ass ny fraueyn, as bee er dty hoiaghey  ayns y cheayn; as yinnagh eh biallys diu.  
42N||17||7||Agh quoi eu ta sharvaant echey traaue, ny bochillagh ollagh, jirrys rish chelleeragh,  tra vees eh er jeet veih'n vagher, Immee as soie gys y voayrd?  
42N||17||8||As nagh jir hoshiaght rish, Fow aarloo my hibber, as kiartee oo hene dy hirveish  orrym's, derrey vee'm erreish gee as giu, us ny lurg shen nee uss gee as giu?   
42N||17||9||Vel booise er da'n charvaant shen, Son jannoo myr v'eh oardit? Er-lhiam nagh vel.
42N||17||10||Myr shen neesht shiuish tra vees shiu er n'yannoo ooilley ny t'er ny harey diu,  abbyr jee. She sharvaantyn neu-frioosagh shin: ta shin er n'yannoo ynrycan ny va  orrin dy yannoo.
42N||17||11||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh er e vurnah gys Jerusalem, dy jimmee eh trooid  mean Samaria as Galilee. 
42N||17||12||As myr v'eh goll stiagh ayns balley dy row, haink ny whail jeih deiney va nyn louranee,  as hass ad foddey veih: 
42N||17||13||As hrog ad seose nyn goraa, as dooyrt ad, Yeesey, Vainshter, jean myghin orrin.
42N||17||14||As tra v'eh er jeeaghyn orroo, dooyrt eh roo, Immee-jee as jeeagh-jee shiu hene  da ny saggyrtyn. As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'ad goll, dy row ad er nyn ghlenney.
42N||17||15||As hyndaa fer jeu back, tra honnick eh dy row eh er ny laanaghey, as lesh ard choraa  hug eh moylley da Jee,
42N||17||16||As huitt eh sheese er e eddin ec ny cassyn echey, cur booise da: as v'eh ny Samaritan.
42N||17||17||As dreggyr Yeesey, gra, Nagh row jeih er ny ghlenney? agh cre vel yn nuy?
42N||17||18||Cha vel er nyn gheddyn t'er jyndaa dy chur gloyr da Jee, agh yn ynrycan joarree  shoh.
42N||17||19||As dooyrt eh rish, Irree, immee royd; ta dty chredjue er dty laanaghey.
42N||17||20||As tra denee ny Phariseeyn jeh, cre'n traa harragh reeriaght Yee? dreggyt eh  ad, gra, Cha jig reeriaght Yee lesh stayd chronnal.
42N||17||21||Chamoo jir ad, Jeeagh shoh, ny jeeagh shid: son cur-my-ner, ta reeriaght Yee  cheu-sthie  jeu.
42N||17||22||As dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Hig y traa dy bee shiu aignagh dy akin unnane jeh  laghyn Mac y dooinney, as cha vaik shiu eh.
42N||17||23||As jir ad riu, jeeagh-jee ayns shoh, as jeeagh-jee ayns shid: ny roie-jee geiyrt  orroo, as ny lhian-jee roo.
42N||17||24||Son myr ta'n tendreil soilshean veih ard dy ard fo yn aer: myr shen myrgeddin vees  Mac y dooinney ayns y laa echeysyn.
42N||17||25||Agh hoshiaght shegin da ymmodee seaghyn y hurranse, as ve beg soit jeh liorish  y sheeloghe shoh.
42N||17||26||As myr ve rish lhing Noe, shen myr vees eh neesht ayns laghyn Mac y dooinney.
42N||17||27||V'ad gee, v'ad giu, v'ad poosey, v'ad er nyn goyrt ayns poosey, derrey'n laa hie  Noe stiagh ayns yn arg: as haink y thooilley as vaih eh ad ooilley.
42N||17||28||As er yn aght cheddin myr ve ayns laghyn Lot, v'ad gee, v'ad giu v'ad kionnaghey,  v'ad creck, v'ad soiaghey biljyn, v'ad troggal thieyn:
42N||17||29||Agh er yn eer laa hie Lot magh ass Sodom, gheayrt neose orroo aile as brimstone  veih niau, as ren eh ad ooilley y stroie: 
42N||17||30||Eer er yn aght cheddin vees eh er y laa vees yn Mac dooinney er ny hoilshaghey.
42N||17||31||Ayns y laa shen, eshyn vees er mullagh y thie, as e chooid sthie, ny lhig da cheet  neose dy chur lesh eh: as eshyn ta ayns y vagher, ny lhig dasyn myrgeddin chyndaa  back
42N||17||32||Cooinee-jee er ben Lot.
42N||17||33||Quoi-erbee ta shirrey e vioys y hauail caillee eh eh: as quoi-erbee nee e vioys  y choayl, saue-ee eh eh.  
42N||17||34||Ta mee ginsh diu, ayns yn oie shen dy bee daa ghooinney ayns un lhiabbee: as bee  yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.  
42N||17||35||Bee daa ven blieh cooidjagh, bee yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.  
42N||17||36||Bee daa ghooinney ayns y vagher; bee yn derrey yeh goit, as y jeh elley faagit.   
42N||17||37||As dreggyr ad, as dooyrt ad rish, C'raad, Hiarn? As dooyrt eshyn roo, Raad erbee  dy vel yn convayrt, shen-y-raad vees ny urlee er nyn jaglym cooidjagh.
42N||18||1||Aa loayr eh coraa-dorraghey roo, dy lhisagh deiney kinjagh padjer y ghoaill, as gyn  ad y ve lhiastey;  
42N||18||2||Gra, Va ayns ard-valley dy row briw nagh row ayns aggle roish Jee, ny soiaghey jeh  deiney.  
42N||18||3||As va ben-treoghe ayns yn ard-valley cheddin, haink huggey, gra, Jean cairys dou  er my noid.  
42N||18||4||As son tammylt cha dug eh geill jee: agh ny lurg shen dooyrt eh rish hene, Ga nagh  vel mee goaill aggle roish Jee, ny jannoo soiaghey jeh dooinney:  
42N||18||5||Ny-yeih er-y-fa dy vel y ven-treoghe shoh dy my voirey, ver-ym cairys jee, er-aggle  liorish cheet cha kinjagh dy jean ee skee jee'm.  
42N||18||6||As dooyrt y Chiarn, Clasht-jee cre ta'n briw neu-chairagh dy ghra.  
42N||18||7||As nagh jean Jee cooilleeney ass lieh e chloan reiht hene, ta geamagh huggey oie  as laa, ga dy vel eh foddey lhiggey shaghey?  
42N||18||8||Ta mee ginsh diu dy jean eh dy tappee goaill cooilleeney er nyn son. Ny-yeih tra  hig Mac y dooinney, vow eh credjue er y thalloo?   
42N||18||9||As loayr eh yn coraa-dorraghey shoh rish shiartanse va treishteil ayndoo hene dy  row ad cairagh, agh soiaghey beg jeh feallagh elley:   
42N||18||10||Hie daa ghooinney seose gys y chiamble dy ghoaill padjer; va'n derrey yeh ny Pharisee,  as y jeh elley ny Phublican.  
42N||18||11||Hass y Pharisee as ghow eh padjer myr shoh rish hene, Yee, ta mee cur booise dhyt,  nagh vel mish myr deiney elley, tranlaasee, neu-chairagh, brishey-poosey, ny foast  myr y publican shoh.  
42N||18||12||Ta mee trostey daa cheayrt 'sy chiaghtin, ta mee cur jaghee jeh ooilley ny t'ayns  my chummal.
42N||18||13||As hass y publican foddey veih, as cha b'lhoys da wheesh as e hooillyn y hroggal  seose gys niau, agh woaill eh er e chleeau, gra, Dy row Jee myghinagh dooys ta my  ghooinney peccoil.
42N||18||14||Ta mee ginsh diu, dy jagh y dooinney shoh sheese gys e hie er ny heyrey roish y  jeh elley: son bee dy chooilley er ta dy hoiaghey eh-hene seose er ny injillaghey  as bee eshyn ta dy injillaghey eh-hene, er ny hoiaghey seose.  
42N||18||15||As hug ad lhieu huggey myrgeddin cloan aegey, dy ventyn roo: agh tra honnick e  ostyllyn shoh, hooar ad foill.  
42N||18||16||Agh deie Yeesey orroo huggey, as dooyrt eh, Lhig-jee da ny paitchyn cheet hym's,  as ny jean-jee ad y lhiettal: son jeh nyn lheid ta reeriaght Yee.  
42N||18||17||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee nagh jean goaill-rish reeriaght Yee myr  lhiannoo beg, cha jed eh er aght erbee stiagh ayn.  
42N||18||18||As denee fer-reill dy row jeh, gra, Vainshter vie, cre t'orrym dy yannoo dy vod  eiraght y ve aym ayns y vea veayn?  
42N||18||19||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou genmys mish mie? cha vel ayn ny ta mie, agh  unnane, ynrycan Jee.  
42N||18||20||Shione dhyt ny annaghyn, Ny jean poosey y vrishey, Ny jean dunverys, Ny jean geid,  Ny jean feanish foalsey y ymmyrkey, Cur arrym da dty ayr as da dty voir.  
42N||18||21||As dooyrt eh, Ooilley shoh ta mee er vreayll veih my aegid.  
42N||18||22||Nish tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh rish, Ta foast ort un red y yannoo: creck  as rheynn ooilley ny t'ayd er ny boghtyn, as bee berchys ayd ayns niau: as tar, as  eiyr orrym's.  
42N||18||23||As tra cheayll eh shoh, daase eh feer trimshagh, son v'eh feer verchagh. 
42N||18||24||As tra honnick Yeesey dy row eh feer trimshagh, dooyrt eh, Cre cha doillee as te  dauesyn ta berchys oc, goll stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee!  
42N||18||25||Son te ny sassey da camel goll trooid croae snaidey, na da dooinney berchagh dy  gholl stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee.
42N||18||26||As dooyrt adsyn cheayll eh, Quoi eisht oddys v'er ny hauail?  
42N||18||27||As dooyrt eh, Ta ny reddyn shoh neu phossible da deiney, agh t'ad possible da Jee.   
42N||18||28||Eisht dooyrt Peddyr, Cur-my-ner, ta shinyn er dreigeil ooilley, as er n'eiyrt ort's.   
42N||18||29||As dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh vel dooinney erbee t'er dreigeil  thie, ny ayr ny moir, ny braaraghyn, ny ben, ny cloan, er graih reeriaght Yee,  
42N||18||30||Nagh vow ymmodee fillee smoo 'sy traa t'ayn nish, as ayns y theihll ta ry-heet  yn vea dy bragh farraghtyn.  
42N||18||31||Eisht ghow eh huggey yn daa ostyl yeig, as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-my-ner ta shin  goll seose gys Jerusalem, as bee dy chooilley nhee ta scruit liorish ny phadeyryn,  my chione yn Mac dooinney, er ny chooilleeney.  
42N||18||32||Son bee eh er ny vrah gys ny Ashoonee, as nee ad craidey mysh, as dellal dy roonagh  rish, as ceau shellaghyn er;
