42N||18||33||As scuitchee ad eh, as ver ad eh gy baase; as y trass laa nee eh girree reesht.    
42N||18||34||As cha hoig ad veg jeh ny reddyn va fys oc er ny reddyn va loayrit. 
42N||18||35||As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er jeet er gerrey da Jericho, dy row dooinney  doal dy row ny hoie rish lhiattee yn raad, shirrey jeirk.  
42N||18||36||As tra cheayll eh yn pobble goll shaghey, denee eh cre v'ayn.  
42N||18||37||As dinsh ad da, dy row Yeesey dy Nazateth goll shaghey.  
42N||18||38||As dyllee eh, gra, Yeesey, vac Ghavid, jean myghin orrym.  
42N||18||39||As hug y vooinjer hie roish oghsan da dy ve ny-host: agh dyllee eshyn wheesh shen  smoo, Vac Ghavid, jean myghin orrym.  
42N||18||40||As hass Yeesey, as doardee eh yn dooinney dy ve er ny choyrt lesh huggey: as tra  v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, denee eh jeh,  
42N||18||41||Gra, Cre bailt mee dy yannoo er dy hon? As dooyrt eh, Hiarn, dy voddym my hoilshey  y gheddyn.  
42N||18||42||As doogrt Yeesey rish, Dty hoilshey dy row ayd: ta dty chredjue er dty hauail.   
42N||18||43||As chelleeragh hooar eh e hoilshey, as deiyr eh er, cur gloyr da Jee: ooilley yn  pobble, tra honnick ad eh, hug ad moylley da Jee. 
42N||19||1||As hie Yeesey stiagh, as jimmee eh trooid  Jericho.  
42N||19||2||As cur-my-ner, va dooinney va enmyssit Zaccheus, va ny ard-ghooinney mastey ny publicanee,  as v'eh berchagh.  
42N||19||3||As v'eh shirrey Yeesey y akin quoi v'eh, as cha dod eh kyndagh rish y pobble, son  v'eh ny ghooinney giare.  
42N||19||4||As roie eh roish, as hie eh seose er billey-sycamore dy gheddyn shilley jeh; son  v'eh dy gholl shaghey yn raad shen.  
42N||19||5||As tra va Yeesey er jeet gys yn ynnyd, yeeagh eh seose, as honnick eh eh, as dooyrt  eh rish, Zaccheus, jean siyr, as tar neose; son jiu ta mish dy ghoaill aght ec dty  hie.  
42N||19||6||As ren eh siyr, as haink eh neose, as hug eh oltaghey-bea gennal da.  
42N||19||7||As tra honnick ad shoh, v'ad ooilley jymmoosagh, gra, Dy row eh er gholl stiagh  dy ee as dy iu marish dooinney dy ghrogh vea.  
42N||19||8||As hass Zaccheus magh, as dooyrt eh rish y Chiarn, Cur-my-ner, Hiarn, yn derrey  lieh jeh my chooid ta mee dy choyrt da ny boghtyn: as my ta mee er ghoaill red erbee  dy molteyragh veih dooinney erbee, ta mee jannoo lhiassaghey kiare-filley da.   
42N||19||9||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Jiu ta saualtys er jeet gys y thie shoh, ayns wheesh as dy  vel eshyn myrgeddin ny vac da Abraham.   
42N||19||10||Son ta Mac y dooinney er jeet dy hirrey as dy hauail shen ny va caillit.  
42N||19||11||As erreish daue shoh y chlahtyn, hie eh ny sodjey er e hoshiaght, as loayr eh coraa-dorraghey  er-y-fa dy row eh er-gerrey da Jerusalem, as liorish dy row ad smooinaghtyn dy beagh  reeriaght Yee dy gerrit er ny hoilshaghey:
42N||19||12||Dooyrt eh er-y-fa shen, Hie dooinney ooasle dy row gys cheer foddey, dy gheddyn  da hene reeriaght, as dy heet back reesht.   
42N||19||13||As deie eh er ny jeih sharvaantyn echey, as livrey eh daue jeih puint, as dooyrt  eh roo, Jean-jee dellal derrey hig-ym.   
42N||19||14||Agh dirree yn theay shen magh n'oi as hug ad chaghteraght geiyrt er, gra, Cha naill-lhieu  yn dooinney shoh dy reill harrin.   
42N||19||15||As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'eh er jeet reesht, erreish da yn reeriaght y gheddyn,  dy doardee eh ny sharvaantyn shen dy ve eit huggey, daue v'eh er choyrt yn argid,  dy gheddyn fys cre-woad va dy chooilley ghooinney er chosney liorish e ghellal.     
42N||19||16||Eisht haink y chied er, gra, Hiarn, ta dty phunt er chosney jeih puint.   
42N||19||17||As dooyrt eh rish, S'mie shen, harvaant vie: er-yn-oyr dy vel oo er ve firrinagh  ayns red feer fardalagh, gow uss yn reill er jeih ard-valjyn.   
42N||19||18||As haink yn nah er, gra, Hiarn, ta dty phunt er chosney queig puint.   
42N||19||19||As dooyrt eh myrgeddin rishyn, Gow uss yn reill neesht er queig ard-valjyn.   
42N||19||20||As haink fer elley, gra, Hiarn, cur-my ner, shoh dty phunt, t'er ny ve aym's tashtit  ayns naptin:   
42N||19||21||Son va mee ayns aggle royd, er-y-fa dy nee dooinney creoi oo: t'ou troggal shen  nagh dug oo sheese, as buinn shen nagh ren oo cuirr.   
42N||19||22||As dooyrt eh rish, Ass dty veeal hene nee'm oo y vriwnys, uss ghrogh harvaant,  Va fys ayd dy row mee my ghooinney creoi, troggal shen nagh dug mee sheese, as buinn  shen nagh chuirr mee:   
42N||19||23||Cre'n-fa nagh dug oo my argid magh er use, tra harrin thie, dy voddin v'er droggal  my chooid hene lesh bishaghey.   
42N||19||24||As dooyrt eh roosyn,va kionfenish Gow-jee yn punt voishyn as cur-jee eh da fer  ny jeih puint.    
42N||19||25||(As dooyrt ad rish, Hiarn, ta jeih puint echey shen.)   
42N||19||26||Son ta mee gra riu, Da dy chooilley unnane ta echey, vees er ny choyrt, as eshyn  nagh vel echey, bee shen hene ny ta echey er ny ghoaill veih.   
42N||19||27||Agh ad shen my noidyn nagh bailliu mish dy reill harrystoo, cur-jee lhieu ad ayns  shoh, as cur-jee ad gy-baase kiongoyrt rhym.   
42N||19||28||As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, hie eh rhymboo, myr v'ad goll seose gys Jerusalem,    
42N||19||29||As haink eh gy-kione, tra v'ad er jeet er-gerrey da Bethphage as Bethany, ec y  chronk va enmyssit cronk ny oliveyn, dy dug eh jees jeh e ostyllyn er chaghteraght,    
42N||19||30||Gra, Gow-jee gys y balley-beg ta rhymbiu; as tra hig shiu gys shen, yiow shiu lhiy  er-eistyr, er nagh ren rieau dooinney markiagh: feayshil-jee as cur-jee lhieu eh  gys shoh.    
42N||19||31||As my enys dooinney erbee j'iu, Cre'n fa ta shiu dy eaysley eh? Shoh myr nee shiu  gra rish, Er-y-fa dy ve feme ec y Chiarn er.   
42N||19||32||As hie ny chaghteryn rhymboo, as hooar ad eh myr v'eh er ghra roo.   
42N||19||33||As myr v'ad feaysley yn lhiy, dooyrt y vooinjer by-liesh eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu  feaysley yn lhiy?   
42N||19||34||As dooyrt adsyn, Ta feme ec y Chiarn er.   
42N||19||35||As hug ad lhieu eh gys Yeesey: as hilg ad nyn gharmadyn er y lhiy, as hug ad Yeesey  ny hoie orroo.   
42N||19||36||As myr v'eh goll, skeayll ad nyn eaddagh er y raad.   
42N||19||37||As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, eer ec goll-sheese cronk ny oliveyn, ghow yn slane  sheshaght jeh e eiyrtyssee toshiaght dy ghoaill boggey, as dy chur moylley da Jee  lesh ard-choraa, son ooilley ny obbraghyn mirrillagh v'ad er n'akin,   
42N||19||38||Gra, Bannit dy row yn Ree ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn: shee ayns niau, as gloyr  ayns yn yrjid.   
42N||19||39||As dooyrt paart jeh ny Phariseeyn rish veih mastey yn pobble, Vainshter, cur oghsan  da dty eiyrtyssee.   
42N||19||40||As dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Ta mee ginsh diu, my chummagh ad shoh nyn jengey,  dy jinnagh ny eer claghyn troggal seose nyn goraa.   
42N||19||41||As tra v'eh er jeet er-gerrey, yeeagh eh er yn ard-valley, as cheayn eh harrish.    
42N||19||42||Gra, Dy beagh toiggal er ve ayd's, dy jarroo ayd's, ayns dty laa shoh hene, jeh  ny reddyn ta bentyn rish dty hee! agh nish t'ad follit veih dty hooillyn.   
42N||19||43||Son hig ny laghyn ort, tra nee dty noidyn jeeg y yannoo mood, as soie-ee ad ad-hene  mygeayrt, as cruinnee ad oo stiagh er dy chooilley heu.   
42N||19||44||As lhieggee ad oo kiart rish y thalloo, as dty chloan cheu-sthie jeed; as cha vaag  ad aynyd un chlagh er clagh elley: er-yn-oyr nagh dug oo tastey da'n earish haink  mish dy dty yeeaghyn.   
42N||19||45||As hie eh stiagh ayns y chiamble, as ren eh toshiaght dy eiyrt magh yn vooinjer  va creck as kionnaghey ayn   
42N||19||46||Gra roo, Te scruit, Ta my hie's thie yn phadjer: agh ta shiuish er n'yannoo eh  ny ooig dy vaarlee.
42N||19||47||As v'eh gynsagh ad gagh laa ayns y chiamble. Agh va ny ard-saggyrtyn, as ny scrudeyryn,  as leeideilee yn phobble shirrey eh y stroie,  
42N||19||48||As cha row fys oc kys dy heet my geayrt-y-mysh; son va ooilley yn pobble feer aggindagh  er clashtyn eh. 
42N||20||1||AS haink eh gy-kione er unnane jeh ny laghyn shen, myr v'eh gynsaghey  yn pobble ayns  y chiamble as preacheil y sushtal, dy ren ny ard-saggrtyn as ny scrudeyryn soiaghey  er, marish y chanstyr, 
42N||20||2||As loayr ad rish, gra, Insh dooin, Cre'n phooar t'ayd dy yannoo ny reddyn shoh?  ny quoi eh hug y phooar shoh dhyt?   
42N||20||3||As dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh roo, Fenyms jiuish myrgeddin un red; as freggyr-jee  mee:   
42N||20||4||Bashtey Ean, nee veih niau ve, ny veih deiney?   
42N||20||5||As loayr ad nyn mast' oc hene, gra, My jir mayd, Veih niau; jir eshyn, Cre'n-fa  eisht nagh chred shiu eh?   
42N||20||6||Agh my jir mayd, Veih deiney; nee ooilley yn pobble nyn glaghey shin; son t'ad dy  shickyr credjal Ean dy ve ny adeyr.   
42N||20||7||As dreggyr ad, nagh voddagh ad ginsh cre voish v'eh.   
42N||20||8||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Chamoo insh yms diuish cre'n phooar t'aym dy yannoo ny reddyn  shoh.    
42N||20||9||Eisht hie eh er e hoshiaght dy loayrt rish y pobble yn coraa-dorraghey shoh: Va  dooinney dy row ren garey-feeyney y hoiaghey, as hoie eh eh rish, eirinnee, as hie  eh gys cheer foddey son choud shen dy hraa.    
42N||20||10||As ec yn imbagh, hug eh fer-mooinjerey gys ny eirinnee, dy choyrt da jeh mess y  gharey-feeyney: agh woaill ny eirinnee eh, as hug ad eh ersooyl follym.   
42N||20||11||As reesht hug eh fer-mooinjerey elley; as woaill ad eshyn myrgeddin, as ghell ad  dy scammyltagh rish, as hug ad eh ersooyl follym.   
42N||20||12||As reesht hug eh yn trass; as vroo ad eshyn myrgeddin, as deiyr ad eh ersooyl.    
42N||20||13||Eisht dooyrt chiarn y gharey-feeyney Cre nee'm? Ver-ym huc my vac graihagh foddee  dy der ad arrym da tra hee-ys ad eh.   
42N||20||14||Agh tra honnick ny eirinnee eh, loayr ad eddyr ad-hene, gra, Shoh yn eirey: tar-jee,  lhig dooin eh y varroo, dy vod yn eiraght ve lhien hene.   
42N||20||15||Myr shen cheau ad eh magh ass y gharey-feeyney, as varr ad eh. Cre nee Chiarn y  gharey-feeyney er-y-fa shen roo?   
42N||20||16||Hig eh as stroie-ee eh ny eirinnee shoh, as ver eh yn garey-feeyney da feallagh  elley. As tra cheayll ad shen, dooyrt ad, Nar lhig eh Jee.   
42N||20||17||As yeeagh eh orroo, as dooyrt eh, Cre shoh eisht ta scruit, Ta'n chlagh ren ny  masoonee y vee-lowal, er jeet dy ve yn ard-chlagh chorneilagh?   
42N||20||18||Quoi-erbee huittys er y chlagh shen, hee eh er ny vroo: agh er quoi-erbee huittys  y chlagh shen, nee ee cha meen as joan jeh.    
42N||20||19||As va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scrudeyryn ayns yn oor cheddin shirrey eh y ghoaill;  agh ghow ad aggle roish y pobble: son dennee ad dy row eh er loayrt yn coraa-dorraghey  shoh nyn noisyn.   
42N||20||20||As va sooill oc er, as hug ad magh peeikearyn va dy lhiggey orroo dy ve deiney  cairagh, er-chee tayrtyn eh nyns e ghlare, as myr shen dy livrey eh gys pooar as  reill y chiannoort.    
42N||20||21||As denee ad jeh, gra, Vainshter, ta fys ain dy vel oo loayrt as gynsaghey cairagh;  chamoo t'ou soiaghey jeh persoon erbee, agh gynsaghey raad Yee dy firrinagh  
42N||20||22||Vel eh lowal dooin keesh y eeck da Cesar, mannagh vel?  
42N||20||23||Agh dennee eh yn foalsaght oc, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey da my  ghoaill ayns ribbey?  
42N||20||24||Jeeagh-jee dou ping: quoi ta'n jalloo as y scrieu t'er cowraghey? Dreggyr ad as  dooyrt ad, Cesar.  
42N||20||25||As dooyrt eh roo, Eeck-jee er-y-fa shen da Cesar shen ny ta bentyn gys Cesar; as  da Jee shen ny ta bentyn gys Jee.  
42N||20||26||As cha voddagh ad greme y ghoaill er e ghoan kiongoyrt rish y pobble: as ghow ad  yindys jeh'n ansoor echey, as chum ad nyn jengey.  
42N||20||27||Eisht haink huggey shiartanse jeh ny Sadduceeyn (ta gobbal yn irree-seose-reesht  veih ny merriu) as denee ad jeh,  
42N||20||28||Gra, Vainshter, ta Moses er scrieu dooin, My ta braar dooinney erbee geddyn baase,  as ben echey, as eh dy gheddyn baase gyn chloan, dy vel e vraar dy phoosey yn ven  echey, as dy hroggal seose sluight gys e vraar.  
42N||20||29||Va er-y-fa shen shiaght braaraghyn: as hooar y braar shinney, tra v'eh er phoosey  ben, baase gyn chloan.  
42N||20||30||As ghow yn nah vraar ee son ben, as hooar eshyn baase dyn chloan.  
42N||20||31||As ghow yn trass ee: as er yn aght cheddin yn chiaght. As cha daag ad cloan, as  hooar ad baase.  
42N||20||32||Er-jerrey ooilley hooar y ven ee hene baase myrgeddin.  
42N||20||33||Ec yn irree-reesht er-y-fa shen, quoi jeu vees ee echey son ben? son v'ee ny ben  da'n chiaght.  
42N||20||34||As dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ta cloan y theihll shoh poosey, as er nyn goyrt  ayns poosey:  
42N||20||35||Agh adsyn vees coontit feeu jeh'n theihll shen, as jeh yn irree-reesht veih ny  merriu, cha vel ad poosey, ny er nyn goyrt ayns poosey.  
42N||20||36||Chamoo oddys ad baase y gheddyn arragh; son t'ad corrym rish ny ainleyn, as nyn  gloan dy Yee, liorish dy vel ad cloan yn irree-seose reesht.  
42N||20||37||Nish dy n'irree ny merriu, hoilshee Moses hene ec y thammag, tra t'eh genmys y  Chiarn, Jee Abraham, as Jee Isaac, as Jee Yacob.  
42N||20||38||Son cha nee Jee ny merriu eh, agh Jee ny bioee: son ta ooilley bio huggeysyn.   
42N||20||39||Eisht dreggyr shiartanse jeh ny scrudeyryn as doo~yt ad, Vainshter, t'ou er ghra  dy mie.  
42N||20||40||As ny lurg shen cha by-lhoys daue question erbee sodjey y chur huggey.  
42N||20||41||As dooyrt eh roo, Kys t'ad gra dy nee Creest mac Ghavid?  
42N||20||42||As dy vel David eh hene ayns lioar ny psalmyn gra, Dooyrt y Chiarn rish my Hiarn's,  Soie uss er my laue yesh,
42N||20||43||Derrey ver-ym dty noidyn son stoyl dty choshey.
42N||20||44||Ta David er-y-fa shen genmys eh ny Hiarn, kys t'eh eisht yn mac echey?
42N||20||45||Eisht ayns clashtyn ooilley yn pobble, dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn,
42N||20||46||Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie jeh ny scrudeyryn, ta geearree shooyll ayns coamraghyn liauyrey,  as shynney lhieu dy vannaghey daue ayns ny margaghyn, as ny stuill syrjey y ve oc  ayns kialteenyn, as ny ard ynnydn-soie ec cuirraghyn.
42N||20||47||T'ad cur-mow thieyn mraane-treoghe, as son scaa dy chraueeaght lhiggey orroo dy  ve mennick ayns padjer: ta briwnys strimmey nyn gour oc shoh. 
42N||21||1||As yeeagh eh seose, as honnick eh ny berchee tilgey ny giootyn oc ayns kishtey yn  stoyr.  
42N||21||2||As honnick eh myrgeddin ben voght treoghe dy row, tilgey ayn daa vite.  
42N||21||3||As dooyrt eh, Ayns firrinys ta mee gra riu, dy vel y ven voght treoghe shoh er hilgey  ayn ny smoo na ad ooilley.  
42N||21||4||Son t'ad shoh ooilley ayns nyn balchey er chur gys ourallyn Yee: agh t'eeish myr  s'boght ee, er choyrt ayn ooilley ny v'eck dy veaghey er.  
42N||21||5||As myr va paart loayrt jeh'n chiamble, kys ve er ny hoiaghey magh lesh clagh yn  aalin, as giootyn, dooyrt eh,  
42N||21||6||Son ny reddyn shoh ta shiu dy akin hig ny laghyn, tra nagh bee faagit un chlagh  er clagh elley nagh bee er ny lhieggal.  
42N||21||7||As denee ad jeh, gra, Vainshter, agh cuin vees ny reddyn shoh? as cre vees yn cowrey  tra hig ny reddyn shoh gy-kione?  
42N||21||8||As dooyrt eh, Cur-jee twoaie nagh bee shiu er nyn molley: son hig ymmodee ayns m'ennym's,  gra, Mish Creest; as ta'n traa tayrn er-gerrey: ny gow-jee shiuish er-y-fa shen geiyrt  orroo.  
42N||21||9||Agh tra chlinnys shiu jeh caggaghyn as irree-magh, ny bee aggle erriu: son shegin  da ny reddyn shoh hoshiaght cheet gy-kione, agh cha bee yn jerrey foast.   
42N||21||10||Eisht dooyrt eh roo, Nee ashoon girree-magh noi ashoon, as reeriaght noi reeriaght.   
42N||21||11||As bee craaghyn-thallooin mooar ayns ymmodee ynnydyn, as gennaghyn, as crampyn,  as shillaghyn agglagh, as bee cowraghyn mooarey veih niau.  
42N||21||12||Agh roish ooilley shoh gowee ad shiu, ss nee ad tranlaase erriu, as livrey ee ad  shiu seose gys quaiylyn, as gys pryssoonyn, as bee shiu er nyn goyrt fenish reeaghyn  as fir-reill er coontey yn ennym aym's  
42N||21||13||As myr shoh hig shiuish dy ve son feanishyn dooys.   
42N||21||14||Kiare-jee eh- er-y-fa shen ayns nyn gree, gyn shiu dy smooinaghtyn ro-laue cre  nee shiu y reggyrt.
42N||21||15||Son ver-yms diu beeal as creenaght, nagh bee ooilley nyn noidyn son loayrt ny shassoo  magh n'oi.  
42N||21||16||As bee shiu er nyn mrah chammah liorish ayraghyn as moiraghyn, as braaragh yn as  deiney mooinjerey, as caarjyn; as ver ad er paart eu ve er nyn goyrt gy-baase.                                           
42N||21||17||As ver yn ymmodee feoh diu er coontey yn ennym aym's. 
42N||21||18||Agh cha jed wheesh reuaig jeh nyn ghing naardey.  
42N||21||19||Fo ooilley nyn seaghyn cum-jee seose nyn gree.  
42N||21||20||As tra hee shiu sheshaghtyn-caggee mygeayrt Jerusalem, eisht toig-jee dy vel y  traartys eck er-gerrey.  
42N||21||21||Eisht lhig dauesyn ta ayns Judea, chea gys ny sleityn; as lhig dauesyn ta cheu-sthie  jee, cosney ass-jee; as ny lhig dauesyn ta mooie er y cheer cheet stiagh aynjee.   
42N||21||22||Son t'ad shoh laghyn y chooilleeney, son jannoo mie dy chooilley nhee ta scruit.   
42N||21||23||Agh smerg dauesyn ta torragh, as dauesyn ta cur keeagh ayns ny laghyn shen: son  bee trimshey mooar ayns y cheer, as corree noi yn pobble shoh.  
42N||21||24||As tuittee ad er foyr y chliwe, as bee ad er nyn ghoaill ersooyl nyn gappeeyn gys  dy chooilley ashoon: as bee Jerusalem er ny stampey sheese liorish ny Ashoonee, derrey  vees traa ny Ashoonee er ny chooilleeney.  
42N||21||25||As bee cowraghyn ayns y ghrian, as ayns ny rollageyn: as er y thalloo seaghyn er  ashoonyn, as angaish; yn faarkey, as ny tonnyn freaney;  
42N||21||26||Creeaghyn deiney gannooinaghey lesh aggle, as lesh jeeaghyn jei ny reddyn ta ry  heet er y thalloo: son bee pooaraghyn yn aer er nyn graa.   
42N||21||27||As eisht hee ad Mac y dooinney cheet ayns bodjal lesh pooar as ard-ghloyr.  
42N||21||28||As tra ghoys ny reddyn shoh toshiaght dy heet gy-kione, eisht jeeagh-jee shiuish  seose, as trog-jee nyn ghing; son ta'n livrey-ys eu tayrn er-gerrey.  
42N||21||29||As loayr eh roo coraa-dorraghey. Cur-jee my-ner yn billey-figgagh as ooilley ny  billjn;  
42N||21||30||Tra t'ad nish cur magh duillagyn, ta shiu fakin as toiggal jiu hene, dy vel y sourey  er-gerrey.  
42N||21||31||Myr shen shiuish neesht, tra hee shiu ny reddyn shoh cheet gy-kione, toig-jee dy  vel reeriaght Yee er-gerrey.  
42N||21||32||Dy firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Nagh bee yn cheeloghe shoh ec kione, derrey vees ooilley  shoh er ny chooilleeney.  
42N||21||33||Nee yn aer as yn ooir cherraghtyn, agh my ghoan's cha jean cherraghtyn.  
42N||21||34||As cur-jee twoaie diu hene, er-aggle ec traa erbee dy bee ny creeaghyn eu rouyr  laadit lesh jooid as meshtyrys, as kiarailyn y vea shoh, as myr shoh yn laa shen  dy heet erriu doaltattym.  
42N||21||35||Son myr ribbey hig eh er ooilley cummaltee ny hooirey.  
42N||21||36||Bee-jee er nyn dwoaie er-y-fa shen, as bee-jee kinjagh ayns padjer, dy vod shiu  ve coontit feeu dy scapail ooilley ny reddyn shoh hig gy-kione, as dy hassoo kiongoyrt  rish Mac y dooinney.  
42N||21||37||As ayns y laa v'eh gynsagh 'sy chiamble, as ec yn oie goll magh as goaill aaght  ec y chronk ta enmyssit cronk ny Oliveyn.  
42N||21||38||As va ooilley yn pobble cheet huggey dy moghey gys y chiamble, dy eaishtagh rish.  
42N||22||1||ISH va feuilley yn arran-millish tayrn er-gerrey, ta enmyssit y Chaisht.  
42N||22||2||As va ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny scrudeyryn shirrey kys oddagh ad eh y choyrt gy-bause;  son v'adayns sggle roish y pobble.  
42N||22||3||Eisht hie yn drogh-spyrryd stiagh ayns Yuaase va slennooit Iscariot, va jeh earroo  yn daa ostyl yeig.  
42N||22||4||As hie eh roish, as loayr eh rish ny ard saggyrtyn as ny captanyn mychione eh y  vrah daue.  
42N||22||5||As ghow adsyn boggey jeh, as ren ad conaant dy chur argid da.  
42N||22||6||As hug eh gialdyn, as v'eh shirrey caa dy vrah eh tra nagh beagh y pobble marish.   
42N||22||7||Eisht haink laa yn arran-millish, tra va'n Eayn-caisht dy ve er ny varroo.  
42N||22||8||As hug eh magh Peddyr as Ean, gra, Immee-jee, as aarlee-jee yn Eayn-caisht dy vod  mayd gee.   
42N||22||9||As dooyrt ad rish, C'raad sailt shin dy yannoo aarloo?   
42N||22||10||As dooyrt eh roo, Cur-my-ner, tra vees shiu er gholl stiagh ayns yn ard valley  hig dooinney nyn guail lesh saagh-craie dy ushtey; eiyr-jee er gys y thie hed eh  stiagh ayn.   
42N||22||11||As abbyr-jee tish y fer-thie, Ta'n mainshter gra rhyt, Cre vel shamyr ny goaldee,  raad nee'm yn Eayn-caisht y ee marish my ostyllyn?  
42N||22||12||As jeeaghee eh diu ard-room mooar vees soit magh: ayns shen jean-jee aarloo.  
42N||22||13||As hie ad as hooar ad myr v'eh er ghra roo: as daarlee ad yn Eayn-caisht.  
42N||22||14||As tra va'n oor er jeet, hoie eh sheese as y daa ostyl yeig marish.  
42N||22||15||As dooyrt eh roo, Lesh yeearree jeean ta mee er ve aignagh yn Eayn-caisht shoh  y ee meriu roish my jean-ym surranse.  
42N||22||16||Son ta mee gra riu, Nagh n'ee-ym maghey shoh jeh, derrey vees eh cooilleenit ayns  reeriaght Yee.   
42N||22||17||As ghow eh yn cappan, as hug eh booise, as dooyrt eh, Gow-jee shoh, as rheynn-jee  eh ny mast' eu hene.  
42N||22||18||Son ta mee gra riu, Nagh n'iu-ym jeh mess y villey-feeyney, derrey hig reeriaght  Yee.
42N||22||19||As ghow eh arran, as hug eh booise, as vrish eh eh, as hug eh eh daue, gra, Shoh  my chorp t'er ny choyrt er nyn son eu shoh jean-jee ayns cooinaghtyn jeem's.
42N||22||20||As er yn aght cheddin yn cappan lurg shibber, gra, Yn cappan shoh yn conaant noa  ayns my uill's, t'er ny gheayrtey er ny son eu.  
42N||22||21||Agh cur-my-ner, ta'n laue echeysyn ta dy my vrah, marym er y voayrd.  
42N||22||22||As dy firrinagh ta'n Mac dooinney goll myr ve kiarit: agh smerg da'n dooinney shen  liorish t'eh er ny vrah.  
42N||22||23||As ren ad toshiaght dy vriaght nyn mast' oc hene, quoi jeu yinnagh shoh.  
42N||22||24||Nish va streeu myrgeddin nyn mast' oc, quoi jeu syrjey veagh coontit.  
42N||22||25||As dooyrt eh roo, Ta reeaghyn ny Ashoonee gymmyrkey reill harrystoo: as as t'adsyn  t'ayns pooar nyn mastey, enmyssit deiney ooasle.  
42N||22||26||Agh cha bee shiuish myr shen: agh quoi-erbee shinney ta nyn mast eu, lhig da ve  myr y fer saa; as eshyn syrjey ta, myr y fer ta shirveish.  
42N||22||27||Son quoi syrjey, eshyn ta ny hoie ec bee, ny'n fer ta shirveish? nagh nee eshyn  ta ny hoie ec bee? agh ta mish nyn mast' eu myr y fer ta shirveish.  
42N||22||28||She shiuish t'er hannaghtyn marym ayns my heaghyn.  
42N||22||29||As ta mee pointeil diu reeriaght, myr ta my Ayr er phointeil dooys.  
42N||22||30||Dy vod shiu gee as giu ec my voayrd ayns my reeriaght, as soie er stuill-reeoil,  briwnys daa heeloghe yeig Israel.  
42N||22||31||As dooyrt y Chiarn, Simon, Simon, cur-my-ner, ta Satan er yeearree shiuish y  ghoaill, dy chreearey shiu myr curnaght:  
42N||22||32||Agh ta mish er ghuee er dty hon's, nagh jean dty chredjue failleil; as tra vees  oo er jyndaa, niartee dty vraaraghyn.  
42N||22||33||As dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, ta mish aarloo dy gholl mayrt chammah gys pryssoon, as  gys baase.  
42N||22||34||As dooyrt eh, Ta mee ginsh dhyt, Pheddyr roish gerrym y chellee jiu dy jean uss  gobbal three keayrtyn dy nhione dhyt mee.  
42N||22||35||As dooyrt eh roo, Tra hug mee shiu magh fegooish sporran, as spagey, as braagyn,  row nhee erbee dy laccal erriu? As dooyrt ad, Cha row nhee erbee.  
42N||22||36||Eisht dooyrt eh roo, Agh nish eshyn ta sporran echey, lhig da y ghoaill eh, as  myrgeddin e spaagey: as eshyn nagh vel cliwe echey, lhig da creck e gharmad, as cliwe  y chionnaghey.  
42N||22||37||Son ta mee gra riu, Dy nhegin da shoh ny ta scruit, ve foast cooilleenit aynym's,  As v'eh er ny earroo marish ny drogh yantee: son ta jerrey er ny reddyn ta my mychione's.   
42N||22||38||As dooyrt ad, Hiarn, cur-my-ner ta daa chliwe ayns shoh. As dooyrt eh roo, Te dy  liooar. 
42N||22||39||As haink eh magh, as hie eh myr v'eh cliaghtey, gys cronk ny Oliveyn; as deiyr  ny ostyllyn myrgeddin er.
42N||22||40||As tra v'eh ec yn ynnyd, dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee padjer, nagh duitt shiu ayns miolagh.   
42N||22||41||As hie eh voue, mysh choud as hilgagh fer clagh, as huitt eh er e ghlioonyn, as  ghow eh padjer  
42N||22||42||Gra, Ayr, my she dty aigney eh, scugh yn cappan shoh voym: ny-yeih cha nee my aigney's,  agh dt'aigney's dy row jeant.  
42N||22||43||As haink huggey ainle veih niau, dy niartaghey eh,  
42N||22||44||As v'eh ayns angaish vooar, as ghow eh padjer ny s'jeeaney: as va'n ollish echey  myr bineyn mooarey folley tuittym gys y thalloo.  
42N||22||45||As tra v'eh er n'irree veih padjer, as er jeet gys e ostyllyn, hooar eh ad nyn  gadley lesh trimshey,   
42N||22||46||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu cadley? irree-jee as gow-jee padjer, nagh duitt  shiu ayns miolagh.  
42N||22||47||As choud as v'eh foast loayrt, cur-my-ner haink sheshaght vooar, as eshyn va  enmyssit Yuaase, fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig, nyn leeideilagh, as hayrn eh er-gerrey  da Yeesey dy chur paag da.  
42N||22||48||Agh dooyrt Yeesey rish, Yuaase, vel oo brah Mac y dooinney lesh paag?  
42N||22||49||Tra honnick adsyn va mygeayrt-y-mysh cre va ry-heet, dooyrt ad rish, Hiarn, bwoaill  mayd lesh y chliwe?  
42N||22||50||As woaill fer jeu fer-mooinjerey yn ard-saggyrt, as ghiare eh yn chleaysh yesh  jeh.  
42N||22||51||As dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh, Slioar shoh hene. As venn eh rish e chleaysh,  as laanee eh eh.  
42N||22||52||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish ny ard saggyrtyn as captanyn y chiamble, as y chanstyr  v'er jeet magh huggey, Vel shiu er jeet magh, myr noi maarliagh, lesh cliwenyn as  luirg?
42N||22||53||Tra va mee meriu gagh laa ayns y chiamble, cha heeyn shiu magh laue m'oi: agh shoh  yn oor eu, as pooar y dorraghys.  
42N||22||54||Eisht ghow ad eh, as leeid ad ersooyl eh, as hug ad lhieu eh gys thie yn ard-saggyrt.  As deiyr Peddyr er foddey ny yei.  
42N||22||55||As tra v'ad er voaddey aile ayns mean ny halley, as er hoie sheese cooidjagh, hoie  Peddyr sheese ny mast' oc.  
42N||22||56||Agh hug ben-aeg dy row tastey da, myr v'eh ny hoie ec yn aile, as yeeagh ee dy  gyere er, as dooyrt ee, v'eh shoh myrgeddin marish.
42N||22||57||As dob eh, gra, Ven, cha vel enney aym er.  
42N||22||58||As tammylt ny lurg shen, honnick fer elley eh, as dooyrt eh, She fer jeu myrgeddin  uss. As dooyrt Peddyr, Ghooinney, cha nee.  
42N||22||59||As mysh oor ny lurg shen, hass fer elley er dy creoi, gra, Ayns firrinys v'eh shoh  myrgeddin marish; son she Galilean eh,
42N||22||60||As dooyrt Peddyr, Ghooinney, cha s'aym cre t'ou dy ghra. As chelleeragh, choud  as v'eh foast loayrt, gherr y kellagh.  
42N||22||61||As hyndaa yn Chiarn, as yeeagh eh er Peddyr; as chooinee Peddyr er yn ockle va'n  Chiarn er ghra rish, Roish gerrym y chellee, nee uss mish y obbal three keayrtyn.   
42N||22||62||As hie Peddyr magh, as cheayn eh dy sharroo.   
42N||22||63||As ren ny deiney v'er ghoaill Yeesey gannidys er, as y woalley eh.  
42N||22||64||As tra v'ad er choodaghey ny sooillyn echey, woaill ad eh er yn eddin, as denee  ad jeh, gra, Jean phadeyrys, quoi ta dy dty woalley?
42N||22||65||As ymmodee reddyn elley loayr ad dy mollaghtagh n'oi.  
42N||22||66||As cha leah as va'n laa rish, haink shanstyr yn phobble, as ny ard-saggyrtyn  as ny scrudeyryn cooidjagh, as hug ad lhieu eh gys y choonceil oc,  
42N||22||67||Gra, Nee oo yn Creest? insh dooin. As dooyrt eh roo, My inshym diu, cha jean shiu  credjal.  
42N||22||68||As my neem's myrgeddin shiuish y qhuestional, cha jean shiu my reggyrt, ny lhiggey  yn raad dou.  
42N||22||69||Ny lurg shoh nee Mac y dooinney soie er laue yesh pooar Yee.  
42N||22||70||Eisht dooyrt ad ooilley, Nee oo eisht Mac Yee? As dooyrt eh roo, Ta shiuish gra  ny ta mee.  
42N||22||71||As dooyrt ad, Cre'n feme sodjey t'ain er feanishyn? son ta shin hene er chlashtyn  veih'n veeal echey hene.
42N||23||1||As dirree yn slane sheshaght jea, as hug ad lhieu eh gys Pilate.  
42N||23||2||As ren ad toshiaght dy loayrt n'oi, gra, Hooar shin eh shoh cur yn ashoon ain er  shaghryn, as lhiettal sleih veih geeck keesh da Cesar, gra, Dy nee eh-hene Creest  yn ree.  
42N||23||3||As denee Pilate jeh, ghra, Nee ree ny Hewnyn oo? As dreggyr eh, as dooyrt eh, T'ou  uss dy ghra eh.  
42N||23||4||Eisht dooyrt Pilate rish ny ard-saggyrt yn as rish y pobble, Cha vel mish er gheddyn  foill erbee ayns y dooinney shoh.  
42N||23||5||As v'ad wheesh shen s'chenney er, gra, T'eh boirey yn pobble, gynsaghey trooid ooilley  Judea, goaill toshiaght veih Galilee derrey shoh.  
42N||23||6||Tra cheayll Pilate jeh Galilee, denee eh nee Galilean va'n dooinney.  
42N||23||7||As cha leah as hooar eh fys dy nee gys reill Herod v'eh bentyn, hug eh eh gys Herod,  va myrgeddin eh-hene ec Jerusalem ec y traa shen.  
42N||23||8||As tra honnick Herod Yeesey, v'eh feer wooiagh: son v'eh aignagh ry-foadey dy  akin eh, er-yn-oyr dy row eh er chlashtyn ymmodee reddyn jeh; as dy row eh jerkal  dy akin mirril ennagh jeant liorish. 
42N||23||9||Eisht denee en ymmodee questionyn jeh; agh cha dug eh ansoor erbee da.   
42N||23||10||As hass ny ard-sagggrtyn as ny scrudeyryn as loayr ad dy elgyssagh-n'oi.  
42N||23||11||As ren Herod as e gheiney-caggee beg y hoiaghey jeh, as chraid ad mysh, as choamree  ad eh lesh coamrey moyrnagh, as hug ad eh reesht gys Pilate. 
42N||23||12||As y laa cheddin va coardail er ny yannoo eddyr Pilate as Herod; son roie v'ad  ayns noidys ry-cheilley.  
42N||23||13||As dele Pilate er ny ard-saggyrtyn cooidjagh, as er ny fir-reill as y pobble.       
42N||23||14||As dooyrt eh roo, Ta shiu er chur lhieu yn dooinney shoh hym's, myr fer ta cur  shaghrynys er y pobble: as cur-my-ner ta mish er veysht eh kiongoyrt riu, as cha  vel mee er gheddyn foill erbee ayns y dooinney shoh, mychione ny reddyn ta shiuish  cur ny lieh; 
42N||23||15||Chamoo ta Herod: son hug mee shiu huggeysyn, as cur-my-ner, cha vel nhee erbee  ta toilchin baase er ny cherraghey er. 
42N||23||16||Smaghtee-ym eh er-y-fa shen, as lhiggym y raad da.  
42N||23||17||Son beign da fer y eaysley daue ec y feailley.  
42N||23||18||As deie ooilley yn cheshaght, gra, Ersooyl lesh y dooinney shoh, as feayshil dooin  Barabbas:
42N||23||19||(Va son irree-magh dy row, va jeant ayns yn ard-valley, as son dunverys tilgit  ayns pryssoon).
42N||23||20||Va Pilate er-y-fa shen aggindagh dy choyrt feaysley da Yeesey, as loayr eh reesht  roo.   
42N||23||21||Agh dyllee adsyn, gra, Jean y chrossey eh, jean y chrossey eh.   
42N||23||22||As dooyrt eh roo yn trass cheayrt Cammah, cre'n olk t'eh er n'yannoo? cha vel mish  er gheddyn oyr baaish erbee ayn: smaghtee-ym eh er-y-fa shen, as lhiggym y raad da    
42N||23||23||As loayr ad ny s'jeeaney lesh ard choraaghyn, guee dy beagh eh er ny chrossey:  as ren y coraa ocsyn as coraa ny ard-saggyrtyn raad y ghoaill.   
42N||23||24||As hug Pilate briwnys cordail rish nyn aigney.   
42N||23||25||As deayshil eh daue, eshyn va son irree-magh as dunverys tilgit ayns pryssoon eh  v'ad hene er n'yeearree; agh livrey eh Yeesey gys nyn aigney.   
42N||23||26||As myr v'ad dy chur lhieu eh, haare ad greme er Simon Cyrenian dy row, myr v'eh  cheet jeh'n cheer, as ersyn hug ad y chrosh, dy ymmyrkey eh geiyrt er Yeesey.   
42N||23||27||As deiyr er earroo mooar dy leih as dy vraane, va myrgeddin-keayney as jannoo  dobberan er e hon.
42N||23||28||Agh hyndaa Yeesey huc, as dooyrt eh Inneenyn Yerusalem, ny keayn-jee er my hon's,  agh keayn-jee er nyn son hene, as son nyn gloan.  
42N||23||29||Son cur-my-ner, ta ny laghyn cheet, tra jir ad, Bannit ta ny mraane gennish, as  ny breinyn nagh ren gymmyrkey, as ny keeaghyn nagh dug bainney.   
42N||23||30||Eisht nee ad toshiaght dy ghra rish ny sleityn, Tuitt-jee orrin; as rish ny cruink,  Coodee-jee shin.   
42N||23||31||Son my t'ad jannoo ny reddyn shoh rish y billey oor, cre vees er ny yannoo rish  y billey creen? 
42N||23||32||As va myrgeddin daa chimmagh elley er nyn leeideil magh marish, dy ve er nyn goyrt  gy-baase.   
42N||23||33||As tra v'ad er jeet gys yn ynnyd ta enmyssit Calvary, ayns shen ren ad eshyn y  chrossey, as ny kimmee; yn derrey yeh er y laue yesh, as y jeh elley er y laue chiare.    
42N||23||34||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey, Ayr jean leih daue; son cha vel fys oc cre t'ad dy yannoo.  As rheynn ad e choamrey, as hilg ad lottyn.  
42N||23||35||As va'n pobble nyn shassoo cur-my-ner: as maroo ren ny fir-reill myrgeddin gannidys  er, as gra, Haue eh feallagh elley; lhig da eh-hene y hauail my she Creest fer reiht  Yee eh.   
42N||23||36||As va ny sidooryn myrgeddin jannoo faghid er, cheet huggey, as chebbal da vinegar,    
42N||23||37||As gra, My she ree ny Hewnyn oo, saue oo hene.   
42N||23||38||As va'n scrieu shoh myrgeddin soit erskyn e chione, ayns letteryn dy Ghreek as  dy Latin, as dy Hebrew, SHOH REE NY HEWNYN.   
42N||23||39||As ren fer jeh ny kimmee v'er nyn groghey loayrt dy lunagh n'oi, gra, My she oo  yn Creest, saue oo hene as shinyn.   
42N||23||40||Agh dreggyr y jeh elley, cur oghsan da, as gra, Nagh vel aggle ort roish Jee, fakin  dy vel uss fo yn vriwnys cheddin?   
42N||23||41||As shinyn dy jarroo dy cairagh; son ta shin er gheddyn toilchinys cooie yn jannoo  ain: agh cha vel y dooinney shoh er n'yannoo aggair erbee.    
42N||23||42||As dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Hiarn, cooinee orryms tra hig oo gys dty reeriaght.    
42N||23||43||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, Dy firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Dy bee uss marym's jiu ayns  Paradise.   
42N||23||44||As ve mysh y cheyoo oor, as va dorraghys harrish ooilley yn cheer gys yn nuyoo  oor.   
42N||23||45||As va'n ghrian dorraghey, as va curtan scarree yn chiamble raipit veih-my cheilley.    
42N||23||46||As tra va Yeesey er n'eamagh lesh ard-choraa, dooyrt eh, Ayr, gys dty laueyn  ta mish chymney my spyrryd: as tra v'eh er ghra shoh, phaart eh.   
42N||23||47||Nish tra honnick y centurion cre va er jeet gy-kione, hug eh moylley da Jee, gra,  Ayns firrinys v'eh shoh ny ghooinney cairagh.   
42N||23||48||As ooilley yn pobble v'er jeet cooidjagh gys y shilley shen, hug ad my-ner ny reddyn  va jeant, as goaill ad nyn gleeau, haink ad rhymboo.
42N||23||49||As ooilley e ainjyssee, as ny mraane deiyr er veih Galilee, hass ad foddey jeh  cur-my-ner ny reddyn shoh.  
42N||23||50||As cur-my-ner va dooinney va enmyssit Joseph, va ny er-coyrlee, as ny ghooinney  mie as cairagh:  
42N||23||51||(Cha row ayrt ny paart echey shoh ayns y choyrle ny yn jannoo oc) v'eh veih Arimathea,  ard-valley jeh ny Hewnyn, (va myrgeddin eh-hene farkiaght son reeriaght Yee.)  
42N||23||52||Hie yn dooinney shoh gys Pilate, as yeearree eh corp Yeesey,  
42N||23||53||As ghow eh neose eh, as hoiII eh eh ayns aanrit, as doanluck eh eh ayns oaie va  cleight ayns creg, raad nagh row rieau dooinney oanluckit roie.  
42N||23||54||As va shen laa yn aarlaghey, as va yn doonaght tayrn er-gerrey.  
42N||23||55||As hie ny mraane myrgeddin haink marish veih Galilee geiyrt er y corp, as hug ad  my-ner yn oaie, as kys va'n corp er ny oanluckey.  
42N||23||56||As haink ad rhymboo, as hooar ad aarloo spisyn as ooilyn; as ghow ad fea er laa  yn doonaght cordail rish yn anney. 
42N||24||1||Nish er y chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, eer sy vadran, haink ad gys yn oaie, cur lhieu  ny spisyn v'ad er gheddyn aarloo, as mraane elley maroo.  
42N||24||2||As hooar ad y chlagh rowlit ersooyl jeh'n oaie.  
42N||24||3||As hie ad stiagh, as cha dooar ad corp y Chiarn Yeesey.  
42N||24||4||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'ad ayns imnea mooar son shoh, cur-my-ner hass daa ghooinney  lioroo ayns coamrey sollys.  
42N||24||5||As myr v'ad ayns aggle, as croymmey sheese lesh nyn eddin gys y thalloo, dooyrt  ad roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey yn vio mastey ny merriu?  
42N||24||6||Cha vel eh ayns shoh, agh t'eh er n'irree: cooinee-jee cre dooyrt eh-hene riu choud's  v'eh foast ayns Galilee,  
42N||24||7||Gra, Shegin da'n Mac dooinney v'er ny lirrey gys laueyn deiney peccoil, as ve er  ny chrossey, as girree reesht er y trsss laa.   
42N||24||8||As chooinee ad er e ghoan,
42N||24||9||As haink ad back veih yn oaie, as dinsh ad ooilley shoh da'n un ostyl yeig, as da  ooilley yn vooinjer elley.  
42N||24||10||She Moirrey Malaine, as Joanna as Moirrey moir Yamys, as mraane elley va maroo,  dinsh ny reddyn shoh da ny ostjllyn,  
42N||24||11||As ghow ad y ghlare oc myr skeeal branlaadee, a cha dug ad geill daue.  
42N||24||12||Eisht dirree Peddyr as roie eh gys yn oaie, as chroym eh sheese, as honnick eh  ny aanrityn nyn lhie er-lheh, as jimmee eh roish, goaill yindys ec ny va er daghyrt.
42N||24||13||As cur-my-ner hie Jees jeu yn laa cheddin gys balley va enmyssit Emmaus, va mysh  shiaght veeilley veih Jerusalem. 
42N||24||14||As v'ad taggloo ry-cheilley mychione dy chooilley nhee v'er daghyrt.  
42N||24||15||As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'ad taggloo as resooney ry-cheilley, dy daink Yeesey  hene er-gerrey, as dy jagh eh maroo.  
42N||24||16||As va ny sooillyn oc er ny lhiettal nagh dug ad enney er.  
42N||24||17||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre ny naightyn shoh ta shiu dy insh yn derrey yeh da'n jeh elley,  myr ta shiu shooyll dy trimshagh er y raad? 
42N||24||18||As dreggyr fer jeu, va'n ennym echey Cleopas, as dooyrt eh rish, Vel uss agh joarree  ayns Jerusalem, as gyn fys ayd er ny reddyn t'ayns shen er jeet gy-kione er ny laghyn  shoh?  
42N||24||19||As dooyrt eh, Cre ny reddyn? As dooyrt adsyn rish, Mychione Yeesey dy Nazareth,  va ny adeyr, as pooaral ayns jannoo as goo, kiongoyrt rish Jee; as ooilley yn pobble:   
42N||24||20||As kys ren ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny fir-reill ain y livrey eh dy ve er ny gheyrey  gys baase, as t'ad er chrossey eh.  
42N||24||21||Agh va shinyn treishteil dy nee eshyn veagh er chur livrey-ys da Israel: as marish  shoh ooilley, jiu yn trass laa neayr as hie ny reddyn shoh er jannoo.  
42N||24||22||Myrgeddin va shiartanse dy vraane jeh'n cheshaght ain, hug orrin lane yindys y  ghoaill, liorish dy row ad dy moghey ec yn oaie:  
42N||24||23||As tra nagh dooar ad yn corp echey, haink ad as dooyrt ad, dy row ad er vakin ashlish  dy ainleyn dinsh daue dy row eh bio.  
42N||24||24||As hie shiartanse jeusyn va marinyn gys yn oaie, as hooar ad eh eer myr va ny mraane  er ghra; agh eh-hene cha vaik ad.  
42N||24||25||Eisht dooyrt eh roo, O shiuish gheiney mee hushtagh, as faase-chredjuagh, nagh  vel goaill baght jeh ooilley ny ta ny phadeyryn er loayrt!   
42N||24||26||Nagh beign da Creest ny reddyn shoh y hurranse as goll stiagh ayns e ghloyr?  
42N||24||27||As goaill toshiaght ec Moses, as ooilley ny phadeyryn, hug eh bun daue er ooilley  ny scriptyryn jeh dy chooilley nhee va bentyn rish hene.  
42N||24||28||As haink ad er-gerrey da'n balley, raad v'ad goll: as v'eh myr dy beagh eh kiarit  dy gholl ny-sodjey.  
42N||24||29||Agh lhie ad er, gra, Fuirree marin, son ta'n fastyr er, as bunnys y laa ceaut.  As hie eh stiagh dy uirriaght maroo.  
42N||24||30||As haink eh gy-kione, myr v'eh ny hoie ec bee maroo, dy ghow eh arran, as vannee  eh, as vrish eh, as hirveish eh orroo eh.  
42N||24||31||As va ny sooillyn oc er nyn vosley, as hug ad enney er; as skell eh ersooyl ass  nyn shilley.  
42N||24||32||As dooyrt y derrey yeh jeu rish y jeh elley, Nagh row ny creeaghyn ain lossey cheu-sthie  j'in, choud as v'eh taggloo rooin er y raad, as choud as v'eh fosley dooin ny scriptyryn?  
42N||24||33||As hrog ad orroo yn oor cheddin, as hyndaa ad gys Jerusalem, as hooar ad yn un  ostyl yeig er nyn jaglym cooidjagh, as y cheshaght va maroo.  
42N||24||34||Dooyrt roo, Ta'n Chiarn er n'irree son shickyrys, as v'eh er ny akin liorish Simon.   
42N||24||35||Eisht dinsh adsyn cre ny reddyn va jeant er y raad, as kys hug ad enney er, liorish  brishey arran.  
42N||24||36||As myr v'ad myr shoh loayrt, hass Yeesey hene ayns y vean oc, as dooyrt eh roo,  Shee dy row hiu.  
42N||24||37||Agh v'ad seaghnit ayns nyn aigney as agglit, as heill ad dy nee scaan v'ad dy akin.   
42N||24||38||As dooyrt eh roo, Cre'n-fa ta shiu seaghnit, as cre'n-fa ta mee-ourys troggal ayns  nyn greeaghyn?  
42N||24||39||Jeeagh-jee er my laueyn as my chassyn dy nee mish mee-hene t'ayn: loaghtee-jee  mee, as jeeagh-jee, son cha vel feill as craueyn ec scaan, myr hee shiu aym's.  
42N||24||40||As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, yeeagh eh daue e laueyn as e chassyn.  
42N||24||41||As choud as nagh row ad foast credjal son boggey, agh goaill yindys, dooyrt eh  roo, Vel veg y veaghey eu ayns shoh?  
42N||24||42||As hug ad da peesh dy eeast roast as dy chere-volley.   
42N||24||43||As ghow eh, as d'ee eh kiongoyrt roo. 
42N||24||44||As dooyrt eh roo, Shoh ny goan loayr mish riu, choud as va mee foast meriu dy beign  da dy chooilley nhee ve cooilleenit va scruit ayns leigh Voses, as ayns ny phadeyryn,  as ayns ny psalmyn my-mychione's.  
42N||24||45||Eisht doshil eh yn tushtey oc, dy voddagh ad ny scriptyryn, y hoiggal,  
42N||24||46||As dooyrt eh roo, Shoh myr te scruit, as shoh myr ve kiarit da Creest dy hurranse,  as dy irree yn trass laa veih ny merriu:  
42N||24||47||As arrys as leih peccaghyn dy ve er nyn breacheil ayns yn ennym echey, mastey dy  chooilley ashoon, goaill toshiaght ec Jerusalem.  
42N||24||48||As ta shiuish nyn veanishyn jeh ny reddyn shoh.  
42N||24||49||As cur-my-ner, ver-yms hiu gialdyn my Ayrey: agh fuirree-jee ayns ard-valley  Yerusalem, derrey vees shiu coamrit lesh pooar veih'n yrjid.  
42N||24||50||As hug eh lesh magh ad choud as gys Bethany: as hrog eh seose e laueyn as vannee  eh ad.  
42N||24||51||As haink eh gy-kione, choud as v'eh dy vannaghey ad, dy row eh er ny scarrey voue,  as er ny hroggal seose gys niau.  
42N||24||52||As hug ad ooashley da, as hyndaa ad gys Jerusalem lesh boggey mooar: 
42N||24||53||As v'ad kinjagh ayns y chiamble, cur moylley as gloyr da Jee.
43N||1||1||Ayns y toshiaght va'n Goo, as va'n Goo marish Jee, as va'n Goo Jee.   
43N||1||2||Va'n Goo cheddin ayns y toshiaght marish Jee.   
43N||1||3||Liorishyn va dy chooilley nhee er ny yannoo; as n'egooish cha row nhee erbee jeant va er ny yannoo;   
43N||1||4||Aynsyn va bea, as va'n vea soilshey deiney.   
43N||1||5||As ren y soilshey soilshean ayns y dorraghys, as cha ren y dorraghys goaill-rish.   
43N||1||6||Va dooinney er ny choyrt veih Jee va enmyssit Ean.   
43N||1||7||Haink eh shoh son feanish, dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh'n toilshey, liorishyn dy vod dagh dy chooilley ghooinney credjal.   
43N||1||8||Cha nee eh va'n soilshey shen, agh v'eh er ny choyrt dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh'n toilshey shen.   
43N||1||9||Shen va'n soilshey firrinagh, ta soilshean ayns dy chooilley ghooinney ta cheet er y theihll.
43N||1||10||V'eh ayns y theihll as va'n seihll er ny yannoo liorishyn, as y seihll cha dug enney er.   
43N||1||11||Haink eh gys e vooinjer hene, agh cha ren e vooinjer hene soiaghey jeh. 
43N||1||12||Agh whilleen as ren soiaghey jeh, dauesyn hug eh pooar dy ve nyn mec dy Yee, eer dauesyn ta credjal ayns yn ennym echey:   
43N||1||13||Va er nyn ruggey, cha nee jeh fuill, ny jeh aigney ny foalley, ny jeh aigney dooinney, agh jeh Jee.   
43N||1||14||As ghow yn Goo er dooghys ny foalley, as ren eh baghey nyn mast' ain (as hug shin my-ner yn ghloyr echey, yn ghloyr myr jeh'n ynrycan Mac er-ny-gheddyn jeh'n Ayr) lane dy ghrayse as dy irrinys. 
43N||1||15||(Dymmyrk Ean feanish jeh, as deie eh, gra, Shoh eh jeh ren mish loayrt, T'eshyn ta cheet my yei er ny hoiaghey roym; son v'eh roym)   
43N||1||16||As jeh'n slane towse echey ta shin ooilley er gheddyn ayrn, as grayse er grayse.   
43N||1||17||Son va'n leigh er ny choyrt liorish Moses agh haink grayse as firrinys liorish Yeesey Creest.   
43N||1||18||Cha vel unnane erbee er vakin Jee ec traa erbee; yn ynrycan Mac v'er ny-gheddyn, ta ayns oghrish yn Ayr, eshyn t'er hoilshaghey eh.   
43N||1||19||As shoh feanish Ean, tra hug ny Hewnyn saggyrtyn as Leyiteyn veih Jerusalem dy enaght jeh, Quoi oo hene? 
43N||1||20||As ghow eh rish, as cha dob eh; agh ghow eh rish, Cha nee mish yn Creest.   
43N||1||21||As denee ad jeh, Quoi eisht? Nee oo Elias? As dooyrt eshyn, Cha nee. Nee oo yn phadeyr shen? As dansoor eh, Cha nee.   
43N||1||22||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Quoi oo? dy vod mayd ansoor y choyrt dauesyn t'er choyrt shin: Cre t'ou gra my-dty-chione hene?   
43N||1||23||Dooyrt eh, Mish coraa fer fockley magh ayns yn aasagh, Kiartee-jee raad y Chiarn, myr dooyrt y phadeyr Esaias.   
43N||1||24||As v'adsyn v'er nyn goyrt, jeh ny Phariseeyn.   
43N||1||25||As denee ad jeh, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n-fa t'ou bashtey eisht mannagh  nee oo yn Creest, ny Elias, ny'n phadeyr shen?   
43N||1||26||Dreggyr Ean ad, gra, Ta mish bashtey lesh ushtey: agh ta fer shassoo nyn mast' eu, nagh vel enney eu er;   
43N||1||27||Eshyn eh ta cheet my yei, agh t'er ny hoiaghey roym, kiangley ny braagyn echey cha vel mish feeu dy eaysley.   
43N||1||28||Va ny reddyn shoh jeant ayns Bethabara er cheu elley jeh Jordan, raad va Ean bashtey   
43N||1||29||Yn nah laa honnick Ean Yeesey cheet ny whail, as dooyrt eh, Cur-my-ner Eayn Yee, ta goaill ersooyl peccah yn theihll.   
43N||1||30||Shoh eshyn mychione dooyrt mee, My yei ta dooinney cheet, t'er ny hoiaghey roym; son v'eh roym.   
43N||1||31||As cha row enney aym's er: agh dy beagh eh er ny hoilshaghey da Israel, shen-y-fa haink mish bashtey lesh ushtey. 
43N||1||32||As dymmyrk Ean feanish, gra, Honnick mee yn Spyrryd cheet neose veih niau myr calmane, as tannaghtyn er.   
43N||1||33||As cha dug mish enney er: agh eshyn ren mish y choyrt dy vashtey lesh ushtey, dooyrt eh shen rhym, Ersyn hee oo yn Spyrryd cheet neose as tannaghtyn er, shen eh ta bashtey lesh y Spyrryd Noo.   
43N||1||34||As honnick mee eh, as dymmyrk mee feanish, dy nee shoh Mac Yee.   
43N||1||35||Yn nah laa reesht va Ean ny hassoo, as jees jeh e ynseydee:   
43N||1||36||As yeeagh eh er Yeesey, myr v'eh shooyl, as dooyrt eh, Cur-my-ner Eayn Yee.  
43N||1||37||As cheayll yn daa ynseydagh eh loayrt, as deiyr ad er Yeesey.   
43N||1||38||Eisht hyndaa Yeesey, as honnick eh ad geiyrt er, as dooyrt eh roo, Cre ta shiu dy hirrey? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Rabbi (ta shen dy ghra, 'sy ghlare ainyn,Vainshter) cre raad t'ou baghey?   
43N||1||39||Dooyrt eh roo, Tar-jee as hee shiu. Haink ad as honnick ad c'raad v'eh baghey, as duirree ad marish yn laa shen: son ve mysh y jeihoo oor.   
43N||1||40||Eer jeh'n jees cheayll Ean loayrt, as deiyr er, va Andreays, braar Simon Peddyr. 
43N||1||41||Hooar eshyn hoshiaght e vraar hene Simon, as dooyrt eh rish, Ta shin er gheddyn yn Messias ta shen dy ghra, Yn Creest.   
43N||1||42||As hug eh lesh eh gys Yeesey. As tra honnick Yeesey eh, dooyrt eh, Uss Simon mac Jona: bee oo enmyssit Cephas, ta shen dy ghra Peddyr.   
43N||1||43||Yn laa er-giyn she aigney Yeesey ve dy gholl magh gys Galilee, as hooar eh Philip, as dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym.   
43N||1||44||Nish va Philip veih Bethsaida, ard valley Andreays as Peddyr.   
43N||1||45||Veeit Philip rish Nathanael, as dooyrt eh rish, Ta shin er gheddyn eshyn, jeh ren Moses ayns y leigh, as ny phadeyryn scrieu, Yeesey dy Nazareth, mac Yoseph. 
43N||1||46||As dooyrt Nathanael rish, Vod nhee erbee mie cheet magh ass Nazareth? Dooyrt Philip rish, Tar royd as hee oo.   
43N||1||47||Honnick Yeesey Nathanael cheet ny whail, as dooyrt eh jehsyn, Cur-my-ner Israelite firrinagh, ayn nagh vel molteyrys erbee.   
43N||1||48||Dooyrt Nathanael rish, Cre'n enney t'ayd orrym's? Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Roish my deie Philip ort, tra v'ou fo yn villey-figgagh, honnick mee oo.   
43N||1||49||Dreggyr Nathanael as dooyrt eh rish, Rabbi, oo mac Yee, oo ree Israel.   
43N||1||50||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee rhyt, dy vaik mee oo fo'n villey-figgagh, vel oo credjal? hee oo reddyn smoo na ad shoh.   
43N||1||51||As dooyrt eh rish, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ny lurg shoh hee shiu niau foshlit, as ainleyn Yee goll seose as cheet neose er Mac y dooinney.
43N||2||1||AS er y trass laa va poosey ayns Cana dy Ghalilee; as va moir Yeesey ayns shen.   
43N||2||2||As va chammah Yeesey cuirt, as e ynseydee, gys y vannish.   
43N||2||3||As tra v'ad laccal feeyn, dooyrt moir Yeesey rish, Cha vel feeyn oc.   
43N||2||4||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cre t'ain dy yannoo rish shen? cha vel my oor foast er jeet.
43N||2||5||Dooyrt e voir rish y vooinjer, Jean-jee shiuish cre-erbee jir eh riu.   
43N||2||6||As va soit ayns shen shey siyn cloaie ry-hoi ushtey, lurg cliaghtey ny Hewnyn son glenney, cummal ghaa ny three dy firkinyn y pheesh.   
43N||2||7||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Lhieen-jee ny siyn lesh ushtey. As lhieen ad ad seose gys yn oirr.   
43N||2||8||As dooyrt eh roo, Tayrn-jee nish, as cur-jee lhieu gys mainshter ny cuirraghyn. As hug ad lhieu eh.   
43N||2||9||Tra va mainshter ny cuirraghyn er vlashtyn er yn ushtey va chyndait gys, feeyn, as nagh row fys echey cre voish ve (agh va fys ec ny sharvaantyn va tayrn yn ushtey~ deie mainshter ny cuirraghyn er y dooinney phoosee    
43N||2||10||As dooyrt eh rish, Ta dy chooilley ghooinney ec y toshiaght soiaghey magh feeyn mie; as tra ta deiney er n'iu dy mie, eisht feeyn smessey: agh t'ou uss er vreayll y feeyn mie derrey nish.    
43N||2||11||Yn toshiaght shoh dy virrilyn ren Yeesey ayns Cana dy Ghalilee, as hoilshee eh magh e ghloyr; as ren e ynseydee credjal ayn.    
43N||2||12||Ny lurg shen, hie eh-hene, as e voir, as e vraaraghyn, as e ynseydee sheese gys Capernaum; as cha nhimmey laa duirree ad ayns shen.    
43N||2||13||As va Caisht ny Hewnyn er-gerrey, as hie Yeesey seose gys Jerusalem,    
43N||2||14||As hooar eh ayns y chiamble feallagh va creck dew, as kirree, as calmaneyn, as y vooinjer va caghlaa argid nyn soie:    
43N||2||15||As tra v'eh er n'yannoo kip dy choyrdyn keylley, deiyr eh ad ooilley ass y chiamble, as ny kirree, as ny dew; as spreih eh magh yn argid ocsyn va caghlaa, as hilg eh harrish ny buird;   
43N||2||16||As dooyrt eh roosyn va creck calmaneyn, Ersooyl-jee lesh ny reddyn shoh, ny jean-jee thie my Ayrey ny hie margee.    
43N||2||17||As chooinee e ynseydee dy row eh scruit, Ta graih jeean dty hie er my chur mow.    
43N||2||18||Eisht dreggyr ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Cre'n cowrey t'ou dy yeeaghyn dooin, fakin dy vel oo jannoo ny reddyn 
43N||2||19||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Lhieg-jee yn chiamble shoh, as trog-yms eh reesht ayns three laa.   
43N||2||20||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn, Shey bleeaney as da-eed va'n chiamble shoh dy hroggal, as Jean uss troggal eh ayns three laa?   
43N||2||21||Agh mychione chiamble e chorp hene loayr eshyn.   
43N||2||22||Shen-y-fa tra v'eh er n'irree veih ny merriu, chooinee ny ynseydee dy row eh er ghra shoh roo: as chred ad yn scriptyr, as y raa va Yeesey er loayrt.   
43N||2||23||Nish tra v'eh ec Jerusalem ec y chaisht, rish earish ny feailley, ren ymmodee credjal ayns yn ennym echey, tra honnick ad y mirrilyn v'eh er n'yannoo.   
43N||2||24||Agh cha hreisht Yeesey eh-hene orroo, er-yn-oyr dy row enney echey er dy chooilley ghooinney,   
43N||2||25||As nagh row feme echey er unnane erbee dy ymmyrkey feanish jeh dooinney: son va ys echey cre va ayns dooinney. 
43N||3||1||VA dooinney jeh ny Phariseeyn enmyssit Nicodemus, Dy ard-ghooinney mastey ny Hewnyn: 
43N||3||2||Haink eh shoh gys Yeesey ayns yn oie, as dooyrt eh rish, Rabbi, ta fys ain dy nee fer-ynsee as t'er jeet veih Jee: son cha vod dooinney erbee ny mirrilyn shen y yannoo t'ou uss dy yannoo, mannagh bee Jee marish.   
43N||3||3||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Mannagh bee dooinney er ny ruggey reesht, cha vod eh reeriaght Yee y akin.   
43N||3||4||Dooyrt Nicodemus rish, Kys oddys dooinney v'er ny ruggey tra t'eh shenn? vod eh goll stiagh yn nah cheayrt ayns brein, e vayrey, as cheet er y theihll? 
43N||3||5||Dreggyr Yeesey, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Mannagh bee dooinney er ny ruggey jeh ushtey as jeh'n spyrryd, cha vod eh goll stiagh ayns reeriaght Yee.   
43N||3||6||Shen t'er ny ruggey jeh'n eill, te foalley; as shen t'er ny ruggey jeh'n Spyrryd, te spyrrydoil.   
43N||3||7||Ny gow yindys dy dooyrt mee rhyt, Shegin diu v'er nyn ruggey reesht.   
43N||3||8||Ta'n gheay sheidey raad saillee, as t'ou clashtyn y sheean eck, agh cha s'ayd cre voish t'ee cheet, ny cre'n raad t'ee goll: myr shen ta dy chooilley unnane t'er ny ruggey Jeh'n Spyrryd.   
43N||3||9||Dreggyr Nicodemus as dooyrt eh rish, Kys oddys ny reddyn shoh y ve?   
43N||3||10||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Vel uss dty er-ynsee ayns Israel, as nagh vel toiggal ayd jeh ny reddyn shoh?   
43N||3||11||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, ta shin loayrt shen ta fys ain er, as gymmyrkey feanish Jeh ny ta shin er vakin; as cha vel shiu soiaghey jeh'n eanish ain.   
43N||3||12||My ta mish er loayrt riu jeh reddyn seihltagh, as nagh vel shiu dy my chredjal, kys nee shiu my chredjal my loayr-ym riu jeh reddyn flaunyssagh?   
43N||3||13||As cha vel dooinney erbee er gholl seose gys niau, agh eshyn haink neose veih niau, eer yn Mac dooinney ta ayns niau.   
43N||3||14||As myr ren Moses yn ard-nieu y hroggal seose ayns yn aasagh, myr shen shegin da Mac y dooinney v'er ny hroggal seose:   
43N||3||15||Nagh jean quoi-erbee ta credjal ayn cherraghtyn, agh dy bee yn vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey.   
43N||3||16||Son lheid y ghraih shen hug Jee da'n theihll, dy dug eh e ynrycan Vac v'er ny gheddyn, nagh jinnagh quoi-erbee chred jagh aynsyn cherraghtyn, agh yn vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn y chosney.   
43N||3||17||Son cha dug Jee e vac gys y theihll, dy gheyrey yn seihll; agh dy voddagh y seihll liorishyn v'er ny hauail.   
43N||3||18||Eshyn ta credjal ayn, cha vel eh er ny gheyrey: agh eshyn nagh vel credjal ayn, t'eh er ny gheyrey hannah, er-yn-oyr nagh vel eh er chredjal ayns ennym yn ynrycan Mac v'er ny gheddyn dy Yee.   
43N||3||19||As shoh yn vriwnys, dy vel soilshey er jeet gys y theihll, as dy row deiney ny s'graihee er y dorraghys (na er y toilshey, er-y fa dy row nyn obbraghyn olk.
43N||3||20||Son ta dy chooilley unnane ta jannoo dy holk, cur feoh da'n toilshey, chamoo t'eh cheet gys y toilshey, son nagh jig brah er ny obbraghyn echey.    
43N||3||21||Agh eshyn ta jannoo firrinys, t'eh cheet gys y toilshey, dy vod e obbraghyn v'er nyn soilshaghey magh, dy vel ad er nyn obbraghey ayns Jee.    
43N||3||22||Ny lurg shoh haink Yeesey as e ynseydee gys cheer Yudea, as duirree eh ayns shen maroo, as ren eh bashtey.    
43N||3||23||As va Ean myrgeddin bashtey ayns Enon, er-gerrey da Salem, er-y-fa dy row palchey dy ushtey ayns shen: as haink ad as v'ad er nyn mashtey.  
43N||3||24||Son cha row Ean foast tilgit ayns pryssoon.    
43N||3||25||Eisht dirree question eddyr paart jeh ynseydee Ean as ny Hewnyn, mychione bashtey. 
43N||3||26||As haink ad gys Ean, as dooyrt ad rish Rabbi, eshyn va mayrt er cheu elley dy Yordan, da ren oo feanish y ymmyrkey, cur my-ner, t'eshyn bashtey, as ta dy chooilley ghooinney cheet huggey.    
43N||3||27||Dreggyr Ean as dooyrt eh, Cha vod dooinney nhee erbee y ghoaill er hene, mannagh bee eh er ny choyrt da veih niau.    
43N||3||28||Ren shiuish shiu hene feanish y ymmyrkey lhiam, dy dooyrt mee, Cha nee mish yn Creest, agh dy vel mee er my choyrt roish.    
43N||3||29||Eshyn dooinney yn phoosee ta ben y phoosee echey: agh ta carrey dooinney yn phoosee ta ny hassoo as geaishtagh rish, goaill boggey mooar jeh coraa yn dooinney poosee: ta shoh my voggey's er-y-fa shen jeant magh.    
43N||3||30||Shegin dasyn bishaghey, agh shegin dooys parail.    
43N||3||31||Eshyn ta cheet veih'n yrjid, t'eh er skyn ooilley: eshyn ta jeh yn thalloo, t'eh thallooinagh, as loayrt jeh'n thalloo: eshyn ta cheet veih niau, t'eh erskyn ooilley.    
43N||3||32||As y red t'eh er vakin as er chlashtyn, shen t'eh gymmyrkey feanish jeh; as cha vel dooinney erbee soiaghey jeh'n eanish echey. 
43N||3||33||Eshyn t'er n'yannoo soiaghey jeh'n eanish echey, t'eh er chur y seal echey huggey, dy vel Jee firrinagh.
43N||3||34||Son t'eshyn ta Jee er choyrt, loayrt goan Yee: son cha nee liorish towse ta Jee cur y Spyrryd da.
43N||3||35||Ta'n Ayr graihagh er y Mac, as t'eh er chur dy chooilley nhee fo yn laue echey.
43N||3||36||Eshyn ta credjal ayns y Mac, ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey: as eshyn nagh vel credjal yn Mac, cha vaik eh yn vea, agh nee Jymmoose Yee tannaghtyn er.
43N||4||1||TRA va fys ec y Chiarn er-y-fa shen, kys va ny Phariseeyn er chlashtyn dy row Yeesey jannoo as bashtey ny sliee dy eiyrtyssee na va Ean.   
43N||4||2||(Ga nagh row Yeesey hene bashtey, agh e ynseydee)   
43N||4||3||Daag eh Judea, as jimmee eh reesht gys Galilee.   
43N||4||4||As beign da goll trooid Samaria.   
43N||4||5||Eisht haink eh gys ard-valley dy Samaria, ta enmyssit Sychar, er-gerrey da'n pheesh dy halloo hug Jacob da e vac Joseph.   
43N||4||6||Nish va chibbyr Yacob ayns shen. Myr va Yeesey er-y-fa shen skee lesh e yurnah, hoie eh sheese ayns shen liorish y chibbyr: as ve mysh y cheyoo oor.   
43N||4||7||Haink ben dy Samaria dy hayrn ushtey: dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Cur dou jough.   
43N||4||8||Son va ny ostyllyn er n'gholl gys y valley dy chionnaghey beaghey.   
43N||4||9||Eisht dooyrt y ven dy Samaria rish,Kys dy vel uss, ta dty Hew, shirrey jough orrym's, ta my ven dy Samaria? son cha vel veg y dellal ec ny Hewnyn rish ny Samaritanee. 
43N||4||10||Dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh r'ee, Dy beagh fys ayd's er gioot Yee, as quoi eh ta gra rhyt, Cur jough dou! veagh oo er hirrey ersyn, as veagh eh er chur dhyt ushtey bio.   
43N||4||11||Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, cha vel red erbee ayd dy hayrn lesh, as ta'n chibbyr dowin: cre voish eisht ta'n ushtey bio shen ayd?  
43N||4||12||Vel uss ny s'ooasle na'n ayr ain Jacob, hug dooin y chibbyr shoh, as diu j'ee eh hene, as e chloan, as y maase echey?   
43N||4||13||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh r'ee, Quoi-erbee iu-ys jeh'n ushtey shoh bee eh paagh reesht:   
43N||4||14||Agh quoi-erbee iu-ys jeh'n ushtey ver-yms da, cha bee eh dy bragh paagh: agh bee yn ushtey ver-ym da ny farrane ushtey ayn nee geill gys y vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn.   
43N||4||15||Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, cur dooys yn ushtey shoh, nagh bee'm paagh, as nagh jig-ym ayns shoh dy hayrn.   
43N||4||16||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Immee as eie er dty heshey, as tar ayns shoh.   
43N||4||17||Dreggyr y ven as dooyrt ee, Cha vel sheshey aym. Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, t'ou er ghra dy mie, Cha vel sheshey aym:   
43N||4||18||Son ta queig deiney er ny ve ayd, as eshyn t'ayd nish, cha nee dty heshey-poost eh: ayns shen t'ou er ghra yn irriney,   
43N||4||19||Dooyrt y ven rish, Vainshter, ta mee cur tastey dy nee phadeyr oo.   
43N||4||20||Ren ny ayraghyn ain ooashlaghey Jee er y clieau shoh; as ta shiuish gra, dy nee ayns Jerusalem ta'n boayl raad lhisagh sleih ooashlaghey.   
43N||4||21||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cred mish, ta'n oor cheet tra nagh jean shiu er y clieau shoh, ny foast ec Jerusalem ooashley 'choyrt da'n Ayr.
43N||4||22||Ta shiuish cur ooashley da, cha s'eu cre: ta fys ainyn cre ta shin cur ooashley da; son ta saualtys jeh ny Hewnyn.   
43N||4||23||Agh ta'n oor cheet, as nish ayn dy jean ny ooashleyderyn firrinagh ooashlaghey yn Ayr ayns Spyrryd as ayns firrinys: son ta'n Ayr shirrey nyn lheid oc shoh dy chur ooashley da.   
43N||4||24||Ta Jee ny Spyrryd, as shegin dauesyn ta ooashlaghey eh, ooashley y choyrt da ayns Spyrryd as ayns firrinys.   
43N||4||25||Dooyrt y ven rish, Ta fys aym dy vel Messias cheet ta enmyssit Creest: tra hig eshyn, inshee eh dooin dy chooilley nhee.   
43N||4||26||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, She mish ta loayrt rhyt eh shen. 
43N||4||27||As er shen haink e ostyllyn, as ghow ad yindys dy row eh taggloo rish y ven: foast cha dooyrt dooinney erbee, Cre t'ou dy hirrey? ny, Cre'n-fa t'ou taggloo r'ee? 
43N||4||28||Daag yn ven eisht yn saagh-ushtey eck, as hie ee rhymbee gys y valley, as dooyrt ee rish ny deiney   
43N||4||29||Tarjee as hee shiu dooinney t'er n'insh dou ooilley ny ren mee rieau: nagh nee shoh yn Creest?   
43N||4||30||Eisht hie ad magh ass y valley as haink ad huggey.   
43N||4||31||Ayns y traa shen ghuee e ostyllyn er, gra, Vainshter, gow beaghey.   
43N||4||32||Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Ta bee aym's dy ee nagh vel fys euish er.   
43N||4||33||Shen-y-fa dooyrt ny ostyllyn yn derrey yeh rish y jeh elley, Vel dooinney erbee er chur lesh nhee erbee huggey dy ee?   
43N||4||34||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Yn beaghey aym's eh, dy yannoo yn aigney echeysyn t'er my choyrt, as dy chooilleeney yn obbyr echey.   
43N||4||35||Nagh vel shiu gra, dy vel kiare meeghyn foast, as eisht ta'n fouyr cheet? cur-my ner ta mish gra riu, Trog-jee seose nyn sooillyn, as jeeagh-jee er ny magheryn; son t'ad bane hannah son y fouyr.   
43N||4||36||As ta'n beaynee geddyn faill, as chaglym mess gys y vea veayn: dy vod chammah yn correyder as y beaynee boggey y ghoaill cooidjagh.   
43N||4||37||As ayns shoh ta'n raa shen firrinagh, Ta fer cuirr, as fer elley buinn.   
43N||4||38||Hug mish shiu magh dy vuinn cooid nagh ren shiu y laboragh: ta deiney elley er laboragh, as ta shiuish er gholl stiagh er y laboraght oc.   
43N||4||39||As ren ymmodee jeh Samaritanee yn ard-valley shen credjal ayn, kyndagh rish raa yn ven, ren feanish y ymmyrkey, Dinsh eh dou ooilley ny ren mee rieau.   
43N||4||40||Myr shoh tra va ny Samaritanee el jeet huggey, ghuee ad er, eh dy uirriaght maroo: as duirree eh ayns shen daa laa.   
43N||4||41||As ren ymmodee elley credjal ayn e coontey e ghoo hene; 
43N||4||42||As dooyrt ad rish y ven, Nish ta shin credjal, cha nee son y raa ayd's; son ta shiu hene er chlashtyn eh, as ta fys ain, dy nee shoh dy jarroo yn Creest Saualtagh y theihll.   
43N||4||43||Nish lurg daa laa jimmee eh veih shen, as hie eh roish gys Galilee:   
43N||4||44||Son ren Yeesey hene feanish y ymmyrkey, nagh vel ooashley ec phadeyr ayns e heer hene,   
43N||4||45||Tra v'eh eisht er jeet gys Galilee, ren ny Galileanee mooar jeh, liorish dy row ad er vakin ooilley ny ren eh ec Jerusalem, ec y feailley: son v'adsyn er ve ec y feailley. 
43N||4||46||Myr shen haink Yeesey reesht gys Cana ayns Galilee, raad v'eh er hyndaa yn ushtey gys feeyn. As va chiarn dy row, va'n mac echey ching ec Capernaum.   
43N||4||47||Tra cheayll eh dy row Yeesey er jeet veih Judea gys Galilee, hie eh huggey, as ghuee eh er, eh dy heet neose dy lheihys e vac: son v'eh raad y vaaish.   
43N||4||48||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish, Mannagh vaik shiu cowraghyn as yindyssyn, cha jean shiu credjal.   
43N||4||49||Dooyrt y chiarn rish, Vainshter, tar neose roish my vow my lhiannoo baase.   
43N||4||50||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Immee royd; ta dty vac bio. As chred y dooinney yn ockle va Yeesey er loayrt rish, as hie eh roish.   
43N||4||51||As tra v'eh nish goll sheese, haink ny sharvaantyn echey ny whail, as dinsh ad da, gra, Ta dty vac bio.   
43N||4||52||Eisht denee eh jeu cre'n oor ren eh toshiaght dy choural: as dooyrt ad rish, Jea ec y chiaghtoo oor daag y chiassaghey eh.   
43N||4||53||Myr shen va fys ec yn ayr dy nee ayns yn oor cheddin va Yeesey er ghra rish, Ta dty vac bio; as ren eh-hene credjal as ooilley e hie.   
43N||4||54||Shoh neesht yn nah virril ren Yeesey, tra v'eh er jeet veih Judea gys Galilee. 
43N||5||1||NY lurg shoh va feailley ny Hewnyn, as hie Yeesey seose gys Jerusalem.   
43N||5||2||Nish ta ec Jerusalem liorish giat ny geyrragh, loghan, ta enmyssit ayns y ghlare Hebrewnagh Bethesda, ta queig porchyn er.   
43N||5||3||Ayndoo shoh va nyn lhie ymmodee dy leih dourinagh, doail, baccee, shirgeydee, as v'ad fieau er gleashaght yn ushtey.   
43N||5||4||Son va ainle goll sheese ec lheid y traa shen ayns yn ushtey, as seiy yn ushtey: quoi erbee eisht va hoshiaght goll sheese lurg seiy yn ushtey, v'eh er ny laanaghey jeh doghan erbee dy row er.   
43N||5||5||As va ayns shen dooinney dy row, va doghan er ve er rish hoght bleeaney jeig as feed.   
43N||5||6||Tra honnick Yeesey eh ny lhie, as fys echey dy row eh er ve myr shen ry-foddey dy hraa, dooyrt eh rish, Nailt ve er dty laanaghey?   
43N||5||7||Dreggyr yn annooinagh eh, Vainshter, cha vel dooinney erbee aym, tra ta'n ushtey seiyt, dy my cur sheese ayns y loghan: agh choud as ta mee cheet, ta fer elley goll sheese roym.   
43N||5||8||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Trog ort, gow seose dty lhiabbee as jean shooyll.   
43N||5||9||As er-y-chooyl va'n dooinney er ny lheihys, as ghow eh seose e lhiabbee, as huill eh: as er y laa shen va'n doonaght.   
43N||5||10||Dooyrt ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen rishyn v'er ny lheihys, She laa yn doonaght t'ayn; cha vel eh lowal dhyt gymmyrkey dty lhiabbee.   
43N||5||11||Dreggyr eshyn ad, Eshyn ren m'y laanaghey, dooyrt eh shen rhym, Trog dty lhiabbee as shooill.   
43N||5||12||Eisht denee ad jeh, Quoi va yn dooinney shen dooyrt rhyt, Trog dty lhiabbee as shooill?   
43N||5||13||As cha row fys echeysyn v'er ny lheihys, quoi v'eh: son va Yeesey er gholl dy lhiattee, liorish dy row chaglym mooar dy leih ayns y voayl shen.   
43N||5||14||Ny lurg shen hooar Yeesey eh ayns y chiamble, as dooyrt eh rish, Cur-my-ner, t'ou er dty laanaghey: ny jean peccah ny smoo, er-aggle dy jig red smessey ort.   
43N||5||15||Jimmee yn dooinney roish, as dinsh eh da ny Hewnyn dy nee Yeesey v'er laanaghey eh.   
43N||5||16||As er-yn-oyr shen ren ny Hewnyn tranlaase er Yeesey, as v'ad shirrey eh y choyrt gy-baase, er-y-fa dy row eh er n'yannoo ny red dyn shoh er laa yn doonaght.   
43N||5||17||Agh dreggyr Yeesey ad, Ta my Ayr gobbraghey derrey nish: as ta mish gobbraghey.   
43N||5||18||Shen-y-fa va ny Hewnyn wheesh shen smoo shleeuit er cur dy baase eh; er-yn-oyr dy row eh cha nee ynrycan er vrishey yn doonaght, agh er ghra myrgeddin dy nee Jee va'n Ayr echey, jannoo eh-hene corrym rish Jee. 
43N||5||19||Eisht dreggyr Yeesey, as dooyrt eh roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha vod y Mac nhee erbee y yannoo jeh hene, agh ny t'eh fakin yn Ayr dy yannoo: son cre-erbee t'eshyn dy yannoo, ta'n Mac jannoo myrgeddin.   
43N||5||20||Son ta'n Ayr graihagh er y Mac, as t'eh soilshaghey da dy chooilley nhee t'eh hene dy yannoo: as soilshee eh da obbragh yn smoo na ad shoh, dy vod shiu yindys y ghoaill.   
43N||5||21||Son myr ta'n Ayr troggal seose, as cur bioys da ny merriu: eer myr shen ta'n Mac bioghey yn vooinjer saillish.   
43N||5||22||Son cha vel yn Ayr briwnys dooinney erbee; agh t'eh er livrey dy chooilley vriwnys gys y Mac:   
43N||5||23||Dy voddagh dy chooilley ghooinney ooashley y choyrt da'n Mac, myr t'ad cur ooashley da'n Ayr. Eshyn nagh vel cur ooashley da'n Mac, cha vel eh coyrt ooashley da'n Ayr ren y choyrt eh.   
43N||5||24||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn ta clashtyn my ghoo's, as credjal ayn syn t'er my choyrt, ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey, as cha jig eh gys coayl-anmey: agh t'eh er gholl veih baase gys bea.   
43N||5||25||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ta'n oor cheet, as nish ayn, tra nee ny merriu clashtyn coraa Mac Yee: as bee adsyn chlinnys er nyn mioghey.   
43N||5||26||Son 'naght myr ta ec yn Ayr bioys ayn hene; myr shen t'eh er choyrt da'n Mac bioys y ve echey ayn hene;   
43N||5||27||As t'eh er choyrt da pooar dy yannoo briwnys myrgeddin, er-y-fa dy nee Mac y dooinney eh.   
43N||5||28||Ny gow-jee yindys jeh shoh: son ta'n oor cheet, tra chlinnys ooilley ny t'ayns ny oaiaghyn e choraa, 
43N||5||29||As hig ad magh; adsyn t'er n'yannoo dy mie, gys irree-seose-reesht y vea; as adsyn t'er n'yannoo dy olk, gys irree-seose reesht y choayl-anmey.   
43N||5||30||Cha voddym jee'm pene nhee erbee y yannoo: myr ta mee clashtyn, ta mee briwnys: as ta my vriwnys cairagh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel mee shirrey my aigney hene, agh aigney yn Ayr t'er my choyrt. 
43N||5||31||My ta mee gymmyrkey feanish jee'm pene, cha vel my eanish firrinagh.   
43N||5||32||Ta fer elley ta gymmyrkey feanish jee'm, as ta fys aym dy vel yn eanish t'eh dy ymmyrkey jee'm firrinagh.   
43N||5||33||Hug shiuish fys gys Ean, as dymmyrk eh feanish gys yn irriney. 
43N||5||34||Agh cha vel mish goaill fenish veih dooinney: agh shoh ta mee dy ghra, dy vod shiu v'er nyn sauail.   
43N||5||35||V'eshyn ny hoilshey gial as sollys: as va shiu booiagh son earish boggey 'ghoaill ayns y soilshey echey.   
43N||5||36||Agh ta feanish stroshey aym's na Ean: son ny obbraghyn hug my Ayr dou dy chooilleeney, ny obbraghyn cheddin ta mee dy yannoo, t'ad gymmyrkey feanish jee'm, dy vel yn Ayr er my choyrt.   
43N||5||37||As ta'n Ayr hene t'er my choyrt, er n'ymmyrkey feanish jee'm. Cha vel shiuish er chlashtyn e choraa ec traa erbee, ny er vakin e chaslys.   
43N||5||38||As cha vel eu yn goo echeysyn tannaghtyn ayndiu: son eshyn t'eh er choyrt, aynsyn cha vel shiu credjal.   
43N||5||39||Ronsee-jee ny scriptyryn, son ayndoosyn ta shiu smooinaghtyn dy vel y vea veayn eu, as she ad shen ta gymmyrkey feanish jeem's.   
43N||5||40||As cha vel shiu booiagh cheet hym's, dy vod yn vea y ve eu. 
43N||5||41||Cha vel mish soiaghey jeh ooashley deiney.   
43N||5||42||Agh ta toiggal aym jiuish, nagh vel graih Yee ayndiu.   
43N||5||43||Ta mish er jeet ayns ennym my Ayrey, as cha vel shiu goaill rhym: my hig fer elley ayns e ennym hene, rishyn nee shiu goaill. 
43N||5||44||Kys oddys shiuish credjal ta geddyn ooashley yn derrey yeh veih yn jeh elley, as nagh vel shirrey yn ooashley ta veih Jee ny lomarcan?   
43N||5||45||Ny smooinee-jee dy jean-yms plaiynt erriu gys yn Ayr: ta ayn ta plaiynt nyn 'oi eu, eer Moses, ayn ta shiu treishteil.   
43N||5||46||Son dy beagh shiu er chredjal Moses, veagh shiu er chredjal aynym's; son scrieu eh jeem's.   
43N||5||47||Agh mannagh gred shiu ny screeuyn echeysyn, kys nee shiu credjal ny goan aym's?
43N||6||1||NY lurg shoh hie Yeesey harrish faarkey Ghalilee, ny Tiberias.   
43N||6||2||As deiyr earroo mooar dy leih er, er-y-fa dy vaik ad ny mirrilyn ren eh orroosyn va doghanit.   
43N||6||3||As hie Yeesey seose er slieau, as hoie eh ayns shen marish e ostyllyn.   
43N||6||4||As va'n Chaisht, feailley ny Hewnyn er gerrey.   
43N||6||5||Tra va Yeesey eisht er hroggal seose e hooillyn, as fakin earroo mooar dy leih cheet huggey, dooyrt eh rish Philip, Cre-voish oddys mayd arran y chionnaghey, dy yannoo magh ad shoh?   
43N||6||6||(As shoh dooyrt eh dy phrowal eh: son v'eh hene kiarit cre dy yannoo.)   
43N||6||7||Dreggyr Philip eh, Cha bee feeagh daa cheead ping dy arran dy liooar daue, dy vod dagh unnane oc kuse y ghoaill.   
43N||6||8||Dooyrt fer jeh ny ostyllyn echey, Andreays, braar Simon Peddyr, rish,   
43N||6||9||Ta scollag ayns shoh ta queig bwilleenyn oarn echey, as daa eeast veggey; agh cre t'ad shen mastey whilleen? 
43N||6||10||As dooyrt Yeesey, Cur-jee er ny deiney soie sheese. Nish va lane faiyr ayns yn ynnyd. Myr shen hoie ny deiney sheese ayns earroo mysh queig thousaneyn.   
43N||6||11||As ghow Yeesey ny bwilleenyn, as tra v'eh er chur booise, rheynn eh ad er e ostyllyn, as rheynn adsyn ad orroosyn myr v'ad soie; as myrgeddin jeh ny eeastyn wheesh as bailloo.  
43N||6||12||Tra v'ad jeant magh, dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Jean-jee yn vrooilliagh ta er-mayrn y haglym cooidjagh nagh bee nhee erbee caillit.   
43N||6||13||Er shen ren ad eh y haglym, as lhieen ad daa vaskad jeig lesh fooilliagh ny queig bwilleenyn oarn, va er-mayrn erreish daue v'er n'ee.   
43N||6||14||Eisht dooyrt ny deiney shen, tra v'ad er vakin y mirril va Yeesey er n'yannoo. She shoh ayns firrinys yn phadeyr shen va ry-hoi cheet gys y theihll. 
43N||6||15||Tra dennee Yeesey er-y-fa shen dy darragh ad, as dy goghe ad eh er-niart, dy yannoo eh ny ree, hie eh seose reesht er slieau eh-hene ny-lomarcan.   
43N||6||16||As tra va'n fastyr er, hie e ostyllyn sheese gys y cheayn.  
43N||6||17||As ghow ad lhuingys, as haink ad harrish y cheayn gys Capernaum: as ve nish dorraghey, as cha row Yeesey er jeet huc.   
43N||6||18||As dhatt y keayn lesh niart stermagh ny geayee.   
43N||6||19||Myr shen tra v'ad er n'ymmyrt mysh kiare veeilley, honnick ad Yeesey shooyl er y cheayn, as tayrn er-gerrey da'n lhong: as ghow ad aggle.   
43N||6||20||Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, She mish t'ayn, ny bee aggle erriu.   
43N||6||21||Eisht ghow ad eh dy arryltagh stiagh ayns y lhong: as chelleeragh va'n lhong ec y thalloo raad v'ad goll.   
43N||6||22||Yn laa er-giyn, tra honnick yn pobble va nyn shassoo cheu elley jeh'n cheayn nagh row baatey erbee elley ayns shen, cheu-mooie jeh'n un vaatey shen va ny ostyllyn er n'ghoaill, as nagh jagh Yeesey maroosyn ayns y vaatey, agh dy row ny ostyllyn er n'gholl ersooyl nyn-lomarcan:   
43N||6||23||(Ny-yeih va baatyn elley er jeet veih Tiberias, er-gerrey da'n boayl ren ad arran y ee ayn, erreish da'n Chiarn v'er chur booise.)   
43N||6||24||Tra honnick y pobble er-y-fa shen nagh row Yeesey ayns shen, ny e ostyllyn, ghow adsyn myrgeddin lhuingys, as haink ad gys Capernaum, briaght son Yeesey.   
43N||6||25||As tra hooar ad eh er y cheu elley jeh'n cheayn, dooyrt ad rish, Rabbi, cuin haink oo ayns shoh?   
43N||6||26||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Ta shiu dy my hirrey's, cha nee er-yn-oyr dy vaik shiu ny mirrilyn, agh son dy d'ee shiu jeh ny bwilleenyn, as dy row shiu jeant magh.   
43N||6||27||Ny bee-jee imneagh son y beaghey ta cherraghtyn, agh son y beaghey shen ta tannaghtyn gys y vea veayn, nee yn Mac dooinney y choyrt diu: son eshyn ta Jee yn Ayr er chowraghey.   
43N||6||28||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre nee mainyn, dy vod mayd obbraghyn Yee y yannoo?   
43N||6||29||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Shoh obbyr Yee, shiu dy chredjal aynsyn t'eh er choyrt. 
43N||6||30||Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen rish, Cre'n cowrey t'ou dy yeeaghyn eisht, dy vod mayd fakin as credjal aynyd? cre ta dty obbyr?   
43N||6||31||D'ee ny ayraghyn ain manna ayns yn aasagh; myr te scruit, Hug eh daue arran veih niau dy ee.   
43N||6||32||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha dug Moses diu yn arran shen veih niau, agh my Ayr ta coyrt diu yn arran firrinagh veih niau.   
43N||6||33||Son arran Yee eshyn ta cheet neose veih niau, as ta cur e vioys son y theihll.   
43N||6||34||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cur dooinyn dy bragh yn arran shoh.   
43N||6||35||As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Mish arran y vea: eshyn ta cheet hym's, cha bee eh dy bragh accryssagh; as eshyn ta credjal aynym, cha bee eh dy bragh paagh. 
43N||6||36||Agh ta mish er ghra riu, dy vel shiu myrgeddin er my akin's, as nagh vel shiu credjal.    
43N||6||37||Hig adsyn ooilley hym's ta'n Ayr dy chur dou; as eshyn ta cheet hym, cha jeanym er aght erbee y yiooldey voym.    
43N||6||38||Son haink mish neose veih niau, cha nee dy yannoo my aigney hene, agh yn aigney echeysyn ren m'y choyrt.    
43N||6||39||As shoh aigney yn Ayr ta er my choyrt, jeh ooilley ny hug eh dou nagh gaillin veg, agh dy droggin eh seose reesht ec y laa jerrinagh.    
43N||6||40||As shoh yn aigney echeysyn ta er my choyrt, dy chooilley unnane ta fakin y Mac as credjal ayn, yn vea dy bragh farraghtyn dy ve echey: as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh.    
43N||6||41||Eisht va ny Hewnyn jymmoosagh rish, er-y-fa dy dooyrt eh, Mish arran y vea haink neose veih niau.    
43N||6||42||As dooyrt ad, Nagh nee shoh Yeesey Mac Yoseph, yn ayr as y voir echey shione dooin? kys eisht dy vel eh gra, Haink mee neose veih niau?    
43N||6||43||Dreggyr Yeesey er-y-fa shen as dooyrt eh roo, Ny lhig da jymmoose ve ny mast' eu.    
43N||6||44||Cha vod dooinney erbee cheet hym's, mannagh jean yn Ayr t'er my choyrt y hayrn eh: as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh. 
43N||6||45||Te scruit ayns ny phadeyryn, As bee ad ooilley ynsit liorish Jee. Dy chooilley ghooinney er-y-fa shen t'er chlashtyn, as er n'ynsaghey veih yn Ayr, t'eh cheet hym's. 
43N||6||46||Cha nee dy vel dooinney erbee er va kin yn Ayr, cheu-mooie jehsyn ta veih Jee, t'eh shen er vakin yn Ayr.    
43N||6||47||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn ta credjal ayn-yms ta'n vea ta dy bragh farraghtyn echey.    
43N||6||48||Mish arran y vea.   
43N||6||49||D'ee ny ayraghyn euish manna ayns yn aasagh, as t'ad marroo.   
43N||6||50||Shoh yn arran ta cheet neose veih niau, dy vod dooinney gee jeh, as gyn baase y gheddyn.   
43N||6||51||Mish yn arran bio, haink neose veih niau: my ee-ys dooinney erbee jeh'n arran shoh, bee eh bio son dy bragh: as yn arran neem's y choyrt, she my eill eh, ver-yms son bioys y theihll. 
43N||6||52||Va ec ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen argane nyn mast oc hene, gra, Kys oddys y dooinney shoh cur dooin e eill dy ee?   
43N||6||53||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh focklagh ta mee gra riu, Mannagh jean shiu feill yn Mac dooinney y ee, as e uill y iu, cha vel y vea eu ayndiu.   
43N||6||54||Eshyn ta gee my eill, as giu my uill, ta'n vea veayn echey, as trog-yms seose eh ec y laa jerrinagh.   
43N||6||55||Son dy firrinagh she bee my eill, as dy firrinagh she jough my uill.   
43N||6||56||Eshyn ta gee my eill as giu my uill, t'eh baghey aynym's, as mish aynsyn   
43N||6||57||Myr ta'n Ayr bio er my choyrt's, as ta mee bio liorish yn Ayr: myr shen neesht vees eshyn ta dy my ee's, bio liorym.   
43N||6||58||Shoh yn arran haink neese veih niau; cha nee myr ren ny ayraghyn eu manna y ee, as t'ad marroo: bee eshyn ta gee jeh'n arran shoh, bio son dy bragh.   
43N||6||59||Ny goan shoh loayr eh ayns y synagogue, myr v'eh gynsaghey ayns Capernaum.    
43N||6||60||Dooyrt ymmodee er-y-fa shen jeh e eiyrtee, tra cheayll ad shoh, Shoh raa creoi, quoi oddys y chlashtyn eh?    
43N||6||61||Tra va fys ec Yeesey ayn hene dy row e eiyrtee jymmoosagh son shoh, dooyrt eh roo, Vel shoh cheet ayns raad y chredjue eu?    
43N||6||62||Cre my hee shiu Mac y dooinney goll seose raad v'eh roie?    
43N||6||63||She yn spyrryd ta bioghey, cha vel yn eill jannoo veg y vie: ny goan ta mish dy loayrt riu, t'ad spyrryd as t'ad bea.    
43N||6||64||Agh ta paart jiuish nagh vel credjal. Son va fys ec Yeesey er-dyn toshiaght, quoi v'ad nagh row credjal, as quoi yinnagh eh y vrah. 
43N||6||65||As dooyrt eh, Shen-y-fa dooyrt mish riu, nagh vod dooinney erbee cheet hym's mannagh bee eh er ny choyrt da liorish my Ayr.    
43N||6||66||Veih yn traa shen hie ymmodee jeh e eiyrtee back, as cha huill ad arragh marish.    
43N||6||67||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish y daa ostyl yeig, Jed shiuish myrgeddin reue?    
43N||6||68||Eisht dreggyr Simon Peddyr eh, Hiarn, quoi gys hem mayd? ayd's ta goan y vea veayn.    
43N||6||69||As ta shin credjal, as shickyr jeh dy nee uss yn Creest, Mac y Jee bio.    
43N||6||70||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Nagh vel mish er reih shiuish yn ghaa-yeig, as ta fer j'iu ny youyl?    
43N||6||71||Loayr eh jeh Yuaase Iscariot mac Simon: son eshyn eh va dy vrah eh, as v'eh fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig. 
43N||7||1||NY lurg shoh duirree Yeesey ayns Galillee: son cha row eh booiagh cummal ayns Judea, er-yn-oyr dy row ny Hewnyn shirrey eh y varroo.    
43N||7||2||Nish va feailley cabbaneyn ny Hewnyn er-gerrey.    
43N||7||3||Dooyrt e vraaraghyn er-y-fa shen rish, Faag y voayl shoh, as immee gys Judea, dy vod ny eiyrtee t'ayd ayns shen myrgeddin fakin ny obbraghyn t'ou dy yannoo.    
43N||7||4||Son cha vel dooinney erbee freayll e obbraghyn follit, as eh-hene shirrey dy ve cronnal: My t'ou jannoo ny reddyn shoh soilshee oo hene da'n theihll.    
43N||7||5||Son chamoo ren e vraaraghyn hene credjal ayn.    
43N||7||6||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cha vel my hraa's foast er jeet: agh ta'n traa euish dy kinjagh jesh diu.    
43N||7||7||Cha vod y seihll dwoaie y chur diuish, agh dooys te cur dwoaie; er-yn-oyr dy vel mee gymmyrkey feanish jeh, dy vel ny obbraghyn echey olk.    
43N||7||8||Immee-jee shiuish seose gys y feailley shoh: cha vel mish son goll seose foast gys y feailley shoh, er-yn-oyr nagh vel my hraa foast er jeet.    
43N||7||9||Tra v'eh er ghra ny goan shoh roo duirree eh myr v'eh ayns Galilee. 
43N||7||10||Agh tra va e vraaraghyn er gholl seose, eisht hie eshyn myrgeddin seose gys y feailley, cha nee dy foshlit, agh myr dy beagh eh dy follit.
43N||7||11||Eisht va ny Hewnyn briaght er e hon ec y feailley, as dooyrt ad, Cre vel eh?   
43N||7||12||As va lane argane mastey yn pobble mychione echey: son va paart gra, She dooinney mie eh: as feallagh elley gra, Cha nee; agh t'eh molley yn pobble.    
43N||7||13||Ny-yeih, cha loayr dooinney erbee dy foshlit jeh, goaill aggle roish ny Hewnyn.    
43N||7||14||Nish mysh mean y feailley, hie Yeesey seose gys y chiamble, as dynsee eh.    
43N||7||15||As ghow ny Hewnyn yindys, gra, Kys ta lheid yn ynsagh ec y dooinney shoh, nagh row eh-hene rieau ynsit?    
43N||7||16||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh, Cha vel my ynsagh lhiam pene, agh leshyn t'er my choyrt.    
43N||7||17||My vees dooinney erbee aggindagh yn aigney echeysyn y yannoo, yiow eh toiggal jeh'n ynsagh, nee veih Jee te, ny vel mee loayrt jee'm pene.
