43N||7||18||Eshyn ta loayrt jeh hene, t'eh shirrey e ooashley hene: agh eshyn ta shirrey yn ooashley echeysyn t'er choyrt eh, t'eh shen firrinagh, as cha vel neu-chairys erbee ayn.    
43N||7||19||Nagh dug Moses yn leigh diu, as cha vel fer j'iu freayll yn leigh? Cre'n-fa ta shiu shirrey my vioys y ghoaill?   
43N||7||20||Dreggyr y pobble eh, as dooyrt ad, Ta drogh-spyrryd breagagh aynyd: Quoi ta shirrey dty vioys y ghoaill?    
43N||7||21||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ta mish er n'yannoo yn un obbyr shoh, as ta shiu ooilley goaill yindys.    
43N||7||22||Hug Moses er-y-fa shen yn giarey chymmylt diu, (cha nee son dy vel eh jeh Moses, agh jeh ny ayraghyn) as ta shiu er laa yn doonaght giarey-chymmylt dooinney.    
43N||7||23||My ta dooinney er y doonaght goaill giarey chymmylt, son nagh bee leigh Voses er ny vrishey; vel shiuish jymmoosagh rhym's, son dy vel mee er n'yannoo dooinney ooilley magh slane er y doonaght?    
43N||7||24||Ny jean-jee briwnys rere yn caslys, agh jean-jee briwnys cairagh. 
43N||7||25||Eisht dooyrt paart jeusyn va veih Jerusalem, Nagh nee shoh eh t'ad shirrey dy varroo?    
43N||7||26||Agh cur-my-ner, t'eh loayrt dy foshlit, as cha vel ad gra veg n'oi: vel dy jarroo fys ec ny firreill dy nee shoh yn Creest firrinagh?    
43N||7||27||Ny-yeih ta enney ain er y dooinney shoh cre-voish t'eh: agh tra hig Creest, cha bee fys ec dooinney erbee cre-voish t'eh.   
43N||7||28||Eisht deie Yeesey ayns y chiamble myr v'eh gynsaghey, gra, Ta chammah enney eu orrym's, aa ta fys eu cre-voish ta mee: as cha vel mish er jeet jee'm pene, agh t'eshyn t'er ny choyrt firrinagh, eshyn cha nione diu.   
43N||7||29||Agh shione dooys eh, son ta mee veih, as t'eh er my choyrt.   
43N||7||30||Eisht v'ad shirrey y ghoaill eh: agh cha dug dooinney erbee laue er, son nagh row yn oor echey foast er jeet.   
43N||7||31||As ren ymmodee jeh'n pobble credjal ayn, as dooyrt ad, Tra hig Creest, jean eh ny shlee mirril na ad shoh ta'n dooinney shoh er n'yannoo?   
43N||7||32||Cheayll ny Phariseeyn dy row yn pobble tallagh myr shoh my-e-chione: as hug ny  Phariseeyn as ny ard-saggyrtyn magh sidooryn dy ghoaill eh.   
43N||7||33||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Foast tammylt beg ta mish meriu, as eisht ta mee goll huggeysyn t'er my choyrt.   
43N||7||34||Shirree shiu mee agh cha vow shiu mee: as y raad ta mish, cha vod shiuish cheet.   
43N||7||35||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn nyn mast' oc hene, C'raad hed eh, nagh vow mayd eh? jed eh gys ny Hewnyn t'er nyn skeayley mastey ny Ashoonee, as adsyn y ynsaghey .   
43N||7||36||Cre'n monney dy raa shoh t'eh er loayrt, Shirree shiu mee, agh cha vow shiu mee: as y raad ta mish cha vod shiuish cheet? 
43N||7||37||Er y laa s'jerree, laa mooar ny feailley, hass Yeesey, as deie eh, gra, My ta dooinney erbee paagh, lhig da cheet hym's as giu.   
43N||7||38||Eshyn ta credjal aynym's, myr ta'n scriptyr er ghra, Ass y chree echeysyn roieys strooanyn dy ushtey bio.   
43N||7||39||(Agh shoh loayr eh jeh'n Spyrryd, v'adsyn va credjal ayn ry-hoi gheddyn: son cha row yn Spyrryd Noo foast er ny choyrt, er yn-oyr nagh row Yeesey foast er ny ghloyraghey.)
43N||7||40||Dooyrt ymmodee jeh'n phobble er-y fa shen, tra cheayll ad y raa shoh, Ayns firrinys shoh yn phadeyr.   
43N||7||41||Dooyrt feallagh elley, She shoh yn Creest. Agh dooyrt paart, Jig Creest ass Galilee?   
43N||7||42||Nagh vel y scriptyr er ghra, dy vel Creest dy heet jeh sluight Ghavid, as ass y balley Bethlehem, raad ruggyr David?   
43N||7||43||Myr shen va streeu mastey'n pobble mychione echey.   
43N||7||44||As va paart jeu son goaill eh; agh cha dug dooinney jeu laue er.   
43N||7||45||Eisht haink ny sidooryn gys ny ard saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn, dooyrt roo, Cre'n-fa nagh dug shiu lhieu eh?   
43N||7||46||Dreggyr ny sidooryn, Cha ren rieau dooinney loayrt myr y dooinney shoh.   
43N||7||47||Eisht dreggyr ny Phariseeyn ad, Vel shiuish myrgeddin er nyn molley? 
43N||7||48||Vel veg jeh ny fir-reill, as jeh ny Phariseeyn er chredjal ayn?
43N||7||49||Agh ta'n pobble shoh, nagh vel toiggal yn leigh, fo mollaght.
43N||7||50||Dooyrt Nicodemus roo (eh haink gys Yeesey ayns yn oie, v'eh fer jeusyn.)
43N||7||51||Vel y leigh ainyn deyrey dooinney erbee roish clashtyn y choyrt da, as prowal oc n'oi cre t'eh er n'yannoo?
43N||7||52||Dreggyr adsyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Nee ass Galilee t'ou uss myrgeddin? jean-jee ronsaghey as jeeaghyn: son cha vel phadeyr erbee er droggal ayns Galilee.
43N||7||53||As jimmee dy chooilley ghooinney roish gys e hie hene.
43N||8||1||HIE Yeesey gys cronk ny Oliveyn. 
43N||8||2||As dy moghey laa-ny-vairagh hie eh reesht gys y chiamble, as haink ooilley yn phobble huggey; as hoie eh sheese, as dynsee eh ad.
43N||8||3||As hug ny scrudeyryn as ny Phariseeyn lhieu huggey ben va goit ayns brishey-poosey; as tra v'ad er hoiaghey ee kiongoyrt rish,
43N||8||4||Dooyrt ad rish, Vainshter, va'n ven shoh goit ayns brishey-poosey, ayns yn eer peccah.
43N||8||5||Nish ta Moses ayns y leigh er chur sarey dooin, e lheid dy ve er ny claghey, agh cre t'ou uss dy ghra?
43N||8||6||Shoh dooyrt ad dy phrowal eh, dy vod dagh cooish chassid y ve oc n'oi. Agh chroym Yeesey sheese, as lesh e vair scrieu eh er y laare, myr nagh beagh eh dy nyn glashtyn.
43N||8||7||As myr lhie ad er son ansoor, hrog eh eh-hene seose, as dooyrt eh roo, Lhig dasyn ta fegooish peccah nyn mast'eu tilgey yn chied chlagh urree.
43N||8||8||As chroym eh sheese reesht, as scrieu eh er y laare.
43N||8||9||As v'adsyn cheayll eh, er nyn gheyrey liorish nyn gooin-sheanse hene, as hie ad magh fer lurg fer jeu, goaill toshiaght veih yn er-shinney gys yn er-saa: as va Yeesey faagit ny-lomarcan, as y ven ny shassoo kiongoyrt rish.
43N||8||10||Tra hrog Yeesey eh-hene seose, as nagh vaik eh unnane erbee agh y ven, dooyrt eh r'ee, Ven, cre vel ad shen dty chassidee? vel dooinney erbee er dty gheyrey?
43N||8||11||Dooyrt ish, Cha vel dooinney erbee, Hiarn. As dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Chamoo ta mish dy dty gheyrey: immee royd, as ny jean peccah arragh.
43N||8||12||Eisht loayr Yeesey roo reesht, gra, Mish soilshey yn theihll: eshyn ta geiyrt orrym's, cha shooyllee eh ayns y dorraghys, agh bee echeysyn soilshey yn vea,
43N||8||13||Dooyrt ny Phariseeyn er-y-fa shen rish, T'ou gymmyrkey feanish jeed hene; cha vel dty eanish firrinagh.
43N||8||14||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh roo, Ga dy vel mee gymmyrkey feanish jee'm pene, foast ta'n eanish firrinagh: son ta fys aym cre-voish haink mee, as c'raad ta mee goll; agh cha s'euish cre-voish haink mee ny c'raad ta mee goll.    
43N||8||15||Ta shiuish briwnys lurg briwnys ny foalley; cha vel mish briwnys dooinney erbee.    
43N||8||16||As foast my ta mee briwnys, ta my vriwnys firrinagh: son cha vel mish my lomarcan, agh mish as yn Ayr t'er my choyrt, t'eh marym.    
43N||8||17||Eer ayns y leigh eu hene te scruit, dy vel feanish daa ghooinney firrinagh.    
43N||8||18||Ta mish gymmyrkey feanish dou hene, as ta'n Ayr t'er my choyrt gymmyrkey feanish dou.    
43N||8||19||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre vel dty Ayr? Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel enney eu orrym's, ny er my Ayr: dy beagh enney er ve eu orrym s, veagh enney er ve eu er my Ayr myrgeddin.    
43N||8||20||Ny goan shoh loayr Yeesey 'sy room tashtee, myr v'eh gynsaghey ayns y chiamble: as cha dug dooinney erbee laue er, son cha row yn oor echey foast er jeet.    
43N||8||21||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Ta mee goll roym, as nee shiu my hirrey, as yiow shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn: raad ta mish goll, cha vod shiuish cheet.    
43N||8||22||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn, Jean eh eh hene y varroo? er-yn-oyr dy vel eh gra, raad ta mish goll, cha vod shiuish cheet.    
43N||8||23||As dooyrt eh roo, Ta shiuish veih heese ta mish veih heose: ta shiuish jeh'n theihll shoh, cha vel mish jeh'n theihll shoh.    
43N||8||24||Dooyrt mee er-y-fa shen riu, dy voghe shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn: son mannagh vel shiu credjal dy nee mish eh, yiow shiu baase ayns nyn beccaghyn. 
43N||8||25||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Quoi oo hene? As dooyrt Yeesey roo, Yn fer cheddin dooyrt mee riu er-dyn toshiaght.    
43N||8||26||Ta ymmodee reddyn aym's dy ghra as dy vriwnys jiuish: agh ta eshyn t'er my choyrt firrinagh as ta mee loayrt rish y theihll shen ta mee er chlashtyn veihsyn.    
43N||8||27||Cha hoig ad dy row eh loayrt roo my chione yn Ayr.    
43N||8||28||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Tra vees shiu erreish yn Mac dooinney y hroggal seose, eisht bee fys eu dy nee mish eh, as nagh vel mee jannoo nhee erbee jee'm pene; agh dy vel mee loayrt ny reddyn shen ta my Ayr er chur roym.    
43N||8||29||As ta eshyn t'er my choyrt marym: cha vel yn Ayr er my aagail my lomarcan: son ta mee dy kinjagh jannoo ny reddyn shen ta dy wooiys eh.    
43N||8||30||Choud as v'eh loayrt ny goan shoh ren ymmodee credjal ayn. 
43N||8||31||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish ny Hewnyn shen va credjal ayn, My nee shiu tannaghtyn ayns my ghoo, eisht bee shiu dy jarroo ny ynseydee ayms;    
43N||8||32||As bee toiggal eu jeh'n irriney, as nee yn irriney shiu y heyrey. 
43N||8||33||Dreggyr adsyn eh, She sluight Abraham shin, as cha row shin rieau ayns bondiaght da dooinney erbee: cre'n aght t'ou gra eisht, Bee shiu er nyn yannoo seyr?   
43N||8||34||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Dy firrinagh-focklagh ta mee gra riu, Quoi-erbee ta cur-rish peccah, t'eh ayns bondiaght peccah.   
43N||8||35||As cha vel y charvaant tannaghtyn kinjagh ayns y thie: agh ta'n Mac tannaght yn kinjagh.   
43N||8||36||My nee yn Mac er-y-fa shen shiuish seyr, bee shiu seyr dy jarroo.   
43N||8||37||Ta fys aym dy nee sluight Abraham shiu; agh ta shiu shirrey mish y varroo, er-y-fa nagh vel my ghoo er ghoaill greme erriu.   
43N||8||38||Ta mish loayrt shen ny ta mee er n'akin ec my Ayr's: as ta shuish jannoo shen ny ta shiu er vakin ec yn ayr euish.   
43N||8||39||Dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad rish, Abraham yn ayr ainyn. Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh shiuish nyn gloan da Abraham, yinnagh shiu obbraghyn Abraham.   
43N||8||40||Agh nish ta shiu shirrey mish y varroo, dooinney t'er n'insh diu yn irriney, ta mee er chlashtyn veih Jee: shoh cha ren Abraham.   
43N||8||41||Ta shiuish cur-rish obbraghyn nyn ayrey hene. Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cha ruggyr shinyn ayns maarderys; cha vel agh un Ayr ain, ta shen, Jee.   
43N||8||42||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh Jee yn Ayr eu, veagh shiu graihagh orrym's; son hie mee magh, as haink mee veih Jee; as cha daink mee jee'm pene, agh eshyn t'er my choyrt.   
43N||8||43||Cre'n-fa nagh vel shiu toiggal my ghlare? te son nagh vel shiu cur geill da my ghoo.   
43N||8||44||Ta shiuish jeh'n ayr eu yn drogh spyrryd, as saynt nyn ayrey ver shiu rish: v'eshyn ny ghunver er-dyn toshiaght, as cha ren eh tannaghtyn 'syn ynrickys, son nagh vel yn irriney ayn. Tra t'eh loayrt breg, t'eh loayrt jeh e chooid hene : son t'eh ny vreagerey, as ayr ny breagey.   
43N||8||45||As ga dy vel mee ginsh diu yn irriney, cha vel shiu dy my chredjal.   
43N||8||46||Quoi jiuish ta cur peccah my lieh? as my ta mee gra yn irriney, cre'n-fa nagh vel shiu dy my chredjal?   
43N||8||47||Eshyn ta veih Jee, t'eh cur geill da goan Yee: agh cha vel shiuish cur geill daue, son nagh vel shiu veih Jee.   
43N||8||48||Eisht dreggyr ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt ad rish, Nagh vel shin gra yn irriney, dy nee Samaritan oo, as dy vel drogh-spyrryd aynyd.   
43N||8||49||Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel drogh-spyrryd aynym's; agh ta mee cur ooashley da my Ayr, as ta shiuish cur mee-ooashley dooys. 
43N||8||50||As cha vel mee shirrey my ghloyr hene: ta fer ayn ta shirrey as briwnys.   
43N||8||51||Dy firrinagh-focklagh ta mee gra riu, My ta dooinney freayll my raa's, cha vaik eh yn baase dy bragh beayn.   
43N||8||52||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn rish, Nish ta fys ain dy vel drogh-spyrryd aynyd. Ta Abraham marroo as ny phadeyryn; as t'ou uss gra, My ta dooinney freayll my raa's, cha jean eh blashtyn er y baase dy bragh beayn.   
43N||8||53||Vel uss ny s'ooasle na'n ayr ain Abraham, ta marroo? as ta ny phadeyryn marroo: quoi t'ou jannoo jeed hene?   
43N||8||54||Dreggyr Yeesey, My ta mee cur ooashley dou hene, cha vel my ooashley agh beggan feeu: she my Ayr ta cur ooashley dou, jehsyn ta shiuish loayrt, dy nee yn Jee eu eh:   
43N||8||55||Ny-yeih cha nione diuish eh; agh shione dooys eh: as dy n'yiarrin nagh nione dou eh, veign my vreagerey goll riuish: agh shione dooys eh, as ta mee freayll yn raa echey.   
43N||8||56||Ghow yn ayr eu Abraham foddiaght dy akin yn laa aym's: as honnick eh eh, as ghow eh boggey.   
43N||8||57||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn rish, Cha vel uss foast jeih bleeaney as da-eed dy eash, as vel oo er vakin Abraham?   
43N||8||58||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Roish my row Abraham, Ta mish.   
43N||8||59||Eisht hrog ad claghyn dy cheau er: agh cheill Yeesey eh-hene voue, as hie eh magh ass y chiamble, goll trooid y cheeid oc as myr shen hie eh shaghey. 
43N||9||1||AS myr va Yeesey goll shaghey, honnick eh dooinney v'er ny ruggey doal.   
43N||9||2||As denee e ostyllyn jeh, gra, Vainshter quoi ren peccah, eh shoh ny e ayr as e voir, dy row eh er ny ruggey doal?   
43N||9||3||Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha nee son peccah dy ren eh shoh, ny e ayr as e voir: agh dy vod dagh obbraghyn Yee v'er nyn soilshaghey magh ayn.   
43N||9||4||Shegin dooys gobbraghey ny obbraghyn echeysyn t'er my choyrt, choud as ta'n laa ayn: ta'n oie cheet tra nagh vod dooinney erbee gobbraghey.   
43N||9||5||Choud as ta mee ayns y theihll, mee soilshey yn theihll.   
43N||9||6||Tra v'eh erreish shoh y loayrt, cheau eh shelley er y thalloo, as ren eh cray jeh'n shelley, as hug eh yn chray rish sooillyn y dooinney doal.  
43N||9||7||As dooyrt eh rish, Immee as oonlee oo hene ayns poyll Siloam (ta shen 'sy ghlare ainyn, Er ny choyrt) Hie eh roish er-y-fa shen, as doonlee eh eh-hene, as haink eh as e hoilshey echey.   
43N||9||8||Dooyrt ny naboonyn er-y-fa shen, as adsyn va roie er vakin eh dy row eh doal, Nagh nee shoh eshyn boallagh soie shirrey jeirk ?   
43N||9||9||Dooyrt paart, She shoh eh: dooyrt feallagh elley, T'eh goll-rish: agh dooyrt eh hene, She mish eh.   
43N||9||10||Shen y fa dooyrt aa rish, Kys va dty hooillyn er nyn vosley? 
43N||9||11||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Ren dooinney va enmyssit Yeesey, cray, as hug eh rish my hooillyn eh, as dooyrt eh rhym, Immee gys poyll Siloam, as oolee oo hene: as hie mee, as doonlee mee mee-hene, as hooar mee my hoilshey.   
43N||9||12||Eisht dooyrt ad rish, Cre vel eh? Dooyrt eshyn, Cha s'aym.   
43N||9||13||Hug ad lhieu gys ny Phariseeyn eshyn va roish shen doal.   
43N||9||14||As she er y doonaght va Yeesey er n'yannoo yn chray, as er vosley ny sooillyn echey.   
43N||9||15||Eisht denee ny Phariseeyn jeh reesht, kys v'eh er gheddyn e hoilshey. Dooyrt eh roo, Hug eh cray er my hooillyn, as doonlee mee, as ta mee fakin.   
43N||9||16||Shen-y-fa dooyrt paart jeh ny Phariseeyn, Cha vel y dooinney shoh veih Jee, er-yn-oyr nagh vel eh freayll yn doonaght. Dooyrt feallagh elley, Kys oddys dooinney ta ny ghrogh-yantagh lheid ny mirrilyn y yannoo? As va streeu nyn mast' oc.   
43N||9||17||Dooyrt ad rish y dooinney doal reesht, Cre t'ou uss dy ghra my-e-chione, dy doshil eh dty hooillyn? Dooyrt eh, She phadeyr eh.   
43N||9||18||Agh cha ren ny Hewnyn credjal mychione echey, dy row eh er ve doal, as dy dooar eh e hoilshey reesht, derrey deie ad er yn ayr as yn voir echeysyn v'er gheddyn e hoilshey.   
43N||9||19||As denee ad jeu, gra, Nee shoh yn mac euish, ta shiu gra va er ny ruggey doal? kys eisht t'eh nish fakin?   
43N||9||20||Dreggyr e ayr as e voir ad, gra, Ta fys ain dy nee shoh yn mac ain, as dy row eh er ny ruggey doal:   
43N||9||21||Agh kys t'eh nish fakin, cha s'ain; ny quoi t'er vosley ny sooillyn echey, cha vel fys ain: t'eh ec eash, fenee-jee jehsyn, loayree eh er e hon hene.   
43N||9||22||Ny goan shoh loayr e ayr as e voir, son dy row ad ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn: son va ny Hewnyn er choardail hannah, my ghoghe dooinney erbee rish dy nee eh va'n Creest, dy beagh eh er ny ghiarey magh ass y synagogue.   
43N||9||23||Shen-y-fa dooyrt yn ayr as y voir echey, T'eh ec eash, fenee-jee jeh hene.   
43N||9||24||Eisht deie ad reesht er y dooinney v'er ny ve doal, as dooyrt ad rish, Cur y moylley da Jee: ta fys ain dy nee drogh-ghooinney eh shoh. 
43N||9||25||Dreggyr eshyn, as dooyrt eh, Cha s'aym's dy nee drogh-ghooinney eh: un red ta fys aym er, dy row mee doal, as nish dy vel my hoilshey aym.   
43N||9||26||Eisht dooyrt ad rish reesht, Cre ren eh rhyt? kys doshil eh dty hooillyn?   
43N||9||27||Dreggyr eshyn ad, Ta mee er n'insh diu hannah, as cha dug shiu geill: cre'n-fa bailliu y chlashtyn reesht eh? vel shiuish myrgeddin son goaill-rish yn ynsagh echeysyn? 
43N||9||28||Eisht doltooan ad eh, as dooyrt ad, T'ou uss 'syn ynsaghey echeysyn: agh ta shinyn ayns ynsaghey Voses.   
43N||9||29||Ta fys ain dy loayr Jee rish Moses: agh son eh shoh, cha s'ain cre veih t'eh.   
43N||9||30||Dreggyr y dooinney as dooyrt eh roo, Ta shen red yindyssagh, nagh s'eu cre veih t'eh? as ny-yeih dy vel eh er vosley my hooillyn's.           
43N||9||31||Nish ta fys ain nagh vel Jee cur clashtyn da drogh-yantee: agh my ta dooinney erbee cur ooashley da Jee, as jannoo e aigney, dasyn t'eh cur clashtyn.   
43N||9||32||Er-dy hoshiaght y theihll cha row eh er ny chlashtyn dy doshil dooinney erbee sooillyn fer va er ny ruggey doal.   
43N||9||33||Er-be dy vel y dooinney shoh veih Jee, cha voddagh eh nhee erbee y yannoo.   
43N||9||34||Dreggyr ad as dooyrt ad rish, V'ou uss er dty ruggey ooilley cooidjagh ayns peccaghyn, as vel oo goaill ort dy ynsaghey shinyn? As ghiare ad magh eh.   
43N||9||35||Cheayll Yeesey dy row ad er yiarey magh eh; as tra v'eh er gheddyn eh, dooyrt eh rish, Vel oo credjal ayns Mac Yee?   
43N||9||36||Dreggyr eshyn as dooyrt eh, Quoi eh, Hiarn, dy voddym credjal ayn?   
43N||9||37||As dooyrt Yeesey rish, T'ou chammah er vakin eh, as she eshyn eh ta taggloo rhyt.   
43N||9||38||As dooyrt eh, Hiarn, ta mee credjal. As hug eh ooashley da. 
43N||9||39||As dooyrt Yeesey, Son briwnys haink mish gys y theihll shoh: dy vod adsyn nagh vel fakin, fakin; as adsyn ta fakin, dy vod ad v'er nyn yannoo doal.   
43N||9||40||As cheayll paart jeh ny Phariseeyn va marish ny goan shoh, as dooyrt ad rish, Vel shinyn doal neesht? 
43N||9||41||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Dy beagh shiu doal, cha beagh peccah eu: agh nish ta shiu gra, Ta shin fakin; shen-y-fa ta nyn beccah tannaghtyn erriu.
43N||10||1||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn nagh vel goll stiagh er y dorrys ayns bwoaillee ny geyrragh, agh ta drappal seose er aght ennagh elley, t'eh shen ny vaarliagh as ny roosteyr.   
43N||10||2||Agh eshyn ta goll stiagh er y dorrys, ta'n fer cheddin bochilley ny geyrragh.   
43N||10||3||Dasyn ta'n dorrysser fosley; as ta ny kirree clashtyn e choraa: as t'eh geamagh er e chirree hene lurg nyn ennym, as dy leeideil ad magh.   
43N||10||4||As tra t'eh cur magh e chirree hene, t'eh goll rhymboo, as ta ny kirree geiyrt er: son ta enney oc er e choraa.   
43N||10||5||As joarree cha n'eiyr ad er, agh roie ee ad er-chea veih: son cha vel enney oc er coraa joarree.   
43N||10||6||Yn coraa-dorraghey shoh loayr Yeesey roo: agh cha hoig ad shen ny v'eh er loayrt roo.   
43N||10||7||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Mish dorrys ny geyrragh.   
43N||10||8||Ta ooilley ny haink roym's, nyn maarlee as nyn roosteyryn: agh cha dug ny kirree geill daue.    
43N||10||9||Mish y dorrys: liorym's my ta dooinney erbee goll stiagh, bee eh er ny hauail, as hed eh stiagh as magh, as yiow eh fassaghey.    
43N||10||10||Cha vel y maarliagh cheet agh dy gheid, as dy varroo as dy stroie: haink mish dy voddagh bea y ve oc, as dy voddagh eh y ve oc ayns mooarane palchey.    
43N||10||11||Mish y bochilley mie: ta'n bochilley mie cur e vioys son ny kirree.    
43N||10||12||Agh eshyn ta failt, as cha nee yn bochilley hene, as nagh vel ny kirree lesh hene, t'eh fakin yn moddey-oaldey cheet, as t'eh faagail ny kirree, as roie er-chea: as ta'n moddey-oaldey dyn dayrtyn ad, as skeayley ny kirree.    
43N||10||13||Ta fer-ny-failley chea, er-y-fa dy nee fer-failt eh, as nagh mooar-lesh son ny kirree.    
43N||10||14||Mish y bochilley mie, as ta enney aym er my chirree, as ta enney ocsyn orrym's.    
43N||10||15||Myr ta enney ec yn Ayr orrym's, shen myr ta enney aym's er yn Ayr: as ta mee scarrey rish my vioys son ny kirree.    
43N||10||16||As kirree elley t'aym, nagh vel jeh'n woaillee shoh: ad shen neesht shegin dou y chur lhiam, as cluinnee ad my choraa; as bee un woaillee ayn, as un vochilley.    
43N||10||17||Shen-y-fa ta my Ayr graihagh orrym's, er-yn-oyr dy vel mee scarrey rish my vioys, dy voddym y ghoaill reesht eh.    
43N||10||18||Cha vel dooinney erbee dy ghoaill voym eh, agh m'aigney hene eh dy scarrey rish: Ta pooar aym dy scarrey rish, as ta pooar aym dy ghoaill reesht eh. Yn sarey shoh hooar mee veih my Ayr.    
43N||10||19||Va streeu er-y-fa shen reesht mastey ny Hewnyn son ny raaghyn shoh.    
43N||10||20||As dooyrt ymmodee jeu, Ta drogh spyrryd ayn, as t'eh ass e cheeayl; cre'n-fa ta shiu geaishtagh rish?    
43N||10||21||Dooyrt feallagh elley, Cha vel ad shoh goan fer ta drogh-spyrryd ayn: Vod drogh spyrryd sooillyn ny doail y osley?    
43N||10||22||As haghyr shoh ec Jerusalem, ec feailley casherickey yn chiamble; as nish va'n geurey. 
43N||10||23||As va Yeesey shooyl ayns y chiamble ayns porch Solomon.   
43N||10||24||Eisht haink ny Hewnyn mygeayrt-y-mysh, as dooyrt ad rish, Caid t'ou freayll shin fo mee-ourys? My she yn Creest oo, insh dooin dy ynrick.   
43N||10||25||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Ta mee er n'insh diu hannah, as cha ren shiu my chredjal: ta ny obbraghyn ta mee dy yannoo ayns ennym my Ayrey gymmyrkey fenish jee'm.   
43N||10||26||Agh cha vel shiuish credjal; er-yn-oyr nagh vel shiu jeh my hioltane, myr dooyrt mee riu.   
43N||10||27||Ta my chirree clashtyn my choraa, as ta enney aym orroo, as eiyree ad orrym. 
43N||10||28||As ta mee cur daue yn vea veayn, as cha jean ad dy bragh cherraghtyn, as cha n'ghow fer erbee ad ass my laue er-niart.   
43N||10||29||Ta my Ayr hug dou ad, pooaral erskyn ooilley: as cha jarg fer erbee y ghoaill ad ass laue my Ayrey.   
43N||10||30||Ta mish as my Ayr unnane.   
43N||10||31||Eisht hrog ny Hewnyn claghyn reesht dy chlaghey eh.   
43N||10||32||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Shimmey yn obbyr vie ta mee er hoilshaghey diu veih my Ayr; son quoi j'eh ny obbraghyn cheddin ta shiu ry-hoi m'y chlaghey?   
43N||10||33||Dreggyr ny Hewnyn eh, gra, Son obbyr vie cha vel shin dy dty chlaghey; agh son goan-mollaghtagh, as er-yn-oyr dy vel uss, ta dty ghooinney, jannoo oo hene Jee.   
43N||10||34||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Nagh vel eh scruit ayns y leigh eu, Dooyrt mee, She Jeeghyn shiu? 
43N||10||35||My t'eh genmys adsyn Jeeghyn, dauesyn va goo Yee er ny choyrt, as nagh vod y scriptyr v'er ny rassey:   
43N||10||36||Vel shiu gra mychionesyn ta'n Ayr er chasherickey, as er choyrt gys y theihll, T'ou loayrt goan-mollaghtagh; er-yn-oyr dy dooyrt mee, She Mac Yee mee?   
43N||10||37||Mannagh vel mee jannoo obbraghyn m'Ayrey, ny cred-jee mee.   
43N||10||38||Agh my ta mee jannoo ad, ga nagh gred shiu mish, cred-jee ny obbraghyn: dy vod shiu toiggal as credjal, dy vel yn Ayr aynym's, as mish aynsyn.   
43N||10||39||Er shoh v'ad reesht son y ghoaill eh: agh chossyn eh ass nyn laueyn   
43N||10||40||As hie eh roish reesht er cheu elley dy Yordan, gys y boayl raad ren Ean hoshiaght bashtey; as duirree eh ayns shen.   
43N||10||41||As va ymmodee cheet huggey, as gra, Cha ren Ean mirril erbee: agh va dy chooilley nhee loayr Ean jeh'n dooinney shoh firrinagh.   
43N||10||42||As ren ymmodee credjal ayn ayns shen.       
43N||11||1||NISH va dooinney dy row ching, va enmyssit Lazarus dy Vethany, balley Voirrey as y chuyr eck Martha.   
43N||11||2||(She yn Voirrey cheddin v'ayn, ish ren ooillaghey yn Chiarn, as rub ny cassyn, echey lesh e folt, yn braar eck Lazarus va ching).   
43N||11||3||Shen-y-fa hug ny shayraghyn echey fys huggey, gra, Hiarn, cur-my-ner, t'eshyn shynney lhiat ching. 
43N||11||4||Tra cheayll Yeesey shoh, dooyrt eh, Cha vel y chingys shoh gys baase, agh son gloyr Yee, dy vod Mac Yee v'er ny ghloyraghey liorish.   
43N||11||5||Nish bynney lesh Yeesey Martha, as y chuyr eck, as Lazarus.   
43N||11||6||Shen-y-fa tra v'eh er chlashtyn dy row eh ching, duirree eh foast daa laa ayns yn un voayl raad v'eh.   
43N||11||7||Eisht ny lurg shen dooyrt eh rish e ostyllyn, Lhig dooin goll reesht gys Judea.
43N||11||8||Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Vainshter, cha voddey neayr as va ny Hewnyn shirrey dty chlaghey; as vel oo son goll gys shen reesht?
43N||11||9||Dreggyr Yeesey, Nagh vel daa oor yeig 'sy laa? My ta dooinney erbee shooyll ayns y laa, cha vel eh snapperal, er-y-fa dy vel eh fakin soilshey yn theihll shoh.   
43N||11||10||Agh my ta dooinney shooyll ayns yn oie, t'eh snapperal, er-y-fa nagh vel soilshey ayn.    
43N||11||11||Ny goan shoh loayr eh: as ny lurg shen dooyrt eh roo, Ta nyn garrey Lazarus ny chadley; agh ta mish goll dy ghoostey eh ass e chadley.    
43N||11||12||Eisht dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Hiarn, my t'eh cadley, nee eh coural.    
43N||11||13||Ny-yeih loayr Yeesey jeh'n vaase echey: agh heill adsyn dy row eh er loayrt jeh fea y ghoaill ayns cadley.  
43N||11||14||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo dy foshlit, Ta Lazarus marroo.    
43N||11||15||As 'smie lhiam er y choontey euish, nagh row mee ayns shen (son niartaghey nyn gredjue) ny-yeih hooin-jee huggey. 
43N||11||16||Eisht dooyrt Thomase ta enmyssit Didymus rish e heshey-ostyllyn, Lhig dooinyn goll neesht, dy vod mayd baase y gheddyn marish.    
43N||11||17||Eisht tra va Yeesey er jeet gys Bethany, hooar eh dy row eh er ve kiare laa hannah 'syn oaie.    
43N||11||18||(Nish va Bethany er-gerrey da Jerusalem, mysh daa veeilley jeh).    
43N||11||19||As va ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn er jeet magh gys Martha as Moirrey, dy gherjaghey ad son nyn mraar.    
43N||11||20||Eisht cha leah as cheayll Martha dy row Yeesey cheet, hie ee magh ny whail: agh hoie Moirrey ayns y thie.    
43N||11||21||Eisht dooyrt Martha rish Yeesey, Hiarn, dy beagh uss er ve ayns shoh, cha beagh my vraar er gheddyn baase.    
43N||11||22||Agh ta fys aym, eer foast, cre-erbee nee oo y yeearree er Jee, dy der Jee dhyt eh.    
43N||11||23||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Nee dty vraar girree reesht.    
43N||11||24||Dooyrt Martha rish, Ta fys aym dy n'irree eh reesht ec yn irree-seose 'sy laa jerrinagh.    
43N||11||25||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Mish yn irree seose-reesht veih ny merriu as yn vea: bee eshyn ta credjal aynym's bio, ga dy vow eh baase;    
43N||11||26||As quoi-erbee ta bio, as credjal aynym's, cha vow eh yn baase dy bragh farraghtyn. Vel uss credjal shoh?    
43N||11||27||Dooyrt ee rish, Ta, Hiarn: ta mee credjal dy nee uss yn Creest Mac Yee va ry-hoi cheet gys y theihll.    
43N||11||28||As tra v'ee er ghra shoh, hie ee rhym bee, as deie ee er e shuyr Moirrey er-lheh as dooyrt ee, Ta'n Mainshter er jeet, as t'eh geamagh ort. 
43N||11||29||Cha leah as cheayll ee shen, dirree ee dy tappee dy tappee, as haink ee huggey.
43N||11||30||Nish cha row Yeesey foast er jeet stiagh ayns y valley, agh v'eh ayns y voayl raad haink Martha ny whail   
43N||11||31||Ny Hewnyn eisht va maree ayns y thie dy gherjaghey ee, tra honnick ad dy dirree Moirrey dy tappee, as dy jagh ee magh, deiyr ad urree, gra, T'ee goll gys yn oaie dy cheayney ayns shen.   
43N||11||32||Eisht tra va Moirrey er jeet raad va Yeesey, as jeeaghyn er, huitt ee sheese ec e chassyn, gra rish, Hiarn, dy beagh uss er ve ayns shoh, cha beagh my vraar er gheddyn baase.   
43N||11||33||Tra honnick Yeesey ee er-y-fa shen keayney, as ny Hewnyn myrgeddin keayney v'er jeet maree, hayrn eh osney hrome, as v'eh seaghnit;   
43N||11||34||As dooyrt eh, C'raad ta shiu er choyrt eh? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Hiarn, tarr as hee oo.   
43N||11||35||Ren Yeesey keayney.   
43N||11||36||Eisht dooyrt ny Hewnyn, Cur-jee my-ner, cre'n ghraih v'echey er.   
43N||11||37||As dooyrt paart jeu, Nagh voddagh yn dooinney shoh, ren fosley sooillyn ny doail, v'er lhiettal baase y dooinney shoh?   
43N||11||38||Hayrn Yeesey er-y-fa shen osney hrome reesht veih e chree, as haink eh gys yn oaie. She ooig v'ayn, as va clagh er e beeal.   
43N||11||39||Dooyrt Yeesey, Scugh-jee yn chlagh. Dooyrt Martha shuyr y varroo rish, Hiarn, ta nish soar trome jeh: son t'eh er ve kiare laa marroo. 
43N||11||40||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Nagh dooyrt mee rhyt, my chredjagh oo, dy vaikagh oo gloyr Yee?
43N||11||41||Eisht scugh ad y chlagh jeh'n boayl raad va'n marroo ny lhie. As hrog Yeesey seose e hooillyn, as dooyrt eh, Ayr, ta mee cur booise dhyt dy vel oo er my chlashtyn. 
43N||11||42||As va fys aym dy vel oo rieau dy my chlashtyn: agh er coontey yn phobble ta mygeayrt-y-moom dooyrt mee shoh, dy vod ad credjal dy vel oo er my choyrt.   
43N||11||43||As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, deie eh lesh ard-choraa, Lazarus, tar magh.   
43N||11||44||As haink eshyn va marroo magh soillit cass as laue ayns aanrityn oanluckee: as bussal mysh e eddin. Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Feayshil-jee eh, as lhig-jee yn raad da.   
43N||11||45||Eisht ren ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn v'er jeet magh gys Moirrey, as v'er vakin ny reddyn ren Yeesey, credjal ayn.   
43N||11||46||Agh hie paart jeu rhymboo gys ny Phariseeyn, as dinsh ad daue cre ny reddyn va Yeesey er n'yannoo.   
43N||11||47||Eisht deie ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn er y choonceil cooidjagh, as dooyrt ad, Cre ta shinyn dy yannoo? son ta'n dooinney shoh jannoo ymmodee mirrilyn. 
43N||11||48||My lhiggys mayd da, nee dy chooilley ghooinney credjal ayn; as hig ny Romanee as ver ad mow chammah yn ynnyd casherick as yn ashoon ain.   
43N||11||49||As va fer jeu va enmyssit Caiaphas, ny ard-saggyrt yn vlein shen, as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel toiggal eu jeh nhee erbee,   
43N||11||50||Chamoo ta shiu goaill eu hene kys dy vel eh ymmyrchagh er ny son ain, un dooinney dy gheddyn baase son y pobble, as gyn y slane ashoon dy herraghtyn. 
43N||11||51||As shoh loayr eh, cha nee jeh hene: agh v'eh ny ard-saggyrt yn vlein shen, as ren e phadeyrys dy voghe Yeesey baase son yn ashoon shen:   
43N||11||52||As cha nee ynrycan son yn ashoon shen, agh myrgeddin dy jinnagh eh cloan Yee va skeaylt dy lhean, y hayrn gys unnaneys ry-cheilley.   
43N||11||53||Eisht veih'n laa shen magh v'ad cur nyn goyrle dy cheilley dy choyrt eh gy baase.   
43N||11||54||Cha jimmee Yeesey er-y-fa shen ny smoo dy foshlit mastey ny Hewnyn; agh hie eh veih shen gys cheer va er-gerrey da'n aasagh, gys ard-valley enmyssit Ephraim, as duirree eh ayns shen marish e ostyllyn.   
43N||11||55||As va caisht ny Hewnyn tayrn er gerrey: as va ymmodee ass y cheer goll seose gys Jerusalem roish y chaisht dy ghlenney ad hene er y hon.   
43N||11||56||As v'ad briaght son Yeesey, as loayrt nyn mast' oc hene, myr v'ad nyn shassoo ayns y chiamble, Cre ta shiu dy smooinaghtyn, nagh jig eh seose gys y feailley?   
43N||11||57||Nish va chammah ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn er chur sarey, my va fys ec dooinney erbee c'raad v'eh, dy row ad dy choyrt briaght er cour y ghoaill eh. 
43N||12||1||EISHT shey laa roish y Chaisht, haink Yeesey gys Bethany, raad va Lazarus v'er ny ve marroo, yn fer cheddin v'eh er hroggal veih ny merriu.   
43N||12||2||Ayns shen ren ad shibber er e hon, as va Martha shirveish orroo: agh va Lazarus fer jeusyn va nyn soie ec y voayrd marish.   
43N||12||3||Eisht ghow Moirrey punt dy ooil dy spikenard feer chostal, as ren ee cassyn Yeesey y ooilaghey, as rub ee e chassyn lesh e folt: as va'n thie er ny lhieeney lesh soar yn ooil.   
43N||12||4||Eisht dooyrt fer jeh ny ostyllyn echey, Yuaase Iscariot mac Simon, va ry-hoi y vrah eh.   
43N||12||5||Cre'n-fa nagh row yn ooil shoh creckit son three cheead ping, as er ny choyrt da ny boghtyn?   
43N||12||6||Shoh dooyrt eh, cha nee ayns kiarail erbee son ny boghtyn, agh dy row eh ny vaarliagh, er va currym y sporran, as eshyn va gymmyrkey ny v'ayn.   
43N||12||7||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey, Faag-jee veue ee: cour laa my oanluckey t'ee er reayll shoh.   
43N||12||8||Son ny boghtyn t'ad eu kinjagh meriu; agh mish cha vel eu kinjagh. 
43N||12||9||Va fys er-y-fa shen ec ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn dy row eh ayns shen: as haink ad, cha nee er coontey Yeesey ny-lomarcan, agh dy voddagh ad Lazarus y akin myrgeddin, eh v'eshyn er hroggal veih ny merriu.   
43N||12||10||Agh hug ny ard-saggyrtyn nyn goyrle dy cheilley, mychione Lazarus myrgeddin y choyrt gy-baase;   
43N||12||11||Son dy row ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn kyndagh rishyn er hreigeil adsyn, as er chredjal ayns Yeesey.   
43N||12||12||Laa-ny-vairagh hie shiartanse mooar dy leih, v'er jeet gys y feailley, tra cheayll ad dy row Yeesey er y raad gys Jerusalem.   
43N||12||13||As ghow ad banglaneyn dy viljyn palm, as hie ad magh ny whail, as deie ad, Hosanna; bannit ta ree Israel ta cheet ayns ennym y Chiarn. 
43N||12||14||As tra va Yeesey er gheddyn assyl aeg, varkee eh er: myr te scruit,   
43N||12||15||Ny gow aggle, inneen Sion: cur-my-ner ta dty ree cheet, markiagh er lhiy assyl.   
43N||12||16||Ny reddyn shoh cha hoig e ostyllyn ec y toshiaght: agh tra va Yeesey er ny ghloyraghey, eisht chooinee ad dy row ny reddyn shoh scruit jeh, as dy row ad er n'yannoo ny reddyn shoh rish.   
43N||12||17||Ren y pobble er-y-fa shen va marish, tra deie eh er Lazarus ass yn oaie, as tra hrog eh eh veih ny merriu feanish y ymmyrkey.   
43N||12||18||Er-yn-oyr shoh va'n pobble myrgeddin er gholl magh ny whail, son dy geayll ad dy row eh er n'yannoo yn mirril shoh.   
43N||12||19||Dooyrt ny Phariseeyn er-y-fa shen nyn mast' oc hene, Nagh vaik shiu, nagh vaardee shiu monney? cur-my-ner ta'n seihll er gholl geiyrt er.   
43N||12||20||As va shiartanse dy Ghreekyn nyn mast' oc, v'er jeet seose dy chur ooashley ec y feailley:   
43N||12||21||Haink ad shoh er-y-fa shen gys Philip, va veih Bethsaida ayns Galilee, as ghuee ad er, gra, Vainshter, veagh shin booiagh dy akin Yeesey.   
43N||12||22||Haink Philip as dinsh eh da Andreays, as reesht dinsh Andreays as Philip shoh da Yeesey.   
43N||12||23||As dreggyr Yeesey ad, gra, Ta'n oor er jeet, dy vel yn Mac dooinney dy ve er ny ghloyraghey.   
43N||12||24||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Mannagh vel y grine curnaght tuittym ayns y thalloo, as goll eig, te cummal ny un ghrine kinjagh: agh my te goll eig: te gymmyrkey magh  mooarane mess.   
43N||12||25||Eshyn shynney lesh e vioys, caillee eh eh: agh eshyn nagh vel soiaghey jeh e vioys 'sy theihll shoh, freillee eh eh gys y vea veayn.   
43N||12||26||My nee dooinney erbee mish y hirveish, lhig da geiyrt orrym; as y raad ta mish, shen y raad myrgeddin vees my harvaant: my nee dooinney erbee mish y hirveish, dasyn ver my Ayr onnor.
43N||12||27||Nish ta my annym seaghnit; as cre jir-ym? Ayr, saue mee veih'n oor shoh: agh er yn oyr shoh haink mee gys yn oor shoh.    
43N||12||28||Ayr, cur gloyr da dty ennym hene. Eisht haink coraa veih niau, gra, Ta mee hannah er ghloyraghey eh, as nee'm eh y ghloyraghey reesht.    
43N||12||29||Dooyrt y pobble er-y-fa shen va kionfenish, as cheayll yn coraa, dy nee taarnagh v'ayn- dooyrt feallagh elley, dy nee ainle ren loayrt rish.    
43N||12||30||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, as dooyrt eh, Cha daink y coraa shoh er y choontey aym's, agh er y choontey euish.    
43N||12||31||Nish ta briwnys y theihll shoh: nish vees prince y theihll shoh er ny hilgey magh.    
43N||12||32||As my veem's er my hroggal seose jeh'n thalloo, tayrn-ym dy chooilley ghooinney hym.    
43N||12||33||(Shoh loayr eh, cowraghey liorish shen cre'n monney dy vaase v'eh dy hurranse)    
43N||12||34||Dreggyr y pobble eh, Ta shin er chlashtyn ass y leigh, dy vel Creest tannaghtyn son dy bragh: as kys t'ou uss gra, dy vel y Mac dooinney dy ve troggit seose? quoi yn Mac dooinney shoh?    
43N||12||35||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Foast tammylt beg ta'n soilshey meriu: shooill-jee choud as ta'n soilshey eu, er-aggle dy jig y dorraghys erriu: son cha vel fys echeysyn ta shooyll ayns y dorraghys c'raad t'eh goll.    
43N||12||36||Choud as ta soilshey eu, cred-jee ayns y toilshey, dy vod shiu ve nyn gloan jeh'n toilshey. Ny goan shoh loayr Yeesey, as jimmee eh roish, as dollee eh eh-hene voue.  
43N||12||37||Agh ga dy ren eh whilleen mirril kiongoyrt roo, foast cha chred ad ayn:   
43N||12||38||As shen myr va goan Esaias y phadeyr cooilleenit, Hiarn, quoi ta er chredjal yn goo ain ? as quoi gys ta roih yn Chiarn er ve soilshit?   
43N||12||39||Shen-y-fa cha voddagh ad credjal, rere myr dooyrt Esaias ayns ynnyd elley.   
43N||12||40||T'eh er lhiggey lhieu dolley ny sooillyn oc, as creoghey nyn gree; nagh vaikagh ad lesh nyn sooillyn, as nagh doigagh ad lesh nyn gree, dy beagh ad er nyn jyndaa, as dy jinnin ad y lheihys.  
43N||12||41||Ny reddyn shoh loayr Esaias, tra honnick eh e ghloyr as loayr eh jeh.   
43N||12||42||Ny-yeih mastey ny eer ard-reiltee ren ymmodee credjal ayn; agh kyndagh rish ny Phariseeyn cha ghow ad rish, er-aggle, dy beagh ad er ny ghiarey-magh veih yn agglish. 
43N||12||43||Son v'ad ny s'aggindee er moylley gheiney, ny moylley Yee.   
43N||12||44||Hrog Yeesey seose e choraa as dooyrt eh, Eshyn ta credjal aynym's, cha nee aynym's t'eh credjal, agh aynsyn t'er my choyrt.   
43N||12||45||As eshyn ta dy my akin, t'eh fakin eshyn t'er my choyrt. 
43N||12||46||Ta mish er jeet my hoilshey gys y theihll, quoi-erbee nee credjal aynym's nagh jean eh tannaghtyn ayns y dorraghys   
43N||12||47||As my ta dooinney erbee ta clashtyn, as nagh vel freayll my ghoan, cha vel mish dy vriwnys eh: son cha daink mee dy vriwnys y seihll, agh dy hauail y seihll.   
43N||12||48||Eshyn ta soiaghey beg jeem's, as nagh vel goaill rish my ghoan, ta shen echey ta dy vriwnys eh: eer yn goo ta mish er loayrt, nee shen y vriwnys eh ec y laa jerrinagh.   
43N||12||49||Son cha vel mish er loayrt jee'm pene; agh yn Ayr t'er my choyrt, eshyn hug sarey dou, cre v'orrym dy ghra, as cre lhisin loayrt.   
43N||12||50||As ta fys aym dy vel yn sarey echeysyn yn vea dy bragh beayn: cre-erbee er-y-fa shen ta mee dy loayrt, she myr ta'n Ayr er ghra rhym, eer myr shen ta mee loayrt. 
43N||13||1||NISH, roish feailley ny Caisht, as fys ec Yeesey, dy row yn oor echey er jeet, tra v'eh dy gholl ass y theihll shoh gys yn Ayr, myr v'eh graihagh er e vooinjer hene, va ayns y theihll, hug eh graih daue gys y jerrey.   
43N||13||2||As myr v'ad gee nyn shibber (va'n drogh-spyrryd nish er choyrt eh ayns cree Yuaase Iscariot mac Simon, dy vrah eh)  
43N||13||3||Va fys ec Yeesey dy row yn Ayr er chur dy chooilley nhee ayns ny laueyn echey, as dy nee veih Jee haink eh, as dy nee gys Jee v'eh goll,    
43N||13||4||Dirree eh veih shibber, as hug eh jeh e gharmadyn, as ghow eh aanrit, as chryss eh eh mysh hene.    
43N||13||5||Eisht hug eh ushtey ayns saagh, as ren eh toshiaght dy niee cassyn e ostyllyn, as dy rubbey ad lesh yn aanrit va ec e chryss.    
43N||13||6||Eisht haink eh gys Simon Peddyr: as dooyrt eshyn rish, Hiarn, vel uss son niee my chassyn's?    
43N||13||7||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, Cre ta mee dy yannoo cha vel oo toiggal nish; agh bee toiggal ayd jeh ny-yei shoh.   
43N||13||8||Dooyrt Peddyr rish, My chassyn's cha niee oo dy bragh. Dreggyr Yeesey eh, mannagh nieeyms oo, cha vod ayrn erbee ve ayd marym.    
43N||13||9||Dooyrt Simon Peddyr rish, Hiarn, cha nee ynrycan eisht my chassyn, agh myrgeddin my laueyn, as my chione.    
43N||13||10||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Eshyn ta nieet, cha vel feme echey agh dy niee e chassyn, as t'eh glen ooilley harrish: as ta shiuish glen, agh cha vel shiu ooilley myr shen. 
43N||13||11||Son va fys echey quoi va ry-hoi y vrah eh: shen-y-fa dooyrt eh, Cha vel shiu ooilley glen.    
43N||13||12||Myr shen erreish da v' er niee ny cassyn oc, as tra v'eh er ghoaill e gharmadyn, as er hoie sheese reesht, dooyrt eh roo, Vel fys eu cre ta mee er n'yannoo riu?    
43N||13||13||Ta shiu genmys mish nyn Mainshter, as Chiarn: as ta shiu gra dy mie; son she shen mee.   
43N||13||14||My ta mish eisht yn Chiarn as y Mainshter eu er niee nyn gassyn, lhisagh shiuish myrgeddin yn derrey yeh eu cassyn y jeh elley y niee.   
43N||13||15||Son ta mish er chur diu sampleyr; shiuish dy yannoo myr ta mish er n'yannoo riu.   
43N||13||16||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cha vel y charvaant ny syrjey na e hiarn, ny eshyn t'er ny choyrt, ny syrjey na eshyn ren y choyrt eh.   
43N||13||17||My ta fys eu er ny reddyn shoh, s'maynrey vees shiu my nee shiu ad y yannoo.   
43N||13||18||Cha vel mee loayrt j'iu ooilley; ta fys aym quoi ta mee er reih: agh dy vod y scriptyr ve cooilleenit, T'eshyn ta gee arran marym, er hroggal e voyn m'oi.   
43N||13||19||Nish ta mee ginsh diu ro-laue, tra hig eh gy-kione, dy vod shiu credjal dy nee mish eh.   
43N||13||20||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu Eshyn ta jannoo soiagh jeh quoi-erbee ta mee dy choyrt, t'eh jannoo soiagh jeem's: as eshyn ta soiaghey jeem's, t'eh soiaghey jehsyn t'er my choyrt.   
43N||13||21||Tra va Yeesey er ghra shoh, v'eh seaghnit ayns e spyrryd, as dymmyrk eh feanish, as dooyrt eh, Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, dy jean fer jiuish mish y vrah.   
43N||13||22||Eisht yeeagh ny ostyllyn er y cheilley ayns ourys quoi er v'eh cheet.   
43N||13||23||Nish va ny lhie er oghrish Yeesey, fer jeh e ostyllyn bynney lesh.   
43N||13||24||Chrie Simon Peddyr er-y-fa shen er, eh dy enaght quoi er v'eh cheet.   
43N||13||25||Myr v'eh eisht ny lhie rish oghrish Yeesey, dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, quoi eh?   
43N||13||26||Dreggyr Yeesey, She eshyn eh da verym greme dy arran, tra vee'm er hummey eh. As tra v'eh er hummey yn greme, hug eh eh da Yuaase Iscariot mac Simon.   
43N||13||27||As lurg y greme, hie yn drogh-spyrryd stiagh ayn. Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish, Shen t'ou dy yannoo, jean eh dy tappee.   
43N||13||28||Nish cha row fys ec dooinney jeu ec y voayrd cre'n-fa loayr eh shoh rish.   
43N||13||29||Son heill paart, er-yn-oyr dy nee ec Yuaase va'n sporran, dy row Yeesey er ghra rish Kionnee ny vees mayd feme cour y feailley: ny eh dy chur jeirk da ny boghtyn.   
43N||13||30||Erreish da eisht v'er n'ghoaill y greme dy arran, hie eh chelleeragh magh: as va'n oie ayn.   
43N||13||31||Shen-y-fa erreish da v'er n'gholl magh, dooyrt Yeesey, Nish ta'n Mac dooinney er ny ghloyraghey, as ta Jee er ny ghloyraghey ayn.   
43N||13||32||My ta Jee er ny ghloyraghey ayn, nee Jee myrgeddin eshyn y ghloyraghey ayn hene, as nee eh dy gerrit eh y ghloyraghey. 
43N||13||33||Chloan veggey, foast tammylt beg ta mish meriu. Nee shiu my hirrey: as myr dooyrt mee rish ny Hewnyn, Raad ta mish goll, cha vod shiuish cheet; myr shen ta mec nish gra riuish.   
43N||13||34||Sarey noa ta mee dy choyrt diu, Shiu dy ve graihagh yn derrey yeh er y jeh elley; myr ta mish er ve graihagh erriuish dy der shiuish myrgeddin graih yn derrey yeh da'n jeh elley.   
43N||13||35||Liorish shoh vees fys ec dy chooilley ghooinney dy vel shiu gynsaghey voym's, my vees shiu graihagh yn derrey yeh er y jeh elley.   
43N||13||36||Dooyrt Simon Peddyr rish, Hiarn, c'raad t'ou goll? Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Raad ta mee goll, cha vod oo geiyrt orrym nish; agh eiyree oo orrym ny lurg shoh.   
43N||13||37||Dooyrt Peddyr rish, Hiarn, cre'n-fa nagh voddym geiyrt ort nish? scarrym rish my vioys er dty ghraih. 
43N||13||38||Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Jean oo scarrey rish dty vioys er my ghraih's? Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Nagh jean y kellagh gerrym, derrey obbys oo mish three keayrtyn. 
43N||14||1||NY lhig da'n cree eu ve seaghnit:. ta shiu credjal ayns Jee, cred-jee myrgeddin aynym's. 
43N||14||2||Ayns thie my Ayrey ta ymmodee ynnydyn-vaghee; dy beagh eh er aght elley, veign er n'insh diu: ta mee goll dy yannoo aarloo ynnyd er nyn son.    
43N||14||3||As my hem's dy yannoo aarloo ynnyd er nyn son, hig-ym reesht, as goym shiu hym pene, raad ta mish dy vod shiuish ve myrgeddin.    
43N||14||4||As ta fys eu cre'n raad ta mee goll, as shione diu yn raad.    
43N||14||5||Dooyrt Thomase rish, Hiarn, cha s'ain cre'n raad t'ou goll, as kys oddys enney y ve ain er y raad?    
43N||14||6||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Mish y raad, yn irriney, as y vea: cha vel dooinney erbee cheet gys yn Ayr, agh lioryms.    
43N||14||7||Dy beagh enney er ve eu orrym's, veagh enney eu er my Ayr myrgeddin: as nish ta enney eu er, as ta shiu er vakin eh.    
43N||14||8||Dooyrt Philip rish, Hiarn, jeeagh dooin yn Ayr, as s'lioar dooin eh.    
43N||14||9||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Vel mish er ve choud shen meriu, as nagh nione dhyt's mee foast, Philip? eshyn t'er n'akin mish, t'eh er vakin yn Ayr; as kys t'ou uss gra eisht, Jeeagh dooin yn Ayr?    
43N||14||10||Nagh vel oo credjal dy vel mish ayns yn Ayr, as yn Ayr aynym's? ny goan ta mish dy loayrt riu, cha vel mee loayrt jee'm pene: agh yn Ayr ta tannaghtyn aynym, eshyn ta jannoo ny obbraghyn.    
43N||14||11||Cred-jee mish, dy vel mee ayns yn Ayr, as yn Ayr aynym's: er-nonney cred-jee mee er graih ny eer obbraghyn.    
43N||14||12||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Eshyn ta credjal aynym's, ny obbraghyn ta mish dy yannoo nee eshyn myrgeddin, as obbraghyn smoo na ad shoh nee eh; er-y-fa dy vel mish goll roym gys my Ayr.   
43N||14||13||As cre-erbee nee shiu y hirrey ayns yn ennym aym's, shen neem's y yannoo, dy vod yn Ayr v'er ny ghloyraghey ayns y Mac.   
43N||14||14||My hirrys shiu nhee erbee ayns yn ennym aym's, nee'm eh y yannoo.   
43N||14||15||My ta shiu graihagh orrym's, freill jee my annaghyn. 
43N||14||16||As guee-yms gys yn Ayr, as ver eh hiu Fer-gerjagh elley dy hannaghtyn meriu son dy bragh.   
43N||14||17||Eer Spyrryd ny firriney, nagh vod y seihll goaill-rish, er-y-fa nagh vel ad dy akin eh, as nagh nione daue eh: agh shione diuish eh, son t'eh tannaghtyn meriu, as bee eh ayndiu.   
43N||14||18||Cha vaag-ym shiu gyn gerjagh; higyms hiu.   
43N||14||19||Foast tammylt beg, as cha vel y seihll dy my akin ny smoo; agh ta shiuish dy my akin: er-yn-oyr dy vel mish bio, bee shiuish bio myrgeddin.   
43N||14||20||Ayns y laa shen vees fys eu dy vel mish ayns my Ayr, as shiuish aynym's, as mish ayndiuish. 
43N||14||21||Eshyn ta my annaghyn's echey, as ta freayll ad, eshyn eh ta graihagh orrym's: as eshyn ta graihagh orrym, ver my Ayr graih da, as ver-yms graih da, as soilshee-ym mee hene da.   
43N||14||22||Dooyrt Yuaase rish, cha nee Iscariot, Hiarn, kys te dy jean oo oo-hene y hoilshaghey dooinyn, as cha nee da'n seihll?   
43N||14||23||Dreggyr Yeesey as dooyrt eh rish, My ta dooinney graihagh orrym, freillee eh my ghoan: as ver my Ayr graih da, as hig mayd huggey, as nee mayd tannaghtyn marish.   
43N||14||24||Eshyn nagh vel graihagh orrym's, cha vel eh freayll my ghoan: as y goo ta shiu dy chlashtyn, cha nee lhiam's eh, agh goo yn Ayr t'er my choyrt.   
43N||14||25||Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, choud's ta mee foast meriu.   
43N||14||26||Agh nee Fer-ny-gherjagh, ta shen, yn Spyrryd Noo, eh nee yn Ayr y choyrt ayns yn ennym aym's, gynsaghey diu dy chooilley nhee, as tayrnee eh dy chooilley nhee gys nyn gooinaghtyn, cre-erbee ta mish er ghra riu.   
43N||14||27||Shee ta mee dy aagail meriu, my hee ta mee dy choyrt diu: cha nee myr ta'n seihll coyrt, ta mish dy choyrt eh diu. Ny lhig da'n cree eu ve seaghnit, chamoo lhig da aggle y ve er.   
43N||14||28||Ta shiu er chlashtyn kys dooyrt mee riu, Ta mee goll roym, as cheet reesht hiu. Dy beagh shiu graihagh orrym, ghoghe shiu boggey, er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee, Ta mee goll roym gys my Ayr: son ta my Ayr ny syrjey na mish.   
43N||14||29||As nish ta mee er n'insh diu ro-laue, tra hig eh gy-kione, dy vod shiu credjal 
43N||14||30||Veih shoh magh cha loayr-ym cooidvooar riu: son ta prince y theihll shoh cheet, as cha vel nhee erbee echey aynym's.   
43N||14||31||Agh dy vod fys y ve ec y theihll dy vel mish graihagh er yn Ayr; as myr hug yn Ayr sarey dou, myr shen ta mee jannoo. Trog-jee erriu, lhig dooin goll roin. 
43N||15||1||NISH y billey-feeyney firrinagh, as my Ayr yn eirinnagh.   
43N||15||2||Dy chooilley vanglane aynym's nagh vel gymmyrkey mess, t'eh dy ghoaill ersooyl: as dy chooilley vanglane ta gymmyrkey mess, t'eh dy phollal, dy vod eh ve ny s'messoil. 
43N||15||3||Nish ta shiuish glen trooid y goo ta mish er loayrt riu.   
43N||15||4||Jean-jee tannaghtyn aynym's, as mish ayndiuish. Myr nagh vod y banglane mess y ymmyrkey jeh hene, mannagh vel eh tannaghtyn ayns y villey-feeyney: chamoo oddys shiuish, mannagh jean shiu tannaghtyn aynym's.   
43N||15||5||Mish y billey-feeyney, shiuish ny banglaneyn: eshyn ta tannaghtyn aynym's, as mish aynsyn, t'eh shoh cur magh mooarane mess: son scarrit voym's cha vod shiu jannoo monney dy vie. 
43N||15||6||Mannagh vel dooinney tannaghtyn aynym's t'eh tilgit magh myr banglane, as t'eh fioghey; as t'ad dyn deiy as dyn dilgey ad ayns yn aile, as t'ad er nyn lostey.   
43N||15||7||My nee shiu tannaghtyn aynym's, as my ghoan's tannaghtyn ayndiuish, shirree shiu cre sailliu, as bee eh jeant er nyn son.   
43N||15||8||Liorish shoh ta my Ayr er ny ghloyraghey, shiu dy chur magh lane mess, as shoh myr vees shiu ny ynseydee aym's.   
43N||15||9||Myr ta'n Ayr graihagh orrym's, myr shen ta mish er ve graihagh erriuish: jean-jee tannaghtyn ayns y ghraih aym's.   
43N||15||10||My nee shiu my annaghyn y reayll, nee shiu tannaghtyn ayns my ghraih: eer myr ta mish er vreayll annaghyn my Ayrey, as tannaghtyn ayns y ghraih echeysyn.   
43N||15||11||Ny goan shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, dy vod y boggey aym's ve er-mayrn ayndiu, as dy vod y boggey euish v'er ny yannoo magh.   
43N||15||12||Shoh my harey, Shiu dy chur graih yn derrey yeh da'n jeh elley, myr ta mish er ve graihagh erriuish.   
43N||15||13||Graih smoo na shoh cha vel ec dooinney erbee, na dooinney dy scarrey rish e vioys son e chaarjyn.   
43N||15||14||She my chaarjyn shiuish, my nee shiu ny ta mish dy harey diu.   
43N||15||15||Veih shoh magh cha vel mee dy enmys shiu sharvaantyn; son cha vel fys ec y charvaant, cre ta e hiarn dy yannoo: agh ta mee er n'enmys shiu caarjyn; son dy chooilley nhee ta mee er chlashtyn veih my Ayr, ta mee er hoilshaghey diuish.   
43N||15||16||Cha vel shiuish er my reih, agh ta mish er reih shiuish, as er chur shiu ayns pooar, dy vod shiu goll magh as mess y ymmyrkey, as dy vod y mess eu ve beayn: cre erbee nee shiu y hirrey er yn Ayr ayns yn ennym aym's, dy vod eh y chur diu eh.   
43N||15||17||Ny reddyn shoh ta mish dy harey diu, dy vod shiu ve graihagh yn derrey yeh er y jeh elley.   
43N||15||18||My ta dwoaie ec y seihll erriu, ta fys eu dy dug eh dwoaie dooys hoshiaght.   
43N||15||19||Dy beagh shiuish jeh'n theihll, veagh y seihll graihagh er e vooinjer hene: agh son nagh vel shiu jeh'n theihll, agh dy vel mish er reih shiu ass y theihll, shen-y-fa ta dwoaie ec y theihll erriu.   
43N||15||20||Cooinee-jee er y raa loayr mish riu, Cha vel y charvaant ny syrjey na e hiarn. My t'ad er n'yannoo tranlaase orrym's, nee ad myrgeddin tranlaase erriuish: my t'ad er vreayll my ghoan's, freillee ad ny goan euish myrgeddin.   
43N||15||21||Agh dy chooilley nhee jeu shoh nee ad riu kyndagh rish yn ennym aym's, er-y-fa nagh vel enney oc ersyn t'er my choyrt.   
43N||15||22||Mannagh beign's er jeet as er loayrt roo, cha beagh peccah er ve oc: agh nish cha vel leshtal oc son nyn beccah.   
43N||15||23||Eshyn ta dwoaie echey orrym's, ta dwoaie echey er my Ayr myrgeddin.   
43N||15||24||Mannagh beign's er n'yannoo nyn mast' oc lheid ny obbraghyn as nagh ren rieau dooinney erbee elley, cha beagh peccah er ve oc: agh nish t'ad er vakin, as er chur dwoaie chammah dooys as da my Ayr.   
43N||15||25||Agh ta shoh, dy vod y raa ve cooilleenit ta scruit ayns y leigh oc, Hug ad dwoaie dou gyn oyr.   
43N||15||26||Agh tra vees Fer-ny-gherjagh er jeet, eh ver-yms hiu veih yn Ayr, ta shen, Spyrryd ny firriney, ta cheet magh veih yn Ayr, nee eh feanish y ymmyrkey jeem's.   
43N||15||27||As nee shiuish myrgeddin feanish y ymmyrkey, er-y-fa dy vel shiu er ve marym er-dyn toshiaght. 
43N||16||1||NY goan shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, son nagh bee nyn gredjue er ny lhaggaghey.   
43N||16||2||Ver ad shiu magh ass ny kialteenyn: as ta'n oor cheet, quoi-erbee varrys shiu, dy smooinee eh dy bee eh shirveish Jee.   
43N||16||3||As ny reddyn shoh nee ad riu, er-yn-oyr nagh vel enney oc er yn Ayr, ny orrym's.   
43N||16||4||Agh ny reddyn shoh ta mish er n'insh diu, tra hig yn earish, dy vod shiu cooinaghtyn dy dinsh mee diu jeu. As ny goan shoh cha loayr mee riu ec y toshiaght, er-y-fa dy row mee meriu.   
43N||16||5||Agh nish ta mee goll roym huggeysyn t'er my choyrt, as cha vel fer j'iu fenaght jee'm c'raad t'ou goll?   
43N||16||6||Agh er-yn-oyr dy vel mee er ghra ny reddyn shoh riu, ta trimshey er lhieeney ny creeaghyn eu.  
43N||16||7||Ny-yeih ta mish ginsh diu yn irriney; Te ymmyrchagh er nyn son mish dy gholl roym: son mannagh jem roym, cha jig Fer ny-gherjagh hiu; agh my hem's roym, verym hiu eh. 
43N||16||8||As tra vees eh er jeet, nee eh yn seihll y gheyrey mychione peccah, as cairys, as briwnys:   
43N||16||9||Mychione peccah, son nagh vel ad credjal aynym's;   
43N||16||10||Mychione cairys, son dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr, as nagh vaik shiu mee arragh; 
43N||16||11||Mychione briwnys, son dy vel prince y theihll shoh er ny vriwnys.   
43N||16||12||Shimmey red ta aym's foast dy ghra riu, agh cha vod shiu ad y ymmyrkey nish.   
43N||16||13||Agh tra hig eshyn, Spyrryd ny firriney, leeidee eh shiu gys dy chooilley irrinys: son cha loayr eh jeh hene, agh cre-erbee nee eh y chlashtyn, shen loayrys eh; as soilshee eh diu reddyn ta ry-heet.   
43N||16||14||Nee eh mish y ghloyraghey: son yiow eh jeh ny ta lhiam's as soilshee eh diuish eh.   
43N||16||15||Ta dy chooilley nhee t'ec yn Ayr lhiam's: shen-y-fa dooyrt mee, dy gow eh jeh ny ta lhiam's, as dy soilshee eh diuish eh.   
43N||16||16||Tammylt beg as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg, as hee shiu mee, er-y-fa dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr.   
43N||16||17||Eisht dooyrt paart jeh e ostyllyn eddyr ad-hene, Cre shoh t'eh dy ghra rooin, Tammylt beg as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg, as hee shiu mee: as, Er-yn-oyr dy vel mee goll roym gys yn Ayr?   
43N||16||18||Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen, Cre shoh t'eh dy ghra, Tammylt beg? cha s'ain cre t'eh dy ghra.   
43N||16||19||Nish va fys ec Yeesey dy row ad aignagh dy enaght jeh, as dooyrt eh roo, Vel shiu briaght nyn mast' eu hene, er-y-fa dy dooyrt mee, Tammylt beg, as cha vaik shiu mee: as reesht, tammylt beg as hee shiu mee?   
43N||16||20||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Dy jean shiuish keayney as dobberan, agh nee yn seihll boggey y ghoaill: as bee shiuish trimshagh, agh bee yn trimshey eu er ny hyndaa gys boggey.   
43N||16||21||Ta ben, tra t'ee er-troailt, as trimshey eck, er-yn-oyr dy vel yn oor eck er jeet: agh cha leah as t'ee er ny livrey jeh'n lhiannoo, cha vel ee ny sodjey cooinaghtyn er yn angaish, son boggey dy vel dooinney er ny ruggey gys y theihll.   
43N||16||22||As ta nish er-y-fa shen trimshey euish: agh hee-yms shiu reesht, as gowee yn cree eu boggey, as y boggey eu cha gow dooinney erbee veue.   
43N||16||23||As ayns y laa shen cha jean shiu nhee erbee y enaght jeem's: Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra riu, Cre-erbee hirrys shiu er yn Ayr ayns yn ennym aym's, ver eh diu eh.   
43N||16||24||Cha vel shiu foast er hirrey nhee erbee ayns yn ennym aym's shir-jee as yiow shiu, dy vod y boggey eu v'er ny yannoo magh.   
43N||16||25||Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey: agh ta'n traa cheet tra nagh loayrym riu ny smoo ayns coraaghyn-dorraghey, agh soilshee-ym diu dy foshlit jeh'n Ayr.   
43N||16||26||Ayns y laa shen nee shiu geearree ayns y ennym aym's: as cha vel mee gra riu, dy guee-ym gys yn Ayr er nyn son:   
43N||16||27||Son ta'n Ayr hene graihagh erriu, er-y-fa dy vel shiuish er ve graihagh orrym's, as dy chred shiu dy daink mee magh veih Jee. 
43N||16||28||Haink mee magh veih'n Ayr, as ta mee er jeet gys y theihll: reesht, ta mee faagail y seihll, as goll roym gys yn Ayr.   
43N||16||29||Dooyrt e ostyllyn rish, Cur-my-ner, nish t'ou loayrt dy foshlit, as cha vel oo loayrt coraa-dorraghey erbee.   
43N||16||30||Nish ta shin shickyr dy vel fys ayd er dy chooilley nhee, as nagh vel feme ayd dooinney erbee dy enaght jeed: liorish shoh ta shin credjal dy daink oo magh veih Jee.   
43N||16||31||Dreggyr Yeesey ad, Vel shiu nish credjal?   
43N||16||32||Cur-my-ner ta'n oor cheet, as eer nish er jeet, dy bee shiu er nyn skeayley dy chooilley ghooinney gys e ynnyd hene, as dy vaag shiu mish my lomarcan: as foast cha vel mee my lomarcan, er-y-fa dy vel yn Ayr marym.   
43N||16||33||Ny reddyn shoh ta mee er loayrt riu, aynym's dy vod shee y ve eu. Ayns y theihll vees seaghyn eu: agh bee-jee dy yien mie, ta mish er gheddyn barriaght er y theihll. 
43N||17||1||NY goan shoh loayr Yeesey; as hrog eh seose e hooillyn gys niau, as dooyrt eh, Ayr, ta'n oor er jeet; jean dty Vac y ghloyraghey, dy vod dty Vac myrgeddin uss y ghloyraghey. 
43N||17||2||Myr t'ou er chur da pooar harrish ooilley sheelnaue, dy vod eh yn vea veayn y choyrt da whilleen as t'ou er chur da.   
43N||17||3||As shoh yn vea veayn, tushtey y ve oc jeed's yn ynrycan Jee firrinagh, as jeh Yeesey Creest t'ou uss er choyrt.   
43N||17||4||Ta mee er ghloyraghey oo er y thalloo: ta mee er chooilleeney yn obbyr hug oo dou dy yannoo.   
43N||17||5||As nish, O Ayr, jean mish y ghloyraghey mayrt hene, lesh y ghloyr v'aym mayrt roish my row seihll ayn.   
43N||17||6||Ta mee er hoilshaghey dty ennym gys ny deiney hug oo dou ass y theihll: lhiat's ad, as hug oo ad dooys; as t'ad er vreayll dty ghoo.   
43N||17||7||Nish t'ad er hoiggal dy nee void's ta dy chooilley nhee t'ou er choyrt dou. 
43N||17||8||Son hug mish dauesyn ny goan hug uss dooys; as t'ad er ghoaill huc hene ad, as er hoiggal ayns shickyrys dy daink mee magh voids, as t'ad er chredjal dy ren oo my choyrt. 
43N||17||9||Ta mee guee ort er nyn son: cha vel mee guee son theihll, agh er ny son ocsyn t'ou er choyrt dou, son she lhiat hene ad.   
43N||17||10||As ta ooilley ny ta lhiam's lhiat's, as ny ta lhiat's lhiam's, as ta mee er my ghloyraghey ayndoo.   
43N||17||11||As nish cha vel mish dy ve ny sodjey ayns y theihll, agh t'ad shoh ayns y theihll, as ta mish cheet hood's. Ayr chasherick, freill trooid dty ennym hene adsyn t'ou er chur dou, dy vod adsyn ve unnane, myr ta shinyn unnane.   
43N||17||12||Choud as va mee maroo ayns y theihll, dreill mee ad ayns dty ennym's: adsyn hug oo dou dreill mee, as cha vel unnane oc caillit, mannagh vel mac y toyrt-mow: dy voddagh yn scriptyr ve cooilleenit.   
43N||17||13||As nish ta mee cheet hood's, as ny reddyn shoh ta mee dy loayrt ayns y theihll, dy vod y boggey aym's y ve oc jeant magh ayndoo hene.   
43N||17||14||Ta mee er chur daue dty ghoo; as ta'n seihll er chur dwoaie daue, er-y-fa nagh vel ad jeh'n theihll, myr nagh vel mish jeh'n theihll.   
43N||17||15||Cha vel mee guee ort dy ghoaill ad ass y theihll, agh oo dy reayll ad veih'n olk.   
43N||17||16||Cha vel adsyn jeh'n theihll, myr nagh vel mish jeh'n theihll.   
43N||17||17||Jean ad y chasherickey son dty irriney: dty ghoo she firrinys eh.   
43N||17||18||Myr t'ou uss er my choyrt gys y theihll, myr shen ta mish myrgeddin er chur adsyn gys y theihll.   
43N||17||19||As er y ghraih ocsyn ta mish dy chasherickey mee hene, dy vod adsyn myrgeddin v'er nyn gasherickey gys yn irriney.   
43N||17||20||Chamoo ta mee guee er ny son oc shoh nyn lomarcan, agh myrgeddin er ny son ocsyn nee credjal aynym's trooid y goo oc.   
43N||17||21||Dy vod ad ooilley ve unnane, myr t'ou uss ayr aynym's, as mish aynyd's; dy vod adsyn myrgeddin ve unnane ayninyn: dy vod y seihll credjal dy ren oo my choyrt.   
43N||17||22||As y ghloyr hug uss dooys, ta mish er chur dauesyn: dy vod ad ve unnane, eer myr ta shinyn unnane.   
43N||17||23||Mish ayndoosyn, as uss aynym's, dy vod ad ve jeant slane firrinagh ayns unnaneys, as dy vod fys ve ec y seihll dy vel oo er my choyrt, as dy vel oo er ve graihagh orroosyn, myr t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's   
43N||17||24||Ayr, ta mee geearree adsyn t'ou er chur dou dy ve marym raad ta mee; dy vod ad fakin my ghloyr t'ou er chur dou: son t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's roish my row yn seihll er ny chroo. 
43N||17||25||Ayr chairagh, cha ghow yn seihll tushtey jeed; agh ta tushtey er ve aym's jeed, as t'ad shoh er hoiggal dy vel oo er my choyrt.   
43N||17||26||As ta mee er hoilshaghey daue dt'ennym's, as nee'm y hoilshaghey eh: dy vod y graih, liorish t'ou er ve graihagh orrym's, ve ayndoo, as mish ayndoosyn.
43N||18||1||TRA va Yeesey er loayrt ny goan shoh, hie eh magh marish e ostyllyn harrish y strooan Cedron, raad va garey, as hie eshyn as e ostyllyn stiagh ayn.   
43N||18||2||As bione da Yuaase neesht va dy vrah eh, yn ynnyd: son boallagh Yeesey dy mennick taaghey yn voayl shen marish e ostyllyn.   
43N||18||3||Hooar Yuaase eisht sheshaght dy gheiney, as sidooryn veih ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny Phariseeyn, as haink eh ayns shen lesh lonteyryn, as torchyn, as armyn.   
43N||18||4||Va fys ec Yeesey er-y-fa shen er dy chooilley nhee harragh er, as hie eh magh, as dooyrt eh roo, Quoi ta shiu dy hirrey?   
43N||18||5||Dreggyr ad eh, Yeesey dy Nazareth. Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Mish eh. As va Yuaase myrgeddin ren y vrah eh ny hassoo maroo. 
43N||18||6||Cha leah eisht as v'eh er ghra roo, Mish eh, hie ad gour nyn drommey, as huitt ad gys y thalloo.   
43N||18||7||Eisht denee eh jeu reesht, Quoi ta shiu dy hirrey? As dooyrt adsyn, Yeesey dy Nazareth.   
43N||18||8||Dreggyr Yeesey, Ta mee er n'insh diu dy nee mish eh. My ta shiu er-y-fa shen dy my hirrey, lhig-jee daue shoh goll roue:   
43N||18||9||Shoh myr va'n raa shen loayr eh cooilleenit, Jeusyn hug oo dou, cha vel mee er choayll unnane.   
43N||18||10||Eisht va cliwe ec Simon Peddyr, as hayrn eh eh, as woaill eh fer-mooinjerey yn ard-saggyrt, as ghiare eh yn chleaysh jeh. Va ennym yn er-mooinjerey shen Malchus. 
43N||18||11||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey rish Peddyr, Cur seose dty chliwe ayns y fine: yn cappan ta my Ayr er chur dou, nagh niu-ym eh?   
43N||18||12||Eisht ghow yn cheshaght, as y captan, as fir-oik ny Hewnyn Yeesey, as chiangle ad eh.   
43N||18||13||As hug ad lhieu ersooyl eh gys Annas hoshiaght (son v'eh shen ny ayr-'sy-leigh da Caiaphas, va ny ard-saggyrt yn vlein shen).   
43N||18||14||Nish she Caiaphas v'er choyrlaghey ny Hewnyn, dy row eh ymmyrchagh un dooinney dy ve er  ny choyrt gy-baase son y pobble.   
43N||18||15||As deiyr Simon Peddyr as ostyl elley er Yeesey. Yn ostyl shen va ainjys ec yn ard-saggyrt er, as hie eh stiagh marish Yeesey gys thie yn ard-saggyrt,   
43N||18||16||Agh hass Peddyr ec y dorrys er cheu mooie. Eisht hie magh yn ostyl elley shen va ainjys ec yn ard-saggyrt er, as loayr eh reeish va currym y dorrys urree, as hug eh lesh stiagh  Peddyr.  
43N||18||17||Eisht dooyrt y ven-aeg va currym y dorrys urree rish Peddyr, Nagh nee fer jeh eiyrtyssee yn dooinney shoh uss neesht? Dooyrt eshyn, Cha nee.   
43N||18||18||As va ny sharvaantyn as ny fir-oik nyn shassoo ayns shen, ec aile geayil v'ad er n'yannoo (son ve feayr) as v'ad dyn jiow ad-hene. 
43N||18||19||Denee yn ard-saggyrt eisht jeh Yeesey mychione e eiyrtyssee, as mychione yn ynsagh echey.   
43N||18||20||Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Loayr mee dy foshlit rish y theihll: dynsee mee kinjagh ayns y cheeill, as ayns y chiamble, raad ta ny Hewnyn kinjagh taaghey, as dy follit cha vel mee er ghra nhee erbee   
43N||18||21||Cre'n-fa t'ou fenaght jeem's? fenee jeusyn t'er my chlashtyn, cre ta mee er ghra roo: cur-my-ner ta fys ocsyn cre ta mee er ghra.   
43N||18||22||As tra v'eh erreish ny goan shoh y loayrt woaill fer jeh ny fir-oik va ny hassoo ayns shen Yeesey lesh bass e laue, gra, Nee shen myr t'ou freggyrt yn ard-saggyrt? 
43N||18||23||Dansoor Yeesey eh, My ta mee er loayrt dy olk, ymmyrk feanish jeh'n olk: agh my loayr mee dy mie, cre'n-fa woaill uss mee?   
43N||18||24||(Nish va Annas er choyrt eh kianlt gys Caiaphas yn ard-saggyrt)   
43N||18||25||As va Simon Peddyr ny hassoo as dy hiow eh-hene: dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen rish, Nagh nee fer jeh e eiyrtyssee uss neesht? Dob eh, as dooyrt eh, Cha nee.   
43N||18||26||Dooyrt fer jeh sharvaantyn yn ard saggyrt (va mooinjerys dasyn va Peddyr er ghiarey yn chleaysh jeh) Nagh vaik mish oo marish ayns y gharey?   
43N||18||27||Eisht dob Peddyr reesht, as chelleeragh gherr y kellagh.   
43N||18||28||Eisht hug ad lhieu Yeesey veih Caiaphas gys halley ny briwnys: as ve moghey, as cha jagh ad-hene stiagh ayns halley ny briwnys, er-aggle dy beagh ad anchasherick; as nagh voddagh ad yn Eayncaisht y ee.   
43N||18||29||Hie Pilate eisht magh huc, as dooyrt eh, Cre ta shiu dy chur gys lieh yn dooinney shoh?
43N||18||30||Dreggyr adsyn as dooyrt ad, Er-be dy nee drogh-yantagh eh, cha beagh shin er livrey hood's eh.   
43N||18||31||Eisht dooyrt Pilate roo Gow-jee shiuish eh, as jean-jee eh y vriwnys cordail rish y leigh eu hene. Dooyrt ny Hewnyn er-y-fa shen rish, Cha vel eh lowal dooinyn dooinney erbee y chur gy-baase:   
43N||18||32||Shoh myr va cooilleenit yn raa loayr Yeesey, cowraghey cre'n baase v'eh dy hurranse.   
43N||18||33||Eisht hie Pilate stiagh reesht ayns halley ny briwnys, as deie eh er Yeesey, as dooyrt eh rish, Nee ree ny Hewnyn oo? 
43N||18||34||Dreggyr Yeesey eh, Vel uss dy ghra shoh jeed hene, ny nee feallagh elley dinsh dhyt eh my-mychione's?   
43N||18||35||Dreggyr Pilate, Vel mish my Hew? she dty ashoon hene as ny ard-saggyrtyn t'er livrey oo seose hym's: Cre t'ou er n'yannoo?   
43N||18||36||Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha vel my reeriaght's jeh'n theihll shoh: dy beagh my reeriaght jeh'n theihll shoh; eisht veagh my harvaantyn er chaggey, nagh beign er my livrey gys ny Hewnyn, agh nish cha nee veih shoh ta my reeriaght.   
43N||18||37||Dooyrt Pilate er-y-fa shen rish, Vel oo dty ree eisht? Dreggyr Yeesey, T'ou uss er ghra eh, ta mee my ree. Er son shoh ruggyr mee, as er-yn-oyr shoh haink mee gys y theihll, dy ymmyrkey feanish gys yn irriney, Ta dy chooilley unnane ta jeh'n irriney clashtyn my choraa. 
43N||18||38||Dooyrt Pilate rish, Cre ta'n irriney shen? as tra v'eh er ghra shoh, hie eh magh reesht gys ny Hewnyn, as dooyrt eh roo, Cha vel mish er gheddyn foill erbee ayn.   
43N||18||39||Agh ta cliaghtey eu mee dy eaysley diu fer ec y Chaisht: nailliu er-y-fa shen mee dy eaysley diu ree ny Hewnyn?   
43N||18||40||Eisht deie ad ooilley reesht, gra, Cha nee eh shoh, agh Barabbas. Nish va Barabbas ny roosteyr.
43N||19||1||EISHT ghow Pilate er-y-fa shen Yeesey, as doardee eh eh dy ve scuitchit.   
43N||19||2||As fee ny sidooryn attey dy ghrineyn, as hug ad eh er e chione, as hug ad er coamrey purple. 
43N||19||3||As dooyrt ad, Dy vannee dhyt's, Ree ny Hewnyn: as woaill ad eh lesh nyn laueyn. 
43N||19||4||Haink Pilate er-y-fa shen magh reesht, as dooyrt eh roo, Cur-my-ner, ta mish dy choyrt lhiam magh hiu eh, dy vod fys y ve eu nagh vel mish er gheddyn foill erbee ayn.   
43N||19||5||Eisht haink Yeesey magh, ceau yn attey dy ghrineyn as y coamrey purple. As dooyrt Pilate roo, Cur-jee my-ner yn dooinney.   
43N||19||6||Shen-y-fa tra honnick ny ard-saggyrtyn as ny fir-oik eh, deie ad, gra, Jean y chrossey eh, jean y chrossey eh. Dooyrt Pilate roo, Gow-jee shiuish eh, as Jean-jee eh y chrossey: son cha vel mish er gheddyn foill er bee ayn.   
43N||19||7||Dreggyr ny Hewnyn eh, Ta leigh ainyn, as liorish y leigh ain lhisagh eh v'er ny choyrt gy-baase, er-y-fa dy ghow eh er dy nee Mac Yee v'eh.   
43N||19||8||Tra cheayll Pilate er-y-fa shen yn raa shoh, v'eh ny s'agglee;   
43N||19||9||As hie Pilate reesht gys halley ny briwnys, as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Cre voish t'ou? Agh cha dug Yeesey ansoor da.   
43N||19||10||Eisht dooyrt Pilate rish, Nagh loayr oo rhym's? nagh vel fys ayd dy vel pooar aym's dy dty chrossey, as pooar dy dty eaysley?   
43N||19||11||Dreggyr Yeesey, Cha voddagh pooar erbee y ve ayd harrym's, mannagh beagh eh er ny  choyrt dhyt veih'n yrjid; shen-y-fa ta peccah smoo lhie ersyn ren m'y livrey hood.   
43N||19||12||As veih shen magh va Pilate shirrey dy eaysley eh: agh deie ny Hewnyn, gra, My lhiggys oo yn raad da yn dooinney shoh, cha nee carrey da Cesar oo: quoi-erbee ta jannoo eh-hene ny ree, t'eh loayrt noi Cesar. 
43N||19||13||Tra cheayll Pilate er-y-fa shen yn raa shoh, hug eh lesh Yeesey magh, as hoie eh sheese er stoyl ny briwnys, ayns ynnyd ta enmyssit yn Pavement, agh ayns Hebrew, Gabbatha.
43N||19||14||As she er laa aarlaghey ny Caisht ve, as mysh y cheyoo oor: as dooyrt eh rish ny Hewnyn, Cur-jee my-ner yn ree eu.    
43N||19||15||Agh dyllee ad, Ersooyl lesh, ersooyl lesh, jean y chrossey eh. Dooyrt Pilate roo, Jean-ym yn ree euish y chrossey? Dreggyr ny ard-saggyrtyn, Cha vel ree ainyn agh Cesar.    
43N||19||16||Er shoh ren eh eshyn y livrey huc dy ve er ny chrossey. As ghow ad Yeesey as leeid ad eh ersooyl.    
43N||19||17||As dymmyrk eh e chrosh, as hie eh magh gys ynnyd yiarragh ad ynnyd y vollag rish, ta enmyssit ayns Hebrew, Golgotha.    
43N||19||18||Raad ren ad eshyn y chrossey, as jees elley marish, fer er dagh cheu, as Yeesey ayns y vean.    
43N||19||19||As ren Pilate screeuyn, as hug eh er y chrosh eh. As va'n screeu, YEESEY DY NAZARETH REE NY HEWNYN.    
43N||19||20||Yn screeu shoh eisht ren ymmodee jeh ny Hewnyn y lhaih, son va'n boayl raad v'eh er ny chrossey er-gerrey da'n ard valley: as ve scruit ayns Hebrew, as Greek, as Latin.    
43N||19||21||Eisht dooyrt ard-saggyrtyn ny Hewnyn rish Pilate, Ny scrieu, Ree ny Hewnyn; agh dy dooyrt eh, She ree ny Hewnyn mee.    
43N||19||22||Dreggyr Pilate, Ny ta scruit aym, te scruit.    
43N||19||23||Eisht ghow ny sidooryn, tra v'ad er chrossey Yeesey, e gharmadyn (as ren ad kiare ayrnyn jeu, ayrn da dy chooilley hidoor) as myrgeddin e chooat: nish va'n cooat ooilley feeit, veih heose dy heese, fegooish seam.    
43N||19||24||Dooyrt ad er-y-fa shen nyn mast' oc hene, Ny lhig dooin y raipey eh, agh lhottyn y hilgey er, quoi echey vees eh: dy voddagh y scriptyr ve cooilleenit, ta gra, Reynn ad my gharmad nyn mast' oc, as er my chooat ren ad lottyn y hilgey. Shoh myr ren ny sidooryn.  
43N||19||25||Nish va nyn shassoo liorish crosh Yeesey, e voir, as shuyr e vayrey, Moirrey ben Cleopas, as Moirrey Malaine.    
43N||19||26||Tra honnick Yeesey er-y-fa shen e voir, as yn ostyl bynney lesh ny hassoo lioree, dooyrt eh rish e voir, Ven, cur-my-ner dty vac.    
43N||19||27||Eisht dooyrt eh rish yn ostyl, Cur-my-ner dty voir. As veih'n oor shen ghow yn ostyl ee gys e hie hene.    
43N||19||28||Ny lurg shoh, son dy row fys ec Yeesey dy row dy chooilley nhee nish cooilleenit, dy voddagh y scriptyr ve jeant mie, dooyrt eh, Ta mee paagh. 
43N||19||29||Nish va saagh er ny hoiaghey lane vinegar: as lhieen ad spunge leih y vinegar, as hug ad eh er hyssop, as heeyn ad eh seose gys e veeal.   
43N||19||30||Tra va Yeesey er-y-fa shen er ghoaill y vinegar, dooyrt eh, Te cooilleenit: as chroym eh e chione, as phaart eh.   
43N||19||31||Shen-y-fa son dy nee laa yn aarlaghey ve, as nagh beagh ny kirp er y chrosh er laa yn doonaght (son va'n doonaght shen ny ard-laa) ghuee ny Hewnyn er Pilate, ny lurgaghyn oc dy ve brisht, as ad dy ve goit ersooyl.   
43N||19||32||Eisht haink ny sidooryn as vrish ad lurgaghyn y chied er, as y jeh elley v'er ny chrossey marish.   
43N||19||33||Agh tra haink ad gys Yeesey, as dy vaik ad dy row eh hannah marroo, cha vrish ad ny lurgaghyn echeysyn. 
43N||19||34||Agh ren fer jeh ny sidooryn lesh shleiy yn lhiattee echey y hoylley, as chelleeragh haink magh ass fuill as ushtey.   
43N||19||35||As dymmyrk eshyn honnick eh feanish, as ta'n eanish echey firrinagh: as ta fys echey dy vel eh gra yn irriney, dy vod shiuish credjal.   
43N||19||36||Son liorish jannoo ny reddyn shoh va'n scriptyr cooilleenit, Cha bee craue jeh er ny vrishey.   
43N||19||37||As reesht ta scriptyr elley gra, Jeeaghee ad ersyn t'ad er hoylley. 
43N||19||38||As ny lurg shoh ren Joseph dy Arimathea (va fer jeh ynseydee Yeesey, agh dy follit, ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn) guee er-Pilate, eh dy lhiggey da corp Yeesey y ghoaill ersooyl; as hug Pilate kied da: Haink eh er-y-fa shen, as hug eh lesh corp Yeesey. 
43N||19||39||As haink myrgeddin Nicodemus (va roie er jeet gys Yeesey ayns yn oie) as hug eh lesh mysh keead punt dy vyrrh as dy aloes kione y cheilley.   
43N||19||40||Eisht ghow ad corp Yeesey, as hoill ad eh ayns aanrityn, lesh spiceyn, myr va cliaghtey ny Hewnyn dy oanluckey.   
43N||19||41||Nish er-gerrey da'n ynnyd raad v'eh er ny chrossey, va garey; as ayns y gharey oaie noa, ayn nagh jagh rieau dooinney er coyrt.   
43N||19||42||Ayns shen ren ad Yeesey er-y-fa shen y oanluckey, son dy nee laa aarlaghey ny Hewnyn ve, as dy row yn oaie er-gerrey daue.
43N||20||1||ER y chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, haink Moirrey Malaine dy moghey, tra ve foast dorraghey, gys yn oaie, as honnick ee yn chlagh goit ersooyl jeh'n oaie.   
43N||20||2||Eisht roie ee, as haink ee gys Simon Peddyr, as gys yn ostyl elley bynney lesh Yeesey, as dooyrt ee roo, T'ad er ghoaill ersooyl y Chiarn ass yn oaie, as cha s'ain c'raad t'ad er choyrt eh.   
43N||20||3||Hie Peddyr er-y-fa shen magh, as yn ostyl elley shen, as haink ad gys yn oaie. 
43N||20||4||Son v'ad ny-neesht er roie cooidjagh: agh va'n ostyl elley er roie ny s'bieau na Peddyr, as er jeet hoshiaght gys yn oaie.    
43N||20||5||As chroym eh sheese, as honnick eh ny aanrityn nyn lhie, ny-yeih cha jagh eh stiagh.    
43N||20||6||Eisht haink Simon Peddyr geiyrt er, as hie eh stiagh 'syn oaie, as honnick eh ny aanrityn nyn lhie.    
43N||20||7||As y naptin va mysh e chione, cha nee ny lhie marish ny aanrityn elley, agh fillit er-y-cheilley ayns ynnyd er-lheh.    
43N||20||8||Eisht hie stiagh myrgeddin yn ostyl elley shen haink hoshiaght gys yn oaie, as honnick eh as ren eh credjal.    
43N||20||9||Son cha row foast toiggal oc jeh'n scriptyr, dy beign da girree veih ny merriu.    
43N||20||10||Eisht hie ny ostyllyn rhymboo reesht gys nyn dhie hene.    
43N||20||11||Agh va Moirrey ny shassoo cheu mooie jeh'n oaie keayney: as myr v'ee keayney, chroym ee sheese as yeeagh ee stiagh ayns yn oaie.    
43N||20||12||As honnick ee daa ainle nyn soie ayns coamraghyn sollys, yn derrey yeh ec y chione, as y jeh elley ec ny cassyn raad va corp Yeesey ny lhie.    
43N||20||13||As dooyrt ad r'ee, Ven, cre'n-fa t'ou keayney? Dooyrt ish roo, Er-yn-oyr dy vel ad er ghoaill ersooyl my Hiarn, as nagh s'aym c'raad t'ad er choyrt eh.    
43N||20||14||As tra v'ee er ghra shoh, hyndaa ee mygeayrt, as honnick ee Yeesey ny hassoo, as cha row fys eck dy nee Yeesey v'ayn.    
43N||20||15||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ven, cre'n-fa t'ou keayney? quoi t'ou dy hirrey? Heill ish dy nee yn gareyder v'ayn, as dooyrt ee rish, Vainshter, my t'ou er chur lhiat ass shoh eh, insh dou c'raad t'ou er choyrt eh, as goym ersooyl eh.    
43N||20||16||Dooyrt Yeesey,Voirrey. Hyndaa ee ee-hene, as dooyrt ee rish, Rabboni, ta shen dy ghra, Vainshter.    
43N||20||17||Dooyrt Yeesey r'ee, Ny benn rhym; son cha vel mee foast er gholl seose gys my Ayr; agh gow gys my vraaraghyn, as abbyr roo, Ta mee goll seose gys my Ayr's as yn Ayr euish, as gys my Yee's as y Jee euish.  
43N||20||18||Haink Moirrey Malaine as dinsh ee da ny ostyllyn, dy row ee er vakin y Chiarn, as dy row eh er loayrt ny goan shoh r'ee.    
43N||20||19||Eisht er y laa cheddin, yn chied laa jeh'n chiaghtin, ayns yn astyr, tra va ny dorryssyn dooint, raad va ny ostyllyn er nyn jaglym cooidjagh ayns aggle roish ny Hewnyn, haink Yeesey as hass eh kiongoyrt roo, as dooyrt eh roo, Shee dy row hiu.   
43N||20||20||As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, yeeagh eh daue e laueyn as e lhiattee. Eisht ghow ny ostyllyn boggey tra honnick ad y Chiarn.   
43N||20||21||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo reesht, Shee dy row hiu; myr ta my Ayr er my choyrt's, myr shen ta mish coyrt shiuish   
43N||20||22||As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, heid eh orroo, as dooyrt eh roo, Gow-jee yn Spyrryd Noo.   
43N||20||23||Da quoi-erbee ta shiuish leih peccaghyn, t'ad er nyn leih daue; as da quoi erbee nagh vel shiu cur feaysley, cha vel ad feayshlit.   
43N||20||24||Agh cha row Thomase, fer jeh'n daa ostyl yeig va enmyssit Didymus, maroo tra haink Yeesey. 
43N||20||25||Dooyrt ny ostyllyn elley er-y-fa shen rish, Ta shin er vakin y Chiarn. Agh dooyrt eshyn roo, Mannagh vaikym ayns ny laueyn echey ynnyd ny treinaghyn, as mannagh derrym my vair ayns ynnyd ny treinaghyn, as my laue y choyrt stiagh ayns e lhiattee, cha greidym.   
43N||20||26||As lurg hoght laa reesht va ny ostyllyn echey sthie, as Thomase maroo: eisht haink Yeesey, as ny dorryssyn dooint, as hass eh kiongoyrt roo, as dooyrt eh, Shee dy row hiu.   
43N||20||27||Eisht dooyrt eh rish Thomase, Sheeyn ayns shoh dty vair, as loaghtee my laueyn; as sheeyn dty laue, as cur ee stiagh ayns my lhiattee: as ny bee mee-chredjuagh, agh credjuagh.   
43N||20||28||As dreggyr Thomase as dooyrt eh rish, My Hiarn, as my Yee.   
43N||20||29||Dooyrt Yeesey rishyn, Homase, Er-y fa dy vel oo er my akin, t'ou er chredjal; bannit t'adsyn nagh vel er vakin, as foast ta er chredjal.   
43N||20||30||As ymmodee cowraghyn elley dy jarroo ren Yeesey ayns fenish e ostyllyn, nagh vel scruit ayns y lioar shoh. 
43N||20||31||Agh t'ad shoh scruit, dy voddagh shiuish credjal dy nee Yeesey yn Creest Mac Yee, as liorish credjal shiu dy chosney bea trooid yn ennym echeysyn.
43N||21||1||LURG shoh hoilshee Yeesey eh-hene reesht da ny ostyllyn, ec faarkey Tiberias; as er yn aght shoh hoilshee eh eh-hene.   
43N||21||2||Va Simon Peddyr, as Thomase sliennooit Didymus, as Nathanael dy Chana ayns Galilee; as mec Zebedee, as jees elley jeh ny ostyllyn er nyn jaglym dy cheilley.   
43N||21||3||Dooyrt Simon Peddyr roo, Ta mish son goll dy eeastagh. Dooyrt adsyn rish, Hem mainyn myrgeddin mayrt. Hie ad magh, as er-y-chooyl ghow ad lhuingys; as yn oie shen cha haare ad monney.   
43N||21||4||Agh 'sy vadran, va Yeesey ny hassoo er y traie: agh cha row fys ec ny ostyllyn dy nee Yeesey v'ayn.   
43N||21||5||Eisht dooyrt Yeesey roo, Chloan, vel shiu er dayrtyn veg y veaghey? Dooyrt adsyn rish, Cha vel.   
43N||21||6||As dooyrt eh roo, Cuir-jee magh yn lieen er y cheu-yesh jeh'n lhong, as bee eh eu. Eisht chuir ad: as nish cha row dy niart oc yn lieen y ghoaill stiagh va lhied y thummyd eeast ayn.   
43N||21||7||Shen-y-fa dooyrt yn ostyl shen bynney lesh Yeesey rish Peddyr, She yn Chiarn t'ayn. Nish tra cheayll Simon Peddyr dy nee yn Chiarn v'ayn, hug eh e chooat-eeastee mysh (son v'eh 'sy lheiney) as hilg eh eh-hene ayns y cheayn.   
43N||21||8||As haink ny ostyllyn elley ayns lhong veg (son cha row ad foddey veih'n thalloo, agh mysh keead stundayrt) sleodey lhieu yn lieen as yn eeast ayn.   
43N||21||9||Cha leah eisht as v'ad er jeet gys y thalloo, honnick ad aile smarageagh, as eeast ny lhie er, as arran liorish.   
43N||21||10||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Cur-jee lhieu jeh'n eeast ta shiu nish er ghoaill.   
43N||21||11||Hie Simon Peddyr er-board, as hayrn eh yn lieen gys thalloo lane dy eeastyn mooarey, shiaght-feed as three-jeig: as son ooilley dy row whilleen ayn, ny-yeih cha vrish y lieen.   
43N||21||12||Dooyrt Yeesey roo, Tar-jee gys nyn mee. Agh cha by-lhoys da fer jeh ny ostyl nyn fenaght jeh, Quoi oo hene? cur enney er dy nee eh va'n Chiarn.   
43N||21||13||Eisht haink Yeesey, as ghow eh arran, as hirveish eh orroo eh, as eeast myrgeddin.   
43N||21||14||Shoh nish yn trass cheayrt hoilshee Yeesey eh-hene da e ostyllyn, erreish da v'er n'irree veill ny merriu.   
43N||21||15||Myr shen tra v'ad erreish bee, dooyrt Yeesey rish Simon Peddyr, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo ny s'graihlee orrym's na orroo shoh? Dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee, Hiarn; ta fys ayd dy vel graih aym ort. Dooyrt eh rish, Jeeagh dy mie da my eayin. 
43N||21||16||Dooyrt eh rish reesht yn nah cheayrt, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo graihagh orrym? Dooyrt eh rish, Ta mee, Hiarn; ta fys ayd hene dy vel graih aym ort. Dooyrt eh rish, Bee dty vochilley mie er my chirree.   
43N||21||17||Dooyrt eh rish yn trass cheayrt, Simon mac Yonas, vel oo graihagh orrym? Va Peddyr mooar-seaghnit dy dooyrt eh rish yn trass cheayrt, Vel oo graihagh orrym? As dooyrt eh rish, Hiarn, ta fys ayd's er dy chooilley nhee, as fys ayd hene dy vel mee graihagh ort. Dooyrt Yeesey rish, Jeeagh dy mie da my chirree.   
43N||21||18||Dy firrinagh firrinagh ta mee gra rhyt, Tra v'ou aeg ren oo oo-hene y chryssey, as jimmee oo raad erbee dy bailt: agh tra vees oo shenn, sheeynee oo magh dty laueyn, as nee fer elley oo y chryssey, as ver eh lesh oo raad nagh nailt.   
43N||21||19||Shoh loayr eh, cowraghey liorish cre'n baase v'eh dy ghloyraghey Jee. As tra v'eh er ghra shoh, dooyrt eh rish, Eiyr orrym.   
43N||21||20||Eisht hyndaa Peddyr mygeayrt, as honnick eh cheet geiyrt orroo yn ostyl bynney lesh Yeesey; yn fer cheddin ren lhie rish e oghrish ec shibber, as dooyrt Hiarn, quoi eh ta dy dty vrah?   
43N||21||21||Honnick Peddyr eh shoh, as dooyrt eh rish Yeesey, Hiarn, as cre'n erree hig er y dooinney shoh?   
43N||21||22||Dooyrt Yeesey rish, My she m'aigney's eh eshyn dy uirriaght derrey hig-ym, cre ta shen dhyt's? Eiyr uss orrym's.   
43N||21||23||Eisht hie yn raa shen magh mastey ny braaraghyn, nagh row yn ostyl shen dy gheddyn baase: agh cha dooyrt Yeesey rish, Cha vow eh baase: agh, My she m'aigney's eh eshyn dy uirriaght derrey hig-yms, cre ta shen dhyt's.  
43N||21||24||Shoh yn ostyl dymmyrk feanish jeh ny reddyn shoh, as ren ny reddyn shoh y scrieu: as ta fys ain dy vel yn eanish echey firrinagh.   
43N||21||25||As ta myrgeddin ymmodee reddyn elley ren Yeesey, dy beagh ad ooilley scruit, ta mee dy heiltyn nagh gummagh y seihll hene ny lioaryn veagh scruit. Amen.
